# Warehouse Management

<a id="enforce-strict-processes-for-packing-and-putaway"></a>
## Enforce Strict Processes For Packing And Putaway

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/enforce-strict-processes-for-packing-and-putaway_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Configuration
- Sale Orders
- Purchase Orders
- Barcodes
- Mobile app behaviour
- Strict processes

### Purpose

In CartonCloud it is possible to configure the mobile application to enforce a strict process for packing and put away.

This configuration is completed within the web app Organisation Settings.

### Configuration

To enable strict processes, in the main menu of CartonCloud, navigate to **More** > **Organisation Settings**.

Then, navigate to the **Warehouse** tab.

Within each section of Sale Order and Purchase Order configurations, there are settings to control how strict the verification and packing process should be. By default, these settings are disabled.

![enforce-strict-processes-for-packing-and-putaway-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/enforce-strict-processes-for-packing-and-putaway-0.png?width=670&height=525&name=enforce-strict-processes-for-packing-and-putaway-0.png)

### Sale Orders

- ***Prevent Sale Orders from being finished if products exist that have not been packed yet:***Stops packers from being able to "finish packing" a Sale Order that has some products whose expected quantities haven't been confirmed packed yet. By default, this is allowed and will automatically set all products of the Sale Order to the expected packed quantity, even if they have not yet been confirmed in the app.
- ***Enforce Strict Process:***Packers will be required to first scan a location, then a product to confirm its quantity. They can not simply select a product from the Sale Order's product list and confirm its quantity.

### Purchase Orders

- ***Prevent Purchase Orders from being verified if unconfirmed quantities exist:***Stops warehouse staff from being able to verify a purchase order as entered the warehouse if it contains unconfirmed product quantities. By default, this is possible and automatically confirms the product quantities with their current values, even if that means confirming a product with quantity 0.
- ***Enforce Strict Process:***Warehouse staff will be required to first scan a product, then proceed with either verifying or allocating the scanned product. In the case of allocation, this requires either a location scan or a manual location search. In the case of verifying, the product quantity needs to be confirmed.

The web app settings mentioned above cannot be modified from within the mobile app, meaning Packers cannot adjust whether or not to follow a strict process.

### Barcodes

If enforce strict process is enabled then pickers will be forced to scan each product out of the warehouse as quantities cannot be entered manually.

If you have not specified a barcode value when creating products in CartonCloud then the system will automatically populate the field of the base unit of measure with its product code.

![enforce-strict-processes-for-packing-and-putaway-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/enforce-strict-processes-for-packing-and-putaway-1.png?width=670&height=220&name=enforce-strict-processes-for-packing-and-putaway-1.png)

### Mobile app behaviour

Should any of the strict settings have been applied, the mobile app user will be informed about the steps to successfully pack or confirm a product (see example screenshots below).

### Strict Processes

The following processes are the ones being enforced should the corresponding strict setting have been activated:

**Scan Picking (Sale Orders)**

- ***Pack:***
  - 1. Scan Location
  - 2. Scan Product

**Scan Putaway (Purchase Orders)**

- ***Verify:***
  - 1. Scan Product
  - 2. Confirm Product Quantities (may happen automatically if only one product matches scanned product barcode)
- ***Allocate:***
  - 1. Scan Product
  - 2. Scan Location (or use Manual Location Entry)

---

<a id="scanning-custom-format-barcodes"></a>
## Scanning Custom Format Barcodes

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/scanning-custom-format-barcodes_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use cases for custom format barcodes
- How to set up custom format barcodes

### Purpose

The CartonCloud mobile app can scan standard format product barcodes by default, however, if you wish to scan a custom format barcode, for example a GS-1 label then you require additional set up steps. These steps include defining Regular Expressions which enable the extraction of certain infromation from the product barcode, for example, the expiry date.

### Use cases for custom format barcodes

There are two ways in which you can use Regular Expression for custom barcodes.

(1) To extract information from the barcode - if you have GS1 or SSCC barcodes which you wish to scan and extract certain information from, such as batch number or expiry date.

(2) To define the length of the barcode - to ensure that only barcodes with a certain length, for example 44 digits long are scanned. If the barcode isn't 44 digits long it will error.

### How to set up custom format barcodes

- Set up the field you wish to capture with the barcode as a Purchase Order Product Custom Field. Follow the steps here .
- Once you have set up the Purchase Order Product Custom Field you will need to create the Regular Expression (Regex). You will need the barcode you will be using to help define the Regex.
- Navigate to the Regex Definitions page by typing Regex Definitions into the Search for anything.
- Click +Add Regex Definition .
- Enter a Name for the Regex and then add the Regex. The Regex will define where in the barcode the information needs to be pulled from. There are some example Regex below, however to learn more about about Regular Expressions, use [https://regex101.com/](https://regex101.com/) which allows you to create and test your own Regular Expressions against real data.

![scanning-custom-format-barcodes-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/scanning-custom-format-barcodes-1.png?width=670&height=222&name=scanning-custom-format-barcodes-1.png)

**Example Regex Definitions:**

| Name | Regex | Use case |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Best Before Date | "15(\d{6})" | To obtain the best before date from the GS1 barcode. |
| Net Weight | /^3102(.{6})$/ | To obtain the net weight from the GS1 barcode. |
| GS1 44 digits | "(^\d{44})$" | To only accept barcodes that are 44 digits long |

If you require assistance setting up your Regex definitions please reach out to the CartonCloud team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

- Once you have created your Regex, navigate back to the relevant Purchase Order Product Custom Field.
- Against the relevant Custom Field, select the relevant Regex Definition from the drop down menu.

![scanning-custom-format-barcodes-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/scanning-custom-format-barcodes-2.png?width=670&height=187&name=scanning-custom-format-barcodes-2.png)

- Scroll down and click Save.
- Repeat this process for the number of different Custom Fields you wish to use custom barcodes for. Note, you can have multiple Custom Fields for one barcode, however, you will need to scan the barcode for each custom field. You can't scan the barcode once and all custom fields related to that barcode are filled in at once. You will have to scan it each time for each custom field.

---

<a id="shipments"></a>
## Shipments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/shipments_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Shipment?
- Shipment Custom Fields
- How to create a Shipment
- How to associate a Container and Purchase Order to a Shipment

### What is a Shipment

A Shipment in CartonCloud is an order before it reaches your warehouse. You can associate Purchase Orders and Containers with Shipments.

### Shipment Custom Fields

Shipment Custom Fields allow you to record custom information against each Shipment. To create a Shipment Custom Field follow the instructions here - [Introduction to Custom Field](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Introduction-to-Custom-Fields). It is recommended you include the below when creating your Shipment Custom Fields:

- Reference number
- Estimated arrival date

### How to create a Shipment

- Navigate to the Shipment page by typing Shipments into the Search for anything bar.
- Click +Add in the top left corner.
- Enter the Shipment details and click Save .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-20-2025-12-49-32-7045-AM.png?width=670&height=309&name=image-png-Nov-20-2025-12-49-32-7045-AM.png)

### How to associate a Container and/or Purchase Order to the Container

- Navigate to the relevant Shipment.
- Click the Containers and/or Purchase Order tab.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-20-2025-12-50-42-8901-AM.png?width=670&height=268&name=image-png-Nov-20-2025-12-50-42-8901-AM.png)

- Click +Add Container or + Add Purchase Order .
- Click Go on the search and tick the relevant Container/Purchase Order to associate with the Shipment.

- Scroll down and select Add Selected Purchase Orders / Add Selected Containers.

---

<a id="warehouse-pod-setup"></a>
## Warehouse POD Setup

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/warehouse-pod-setup_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- Setup Steps

### Purpose

The Warehouse POD (Proof Of Delivery) Module is an Add-On feature available for CartonCloud Warehouse accounts.

The POD functionally allows for pick-up from warehouse orders to be signed for upon collection. This helps to ensure you have a record of when and who collected the order.

It is recommended that a device (tablet or similar) be situated in a central location and logged in as the user who has access to the POD feature (one driver user is allocated with the Warehouse POD module). This enables a seamless process when the order is collected and the driver can sign for the collection easily.

### Prerequisities

If you are a Warehouse-only CartonCloud account (do not have access to the Transport module), then the Warehouse POD module is a paid add-on. Please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) for more information and to get access.

### Setup Steps

1. **Enable the** **'Automatically generate a Consignment from a Sale Order'**
  - Enable this setting for the Customer/s you wish to use the Warehouse POD module for.
  - This setting is found at the Customer settings level. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Warehouse-Management#consignment) for more information.
2. **Set up Transport Products**
  - This allows you to enter what is being picked up from the warehouse (e.g a pallet).
  - This is an optional step, but it is advised.
  - See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Setting-up-Transport-Products) for steps on creating Transport Products.
3. **Map Product Units of Measure to Transport Products**
  - This allows for a seamless flow from Sale Order to Consignment and ensures the correct Transport Products are added from the Sale Order.
  - See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products) for steps on how to map Product Units of Measure to Transport Products.
4. **Set up Driver User**
  - Create a new user and assign it to the Driver role.
  - This is the user who will be logged into the device situated in a central location for driver sign off upon collection.
  - See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Creating-or-Inviting-New-Users) for steps on how to create a new user.
  - Once the user is created, you will need to select Edit Delivery Runs and assign the Pickup from Warehouse Delivery Run to the user.
5. **POD Email Notification**
  - If you wish the customer to receive the POD notification, you can set this up at the Customer Settings. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Customer-Settings-Email-Notifications) for more information.
6. Rate Card
  - To ensure no transport rates are charged, you will need to follow the steps below:
    - Add a new Rate Card and call it '**No Charge**'.
    - Add a new Zone Set called Warehouse POD and select **Income** as the Type.
![warehouse-pod-setup-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/warehouse-pod-setup-0.png?width=670&height=177&name=warehouse-pod-setup-0.png)

1.
  -
    - Assign Zone definitions by selecting Add the first one to get started .
    -
    - Select **+Add Entry**.
    - Select the relevant Country and then select **All** for Zone.
    -
    - Navigate to the Rate Card created in the first step and select the Transport Rates tab.
    - Add a new rate.
    - Ensure you select From and To Zone as **All**.
    - Select **Yes** against **No Charge**.
    -
    - Against the Customer's Rate Card, select **Transport Rates** > **Rate Card Cascade**. Select the **No Charge** Rate Card.
2. Pick Up Delivery Run

-
  - Navigate to the Delivery Runs page, **Transport** > **Delivery Runs**.
  - Select the Pickup from Warehouse Delivery Run.
  - Select the **Details** tab and click **Edit**.
  - Click the drop down arrow for Advanced Options.
  - Update the **Final Consignment Delivery Status** to **Collected**.
  - Click **Save**.

---

# Warehouse Management > Products

<a id="Add-a-Product"></a>
## Add a Product

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/Add-a-Product_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Adding a single product
- Bulk Importing Products
- Video Guide

### Purpose

To create a single Product or to create multiple products in bulk.

### Adding a single product

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Select **+Add Product**.

![add-a-product-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-product-0.jpeg?width=670&height=149&name=add-a-product-0.jpeg)

- Using the below field descriptions, fill in the relevant information.

**Product Fields**

| Field | Required | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Customer | Yes | The Customer associated with the Product. A Product can only be used and associated with one single Customer, however, you can create multiple products (one for each customer) with the same name and code. | Yatala Pie Shop |
| Name | Yes | The name of the product. | Beef Pie 1 x 110gm |
| Product Code | Yes | The code / SKU for the product that your customer refers to. This is used for matching when importing orders via [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers) or through [Available Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Available-Integrations) Please note, each Product Code for a Customer must be unique. You can not have the same Product Code for Products for the same Customer. *Only UTF-8 Special characters are supported in the product code. For a list of supported special characters please click [here](https://www.fileformat.info/info/charset/UTF-8/list.htm)* | BEEF110 |
| Tags | No | If you wish to associate any Tags with the Product. See [Tags](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Tags) for more information. |  |
| Product Description | Optional | Additional information about the product can be displayed on documents such as picking slips, consignment notes, and other exports. | Made from 100% premium quality grass-fed Angus beef |
| Product Type | Yes | The product type of this product. This is often used to restrict where in the warehouse the product can be stored (i.e., Temperature Zones or Dangerous / Non-Dangerous goods). However, it is also used to control Storage Charges, see [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for more information.   See [Product Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Types) for more information. | Chilled |
| Storage Charge Method | Yes | How Storage Charges are applied to this product. See [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for specific details on how each Storage Charge Method works. | Per Location |
| Product Volume | No | The volume of the product in cubic meters (L x W x H). This can be used to control Storage Charges (see [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for more information) and can also be used to automatically populate the cubic of a Consignment | 0.0034 |
| Product Weight | No | The weight of the product is in kilograms. This can be used to control Storage Charges and can also be used to automatically populate the weight of a Consignment.      The unit of measure the product weight is displayed in can be changed from the Organisation Settings. Please see [Changing the unit of measure in your tenancy](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Changing-the-unit-of-measure-in-your-tenancy) | 0.110 |
| Country of Origin | No | The Country of Origin of the product. This is useful if needing the Country of Origin for import/export purposes. | Australia |
| HS Code | No | The Harmonized System Code (HS Code) is an international standard for classifying products in cross-border trade. Adding the correct HS Code to your products ensures compliance with customs regulations and accurate calculation of duties and taxes. | 6601.99 |
| Product Group | No | If you wish to add the Product to a Product Group. See [Product Group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Group) for more information. |  |
| Product Group | No | The Product Group is utilised to filter the Product List and in the Customer Stock Report. See [Product Group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Group) for more information. |  |
| Product Unit of Measure |  |  |  |
| Measurement Category | Yes | The way in which the product will be measured. For example, if you measure the products in Units, Cartons, Inners etc, the Measurement Category will be Count. | Count |
| Base Measurement | Yes | The smallest pickable [unit of measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products+Units+of+Measure) for this product (or can be the measurement the client wants to see the product measured in). For example, we may sell them individually as units with our Beef Pie example, so the Base Measurement is "Unit". See [Products Units of Measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products+Units+of+Measure) for more information. | Unit |
| Barcode |  | The barcode for the Base Measurement (i.e., the Barcode on a single unit). Note you can define different barcodes for the different size packs using the Conversion Measurements below. The barcodes can the be used on the mobile app for scan picking and putaway. | 10003998392 |
| +Add New Measurement |  | If you wish to add a new Product Unit of Measure upon adding conversions you can do so by clicking **+Add New Measurement**.  ![add-a-product-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-product-1.jpeg?width=670&height=111&name=add-a-product-1.jpeg)      Enter the information for the new Product Unit of Measure. If mapping the Product Unit of Measure to a Transport Product/Consignment Field and Product Type you can do so from here. See [Mapping Product Unit of Measures to Consignment Fields/Transport Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products)  for more information.    ![add-a-product-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-product-2.jpeg?width=670&height=420&name=add-a-product-2.jpeg) |  |
| + Add Another Conversion |  | By clicking **Add Another Conversion**you can add conversion measurements. For example, with the Beef Pies example, you have may have 10 pies in 1 Carton. You would add a Conversion Measurement of Carton with a Conversion Factor of 10.  Ensure you take note of the Example column when adding the conversion to ensure you have set it up correctly.   ![Add a Product_4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Add%20a%20Product_4.jpeg?width=670&height=57&name=Add%20a%20Product_4.jpeg) If you wish to add another conversion you can select **+Add Another Conversion**. With the Beef Pie example, you may add a pallet conversion, you have 48 cartons per pallet so you would have 480 units per pallet.  ![add-a-product-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-product-3.jpeg?width=670&height=56&name=add-a-product-3.jpeg)      *It's also important to note that each measurement can have its own barcode. This allows you to scan a Carton and have it register that you've picked 10 units or scan an entire pallet to receive in 480.* | Measure: Carton Conversion Factor: 10  Example: 10 Units per Carton |
| Random Weight Product |  | A random weight product is a product whereby the weight of each unit that's picked needs to be recorded. For example, this is common when packing cartons of meat, in which each carton is a slightly different weight, and the customer charges per Kilo. For example, you may have boxes of expensive sirloin steaks; each weighs approximately 20kg; however, each box varies. By making a product random weight, when picking items, the user must enter the exact weight of each item (i.e., 19.45kg); this information is then sent back to the customer in their [Pack Notification Email](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Configuring+Outgoing+Notification+Emails+to+Customers) to bill the receiver for exactly 19.45kg. | No |
| Warning Threshold |  | The number of days before expiration in which CartonCloud will send out an automated email advising the stock will be expiring in x number of days. This is useful for advising clients that their stock will expire soon and should be cleared out (possibly through a discount or promotion). This email can be configured through the [Configuring Outgoing Notification Emails to Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers) | 10 |
| Expiry Threshold |  | The number of days before expiration that the product will no longer be automatically selected on import. For example, products within 2 days of expiration probably shouldn't be sent out to customers as they won't last long enough once they arrive. Therefore, if an expiry threshold of 2 was used, the stock will no longer be selected automatically if the order is within two days of expiration.      *Note, however; you can manually select stock for an order which is either Expired or within the Expiry Threshold.* | 2 |
| Product Custom Fields |  | If you have Product Custom Fields enabled, fields you have defined will appear on the screen for entry. For example: "Supplier Code."   See: [Product Custom Fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Fields) for more information |  |
| Low Stock Threshold |  | This is the quantity in which the stock levels are considered low and requires attention. When the stock on hand hits this number, a [Low Stock Notification](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Configuring+Outgoing+Notification+Emails+to+Customers) will be sent. This email can be configured through the [Configuring Outgoing Notification Emails to Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers) |  |
| Initial Status of Purchase Order Product | Yes | When assigning stock to a Purchase Order, this value sets the Product Status of that stock. For example, if you selected "Quarantine", all stocks created would default to Quarantine Status. You can modify and create your own [Product Status](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Statuses) if required. | OK |
| Stock Selection Method | Yes | When assigning stock for a Sale Order, this determines how the system will pick a stock. See the article: [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/How+CartonCloud+chooses+outgoing+stock+-+Stock+Selection+Methods) for more information.   Warehouse location pick efficiency only.   FEFO (First Expiry First Out) - Closest expiry date is selected first.   FIFO (First In First Out) - Longest time since arrival is selected first.   LIFO (Last In First Out) - Shortest time since arrival is selected first. | FIFO |
| If finished Bill of Material products (BOMs) are out of stock, take from individual components during Sale Order import. |  | This setting is only relevant for the Bill of Material Products - Products made up of other products (such as a Hamper).   As per customer default setting - This setting for the Product will be enabled or disabled depending on what the Customer's Setting is set to.   Yes - A finished BOM product will be created by picking the individual products that make up that product.   No - If the finished BOM product is out of stock, the entire Sale order will be rejected.   See the [Bill of Materials (BOM)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Bill-of-Materials-BOM) article for further details. |  |
| Reallocation |  | To turn reallocation on or off for this product. By default the reallocation setting applied at the customer level will be applied to the product. See [Reallocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Reallocation) for more information.  Drop down options  As per customer default setting - will apply the settings set up at the customer level  No - reallocation will not be enabled for this product Yes - reallocation will be enabled for this product    Scannable Field: if using reallocation you will need to select a field that can be used to reallocate with |  |
| Purchase Order Product Expiry Date Required? |  | Determines whether the expiry date field is required for Purchase Order Products that use this product (see [Purchase Order Products Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Custom+Fields+for+Purchase+Order+Products)). |  |
| Purchase Order Product Custom Fields Required? (per field) |  | Determines whether each custom field is required for Purchase Order Products that use this product (see [Purchase Order Products Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Custom+Fields+for+Purchase+Order+Products)). |  |

- Click Save .

### Bulk Importing Products (Export/Import CSV)

Once you have created your first Product, you can create Products in bulk using the export/import function.

See [Exporting and Importing Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/exporting-and-importing-products)  for steps on creating Products in bulk.

### Video Guide

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/U0Ul0roLX4o

<a id="add-a-product"></a>
## Add a Product

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-a-product_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Adding a single product
- Bulk Importing Products
- Video Guide

### Purpose

To create a single Product or to create multiple products in bulk.

### Adding a single product

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Select **+Add Product**.

![add-a-product-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-product-0.jpeg?width=670&height=149&name=add-a-product-0.jpeg)

- Using the below field descriptions, fill in the relevant information.

**Product Fields**

| Field | Required | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Customer | Yes | The Customer associated with the Product. A Product can only be used and associated with one single Customer, however, you can create multiple products (one for each customer) with the same name and code. | Yatala Pie Shop |
| Name | Yes | The name of the product. | Beef Pie 1 x 110gm |
| Product Code | Yes | The code / SKU for the product that your customer refers to. This is used for matching when importing orders via [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers) or through [Available Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Available-Integrations) Please note, each Product Code for a Customer must be unique. You can not have the same Product Code for Products for the same Customer. *Only UTF-8 Special characters are supported in the product code. For a list of supported special characters please click [here](https://www.fileformat.info/info/charset/UTF-8/list.htm)* | BEEF110 |
| Tags | No | If you wish to associate any Tags with the Product. See [Tags](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Tags) for more information. |  |
| Product Description | Optional | Additional information about the product can be displayed on documents such as picking slips, consignment notes, and other exports. | Made from 100% premium quality grass-fed Angus beef |
| Product Type | Yes | The product type of this product. This is often used to restrict where in the warehouse the product can be stored (i.e., Temperature Zones or Dangerous / Non-Dangerous goods). However, it is also used to control Storage Charges, see [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for more information.   See [Product Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Types) for more information. | Chilled |
| Storage Charge Method | Yes | How Storage Charges are applied to this product. See [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for specific details on how each Storage Charge Method works. | Per Location |
| Product Volume | No | The volume of the product in cubic meters (L x W x H). This can be used to control Storage Charges (see [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for more information) and can also be used to automatically populate the cubic of a Consignment | 0.0034 |
| Product Weight | No | The weight of the product is in kilograms. This can be used to control Storage Charges and can also be used to automatically populate the weight of a Consignment.      The unit of measure the product weight is displayed in can be changed from the Organisation Settings. Please see [Changing the unit of measure in your tenancy](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Changing-the-unit-of-measure-in-your-tenancy) | 0.110 |
| Country of Origin | No | The Country of Origin of the product. This is useful if needing the Country of Origin for import/export purposes. | Australia |
| HS Code | No | The Harmonized System Code (HS Code) is an international standard for classifying products in cross-border trade. Adding the correct HS Code to your products ensures compliance with customs regulations and accurate calculation of duties and taxes. | 6601.99 |
| Product Group | No | If you wish to add the Product to a Product Group. See [Product Group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Group) for more information. |  |
| Product Group | No | The Product Group is utilised to filter the Product List and in the Customer Stock Report. See [Product Group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Group) for more information. |  |
| Product Unit of Measure |  |  |  |
| Measurement Category | Yes | The way in which the product will be measured. For example, if you measure the products in Units, Cartons, Inners etc, the Measurement Category will be Count. | Count |

<a id="bill-of-materials-bom"></a>
## Bill of Materials (BOM)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/bill-of-materials-bom_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use Cases
- How to steps
  - Create a new Product for the Bill of Material Product
  - Add Products to the Bill of Material
  - Build Bill of Materials stock OR use existing individual product stock
    - To pick from the existing individual product stock
    - To build Bill of Materials stock
- Update Bill of Material

### Purpose

Bill of Materials (BOM) in CartonCloud is a combination of Products that make up one Product. Bill of Materials can also be referred to as kitting. Kitting (in warehouse terms) is used to combine multiple products into a single unit that is then sold to end customers. For example, products that result from kitting include hampers, gift packages, subscription boxes and bundles.

Bill of Materials facilitate the Product building process and allow you to track stock for the resulting Product.

### Use Cases

For example, if your Customer is a coffee company they may sell an International Coffee Hamper to their customers. This hamper contains 3 x bags of beans from Brazil, 2 x bags from Costa Rica and 1 x bag from Tanzania. Each of these bags of coffee would be set up as their own individual Product in CartonCloud.

By creating a Bill of Materials, you can combine these Products to create the International Coffee Hamper Product. This means that when a new order is received containing the International Coffee Hamper Product, CartonCloud will inform the picker of what individual products will need to be included to create the final Bill of Materials Product (the International Coffee Hamper).

### How To Steps

If you are creating multiple Bill of Materials and have already created the Products needed for the Bill of Materials you can use the export and import feature to create your new Bill of Materials. See the [Exporting and Importing Bill of Materials](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/eAFpIQ) page for more information.

To create a Bill of Material, you will need to:

**1. Create a new Product for the Bill of Material Product**

- Create a new Product for the Bill of Material product. This will be the final Product that is a combination of existing Products. In the example scenario, this would be a Product called 'International Coffee Hamper'.
- Please see the [Add a Product](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Add+a+Product) page for steps on how to create a new Product.

**2. Add Products to the Bill of Material**

- Navigate to the Product, **Warehouse**>**Products** and select the relevant Product.
- Select the Bill of Materials tab.

![bill-of-materials-bom-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-0.png?width=670&height=189&name=bill-of-materials-bom-0.png)

- In the Product Bill of Materials window, you can add the Products that make up the Product you are viewing.
- Search for the Product in the **Search for a Product bar**, enter the quantity in the **Quantity** box and then click the green **+** button to add the Product.

![bill-of-materials-bom-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-1.png?width=670&height=173&name=bill-of-materials-bom-1.png)
![bill-of-materials-bom-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-2.png?width=670&height=189&name=bill-of-materials-bom-2.png)

- Repeat the above step until all Products which make up the end Product have been added.
- Click Save .

![bill-of-materials-bom-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-3.png?width=670&height=278&name=bill-of-materials-bom-3.png)

**3. Build Bill of Materials stock OR use existing individual product stock**

Once you have created the Bill of Materials there are two options for how you pick the stock. You can either;

(a) **pick from the existing individual product stock** (this option is only available if you are importing Sale Orders not manually creating them in CartonCloud, however, there is a work around if adding the order manually. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com#manually-add-BOM-products-to-a-sale-order) for more details) or;

(b) **build Bill of Materials stock and only pick from that available stock** (if you choose this option you will need to physically bundle the stock before picking otherwise your pickers will not know what products are associated with the BOM as CartonCloud will not list them when picking).

It is recommended that you pick from the existing individual product stock as this prevents you from having to manually build the BOM stock in CartonCloud and avoids the risk of stock shortages. You can only choose this option if you are importing Sale Orders not manually creating them in CartonCloud.

**To pick from the existing individual product stock**

Note: this option is only available if you are importing Sale Orders not manually creating them in CartonCloud.

When a Sale Order is received containing BOM products, by default, CartonCloud will only assign BOM stock to fulfil the order and not look at the individual product stock. This workflow relies on the fact that you are physically building your Bill of Materials and then replicating this in CartonCloud by creating Bill of Materials stock. If you do not wish to follow this workflow and would rather build the Bill of Materials as you are picking (pick individual products to then create the Bill of Materials product) you will need to change the Product and/or Customer Settings.

This setting is called **If finished Bill of Material Products (BOMs) are out of stock, take from individual components** and can be configured from either the **Customer** or **Product** settings.

**Customer Setting**

This setting will apply to all Products belonging to that Customer. If you want to change each product's settings individually, you will need to configure this at the Product settings.
To allow BOM products for a customer to be built during Sale Order import:

- Navigate to the Customers page, Contacts>Customers.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Select the blue **Edit** button towards the bottom left of the page.
- Select the **Warehouse Management** tab and then the **Sale Order** sub-tab.
- Scroll down to the setting **If finished Bill of Material products (BOMs) are out of stock, take from individual components.**
- Select **Yes** from the drop-down menu.

![bill-of-materials-bom-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-4.png?width=670&height=384&name=bill-of-materials-bom-4.png)

- Scroll to the bottom of the page and select **Save**.
- Imported Sale Orders for that Customer will now take individual products to build a Bill of Materials Product when required.

**Product Setting**

This setting will only apply to the particular Product. By default, the Product setting will use the Customer setting; however, this setting will be overridden if the Product setting is changed.
**To allow specific BOM products to be built during Sale Order import:**

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouses**>**Products**.
- Select the relevant Product.
- Select the green **Edit** button in the top left of the page.
- Scroll down towards the bottom of the page until you see the setting **If finished Bill of Material products (BOMs) are out of stock, take from individual components during Sale Order import.**
- Change the setting to **Yes** from the drop-down menu.
- Select **Save**.

![bill-of-materials-bom-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-5.png?width=511&height=377&name=bill-of-materials-bom-5.png)

- Imported Sale Orders containing the Bill of Materials Product will now take individual products to build that BOM product if required.

**To build Bill of Materials stock**

Note: Note, if you are choosing to pick Bill of Materials stock you will need to physically bundle the stock before picking otherwise your pickers will not know what products are associated with the BOM as CartonCloud will not list them when picking.

- Within the **Build Product From Product Bill Of Materials** window, enter the number of products you wish to generate from the Bill of Materials in the **Quantity To Create** window.
- When you enter a quantity in the Quantity to Create window, the Available, Used and Remaining columns will update.
- Click the green **Build** button.

**What is available, used and remaining stock?**

- Available - The available stock based on the **Minimum Purchase Order Product Status** in the **Warehouse Management** tab of the [Customer settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Edit+Customer+or+Customer+Settings)for the Customer that the Product belongs to
- Used - Quantity To Create multiplied by the ratio that makes up that product (which can be seen under the "One" column).
- Remaining - Available stock minus the used stock

Note: You must create stock for the Bill of Materials Product; otherwise, when a Sale Order is generated containing the Bill of Materials Product, there will be no stock to add to the Sale Order. However, the exception to this is if the Sale Order is created using the **import feature** and the correct **Customer and Product settings are configured,** then CartonCloud will take stock from the individual Products if the Bill of Materials Product stock is depleted. Please see the [Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=536609777#BillofMaterials(BOM)-settings) section of this article for more information.

![bill-of-materials-bom-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-6.png?width=564&height=234&name=bill-of-materials-bom-6.png)

CartonCloud will automatically create a corresponding Purchase Order and Sale Order in the system as a reference for the activity when you create a build. Creating the Sale Order will ensure the stock is not available for new Sale Orders that come through containing the Bill of Materials Product. In addition, creating the Purchase Order will allow you to allocate the stock to its own Warehouse Location. This stock will then be available for picking when required (when a new Sale Order containing the Bill of Materials Product is received).

- A pop-out window will appear, prompting you to enter a reference for the build and asking if you wish to make the Purchase Order and Sale Order records generated from this build as "adjustments". If you mark them as 'adjustments', then they will not charge the Customer.

![bill-of-materials-bom-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-7.png?width=488&height=352&name=bill-of-materials-bom-7.png)
If you wish to add additional Product quantities to an existing build and the resulting Purchase Order and Sale Order, you can do so by repeating the above build process. However, at the end, when the pop-out window appears, select **Add to an Existing Adjustment Reference From Today**(provided it is the same day).

**Manually add BOM products to a Sale Order (that haven't been built)**

- From the new Sale Order you have created, click Add Products.
- Search for the BOM you are wanting to add to the order.
- Type in the quantity in QTY field.
- Click Search .

![bill-of-materials-bom-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-8.png?width=670&height=138&name=bill-of-materials-bom-8.png)

- See that there is no stock available as no BOM products have been pre-built in CartonCloud.

![bill-of-materials-bom-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-9.png?width=670&height=177&name=bill-of-materials-bom-9.png)

- Click Add Without Assigning Stock .

![bill-of-materials-bom-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-10.png?width=670&height=177&name=bill-of-materials-bom-10.png)

- Click Auto Assign All Unassigned Stock .

![bill-of-materials-bom-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-11.png?width=670&height=150&name=bill-of-materials-bom-11.png)

- See that the child products of the BOM product have been added to the order.

![bill-of-materials-bom-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-12.png?width=670&height=162&name=bill-of-materials-bom-12.png)

### Update a Bill of Materials

You can change the Products or quantities that make up the Bill of Materials at any time.

Updating the Bill of Materials will not affect historical data related to past builds of that Product. For example, if the hamper contains 3 x bags of Brazilian coffee but now only contains 2, the previous adjustment Sale Orders (created from the build) will not change.

If you are updating multiple Bill of Materials you can do so using the export and import function. See the [Exporting and Importing Bill of Materials](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom) page for more information.

**To delete an existing product:**

![bill-of-materials-bom-13](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-13.png?width=670&height=308&name=bill-of-materials-bom-13.png)

- Select the red minus button.
- Once changes have been made, select **Save**.

**To update the quantity of a Product:**

- Enter a new number in the **Quantity** field.

![bill-of-materials-bom-14](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-14.png?width=670&height=308&name=bill-of-materials-bom-14.png)

- Once changes have been made, select **Save**.

**To add a new Product:**

- Use the **Search for a Product** bar, enter the quantity in the **Quantity**field and select the green **+** button.

![bill-of-materials-bom-15](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bill-of-materials-bom-15.png?width=670&height=308&name=bill-of-materials-bom-15.png)

**To clear a Bill of Material:**

- Select the red **Clear Bill** button at the bottom of the screen.
- A browser prompt will appear to check that you are sure as this cannot be undone.

---

<a id="cross-customer-picking"></a>
## Cross Customer Picking

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/cross-customer-picking_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Considerations
- How to turn on Cross Customer Picking

### Purpose

Cross customer picking allows any product (regardless of Customer) to be added to any Sale Order. This is useful if you have Customers in your warehouse that share products.

For example, if you have two Customers and each has one Product:
Customer A → Leg of Ham
Customer B → Balloons

Normally, CartonCloud would prevent you from creating a Sale Order for Customer B and adding a Leg of Ham to it. However, by turning on Cross Customer Picking you're enabling this functionality. With Cross Customer Picking, any product can be added to any Sale Order.

### Considerations

Turning on this setting will be applied to **every Customer** in your tenancy. This means, that any product for any customer will be able to be added to any Sale Order.

### How to turn on Cross Customer Picking

- Navigate to More > Organisation Settings .
- Select the Warehouse tab.
- Scroll down to Cross Customer Picking and enable Allow adding any customers stock to any Sale Order .
- Click Save .

---

<a id="customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold"></a>
## Customer Specific Shelf Life (Expiry Threshold)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Step 1 - Create an Address Custom Field
- Step 2 - Create Customer Product Custom Fields
- Step 3 - Edit Product Settings
- Step 4 - Update the Address String
- Testing

### Purpose

It is a common requirement when working with food items to deliver stock that has a Minimum Life on Receipt (known as MLOR or Receiving Limit). Each retailer and or customer will have their own policy in place for handling this requirement, including their own specific limits. CartonCloud has the ability to handle this requirement by setting up an Expiry Threshold Group.

Note, this is separate from the Expiry Threshold setting that sits against the Product Settings.

### Step 1 - Create an Address Custom Field

The delivery address custom field will be used to record the specific MLOR value.

For example, a sale order or consignment going to Woolworths may have stock that requires an MLOR of 185 days. Creating this field against the delivery address points the system to use the specific MLOR setting for Woolworths.

To create the Custom Field:

- Navigate to the Custom Fields page by typing Custom Fields into the Search for anything bar.
- Select Address > +Add Custom Field .
- Name the field, custom_expiry_threshold_group.

Note, the field name MUST be exactly **custom_expiry_threshold_group**

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-0.png?width=670&height=326&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-0.png)

### Step 2 - Create Customer Product Custom Fields

To create a Customer Product Custom Field:

- Navigate to Contacts > Customers .
- Select the relevant Customer and click Edit .
- Select the Warehouse > Product tab.
- Name the Custom Field. The name MUST start with Expiry Threshold Days.
- Create the required number of fields.

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-1.png?width=670&height=375&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-1.png)

### Step 3 - Edit Product Settings

- Navigate to the Product page, Warehouse > Products .
- Select the relevant Product and Edit .
- Update the Stock Selection Method to "FEFO By Address Group"

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-2.png?width=670&height=305&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-2.png)

### Step 4 - Update the Address Setting

Whenever a new address (or existing address during the set-up phase) is added to CartonCloud, the Expiry Threshold Group custom fields **MUST** be updated.

This field is the link between the product settings and the stock selection process based on the Delivery Address for a specific customer.

**For new Addresses:**

- Navigate to Addresses by typing Addresses into the Search for anything bar.
- Select +Add Address .
- Update the MLOR Threshold Group.

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-3.png?width=670&height=427&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-3.png)

**For existing Addresses:**

- Navigate to Addresses by typing Addresses into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the relevant Address and click Edit.
- Update the threshold group.
- Click Save.

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-4.png?width=670&height=409&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-4.png)

From the view page, the selected Expiry Threshold Group will be set

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-5.png?width=670&height=408&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-5.png)

### Testing

In this following example, the customer is delivering to a Woolworths Store.

The Expiry Threshold for this Product and the Woolworths store is set to 195

Creation date for the Sale Order is 24/03/2021

This means that the stock selected for this Sale Order MUST have an expiry date > 05/10/2021

You can use a [Date Calculator](https://www.timeanddate.com/date/dateadded.html?d1=24&m1=3&y1=2021&type=add&ay=&am=&aw=&ad=195&rec=) to quickly work out the expected date.

The Product being used has 3 expiry dates available in the warehouse:

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-6.png?width=670&height=368&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-6.png)

A sales order has been created using a delivery address to a Woolworths store:

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-7.png?width=670&height=418&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-7.png)

Now add the product:

![customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-8.png?width=670&height=414&name=customer-specific-shelf-life-expiry-threshold-8.png)
CartonCloud had taken the settings for the Expiry Threshold Group and the delivery address and selected the stock that has an expiry date > 195 days.

<a id="deactivating-and-reactivating-products"></a>
## Deactivating and Reactivating Products

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/deactivating-and-reactivating-products_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use cases
- How to deactivate a product
- How to reactivate a product
- How to reactivate or deactivate products in bulk

### Purpose

Products can not be deleted as they may be in use by other records such as Purchase Order Products. For this reason, the only way to remove Products from being visible is to deactivate them.

Once you have deactivated a product you are able to reactivate it at any time.

### Use cases

- Your customer no longer stocks a certain product.

### How to deactivate a Product

- Navigate to the Products page, Warehouse > Products .
- Select the relevant Product.
- Select the red Deactivate button.

![deactivating-and-reactivating-products-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deactivating-and-reactivating-products-0.png?width=670&height=195&name=deactivating-and-reactivating-products-0.png)

- You will then receive a success message and see a new red banner informing you that the Product is deactivated.

![deactivating-and-reactivating-products-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deactivating-and-reactivating-products-1.png?width=670&height=195&name=deactivating-and-reactivating-products-1.png)

### How to reactivate a product

- Navigate to the Products page, Warehouse > Products .
- Select the relevant Product.
- Select the green Reactivate button.

![deactivating-and-reactivating-products-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deactivating-and-reactivating-products-2.png?width=670&height=195&name=deactivating-and-reactivating-products-2.png)

### How to reactive or deactivate Products in bulk

There are two ways to reactivate or deactivate Products in bulk:

(1) Export Products, edit the file and re-import the file

(2) Use the tick selection on the Products list page

**Option 1:**

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Select **More**>**Export Products**.

![deactivating-and-reactivating-products-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deactivating-and-reactivating-products-3.png?width=670&height=178&name=deactivating-and-reactivating-products-3.png)

- Open the excel file and edit column C to either Yes (to reactivate) or No (to deactivate) the Product.

![deactivating-and-reactivating-products-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deactivating-and-reactivating-products-4.png?width=670&height=108&name=deactivating-and-reactivating-products-4.png)

- Save the file and navigate back to the Products page in CartonCloud.
- Select **More**>**Import Products**.
- Select the file and click **Upload File**.

**Option 2**

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Using the tick box on the far left side, select the relevant Products.
- Click the red Deactivate button or the green Reactivate button.

![deactivating-and-reactivating-products-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deactivating-and-reactivating-products-5.png?width=670&height=295&name=deactivating-and-reactivating-products-5.png)

---

<a id="directly-shippable-products"></a>
## Directly Shippable Products

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/directly-shippable-products_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- Use Cases
- Prequisites
- Directly Shippable Products and the Pack Screen

### Purpose

Directly Shippable Products are Products Unit of Measure flagged as being “directly shippable” and automatically create their own Consignment Item when using the Pack Screen and/or Auto-Generating Consignment Items.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/2g-pp5NCidw

### Benefits

- **Faster packing workflows** — eliminates the need to manually create consignment items or select Unit Of Measures when products ship in their original packaging.
- **Better visibility of pack structure** — each unit is automatically allocated its own consignment item, providing a clear packing structure.
- **Flexible control** — pin, lock, and unlock icons (or barcodes) give you control over how scanned items are grouped, allowing for customisation without slowing down the process.
- **Reduced packing errors** — product dimensions and weights are automatically pulled from the Product Packaging settings, ensuring consistency across Consignments.

### Use Cases

When scanned in the Pack Screen, Directly Shippable items automatically create their own consignment item with dimensions and weights pulled directly from the product record. This is ideal for items that ship in their original packaging, such as TVs, boxed appliances, or palletised goods as it eliminates the need to manually re-enter dimensions and weight data. When working with auto-generated consignment items, directly shippable products will generate their own individual consignment items in the same way.

### Prequisites

- Understand the Pack Screen and the related requirements. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Pack-Screen) for more information.
- Enable the Directly Shippable Product from the Unit of Measure set up:
  - Navigate to **Warehouse > Products**.
  - Select the relevant Product.
  - Navigate to the Measurements section.
  - Click **Edit** against the relevant Unit of Measure.

![directly-shippable-products-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/directly-shippable-products-0.png?width=670&height=321&name=directly-shippable-products-0.png)

- Tick **Directly Shippable**.
- Update the **Length, Width, Height, and Gross Weight** (optional but recommended).
- Ensure the UOM is linked to a **Transport Product**. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products) for instructions.

### Directly Shippable Products and the Pack Screen

When a Product Unit of Measure is flagged as being Directly Shippable, it enables additional features during packing via the Pack Screen:

- A carton icon is shown beside the Unit of Measure on the Pack Screen to highlight that it is a Directly Shippable Product.
- Clicking or scanning the Directly Shippable Product automatically creates a Consignment Item for each unit.
- Weights and dimensions from the linked Product Unit of Measure and Transport Product are applied.
- By default, the weight of the Directly Shippable Product is applied to the Consignment Item; however, by selecting the weight icon next to the weight, the Transport Product weight can be added.

| **Logic** | **Behaviour** |
| --- | --- |
| Unlocked | Other products can be added to the Consignment Item. |
| Locked | When a product is scanned, it creates its own Consignment Item with no other products able to be added to the Consignment Item. This behaviour is selected by default for Directly Shippable Products. |
| Pinned | When selected, additional products will be added to the Consignment Item when scanned, even if it is a Directly Shippable Product. This is most commonly used if you are packing onto pallets. |

The above logic (unlock, lock, pin)  is available via Action Barcdoes:

- Unlock consignment item - CCACT004
- Lock consignment item - CCACT005
- Pin consignment item - CCACT003

See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hubfs/Knowledge%20Base%20Files/Action%20Barcodes_Dec.pdf) for a printer-friendly version.

---

<a id="edit-products-in-bulk"></a>
## Edit Products in Bulk

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/edit-products-in-bulk_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- To make changes to products in bulk

### Purpose

There may be times when you need to update Product properties in bulk. This feature will allow you to update the following fields against a product in bulk,

- Product Type
- Storage Charge Method
- Allow Zero Storage Charge
- Require Weight
- Warning Threshold Days
- Expiry Threshold Days
- Enable Low Stock Notification
- Low Stock Threshold

### To make changes to Products in Bulk:

- On the Products page select the **More** button, then select **Edit Products in Bulk** from the drop-down menu.

![edit-products-in-bulk-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/edit-products-in-bulk-0.png?width=670&height=279&name=edit-products-in-bulk-0.png)

- Once there, you can search using the filters, or just click "Search" to bring up all results
- It's important to note that the "Select All Products on this page" checkbox can be used to quickly select all products for changes.
- Changes can then be made by clicking the **Bulk Edit** button at the bottom of the page.

![edit-products-in-bulk-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/edit-products-in-bulk-1.png?width=670&height=299&name=edit-products-in-bulk-1.png)

- The Editing Box will then appear allowing you to select what to change. Note that by default fields will not be modified - so only make changes to those fields that you want to be modified.

![edit-products-in-bulk-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/edit-products-in-bulk-2.png?width=670&height=313&name=edit-products-in-bulk-2.png)

- Then click**Save**, and the products you selected will be updated with the new value.
