<a id="exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom"></a>
## Exporting and Importing Bill of Materials (BOM)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- Use cases
- Prerequisites
- How to export and import bill of materials (BOM)

### Purpose

To use the export and import function to either create or edit multiple [Bill of Materials](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/8QP8Hw) in bulk.

Note, if you wish to use this function to create a Bill of Materials (BOM), you will need to first create all the Products that will be used to create the Bill of Materials (including the final product) in CartonCloud.

### Benefits

- You can edit and create multiple Bill of Materials in one step.
- Saves time and manual repetitive work.

### Use Cases

- If your Customer requests to create multiple Bill of Materials.
- If your Customer requests changes to multiple Bill of Materials.

### Prerequisites

You must have already created in CartonCloud the:

- Final Product of the Bill of Materials.
- Products that will make up the Bill of Materials.

### How to export and import bill of materials (BOM)

Ensure you have created all Products required to create the Bill of Materials (including the Product that will become the final Product of the Bill of Materials).

To either create a new Bill of Materials or edit an existing Bill of Materials, you will need to:

### 1. Export the existing Bill of Materials from CartonCloud:

- Navigate to the Products page, Warehouse > Products .
- Select the blue More button in the top left corner.
- Select Export Bill of Materials from the drop-down menu.

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-0.png?width=670&height=133&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-0.png)

- Select the bell icon in the top right corner.
- Click Download Here for the Bill of Materials Export.

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-1.png?width=345&height=314&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-1.png)

### 2. Edit the exported file

To create a new Bill of Materials:

- Open the downloaded excel file.

**Leave the ID column blank.**

- Type the Customer's name into the Customer column.

Ensure you have typed the Customer name exactly as it appears in CartonCloud.

- Enter the final Bill of Materials Product code into the Parent Product Code column.
- Find the Product code, by navigating to the Products list view page and find the Product code under the Code column.

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-2.png?width=596&height=267&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-2.png)

- Enter the Product code for one of the Products that make up the Bill of Materials into the Child Product Code column.
- Enter the quantity into the Quantity column. ​​​​​​​

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-3.png?width=670&height=215&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-3.png)

- Repeat the above process for each Child Product Code that will be included in the Bill of Materials.

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-4.png?width=670&height=237&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-4.png)

### To modify an existing Bill of Materials:

**To edit the quantity of a Child Product:**

- Change the value in the Quantity column for the relevant Product.

**To edit or remove a Product that makes up the Bill of Materials:**

- Edit the product code in the Child Product Code column or delete the row if you wish to delete the Product.

**To edit the final Product of the Bill of Materials:**

- Edit the product code in the Parent Product Code column for each product row included in that Bill of Materials.

**To add a Product to an existing Bill of Materials:**

- Insert a new row under the Bill of Materials you wish to add to.
- Copy and paste the Customer and Parent Product Code from the relevant Bill of Materials.
- Enter the new Child Product Code and Quantity.

### 3. Import the edited file back into CartonCloud:

- Navigate back to the CartonCloud Products page.
- Select the blue More button in the top left corner.
- Select Import Bill of Materials from the drop-down menu.

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-5.png?width=670&height=119&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-5.png)

- Click Choose file and then select the relevant file to import.
- Select Upload File .

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-6.png?width=507&height=131&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-6.png)

- Select the bell icon in the top right corner.
- Click View Results Here for the Bill of Materials Import.

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-7.png?width=320&height=325&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-7.png)

- You will then be directed to the Import Results page.
- Under the Created tab, you will be able to see all new Bill of Materials successfully created.

![exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-8.png?width=670&height=156&name=exporting-and-importing-bill-of-materials-bom-8.png)

- Under the Updated tab, you will be able to see all modifications that have been made to the existing Bill of Materials in CartonCloud. By hovering over the green highlighted boxes, you will be able to see what change took place.

| **Tab** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Summary | Status: if the import was successful or not. Details: further details in regards to the status. Original file: the file that was imported into CartonCloud. |
| Created | New Bill of Materials that have been successfully created and imported into CartonCloud. |
| Updated | Existing Bill of Materials that have successfully been updated in CartonCloud. |
| Ignored | Existing Bill of Materials that were ignored during the import process as no changes were made. |
| Errors | Errors occurred during the import process, and therefore, the changes requested were not made. |

If you do receive an error, select the Error tab and hover your mouse over the red highlighted box. A message will appear explaining why the error occurred.

---

<a id="exporting-and-importing-products"></a>
## Exporting and Importing Products

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/exporting-and-importing-products_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to export and import products
- Editing the file (import file field descriptions)
- Video guide

### Purpose

By utilising the export/import Product Master functionality you are able to add new Products or update existing Products in bulk.

### How to export and import products

- Navigate to the Products page, Warehouse > Products .
- Select More > Export Products .
- Select the bell notification in the top right corner and click Download Here .
- Open the downloaded file.
- In this file, you can edit the existing Products or add new Products.

When adding new Products, ensure you keep the id column blank.

- Save the file.
- Navigate back to the CartonCloud Product page.
- Select More > Import Products .
- Click Choose file and select the relevant file.
- Select Upload File .
- You will then receive a notification once the import has been processed and a link to view the import. Click the notification bell and then View Results here .
- From here you will be able to view the products that were created, updated, ignored and the ones with errors. If there was an error in the file, the products without errors will still be updated and created successfully.

![exporting-and-importing-products-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-products-0.png?width=670&height=179&name=exporting-and-importing-products-0.png)

-
  - Summary : a summary of the import and access to the original file.
  - Created : the new products that were created
  - Ignored : the products that remained unchanged
  - Errors : the products that had errors and did not import. The fields that errored will be highlighted red.

![exporting-and-importing-products-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-products-1.png?width=670&height=190&name=exporting-and-importing-products-1.png)

![exporting-and-importing-products-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-products-2.png?width=670&height=117&name=exporting-and-importing-products-2.png)

- You can also access and view the Product Import results via the Import Log if needed.
- Navigate to More > Import Log > Click View Results Here .

![exporting-and-importing-products-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-and-importing-products-3.png?width=670&height=224&name=exporting-and-importing-products-3.png)

### Editing the file (Import file field descriptions)

The table below explains what each field on the file is for and what can be entered into each field.

| Field | Description | Options | Required |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Customer | The customer of the Product. |  | Yes |
| Id | Leave this column blank if you are creating a new Product. This is automatically generated by CartonCloud when a new Product is created. |  |  |
| Active | If the Product is active or not. | Yes, No | Yes |
| Name | The Product Name |  | Yes |
| Code | The Product Code |  | Yes |
| Tags | Tags associated with the Product. See [Tags](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Tags) for more information. |  | No |
| Product Description | Additional description about the Product. |  |  |
| Type | The Product type. For example, Chilled, Frozen, Ambient. | Refer to your [Product Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Types) | Yes |
| Storage Charge Method | The method for how the storage should be charged, refer to [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) | Per Location   Per Pallet   Volume Based   Weight Based   Per Item | Yes |
| Storage Unit of Measure Aggregation | If you have selected the Storage Charge Method Per Unit of Measure you will need to select an Aggregation option. For more information see [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges)  Aggregation options:   As per rate card default setting. =Default   Per SKU, Per Location (and Bulk Location Pallets) = Location    Per SKU, Across the Entire Warehouse = Warehouse | Default  Warehouse  Location | Yes |
| Allow Zero Storage Charge | Allows storage to be charged at $0. This means no charge error will come up if storage charges equal $0. | Yes No |  |
| Per Item Storage Charge | Amount to charge per item if Per Item Storage Charge Method is selected |  |  |
| Volume (cubic meters) | The Volume of the Product in m3, ie: 0.0025 |  |  |
| Weight (kilograms) | The Weight of the Product in KG, ie: 6.25 (for 6.25kg) |  |  |
| Country of Origin | The Country of Origin of the product. This is useful if needing the Country of Origin for import/export purposes. |  |  |
| Harmonised System Code | The Harmonized System Code (HS Code) is an international standard for classifying products in cross-border trade. Adding the correct HS Code to your products ensures compliance with customs regulations and accurate calculation of duties and taxes. |  |  |
| Measurement Category | The measurement category for the Base Measurement, normally this is Count | Count | Yes |
| Base Measurement | The Code for the Base Unit Of Measure | Refer to your [Products Units of Measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products+Units+of+Measure) | Yes |
| Random Weight | Whether the product is a Random Weight Product or not, refer to: [Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products) for information on Random Weight | 0, 1 |  |
| Stock Selection Method | When assigning Sale Order Products, this determines the automatic stock selection algorithm used to calculate the best stock to assign. Options are:   Warehouse location pick efficiency only.   FEFO (First Expiry First Out) - Closest expiry date is selected first.   FIFO (First In First Out) - Longest time since arrival is selected first.   LIFO (Last In First Out) - Shortest time since arrival is selected first.  FEFO By Address Group (First Expiry First Out) - For use in conjunction with [MLOR](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Specific-Shelf-Life-Expiry-Threshold) | Location Efficiency   FEFO   FIFO   LIFO   FEFO By Address Group | Yes |
| Strict Stock Selection | With Strict Stock Selection turned on the stock selection method is enforced even if it means splitting a full pallet or picking from a part pallet to build a full pallet. | Yes  No | Yes |
| Ignore Expiry Date during Stock Selection | The expiry date will not be taken into consideration during stock selection. | Yes No | Yes |
| Stock Sub-Selection Method | Once you have selected a Stock Selection Method you must then choose a Sub-Selection Method. This means that if after the system uses the stock selection method if multiple locations meet that method's requirement the sub-selection method will be used to further optimise how you select stock. This logic is secondary to the Stock Selection method, and will never override it. The available Stock Sub-Selection Methods:   Location Efficiency: The system will look at all the pallets available meeting the Stock Selection Method, then choose the location with the highest location efficiency first.   Minimise Storage: The system will look at all the pallets available meeting the Stock Selection Method, then choose the option which minimises the storage quantity by as much as possible, attempting to empty locations.   Minimise Picks: The system will look at all the pallets available meeting the Stock Selection Method, then choose the option which minimises the number of locations that Pickers will need to visit to pick the order.   See [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-CartonCloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-Stock-Selection-Methods) for more information. | Location Efficiency  Minimise Storage  Minimise Picks |  |
| Split BOM on insufficient stock | With this setting turned on, if there is no built Bill of Materials products CartonCloud will assign stock to the Sale Order from the individual products rather than the built stock. | Default, Yes, No | Yes |
| Warning Threshold | The number of days prior to expiration that the Expiration Warning Email is sent |  |  |
| Expiry Threshold | The number of days prior to expiration that the product will no longer be able to be sent |  | Yes |
| Low Stock Notifications | Are Low Stock Notifications (emails) enabled with this product? | Yes, No | Yes |
| Low Stock Threshold | The low stock amount that should trigger an email, ie: 80, will trigger when the stock drops below 80. |  |  |
| Product Group | The Product Group the Product belongs to. The Product Group is utilised to filter the Product List and in the Customer Stock Report. See [Product Group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Group) for more information. |  |  |
| POP Initial Status | When assigning stock to a Purchase Order, this value sets the Product Status of that stock. For example, if you selected "Quarantine", then all stocks created would default to Quarantine Status. | OK, Quarantine (see [Product Statuses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Statuses) for full list) | Yes |
| POP Expiry Date Required? | Whether the product requires an expiry date to be entered. | No   Yes   [ blank ] - Use the Customers setting, see [How to make Expiry Dates optional](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/How+to+make+Expiry+Dates+optional) | Yes |
| Is Reallocation Enabled? | To enable reallocation for the product | No  Yes | No |
| Reallocation Scannable Field | The field you wish to be able to reallocate with | custom_field_1 [insert number] | No |
| POP Custom Field [ x ] Required? | Whether or not a particular Custom Field is required to be recorded for this product. | [ blank ] - Use the Customers setting,    No   Incoming and Outgoing   Outgoing |  |
| Custom Field [ x ] | What to insert into each of the Custom Fields defined within the Products themselves. |  |  |
| Product Unit of Measure Conversions |  |  |  |
| Conversion Measurement | The [Products Units of Measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products+Units+of+Measure) for the conversion qty. For example, if your products base unit of measure is Cartons, and there are 48 cartons per pallet, then you would put PLT here. |  | Yes |
| Qty Per Base | To use the example above, converting from CTN to PLT you would enter the number 48 into this field so the system knows you have 48 cartons per pallet. |  | Yes |
| Description | The product name that is displayed on Pick Slips. Often used if the Product Description of a specific Unit Of Measure differs significantly from the Product Name. |  |  |
| Code | The product code for the Conversion Measurement. |  | Yes |
| Barcode | The barcode for the unit of measure, allowing for Scan Picking. Typically each unit of measure will have its own Unit Of Measure, allowing Cartons to be scanned independently of Units etc. |  |  |
| Gross Weight | The gross weight of the Product Unit of Measure (this is total weight including the product and packaging) |  |  |
| Length | Length of the Product Unit of Measure |  |  |
| Width | Width of the Product Unit of Measure |  |  |
| Height | Height of the product unit of measure |  |  |
| Directly Shippable | If the Product is Directly Shippable. Directly Shippable Products automatically create their own Consignment Item when using the Pack Screen and/or Auto-Generating Consignment Items. | Yes  No |  |

### Video Guide

<a id="how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product"></a>
## How to create multiple product codes per Product

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to create multiple product codes for a product

### Purpose

When using an Integration to receive or send orders from and to other platforms (such as Shopify), you may face a situation where the other systems use different Product Codes to those set up in CartonCloud. In this case, you will need to create multiple Product Codes for one Product. This will ensure the integration works effectively and the correct products are matched across the different platforms.

### How to create multiple product codes for a product

To create multiple Product Codes for one Product, you need to add another Product Unit Of Measure with the other Product Code(s) you want to support. You then need to have a 1-1 conversion with the Base Unit of Measure.

- Navigate to the relevant Product you wish to add another Product Code to, **Warehouse**>**Products>Select the appropriate Product.**
- Within the**Measurements window,**click**Add New Conversion.**

**![how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-0.png?width=670&height=261&name=how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-0.png)**

- Select the Product Unit of Measure you wish to use. If you would like to create a new Product Unit of Measure, please click here for instructions on adding a Product Unit of Measure.
- Enter the additional Product Code .
- Enter the conversion of 1 for the Base Unit of Measure.

![how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-1.png?width=670&height=298&name=how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-1.png)

- Click Save .

![how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-2.png?width=670&height=236&name=how-to-create-multiple-product-codes-per-product-2.png)

---

<a id="how-to-make-expiry-dates-optional"></a>
## How to make Expiry Dates optional

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-make-expiry-dates-optional_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Configuring the default for the customer
- Changing a single product to not follow the default
- Updating products in bulk

### Purpose

Making expiry dates optional can be performed on a per-Customer and per-Product basis.

Expiry Dates will still appear throughout the application, however, they no longer need to be entered if they're made optional.

### Configuring the default for the customer

By default, all Products are set up to have Expiry Dates turned on/off from the Customer Settings.

From the Edit Customer page, you can disable **Expiry Date required?** for all of the Customer's products in one go.

Note that each Product then has an option which allows it to either default to the Customer settings or override them for that particular product.

From the Edit Product page.

### Changing a Single Product to not follow the default

From the Edit Product screen, you can configure how to handle Expiry Dates:

### Updating Products in Bulk

Using the[Product Export/Import](https://help.cartoncloud.com/kb2/setting-up-cartoncloud/setting-up-the-wms-warehouse-management-system/setting-up-products#SettingupProducts-BulkImportingProducts(Export/ImportCSV))[,](https://help.cartoncloud.com/kb2/setting-up-cartoncloud/setting-up-the-wms-warehouse-management-system/setting-up-products#SettingupProducts-BulkImportingProducts(Export/ImportCSV)) you can change the Expiry Date settings for Products in bulk.

<a id="product-code-filtering"></a>
## Product Code Filtering

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-code-filtering_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to steps

### Purpose

Customers often have Product Codes stored within their systems that are not pickable items from a 3PL perspective, such as Freight Lines, Tax Codes, Discount Codes etc.

With Product Code Filtering, customers can now take control of what Product Codes they want excluded from the Sale Orders automatically when created.

### Prerequisites

Currently, this is only available to users with the 'Customer' user role. Administrators can enable the Customer permission to their account by [editing their permissions](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Edit-User).

### How to steps

- Under the 'Customer' user role, navigate to More > Settings
- Select Products .
- Enter the Product Codes that you would like CartonCloud to ignore from the order as shown below. Once you are done select Save.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-20-2025-04-59-30-4704-AM.png?width=670&height=286&name=image-png-Nov-20-2025-04-59-30-4704-AM.png)

Note - there is no requirement for the Product Codes that need to be ignored to be added as Product Codes within CartonCloud.

The excluded codes will show against the Sale Order history

![product-code-filtering-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-code-filtering-1.png?width=670&height=141&name=product-code-filtering-1.png)

---

<a id="product-group"></a>
## Product Group

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-group_

### Table of Contents

- What are Product Groups
- How to create a Product Group
- How to assign a Product Group to a Product

### What are Product Groups

A Product Group is assigned to Products and then can be used to filter Products by Product Group and also include it on the Customer Stock Report.

- When on the Products page you can apply to filter the list by Product Groups.
- When exporting Products you can filter the list by Product Groups.
- On the Customer Stock Report you can choose to include the Product Group.

### How to create a Product Group

- Use the Search for anything bar and type in Product Groups.
- Select the Add Product Group button.

![product-group-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-group-0.png?width=670&height=108&name=product-group-0.png)

- Select the Customer , Product Type , Name and Description for the Product Group.
- Select Save .

![product-group-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-group-1.png?width=670&height=321&name=product-group-1.png)

### How to assign a Product Group to a Product

You can assign a Product Group to a Product when adding a Product ([Add a Product](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Add-a-Product)) or when editing a Product ([Exporting and Importing Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Exporting-and-Importing-Products)).

---

<a id="product-settings"></a>
## Product Settings

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-settings_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to access Product Settings
- Edit Product Settings in Bulk

### Purpose

Product Settings allow you to configure and customise the Product to best suit your operational and Customer needs.

### How to access Product Settings

- Navigate to the Products page, Warehouse>Products.
- Select the relevant Product.
- Click the green Edit button in the top left corner.

![product-settings-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-settings-0.png?width=670&height=327&name=product-settings-0.png)

### Edit Product Settings in Bulk

To edit Product Settings in bulk, please see [Exporting and Importing Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Exporting-and-Importing-Products).

### Product Settings/Fields

| Product Setting | Explanation | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Name | The name of the product | Beef Pie 1 x 110gm |
| Product Code | The code / SKU for the Product. This code is used when importing new orders via Parsers.  Special characters ARE NOT supported in the Product Code. | BEEF110 |
| Tags | The Tags added against the Product. See [Tags](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Tags) for more information. |  |
| Description | Additional information about the Product. This description can be used on documents such as Picking Slips and Consignment Notes. | Made from 100% premium quality grass-fed Angus beef. |
| Product Type | The Product Type of the Product. Product Type is used to restrict where in the warehouse the Product can be stored (e.g. Temperature Zones or Dangerous Goods) and to control [Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges)).      See [Product Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Types) for more information. | Chilled |
| Storage Charge Method | How Storage Charges are applied to this Product.   Per Location  Per Item Volume Based Weight Based Per Location (and bulk location pallets) Per Pallet (based on qty) Per Unit of Measure   See [Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for more information. | Per Location |
| Allow Zero Storage Charge | Allows storage to be charged at $0. This means no charge error will come up if storage charges equal $0. |  |
| Product Volume (in Cubic Meters) | The volume of the Product in cubic meters (L x W x H). This can be used to control [Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) and [automatically populate the cubic of a Consignment.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-a-Product) | 0.0034 |
| Product Weight (in Kilograms) | The weight of the Product is in kilograms. This can be used to control [Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) and [automatically populate the cubic of a Consignment.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-a-Product) | 0.110 |
| Country of Origin | The Country of Origin of the product. This is useful if needing the Country of Origin for import/export purposes. | Australia |
| HS Code | The Harmonized System Code (HS Code) is an international standard for classifying products in cross-border trade. Adding the correct HS Code to your products ensures compliance with customs regulations and accurate calculation of duties and taxes. | 6601.99 |
| Product Group | If the Product belongs to a Product Group. See [Product Group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Group) for more information. |  |
| Random Weight Product | A random weight Product is a Product where the weight of each unit that's picked needs to be recorded. For example, when packing cartons of meat, each carton is a slightly different weight, and the customer charges per kilogram.  You will have to enter the exact weight of each item upon picking it. This information is then sent back to the Customer in their [Pack Notification Email](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers) to bill the receiver for the exact weight. | No |
| Warning Threshold Days | The number of days before expiration in which a warning threshold stock notification will be sent to the Customer.  This is useful for advising a client that their stock will expire soon and should be cleared out (possibly through a discount or promotion). This email can be configured through the [Outgoing Notification Emails](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers). | 10 |
| Expiry Threshold Days | The number of days before expiration that the Product will no longer be automatically selected on import. For example, products within 2 days of expiration probably shouldn't be sent out to customers as they won't last long enough once they arrive. Therefore, if an expiry threshold of 2 was used, the stock will no longer be selected automatically if the order is within 2 days of expiration. | 2 |
| Enable Low Stock Notification | If enabled, you can set the stock quantity in which a low stock notification will be sent to the Customer. | Yes |
| Low Stock Threshold Days | When it is reached, the quantity in which a low stock notification will be sent to the Customer.  This email can be configured through the [Outgoing Notification Emails](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers) | 10 |
| Initial Status of Purchase Order Product when created | The status that a Purchase Order Product will automatically be assigned to when the Product is added to a Purchase Order.  For example, if you select 'Quarantine, ' all Products added to the Purchase Order will automatically be in a 'Quarantine' status.   You can modify and create your [Product Status](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Statuses) if required. | OK |
| UOM Barcode | The barcode for the Base Unit of Measurement. You can define different barcodes for the different Units of Measurement.  The Unit of Measurement barcode can be used for [Scan Move](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Scan-Move-2-0-Basic-Move). | 10003998392 |
| Stock Selection Method | The method utilised to determine what stock is assigned to a Sale Order.   Warehouse location pick efficiency only. FEFO (First Expiry First Out) - Closest expiry date is selected first. FIFO (First In First Out) - Longest time since arrival is selected first. LIFO (Last In First Out) - Shortest time since arrival is selected first.     See the article: [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-CartonCloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-Stock-Selection-Methods) for more information. | FEFO |
| Strict Stock Selection | If strict mode is enabled, then FEFO / FIFO / LIFO will be enforced even if it causes splitting of full pallets or picking from part pallets to build full pallets.    See the article: [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-CartonCloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-Stock-Selection-Methods) for more information. | Yes |
| Stock Sub-Selection Method | Once you have selected a Stock Selection Method, you must choose a Sub-Selection Method. This means that after the system uses the stock selection method if multiple locations meet that method's requirement, the sub-selection method will be used to optimise further how you select stock. This logic is secondary to the Stock Selection method and will never override it.  Location Efficiency  Minimise Storage Minimise Picks   See the article: [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-CartonCloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-Stock-Selection-Methods) for more information. | Location Efficiency |
| If finished Bill of Material products (BOMs) are out of stock, take from individual components during Sale Order import | CartonCloud will take stock from individual products if the BOM products are out of stock.  See [Creating a Sale Order with BOM products yet to be built](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Creating-a-Sale-Order-with-BOM-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built)or [Bill of Materials (BOM)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Bill-of-Materials-BOM) for more information. | Yes |
| Reallocation | If you wish to enable reallocation for this product. The settings applied at the customer level will apply to the product by default.   **As per customer default setting**: will apply the same setting applied at the customer settings level **No**: reallocation will not be enabled for this product  **Yes - Optional Confirmation:** reallocation will be enabled for this product  **Yes - Confirmation Required**: packers must complete the reallocation step before continuing in the mobile picking workflow.  See [Reallocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Reallocation) for more details |  |
| Scannable field | If reallocation is enabled you will need to select a scannable field. This can either be the POP label or a POP custom field. This is the field you can reallocate with. |  |

See [Exporting and Importing Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Exporting-and-Importing-Products) to edit Products in bulk.

<a id="product-statuses"></a>
## Product Statuses

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-statuses_

### Table of Contents

- What are product statuses?
- Modifying product statuses
- Product status to decide whether to charge for storage
- Problem Stock Report
- Changing the product status on a Sale Order

### What are product statuses?

Product Statuses are used to label stock as Damaged, Missing, Lost, Quarantine etc. You can also configure Stock with a particular Product Status to count toward Storage Charges or not. For example, stock with a Missing Status probably shouldn't be charged storage (you don't have it after all!)

### Modifying product statuses

To access the Product Statuses page:

- Navigate to Warehouse > Products.
- From the Related drop down menu select Product Stauses .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products%201-png-2.png?width=670&height=200&name=products%201-png-2.png)

Once there, you'll see that some Product Statuses have a locked icon, these are used internally by CartonCloud and cannot be modified or deleted.
![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products%20111-png.png?width=670&height=238&name=products%20111-png.png)

For all the others, however, you can edit them, and**you can delete them if they're not in use by any Purchase Order Products**.

### How to create a Product Status

- Navigate to the Product Statuses page by typing **Product Statuses** into the Search for anything bar.
- Click **+Add Product Status**.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products%2011-png.png?width=670&height=238&name=products%2011-png.png)

- Enter the **Name** of the status and click **Save**.

### Product status to decide whether to charge for storage

Charge storage is an option you can control on Product Statuses. If you set this to Yes (default), then stock that has that status will be charged storage.
If you set it to No, then stock with that status will not be charged storage. For example, you may not want to charge for stock that has the status *Missing*.

### Problem Stock Report

All stock with a product status other than OK will appear on the [Problem Stock Report](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=530055692) , which can be generated by Customers who are logged in to CartonCloud.

### Changing the Product Status on a Sale Order

If you change the status of a stock to a status other than OK on an existing Sale Order in a status less than Packed, that particular stock will be removed from the order and replaced by stock that is in a status of OK.

---

<a id="product-types-add-view-edit-delete"></a>
## Product Types (Add/View/Edit/Delete)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-types-add-view-edit-delete_

### Table of Contents

- Add a Product Type
- View Product Type
- Edit Product Type

### Add a product type

- Type 'Product Types' into the Search for anything bar.
- Select +Add Product Type .
- Then complete the fields on the page. A description of the fields is provided below.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-20-2025-05-54-48-3900-AM.png?width=670&height=303&name=image-png-Nov-20-2025-05-54-48-3900-AM.png)

| **Field** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Name | The full name of the product type. |
| Code | The code you would like to display on labels for items with this product type. |
| Alias | A shorter name to display |
| Store Priority | This field affects what Product Type pushes through to a Consignment when creating it from a Sale Order. As Consignments can only have one Product type, in the scenario where you have both Chilled and General freight going together, you would likely want to give Chilled a higher priority, so all the freight then travels in a chilled vehicle. |
| Set Product Type as Default | Will set all new products created to have this product type. Only one product type will ever be ticked with this setting. |

- Select Save .

### View Product Type

- To view a product type, in the Product Types page, select View .
- From here you can view/edit warehouse locations, products and product group associations.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-20-2025-05-57-19-9826-AM.png?width=670&height=250&name=image-png-Nov-20-2025-05-57-19-9826-AM.png)

### Edit Product Type

- Select Edit against the Product Type.

If you need to update the name of a Product Type you can do so, however, it will change the name of the Product Type for existing products using the Product Type.

<a id="products"></a>
## Products

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/products_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Product
- Product Settings
- Product Types
- Product Statuses
- Products Unit of Measure
- How to add a Product
- Product Tags

### What is a Product

Products in CartonCloud are not the stock itself but rather the SKU or Product Master. In other words, a Product is a template that stores information, characteristics and rules associated with a particular item in your warehouse.

- Products are Customer-specific. Each of your Customers will have a number of Products that are only applicable to that particular Customer. Ensure you have [created a Customer](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/tQCYHw) before creating Products.
- Products are highly customisable, so depending on someone's operation and a Customer's requirements, they can be set up differently. How they are set up drives much of the logic within CartonCloud surrounding Warehouse Allocation, Stock Picking, Pricing and Consignment allocation.
- Once Products have created, [Purchase Orders](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Purchase+Orders) are used to bring the stock of Products into the system. This stock recorded against a Purchase Order is what we call [Purchase Order Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Adding+Purchase+Order+Products). Similarly, Sale Orders are then used to record movements of Purchase Order Products leaving the Warehouse.

![products-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-0.png?width=670&height=327&name=products-0.png)

### Product Settings

When creating a Product, there are a number of different settings you will need to configure. You can edit these settings at any time and can do so in [bulk by exporting/importing the products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/exporting-and-importing-products). Please click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-settings) for more information on Product Settings and [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/exporting-and-importing-products) for information on how to edit Product Settings in bulk.

### Product Types

[Product types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/fAaYHw) can be used to split your Products into different categories and then charge differently for storing or transporting a particular product type. They can also be used to restrict storing certain product types to certain warehouse locations. Some examples of common product types are General, Chilled, Dangerous Goods, Fragile; however, what you name a product type is completely up to you.

### Product Statuses

[Product Statuses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/HwO_Hw) are used to label stock as Damaged, Missing, Lost, Quarantine etc. Please click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/HwO_Hw) for more information on Product Statuses.

### Products Unit of Measure

In CartonCloud, all products are measured in a particular *Unit Of Measure*. Please click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/EAO_Hw) for more information.

### How to add a Product

To add a Product, follow the steps [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/FgC_Hw).

### Product Tags

To add a Tag to a Product, follow the steps [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/tags).

---

<a id="products-customer"></a>
## Products (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/products-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Products in CartonCloud
- Viewing a product
- Adding a product

### Products in CartonCloud

Products in CartonCloud are not the stock itself but rather the SKU or Product Master. In other words, a Product is a template that store information, characteristics and rules associated with a particular item in your warehouse.

You will need to set up products with your 3PL provider / CartonCloud account owner so that when orders are entered the product information is already in the system.

Products are highly customisable, you can select the stock selection method (how the stock is allocated to orders) and the

Purchase Order Products

(for example, batch number or serial number) and

Product Custom Fields

(e.g supplier codes or dangerous goods information). Speak to your 3PL provider / CartonCloud account owner about setting these fields up for your account.

### Viewing a product

On the Products page, you can find a list of all the Product Masters you have set up with you Warehouse Supplier.

![products-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-customer-0.png?width=670&height=130&name=products-customer-0.png)

From here by selecting any of the Products you can then view that Product's Information including the Current stock you have stored of that Product within the Warehouse. To do this, select the **Stock** Tab once you are viewing a product.

![products-customer-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-customer-1.png?width=670&height=194&name=products-customer-1.png)

### Adding a product

Depending on your account settings (this is determined and set up by your 3PL / CartonCloud account owner), you may have the ability to add your own products directly through the system.

Please note that once they are entered the Product record can only be edited by Warehouse Administrators from that point forward.

- Navigate to the Products page, Warehouse > Products .
- Select +Add Product .

![products-customer-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-customer-2.png?width=670&height=362&name=products-customer-2.png)

- Fill in the fields to create the Product and use the field descriptions on this page to assist you.
- Click Save .

<a id="products-units-of-measure"></a>
## Products Units of Measure

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/products-units-of-measure_

### Table of Contents

- What are Products Units of Measure
- Example
- Benefits
- How to steps
- Making changes to Products Units of Measure
- Search for a Product UOM Barcode

### What are Products Units of Measure

All products in CartonCloud are measured in a particular unit of measure. Each product contains a Base Unit Of Measure, which is the smallest sellable quantity of the product. CartonCloud uses the Base Unit of Measure to convert the quantity into other units of measure using the conversions set up against the product.

### Example

For example, if you sell bottles of lemonade by the individual bottle and in cartons (with 6 bottles to a carton) you can set up conversions from **Units to Cartons**. Same with pallets, if the lemonade can be sold by the pallet and you have 10 cartons per pallet you can set up a **Units to Pallets** conversion.

Base Unit of Measure = Units

Conversion = 6 Units Per Carton

Conversion = 60 Units Per Pallet

![products-units-of-measure-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-0.png?width=670&height=148&name=products-units-of-measure-0.png)

### Benefits

- Sale Order optimisation will try to prevent breaking larger quantities where possible, so if you have a location that contains 3 bottles, and another with 6 bottles, it'll prioritise taking from the 3 bottles as this cannot be sold as a Carton.
- Handling charges for both Sale Orders and Purchase Orders will be *Scaled* *automatically*. So, if you're picking 6 bottles from a location, it'll automatically charge handling for 1 carton rather than 6 bottles.
- Pick Lists will be shown in Scaled Quantities (so rather than saying to pick 60 Bottles, it'll say 10 Cartons).
- Stock Reports can be shown in Scaled Quantities (very useful when dealing with Pallet Conversions).

Note: always set up the base unit of measure as the smallest sellable or trackable quantity of a product

### How To Steps

**Video Overview**

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/9JXMVZ0YCm4

How to create a Product Unit of Measure

- Navigate to the Products Unit of Measure page by typing **Product Units of Measure** into the Search for anything bar.
- Select **+Add Product Unit of Measure**.

![products-units-of-measure-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-1.png?width=670&height=132&name=products-units-of-measure-1.png)

- Enter the **Name** for the Product Unit of Measure and the **Code**.
- Select the **Category** (Mass, Volume, Count).
- Enable the **Oversize Warnings** if you wish to be notified of when you may be over-allocating to a warehouse location. See [Oversize Warnings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products+Units+of+Measure#ProductsUnitsofMeasure-oversize) for more information.
- If you wish to link the Product Unit of Measure to a Transport Product/Consignment, see [Mapping Product Unit of Measures to Consignment Fields/Transport Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products) for more information.

![products-units-of-measure-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-2.png?width=670&height=323&name=products-units-of-measure-2.png)

- Click **Save**.

#### **Oversize Warning**

When allocating products to a warehouse location, CartonCloud can be set up to warn you if you try to allocate more than a specific quantity of a product to a single location. For example, if you have a product measured in Pallets, then by default if you try to allocate all of these to a single location, CartonCloud will warn you that what you're doing may cause under billed storage charges and to potentially split the quantity into multiple locations.
We understand that you may need to store other items as well, such as IBCs, stillages, or Large, Block Items. Therefore, the 'Oversize Warning' may be used to notify you when you're trying to allocate more than 1 of those items to a single location. So, if for example, you try to allocate 3 IBCs to a single location, it'll warn you that this may cause underbilled storage.

#### **Modifying Product Unit of Measures**

CartonCloud comes with a number of pre-defined Product Units of Measure. These cannot be modified, therefore, appear locked with the lock symbol.

![products-units-of-measure-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-3.png?width=670&height=40&name=products-units-of-measure-3.png)

For the Product Units of Measure you have created, you can edit the measure by clicking on the Product Unit of Measure.

**Deleting a Product Unit of Measure**

If a Product Unit of Measure is in use (a current Consignment is using the Product Unit of Measure), then the measure CAN NOT be deleted. If the Product Unit of Measure is not in use (for example, it has just been created) then it can be deleted.

To delete a Product Unit of Measure (that is not in use):

- Select the Product Unit of Measure you wish to delete.
- Click the arrow next to the Cancel button.
- Click **Delete**.

![products-units-of-measure-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-4.png?width=670&height=318&name=products-units-of-measure-4.png)

#### **Setting up Product Unit of Measurements when creating a Product**

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Click +Add Product and follow the steps [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-a-Product).
- Once you get to the Measurement section, select the Measurement Category from the drop-down menu.
- Select the Base Measurement from the drop-down (*the Base Measurement is the smallest pickable unit of measure for this product*). If the Unit of Measure you wish to use is not there, select **+Add New Measurement** to create a new measurement.
- Enter a Barcode if you wish to use a barcode.

![products-units-of-measure-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-5.png?width=670&height=190&name=products-units-of-measure-5.png)

- To add a conversion, select **+Add Another Conversion**.
- Select the conversion measure from the **Measure** drop-down.
- Enter the **Conversion Factor.**
- Enter a Barcode if you wish to use a barcode.
- Use the Example column to confirm you are using the correct conversions.
- Using the same lemonade example, a Carton Measure with a Conversion Factor of 6 will need to be added and a Pallet Measure with a Conversion Factor of 60 will need to be added.

![products-units-of-measure-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-6.png?width=670&height=224&name=products-units-of-measure-6.png)

- Once you have created your Product you can check the conversions, on the Products page using the Measurement Conversion Calculator.
- Enter the unit quantity and click Convert. You can change the measure using the dropdown.

![products-units-of-measure-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-7.png?width=518&height=375&name=products-units-of-measure-7.png)

### Making changes to a product unit of measure on a product

You will need to adjust your product if any of these situations arise:

1. The conversions you entered are not correct
2. You find that you only ship in full cartons, and would prefer the Base Measurement to be in Cartons instead of Units
3. After a few months, the product packaging changes from 6 per carton to 8 per carton
4. If the product conversion has been set up inverted

Each of these cases requires a different change to be made and the process to make these changes is outlined below.

**1. Problem:**The conversions you entered are not correct.**Solution:**Add/edit conversion measurement and barcode

- Navigate to the relevant Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**>**select the relevant Product**.

![products-units-of-measure-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-8.png?width=670&height=345&name=products-units-of-measure-8.png)

- Select **Edit** against the Unit of Measure you wish to edit.
- Update the **quantity** against the **Unit per Carton**.

![products-units-of-measure-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-9.png?width=670&height=320&name=products-units-of-measure-9.png)

- Click **Save**.

**2. Problem:** You find that you only ship in full cartons, and would prefer the Base Measurement to be in Cartons instead of Units. **Solution:**Change the base unit of measure

Changing the Base Unit Of Measure will modify all history of the product to reflect quantities in the new measurement. For example, if you've been packing orders of Lemonade using units when you convert the Base Unit of Measure, it will modify all figures to be shown in Cartons. It will apply the 'conversion factor' to all stocks, which means it will either multiple or divide all quantities by the amount you specify.

This works if you have been packing orders in Cartons, however, if this is not the case you will end up with decimal quantities which may cause issues with stock selection in the future.

For example, if we are converting the Lemonade Base Unit of Measure from Unit to Cartons but there was an order that was 7 units. When the conversion factor of 6 is applied it will divide all records by 6 so the Sale Order will show that we packed 1.1667 of Lemonade.

Note: It is recommended that you only change the Base Unit of Measure if you have only just added the product or if you are certain that you've never packed an odd number of units. Changing the Base Unit Of Measure will also delete ALL existing Conversion Measurements. So, if you still require these you'll need to add them back in when you're done.

**To change the base unit of measure:**

- On the relevant Product page, select **Change Base Unit Of Measure**at the top of the Product page.

![products-units-of-measure-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-10.png?width=670&height=222&name=products-units-of-measure-10.png)

- Select the New Base Unit of Measure you want the product to be measured in.
- Enter the scaling factor. Ensure the conversion factor is going in the right direction (e.g 6 Units per Carton, rather than 6 Cartons per Unit).

![products-units-of-measure-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-11.png?width=670&height=313&name=products-units-of-measure-11.png)

- Scroll down and click **Save**.

**Tip:**Keep in mind that any existing Conversion Measurements have been deleted, so if you need to convert from say, Cartons to Pallets, you'll need to add this Conversion Factor back in by following Step 1.

**3. Problem:**After a few months, the product packaging changes from 6 per carton to 8 per carton.**Solution:**Changing the base unit of measure without scaling

- On the relevant Product page, select **Change Base Unit Of Measure**at the top of the Product page.

![products-units-of-measure-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-12.png?width=670&height=222&name=products-units-of-measure-12.png)

- Select the New Base Unit of Measure you want the product to be measured in.
- Enter the scaling factor of 1.

![products-units-of-measure-13](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-13.png?width=670&height=313&name=products-units-of-measure-13.png)

- Scroll down and click **Save**.

**Tip:** Keep in mind that any existing Conversion Measurements have been deleted, so if you need to convert from say, Cartons to Pallets, you'll need to add this Conversion Factor back in by following Step 1.

4. **Problem**: If the product conversion has been set up inverted. **Solution**: Swap the unit conversions using the 'Swap' button.

- Navigate to the relevant Product you wish to edit.
- Click Edit against the unit of measure that has the incorrect conversions.

![products-units-of-measure-14](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/products-units-of-measure-14.png?width=519&height=220&name=products-units-of-measure-14.png)

- Select the blue Swap button. This will change the conversion from 20 cartons per unit to 20 units per carton.
- Scroll down and click Save .

### Search for a Product UOM Barcode

You can scan a Product UOM barcode directly into the Search for anything bar to return matching product results. This avoids having to manually search for product barcodes.

---

<a id="setting-up-product-custom-fields-optionalsetting-up-product-custom-fields-optional"></a>
## Setting up Product Custom Fields (optional)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-product-custom-fields-optionalsetting-up-product-custom-fields-optional_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Enabling Product Custom Fields

### Purpose

Up to 10 Custom Fields can be applied to Product records. This differs from [Purchase Order Product Custom Fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Custom+Fields+for+Purchase+Order+Products) (which are fields used to record information against inbound stock) in that the custom field is applied directly against the Product record, and cannot be altered by individual stock records.

This is useful for storing additional information such as:

- Supplier Codes
- Dangerous Goods Information / DG Class
- Special Handling Instructions
- Other identifiers or information that's needed to be stored.

Custom fields are specified on a Per-Customer basis, allowing each customer to have their own set of Custom Fields.

Custom Fields can be displayed on Picklists, Con Notes and etc via [Document Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Document+Template+Placeholders), they can also be shown on Stock Reports and Exports.

Setting these up can be beneficial later on when you want to use the Custom Field as a filter on a report.

### Enabling Product Custom Fields

If you wish to store custom information against Products you will need to create Product Custom Fields.

- First, navigate to the Edit Customer Page by selecting Contacts in the Main menu followed by Customers in the drop-down.
- Then find and select the Customer.
- Once viewing the Customer record click Edit down the bottom left.
- From the Edit Customer Screen open the tab Warehouse Management and beneath this select the sub-tab Product .

![setting-up-product-custom-fields-optionalsetting-up-product-custom-fields-optional-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-product-custom-fields-optionalsetting-up-product-custom-fields-optional-0.png?width=670&height=272&name=setting-up-product-custom-fields-optionalsetting-up-product-custom-fields-optional-0.png)

- Enter the name of the Custom Field (unlike the Organisation level custom fields, these can only be set up to record plain text).
- Once you've added in the Custom Fields you want, click Save down the bottom. The Custom Fields will now appear when Adding or Editing a Product .

---

<a id="setting-up-product-types-location-types"></a>
## Setting up Product Types (Location Types)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-product-types-location-types_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Example of Product Types

### Purpose

Product types can be used to split your Products into different categories and then charge differently for storing or transporting a particular product type. They can also be used to restrict storing certain product types to certain warehouse locations. Some examples of common product types are General, Chilled, Dangerous Goods, Fragile; however, what you name a product type is completely up to you.

It's easiest to explain what Product Types do by providing some examples. The following are a few common scenarios in which Product Types are used. There are short instructions provided on how to implement each example, but it is not necessary to follow these just now, we recommend just seeing what is possible to gain an understanding of Product Types.

Once you have read the examples below, consider what Product Types your warehouse would hold.

Then create the Product Types you would like to store in your warehouse by navigating to the **Product Types** page which is best done by typing "Product Types" in the **Search for anything!** bar.

Then, using the [Add a Product](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Add-a-Product) article for assistance if required, click **+Add Product Type** and create the Product Types you need.

### Example of Product Types

#### **Example 1 - Different Temperature Zones**

For example, you may have a temperature-controlled facility in which you store and deliver products in three different temperature zones:

1. Chilled
2. Frozen
3. Ambient

These three temperature zones can be implemented as different Product Types.

Then, when creating products (later on in the setup) each product must be of a specified type (either Chilled, Frozen or Ambient).

When Adding Warehouse Locations you can also specify which type they are (either Chilled, Frozen or Ambient), which by default will prevent a Chilled Product from being able to be allocated to a Frozen Location (however this can be overwritten by allowing the Warehouse Location to accept multiple Product Types, this is useful if you want to allow your Chilled locations to store Ambient product for example)

The Product Types can then be used to affect Storage Charges, whereby you may charge different rates for Chilled Storage vs Frozen Storage (we will look into how to do this later when setting up warehouse rates).

In addition, Consignments also use Product Types as a field to control their charging (and if desired, allocation logic). Differing rates can be loaded depending on the Consignments Product Type.

#### **Example 2 - Different rates for Inside and Outside storage**

Product Types can be used to charge different storage rates depending on if an item is stored inside or outside.

First, three product types would be created:

1. General
2. Inside Storage
3. Outside Storage

All products would then be set as the type General.

Then, when creating Warehouse Locations; outdoor locations should be set as the location type "Outside Storage", while indoor locations would be set as location type "Inside Storage". Additionally, both warehouse location types should be allowed to store the product type "General".

Now, as both types of locations can accept General products, the products coming in can be stored in either the Outside or the Inside locations, however, the Storage Charges can differ for the different types.

Lastly, within the Customers [Rate Card](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/View-Rate-Card), modify the 'Charge Type Product Option' (see [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for more information)  to "Warehouse Location" so storage is charged based on the type of the Location rather than the type of the product.

#### **Example 3 - Dangerous Goods Handling**

Similar to different temperature zones, you may have two types of products: General and Dangerous Goods, each of which needs to be stored in a specific area.

Start by creating the Product Type "Dangerous Goods"

Now, create both products and warehouse locations of the different types. Make sure when adding the Warehouse Locations that you do not allow them to store stock of the other type, for example, A general location should not be allowed to store a Dangerous Good.

#### **Example 4 - Different rates for different pallet sizes**

If you have a customer or customers with different sized pallets that can be stored throughout your warehouse, you can use product type to manage this requirement. Firstly, create the following product types;

1. Standard Pallet
2. Oversized Pallet

- Now update the products to reflect the new product types for that customer or customers.
- Make sure that the customer or customers setting in Customer Charges for the Charge Product Type option is set to products.
- Then add the customer's storage charges for each product type

---

<a id="setting-up-products"></a>
## Setting up Products

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-products_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Adding a single product
- Bulk Importing Products
- Video Guide

### Purpose

To create a single Product or to create multiple products in bulk.

### Adding a single product

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Select **+Add Product**.

![setting-up-products-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-products-0.png?width=670&height=150&name=setting-up-products-0.png)

- Using the below field descriptions, fill in the relevant information.

**Product Fields**

| Field | Required | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Customer | Yes | The Customer associated with the Product. A Product can only be used and associated with one single Customer, however, you can create multiple products (one for each customer) with the same name and code. | Yatala Pie Shop |
| Name | Yes | The name of the product. | Beef Pie 1 x 110gm |
| Product Code | Yes | The code / SKU for the product that your customer refers to. This is used for matching when importing orders via [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers) or through [Available Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Available-Integrations) Please note, each Product Code for a Customer must be unique. You can not have the same Product Code for Products for the same Customer. *Only UTF-8 Special characters are supported in the product code. For a list of supported special characters please click [here](https://www.fileformat.info/info/charset/UTF-8/list.htm)* | BEEF110 |
| Tags | No | If you wish to associate any Tags with the Product. See [Tags](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Tags) for more information. |  |
| Product Description | Optional | Additional information about the product can be displayed on documents such as picking slips, consignment notes, and other exports. | Made from 100% premium quality grass-fed Angus beef |
| Product Type | Yes | The product type of this product. This is often used to restrict where in the warehouse the product can be stored (i.e., Temperature Zones or Dangerous / Non-Dangerous goods). However, it is also used to control Storage Charges, see [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for more information.   See [Product Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Types) for more information. | Chilled |
| Storage Charge Method | Yes | How Storage Charges are applied to this product. See [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for specific details on how each Storage Charge Method works. | Per Location |
| Product Volume | No | The volume of the product in cubic meters (L x W x H). This can be used to control Storage Charges (see [View Rate Card - Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges) for more information) and can also be used to automatically populate the cubic of a Consignment | 0.0034 |
| Product Weight | No | The weight of the product is in kilograms. This can be used to control Storage Charges and can also be used to automatically populate the weight of a Consignment.      The unit of measure the product weight is displayed in can be changed from the Organisation Settings. Please see [Changing the unit of measure in your tenancy](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Changing-the-unit-of-measure-in-your-tenancy) | 0.110 |
| Product Group | No | If you wish to add the Product to a Product Group. See [Product Group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Group) for more information. |  |
| Product Group | No | The Product Group is utilised to filter the Product List and in the Customer Stock Report. See [Product Group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Product-Group) for more information. |  |
| **Product Unit of Measure** |  |  |  |
| Measurement Category | Yes | The way in which the product will be measured. For example, if you measure the products in Units, Cartons, Inners etc, the Measurement Category will be Count. | Count |
| Base Measurement | Yes | The smallest pickable [unit of measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products+Units+of+Measure) for this product (or can be the measurement the client wants to see the product measured in). For example, we may sell them individually as units with our Beef Pie example, so the Base Measurement is "Unit". See [Products Units of Measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products+Units+of+Measure) for more information. | Unit |
| Barcode |  | The barcode for the Base Measurement (i.e., the Barcode on a single unit). Note you can define different barcodes for the different size packs using the Conversion Measurements below. The barcodes can the be used on the mobile app for scan picking and putaway. | 10003998392 |
| +Add New Measurement |  | If you wish to add a new Product Unit of Measure upon adding conversions, you can do so by clicking **+Add New Measurement**.          Enter the information for the new Product Unit of Measure. If mapping the Product Unit of Measure to a Transport Product/Consignment Field and Product Type you can do so from here. See [Mapping Product Unit of Measures to Consignment Fields/Transport Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products)  for more information.    ![setting-up-products-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-products-2.png?width=670&height=421&name=setting-up-products-2.png) |  |
| + Add Another Conversion |  | By clicking **Add Another Conversion**you can add conversion measurements. For example, with the Beef Pies example, you have may have 10 pies in 1 Carton. You would add a Conversion Measurement of Carton with a Conversion Factor of 10.  Ensure you take note of the Example column when adding the conversion to ensure you have set it up correctly.   ![setting-up-products-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-products-3.png?width=670&height=57&name=setting-up-products-3.png) If you wish to add another conversion you can select **+Add Another Conversion**. With the Beef Pie example, you may add a pallet conversion, you have 48 cartons per pallet so you would have 480 units per pallet.    ![setting-up-products-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-products-4.png?width=670&height=79&name=setting-up-products-4.png)      *It's also important to note that each measurement can have its own barcode. This allows you to scan a Carton and have it register that you've picked 10 units or scan an entire pallet to receive in 480.* | Measure: Carton Conversion Factor: 10  Example: 10 Units per Carton |
| Random Weight Product |  | A random weight product is a product whereby the weight of each unit that's picked needs to be recorded. For example, this is common when packing cartons of meat, in which each carton is a slightly different weight, and the customer charges per Kilo. For example, you may have boxes of expensive sirloin steaks; each weighs approximately 20kg; however, each box varies. By making a product random weight, when picking items, the user must enter the exact weight of each item (i.e., 19.45kg); this information is then sent back to the customer in their [Pack Notification Email](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Configuring+Outgoing+Notification+Emails+to+Customers) to bill the receiver for exactly 19.45kg. | No |
| Warning Threshold |  | The number of days before expiration in which CartonCloud will send out an automated email advising the stock will be expiring in x number of days. This is useful for advising clients that their stock will expire soon and should be cleared out (possibly through a discount or promotion). This email can be configured through the [Configuring Outgoing Notification Emails to Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers) | 10 |
| Expiry Threshold |  | The number of days before expiration that the product will no longer be automatically selected on import. For example, products within 2 days of expiration probably shouldn't be sent out to customers as they won't last long enough once they arrive. Therefore, if an expiry threshold of 2 was used, the stock will no longer be selected automatically if the order is within two days of expiration.      *Note, however; you can manually select stock for an order which is either Expired or within the Expiry Threshold.* | 2 |
| Product Custom Fields |  | If you have Product Custom Fields enabled, fields you have defined will appear on the screen for entry. For example: "Supplier Code."   See: [Product Custom Fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Fields) for more information |  |
| Low Stock Threshold |  | This is the quantity in which the stock levels are considered low and requires attention. When the stock on hand hits this number, a [Low Stock Notification](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Configuring+Outgoing+Notification+Emails+to+Customers) will be sent. This email can be configured through the [Configuring Outgoing Notification Emails to Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers) |  |
| Initial Status of Purchase Order Product | Yes | When assigning stock to a Purchase Order, this value sets the Product Status of that stock. For example, if you selected "Quarantine", all stocks created would default to Quarantine Status. You can modify and create your own [Product Status](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Statuses) if required. | OK |
| Stock Selection Method | Yes | When assigning stock for a Sale Order, this determines how the system will pick a stock. See the article: [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/How+CartonCloud+chooses+outgoing+stock+-+Stock+Selection+Methods) for more information.   Warehouse location pick efficiency only.   FEFO (First Expiry First Out) - Closest expiry date is selected first.   FIFO (First In First Out) - Longest time since arrival is selected first.   LIFO (Last In First Out) - Shortest time since arrival is selected first. | FIFO |
| If finished Bill of Material products (BOMs) are out of stock, take from individual components during Sale Order import. |  | This setting is only relevant for the Bill of Material Products - Products made up of other products (such as a Hamper).   As per customer default setting - This setting for the Product will be enabled or disabled depending on what the Customer's Setting is set to.   Yes - A finished BOM product will be created by picking the individual products that make up that product.   No - If the finished BOM product is out of stock, the entire Sale order will be rejected.   See the [Bill of Materials (BOM)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Bill-of-Materials-BOM) article for further details. |  |
| Reallocation |  | To turn reallocation on or off for this product. By default the reallocation setting applied at the customer level will be applied to the product. See [Reallocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Reallocation) for more information.  Drop down options  As per customer default setting - will apply the settings set up at the customer level  No - reallocation will not be enabled for this product Yes - reallocation will be enabled for this product    Scannable Field: if using reallocation you will need to select a field that can be used to reallocate with |  |
| Purchase Order Product Expiry Date Required? |  | Determines whether the expiry date field is required for Purchase Order Products that use this product (see [Purchase Order Products Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Custom+Fields+for+Purchase+Order+Products)). |  |
| Purchase Order Product Custom Fields Required? (per field) |  | Determines whether each custom field is required for Purchase Order Products that use this product (see [Purchase Order Products Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Custom+Fields+for+Purchase+Order+Products)). |  |

- Click Save .

### Bulk Importing Products (Export/Import CSV)

Once you have created your first Product, you can create Products in bulk using the export/import function.

See [Exporting and Importing Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Exporting-and-Importing-Products) for steps on creating Products in bulk.
