<a id="tags"></a>
## Tags

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/tags_

### Table of Contents

- What are Tags in CartonCloud
- Product Tags
  - Product Tag Visibility
  - Product Tag Use Cases
  - How to add a Product Tag

### What are Tags in CartonCloud

Tags are a flexible system that allow you to categorise, search and manage your data in CartonCloud more easily. Product Tags are the first entity in CartonCloud to have this feature; however, in the future, more entities in CartonCloud will have the Tags functionality.

### Product Tags

Product Tags allow you to add one or more tags to a Product directly from within the edit product screen. Any newly created Product Tag is automatically added to the pre-defined list, making it available for future use.

#### **Product Tags are visible:**

- On the product view page for easy reference.
- In the Customer Stock Report with an optional Tags column, it displays a comma-separated list of tags for each product.
- On the Product export. This allows you to add Product Tags via the Product export/import function .

#### **Product Tag Use Cases:**

- Tags can be used to categorise Products by attributes such as 'Perishable', 'Fragile', and 'Hazardous' for easier filtering in reports.
- Your Customers may require custom tags such as supplier names for easier tracking of sourcing and stock issues.
- To identify Products for seasonal sales or marketing campaigns such as 'Christmas', 'Clearance', 'New Arrival'.
- To track where Products are in their product lifecycles, such as 'Discontinued' or 'End-of-life'.
- To report on product insights such as 'High Turnover' or 'Slow Moving'.

#### **How to add a Product Tag**

- Navigate to the Products page, Warehouse > Products .
- Select the relevant Product and click Edit .
- Within the Tags field, start typing the Tag you wish to add to the Product. If it is an existing Tag, you will be able to select it from the drop-down. If it is a new Tag, click the Add button that appears on the drop-down once you have finished typing the new Tag.

![tags-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/tags-0.png?width=670&height=309&name=tags-0.png)

- The Tag has now been created and will be available for future use.

![tags-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/tags-1.png?width=670&height=311&name=tags-1.png)

- Scroll down and select Save .
- The Tag will now appear on the View Product page.

![tags-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/tags-2.png?width=670&height=332&name=tags-2.png)

---

<a id="variable-weight-packing"></a>
## Variable Weight Packing

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/variable-weight-packing_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Random weights
  - Enabling random weight for a product
  - Confirming random weights
  - Total weight
  - Per-unit weight
  - Random weights in the list view

### Purpose

CartonCloud allows users to confirm weights for products that have been set up as **Random Weight Product** when packing an order on the mobile app.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/XqBNOxnTe3Y

### Random weights

**Enabling Random Weight for a Product**

The random weight characteristics have to be enabled on the CartonCloud web app for a product that has random weight to be collected for as part of the packing process.

To access this option, navigate to the product's page on CartonCloud, choose **Edit** and change **Random Weight Product** to *Yes*and save your changes.

![variable-weight-packing-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/variable-weight-packing-0.png?width=670&height=210&name=variable-weight-packing-0.png)

![variable-weight-packing-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/variable-weight-packing-1.png?width=670&height=437&name=variable-weight-packing-1.png)

**Confirming Random Weights**

- From the Picking 2.0 mode, select the Sale Order you wish to pack.
- Select a product line to pack. You will now be on the verify screen. Select Confirm Weight (once other prior steps are complete).

![variable-weight-packing-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/variable-weight-packing-2.png?width=231&height=461&name=variable-weight-packing-2.png)

- Enter the individual per unit weight or the total weight.

![variable-weight-packing-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/variable-weight-packing-3.png?width=244&height=485&name=variable-weight-packing-3.png)

- Once the weight has been entered it will now appear against that product line.

![variable-weight-packing-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/variable-weight-packing-4.png?width=258&height=513&name=variable-weight-packing-4.png)

<a id="view-product-details"></a>
## View Product

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/view-product-details_

### Table of Contents

- Details
- Product Packagings
- Stock
- Filtered Report
  - Report Overview
  - Report Columns
  - Searching by Custom Field
  - Report Column Sorting
  - Report Options

### Details

The Details tab provides an overview of the most important details belonging to the currently viewed Product. To change any of the details on this page select **Edit** and you will be taken to the [Edit Product page](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-settings) where you can make changes.

#### **Measurements**

From within the Measurements box, you can see the [Products Units of Measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Products-Units-of-Measure) conversions for the Product.

You can also add new conversions by selecting the 'Add New Conversion button. Please note, when adding new conversions the Code must much the Product Code of the related Product. In addition, the Code can not be the same as another Product Code of a Product from the same Customer.

![view-product-details-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-product-details-0.png?width=480&height=494&name=view-product-details-0.png)

### Product Packagings

For information on Product Packagings, see [Products Unit of Measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Products+Units+of+Measure).

### Stock

From this page, you are able to see all stock of this Product within your Warehouse, including the allocated Warehouse Location.

By selecting the checkbox on each line followed by the **Move** button you are also able to move the highlighted Purchase Order Product to a different location.

You are also able to Print Purchase Order Product Labels from this page by selecting the desired Products then selecting **Print Label**.

### Filtered Report

The Filter Product report is very similar to the Customer Stock Report however, it is prefiltered to only include the specific Product you are currently viewing (and therefore that Product only belongs to a single Customer).

### Report Overview

The Filter Product Report is used to track the inventory of the Product stored in the given Warehouse that the report is being run on. It is possible to view the report either in the web browser by just clicking the "Show Report" button or to export the report into an XLS file by using the **Export Excel** button.

Various columns can be added to gain the desired details on Warehouse Inventory. The available columns are covered in the section below.

#### Report Columns

There are a number of default columns that can be added to the Warehouse Stock Report, plus any custom fields. The custom fields may include, for instance, Batch or Lot Numbers and other useful information. The table below lists the default columns that are always available in the report and what they mean. The several of the default columns are "locked" columns. This means that they cannot be removed from the report. They can only be sorted in your desired order.

| Column Name | Locked | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Code | Yes | The code of the Product line |
| Product Name | Yes | The name of the Product line |
| Product Status | Yes | The status of the Product line |
| UOM | Yes | The Unit Of Measure of the Product line |
| Location | No | The Warehouse Location of the Product line |
| In Warehouse | Yes | The amount of stock in the Warehouse of the Product line. This amount is a sum of both Allocated and Free columns |
| Allocated | No | The amount of stock of the Product line that has been allocated to Sale Orders |
| Free | Yes | The amount of stock of the Product line that has not been allocated to Sale Orders |
| Incoming | No | If the Incoming column is part of the report, then the amounts of any stock on Purchase Orders with status of "Not Yet Received" or greater and which have stock that is not yet allocated to a Warehouse Location will appear in this column on the Report |
| ID | No | The ID of the Product line |
| Expiry | No | The set Expiry Date of the Product line |
| Pallet Id | No | If the Product line is stored in a bulk Warehouse Location, then it will show a Pallet Id representing what Pallet it resides on in that Warehouse Location |
| Product Group | No | The Product Group of the Product line if any |
| Product Type | No | The Type of the Product line |
| Purchase Order Reference | No | The reference of the Purchase Order that the Product line belongs to |
| Arrival Date | No | The arrival date of the Purchase Order that the Product line belongs to |
| # Pallets | No | The number of pallets at the given Warehouse Location |
| Tags | No | The Tags that have been added to the Product. |

#### Searching by Custom Field

In addition to the above fields, there are also custom fields that will appear. Both Purchase Order Product and Product custom fields will appear as options on the Report. If the custom field is a Purchase Order Product custom field it will have (POP) after the field name. Similarly, for Product custom fields there will be a (P) after the field name. This allows you to search for stock by custom field.

For example, if you wish to search for a particular Serial Number you will need to:

- Include the Serial Number POP Custom Field in the report column.

![view-product-details-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-product-details-1.png?width=670&height=192&name=view-product-details-1.png)

- Type the Serial Number into the Search Text field.
- Click Show Report .
- All stock with that serial number will now show in the report.

![view-product-details-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-product-details-2.png?width=670&height=302&name=view-product-details-2.png)

#### Report Column Sorting

The Warehouse Stock Report columns can be dragged and dropped in the order desired by simply clicking and dragging a tag to the desired position in the column order. Note that dragging fields to different places in the column order will result in slightly different results being displayed in the report as these options are also used to split the Product lines.

#### Report Options

There are several options in the Report that alter the result that is displayed or exported. The below table lists the options and explains what change they have on the Report.

| Option | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Show all stock | If this option is checked then you will both in stock and out of stock products appear in the report. NOTE: If you export the report to excel with this option set then you will get an excel file that has a sheet for In stock products and another sheet for Out of stock products |
| Automatically Scale Units | This option will make all stock counts showing in columns "In Warehouse", "Allocated", "Free", and "Incoming" in their highest possible unit of measure conversion (eg. If the Product line's highest unit of measure is a Pallet, then the counts shown in the report will be in Pallets with this option checked). See below for a way to scales to other UOM levels. |
| Show Stock as at a Historic Date | Checking this option will show a date field to choose which date you want to see stock for |
| Specify Date | This field appears if "Show Stock as at a Historic Date" is checked. You can enter the date you wish to see the historic data for in this field |

# Warehouse Management > Purchase Orders

<a id="prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option"></a>
## 'Prevent Changes' Stock Selection Lock Option

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Scope
- What happens when you select 'prevent changes'
- How to select 'Prevent changes to stock selection'
  - When editing products on a sale order

### Purpose

When adding products to a Sale Order or editing existing products on a Sale Order you are able to select the **Prevent Changes** box and hold that stock selection criteria (custom fields, expiry dates) to that Sale Order. Sale Orders submitted over API/Parsers have **Prevent Changes**selected by default.

### Scope

The Prevent Changes option is available when:

- When adding products to a Sale Order.
- When editing products on a Sale Order.

The Prevent Changes option is selected by default for orders submitted over API/Parsers.

### What happens when you select Prevent Changes

Once you have selected the Prevent Change box, that stock selection criteria will be saved against that product on the Sale Order. This means when CartonCloud conducts its stock optimisation process it will look for stock that meets the criteria you have locked against the product. Therefore, CartonCloud will not allow you to pick stock that varies from the criteria you have locked against the product, for example, the expiry date.

Note, it will only save criteria for expiry dates and custom fields, not warehouse locations.

### How to select Prevent Changes to stock selection

When adding a product to a Sale Order

- Navigate to the Sale Order page, **Warehouse**>**Sale Orders**.
- Select the relevant Sale Order
- Select the **Products** tab.
- Select **+Add Product**.

### ![prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-0.png?width=670&height=154&name=prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-0.png)

- Search for the applicable product.
- Tick the **PREVENT CHANGES** box for the relevant product line or select **Prevent Changes: Select All** to select all product lines

Note, if you choose the Select All option, CartonCloud will ignore the lines with 0 quantity.

- Select the **Take Stock**button.

**When editing product on a Sale Order**

- Navigate to the Sale Order page, **Warehouse**>**Sale Orders**.
- Select the relevant Sale Order
- Select the **Products** tab.
- Select **Edit** against the relevant product line.

### ![prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-1.png?width=670&height=152&name=prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-1.png)

- Tick the **PREVENT CHANGES** box for the relevant product line or select **Prevent Changes: Select All** to select all product lines

Note, if you choose the Select All option, CartonCloud will ignore the lines with 0 quantity.

![prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-2.png?width=670&height=193&name=prevent-changes-stock-selection-lock-option-2.png)

- Select **Save**.

<a id="add-a-purchase-order"></a>
## Add a Purchase Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-a-purchase-order_

### Table of Contents

- How to add a Purchase Order
- Adding Products to the Purchase Order

### How to add a Purchase Order

- Navigate to the Purchase Orders screen, **Warehouse**>**Purchase Orders**.
- Click **+Add New Purchase Order**.

![add-a-purchase-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-purchase-order-0.png?width=670&height=181&name=add-a-purchase-order-0.png)

- Select the Customer you wish to create a Purchase Order for.
- Select the status of the order, arrival date of the stock, the customer's reference for the order and any relevant special instructions.

![add-a-purchase-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-purchase-order-1.png?width=670&height=191&name=add-a-purchase-order-1.png)

- Click **Save**.
- You will now arrive on the **View Purchase Order** page where the remaining details of the Purchase Order can be added.
- Specifically, you will need to add Products to the order, check the charges are correct (and what you expect) and if required upload an invoice to be stored against the order using the **Upload Invoice** button.

### Adding Products to the Purchase Order

To add Products to the Purchase order:

- Select the **Products** tab.
- Select **Add Product**.
- Search for the product you wish to add to the order and fill in the applicable fields.

![add-a-purchase-order-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-purchase-order-2.png?width=670&height=439&name=add-a-purchase-order-2.png)

- Select **Save** or if you wish to add additional Products, select **Save and Add Another**.
- The product's stock record will now be viewable on the Products tab as shown below.

![add-a-purchase-order-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-purchase-order-3.png?width=670&height=175&name=add-a-purchase-order-3.png)

- Once all Purchase Order's details are completed, you can then step through the status updates such as Draft → Approved → Received → Verified & Allocated at the appropriate stages of the stock's physical movement.

For further assistance, see the [View Purchase Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/View+Purchase+Order)page article.

It's important to know that a Purchase Order's status *can* be rolled back, however, there are some implications with doing so. They can also be deleted entirely, and this is covered in[Deleting a Purchase Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Deleting+a+Purchase+Order).

---

<a id="adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order"></a>
## Adding a comment to a Purchase Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- How to add a comment to a purchase order

### Purpose

To add a comment to a Purchase Order through the web app for users (excluding customers) to view (on the web app).

### Benefits

- To record important information against the Purchase Order.
- To communicate key information in relation to the Purchase Order with other users.

### How to add a comment to a Purchase Order

- Navigate to the Purchase Order page, Warehouse > Purchase Orders .
- Select the Purchase Order you wish to add the comment to.
- Select the Comments tab.

![adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-0.png?width=670&height=344&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-0.png)

- Select Add comment .

![adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-1.png?width=670&height=341&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-1.png)

- Enter the comment and click Submit .

![adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-2.png?width=670&height=341&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-purchase-order-2.png)

This comment can now be viewed against the Purchase Order on the web app by other users (excluding customers).

---

<a id="adjusting-stock-quantity"></a>
## Adjusting Stock Quantity

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adjusting-stock-quantity_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How stock adjustments work
- How to make a stock adjustment (increase or decrease quantity)
- How to make stock adjustments in bulk

### Purpose

To make a stock adjustment.

### How stock adjustments work

When you make a stock adjustment (increase or decrease stock quantity) via Adjustment Records, there is a clear traceable path for what stock was adjusted.

You can either **increase** or **decrease** the stock quantity.

When you **increase** the Purchase Order Product stock quantity, a new Purchase Order record will be created (stock is coming in).

When you **decrease** the Purchase Order Product stock quantity, a new Sale Order record will be created (stock is going out).

Depending on your Customer settings, each adjustment made for a day will be added to the same record (per customer). For example, if you decrease the quantity of stock A for one customer and then later in the day decrease the quantity of stock B for the same customer, the decreased quantity from both stock A and B will be added to the same Sale Order. If you wish for a new order to be created each time an adjustment is made, you can change this in the [Sale Order Customer Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/customer-settings-warehouse-management).

### How to make a stock adjustment (increase or decrease quantity)

**Please ensure you have read and followed the steps outlined [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/tQe_Hw) to find the stock you wish to adjust.**

- Locate the stock you wish to adjust (using the instructions outlined here ).
- Click Adjust Stock .

![adjusting-stock-quantity-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adjusting-stock-quantity-0.png?width=670&height=317&name=adjusting-stock-quantity-0.png)

- Scroll down to the bottom and select Update as adjustment from the Qty to Update Method dropdown.

It is recommended that you use the 'Update as adjustment' option and not the 'Update quantity directly' option. This is because if you select the 'Update quantity directly' option, you will be directly modifying the Initial, Onhand and Free quantities with no traceability.

![adjusting-stock-quantity-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adjusting-stock-quantity-1.png?width=670&height=155&name=adjusting-stock-quantity-1.png)

- Enter the quantity to adjust in the Unit Quantity Onhand field.

![adjusting-stock-quantity-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adjusting-stock-quantity-2.png?width=670&height=138&name=adjusting-stock-quantity-2.png)

- Click Edit Qty .
- Using the Stock Movement Report, you will be able to find the adjusted stock record. In addition, you will see if it is an adjustment from the Purchase Order list view and directly within the Purchase Order Product.

![adjusting-stock-quantity-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adjusting-stock-quantity-3.png?width=670&height=113&name=adjusting-stock-quantity-3.png)
![adjusting-stock-quantity-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adjusting-stock-quantity-4.png?width=670&height=240&name=adjusting-stock-quantity-4.png)

### How to make stock adjustments in bulk

To make stock adjustments in bulk, you need to know the customer the stock relates to.

- Navigate to the relevant Customer, Contacts > Customers .

- Under Stock Reports , select Stock Report (detailed) .

![adjustment_7.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka0RF0000007GCv&feoid=00N5j00000Jctsg&refid=0EM5j0000041nRf)

- Click Edit Stocks .

![adjustment_8.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka0RF0000007GCv&feoid=00N5j00000Jctsg&refid=0EM5j0000041nRp)

- Change the stock quantity against the relevant Purchase Order Product by changing the value in the In Warehouse text box.

![adjustment_9.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka0RF0000007GCv&feoid=00N5j00000Jctsg&refid=0EM5j0000041nSE)

- Once you have made the adjustments within that Product Code, select Save. Continue this process for each Product Code.

![adjustment_10.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka0RF0000007GCv&feoid=00N5j00000Jctsg&refid=0EM5j0000041nSJ)

- Click Stop Editing Stocks once you have made all relevant changes.

![adjustment_11.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka0RF0000007GCv&feoid=00N5j00000Jctsg&refid=0EM5j0000041nSi)

In the below video, Tony steps through how to make stock adjustments in bulk.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/OOZYbaPPNA8

---

<a id="backorder-management"></a>
## Backorder Management

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/backorder-management_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits / Use Cases
- Considerations
- Backorder Management Available Workflows
- Viewing Awaiting Stock Orders
- Managing Awaiting Stock Orders
- Email Notifications
- Backorder Management on the Mobile App
- Further enhancements coming in May

### Purpose

Backorder Management enables you to efficiently handle orders that contain out-of-stock products. Through the Sale Order status ‘Awaiting Stock’, orders can be managed and tracked through to fulfilment.

### Benefits / Use Cases

- Manage orders and stock more efficiently and effectively.
- Greater transparency on order and stock management.
- Prevent revenue leakage with the ability to split shipments.
- Improve order management processes.
- Create a more valuable service and experience for your customers.

### Considerations

- There are two tiers of Backorder Management:
  - Essentials Backordering: available to all CartonCloud accounts.
  - Advanced Backordering: only available to WMS Premium accounts, Advanced Backordering offers additional settings and workflows for Backorder Management.
- Backorder Management supports orders that originated from a Self-Managed Shopify Integration.
- If using Backorder Management, it is important that you read the available workflows below and enable the correct settings.
- Cross Customer Picking is supported with Backorder Management.

### Backorder Management Available Workflows

When an order is imported with products that are out of stock, there are two Customer settings that control the order’s behaviour:

- Sale Order Importing
- Automatic Sale Order Stock Allocation

If using Backorder Management, you will need to select the correct settings to enable the desired workflow for your operations. The applicable settings and corresponding workflow are outlined below:

| **Sale Order Importing Setting:** *If Sale Order is Imported and (any) product(s) are out of stock (or not enough stock)* | **Automatic Sale Order Stock Allocation Setting:** *Automatically allocate stock as it becomes available for Awaiting Stock Sale Orders* | **Workflow** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Assign whatever stock is available, keeping unavailable quantities as unassigned products. | Always | Upon import, the Sale Order will be in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status. Products that are in stock will be assigned to the order, and items not in stock will be left as unassigned products.  By allocating available stock, Awaiting Stock orders will essentially “Hold” stock, preventing other orders from taking it. Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the unassigned products, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order. **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. Once all unassigned products are assigned, the order will be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |
| Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order. | Always | Upon import, the Sale Order will be split:   Stock that is available on one Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status   Stock that is not available on another Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status   Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order. **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. Once all unassigned products are assigned, the order will be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |
| Assign whatever stock is available, keeping unavailable quantities as unassigned products | Never | Upon import, the Sale Order will be in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status, and products that are in stock will be assigned to the order, and items not in stock will be left as unassigned products.  Stock will have to be manually assigned to the Sale Order once it becomes available. |
| Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order | Never | Upon import, the Sale Order will be split:   Stock that is available on one Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status   Stock that is not available on another Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status   Stock will have to be manually assigned to the Sale Order once it becomes available. |
| Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, but only if stock is not expected to arrive in a configured number of days.  ***[Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Backordering) Only Workflow*** | Always | Upon import, the Sale Order will be split:   Stock that is available on one Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status   Stock that is not available on another Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status   However, this **will only occur** if the stock is **not** expected to arrive in the configured number of days. If the stock is expected to arrive in the configured number of days, the order will not be split.  Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the unassigned products, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order. **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. Once all unassigned products are assigned, the order will be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |
| Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, but only if stock is not expected to arrive in a configured number of days.  ***[Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Backordering) Only Workflow*** | Never | Upon import, the Sale Order will be split:   Stock that is available on one Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status   Stock that is not available on another Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status   However, this **will only occur** if the stock is **not** expected to arrive in the configured number of days. If the stock is expected to arrive in the configured number of days, the order will not be split.  Stock will have to be manually assigned to the Sale Order once it becomes available. |
| Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, but only if stock is not expected to arrive in a configured number of days.  ***[Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Backordering) Only Workflow*** | Only if all of the stock for the Sale Order is available. | Upon import, the Sale Order will be split:   Stock that is available on one Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status   Stock that is not available on another Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status   However, this **will only occur** if the stock is **not** expected to arrive in the configured number of days. If the stock is expected to arrive in the configured number of days, the order will not be split.  Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order **only if the allocation will completely fulfil the Sale Order.** **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. The order will then be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |
| Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, but only if stock is not expected to arrive in a configured number of days.  ***[Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Backordering) Only Workflow*** | Only if the remaining stock on an order is expected within X configured number of days | Upon import, the Sale Order will be split:   Stock that is available on one Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status   Stock that is not available on another Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status   However, this **will only occur** if the stock is **not** expected to arrive in the configured number of days. If the stock is expected to arrive in the configured number of days, the order will not be split.  Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order **only if the unassigned stock of the order arrives within the configured number of days.** **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. The order will then be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |
| Assign whatever stock is available, keeping unavailable quantities as unassigned products. ***[Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Backordering) Only Workflow*** | Only if all of the stock for the Sale Order is available. | Upon import, the Sale Order will be in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status. Products that are in stock will be assigned to the order, and items not in stock will be left as unassigned products.  By allocating available stock, Awaiting Stock orders will essentially “Hold” stock, preventing other orders from taking it. Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order **only if the allocation will completely fulfil the Sale Order.** **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. The order will then be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |
| Assign whatever stock is available, keeping unavailable quantities as unassigned products. ***[Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Backordering) Only Workflow*** | Only if the remaining stock on an order is expected within X configured number of days | Upon import, the Sale Order will be in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status. Products that are in stock will be assigned to the order, and items not in stock will be left as unassigned products.  By allocating available stock, Awaiting Stock orders will essentially “Hold” stock, preventing other orders from taking it. Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order **only if the unassigned stock of the order arrives within the configured number of days.** **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. The order will then be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |
| Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order. ***[Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Backordering) Only Workflow*** | Only if all of the stock for the Sale Order is available. | Upon import, the Sale Order will be split:   Stock that is available on one Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status   Stock that is not available on another Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status         Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order **only if the allocation will completely fulfil the Sale Order.** **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. The order will then be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |
| Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order. ***[Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Backordering) Only Workflow*** | Only if the remaining stock on an order is expected within X configured number of days | Upon import, the Sale Order will be split:   Stock that is available on one Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status   Stock that is not available on another Sale Order in an ‘Awaiting Stock’ status         Once stock becomes available (once the Purchase Order containing the stock reaches the status configured in the Minimum POP status setting) for the ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, the stock will be automatically assigned to the Sale Order **only if the unassigned stock of the order arrives within the configured number of days.** **Note:** Auto-allocation is only triggered when a Purchase Order changes its status. Therefore, any changes in POPs linked to a Purchase Order (e.g. changes to individual Purchase Order Products) or changes to the *Minimum Purchase Order Status* setting **will not** trigger the automatic allocation process. The order will then be updated from ‘Awaiting Stock’ to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status. |

**To access the above Customer Settings:**

- Navigate to the relevant Customer you wish to enable the Backorder Management workflow, **Contacts** > **Customers**.
- Click **Edit** at the bottom of the page.
- Navigate to the **Warehouse Management** > **Sale Order** tab.
- The applicable settings are under **When a New Sale Order is Imported** and **Automatic Sale Order Stock Allocation** heading.

Note, the setting 'Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new "Awaiting Stock" Sale Order, but only if stock is not expected to arrive in a configured number of days' is only available for [Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-backordering).

![backorder-management-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-0.png?width=670&height=253&name=backorder-management-0.png)

Note, the setting 'Only is all of the stock for the Sale order is available' and 'Only if the remaining stock on an order is expected within configured number of days' is only available for [Advanced Backordering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-backordering).

![backorder-management-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-1.png?width=670&height=316&name=backorder-management-1.png)

### Viewing Awaiting Stock Orders

**To view Awaiting Stock orders:**

- Navigate to the Sale Order page, **Warehouse** > **Sale Orders**.
- Along the filter panel, select **Awaiting Stock**.

![backorder-management-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-2.png?width=670&height=177&name=backorder-management-2.png)

- From here, you will see all orders in Awaiting Stock status.

**To view split Awaiting Stock Sale Orders:**

- Navigate to the ‘**Awaiting Stock**’ Sale Order (following instructions above).
- Select the **Group** tab on the Awaiting Pick and Pack Sale Order.

![backorder-management-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-3.png?width=670&height=325&name=backorder-management-3.png)

- You will be able to see the split orders and access them by selecting the order.

![backorder-management-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-4.png?width=670&height=213&name=backorder-management-4.png)

**To view the history logs on a split Sale Order:**

- By selecting the **History** tab against the Sale Order, you will be able to see in the history logs if the order was split.

![backorder-management-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-5.png?width=670&height=193&name=backorder-management-5.png)

### Managing Awaiting Stock Orders

For orders in Awaiting Stock status, there are three options to manage the order:

#### **1) Wait until stock is available**

If you would like to wait for the entire order to be fulfilled before shipping, you can leave the Sale Order in the ‘Awaiting Stock’ status until all products become available. Once the products are available, you can either assign the stock manually, or, if enabled, it can assign automatically.

**Automatic Assignment:**

Refer to the Automatic Sale Order Stock Selection Setting mentioned [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com#backorder-management-available-workflows).

**Manual Assignment:**

- Navigate to the Awaiting Stock order.
- Select the **Products** tab.
- Click either **Auto Assign All Unassigned Stock** or **Assign** against the product line.

![backorder-management-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-6.png?width=670&height=290&name=backorder-management-6.png)

- The order will now be updated to Awaiting Pick and Pack status.

#### **2) Split the order**

If you would like to ship available stock and maintain the unavailable stock on an ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, you can split the order manually or automatically.

**To split the order automatically:**

Refer to the Sale Import Setting mentioned [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com#backorder-management-available-workflows).

**To split the order manually:**

- Navigate to the Awaiting Stock order.
- On the Details tab, select **Manage Available Products**.

Note, if you do not have any available products assigned, the button will not be available as the order cannot be split.

- You will have two options: select the second option, **Split unavailable products to a new order and update this order to ‘Awaiting Pick and Pack’ status**.
- Click **Confirm**.

![backorder-management-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-8.png?width=670&height=210&name=backorder-management-8.png)

- You will be able to view the split Sale Order by selecting the Group tab on the Awaiting Pick and Pack Sale Order.

![backorder-management-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-9.png?width=670&height=325&name=backorder-management-9.png)

- You will be able to see the split orders.

![backorder-management-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-10.png?width=670&height=213&name=backorder-management-10.png)

#### **3) Remove unavailable products and ship what is available**

If you would like to remove unavailable products and ship what is available, you can do so manually or automatically.

**To remove unavailable products automatically:**

Refer to the Sale Import Setting mentioned [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com#backorder-management-available-workflows).

**To remove unavailable products manually:**

- Navigate to the Awaiting Stock order.
- On the Details tab, select **Manage Available Products**.

Note, if you do not have any available products assigned, the button will not be available.

*![backorder-management-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-11.png?width=670&height=320&name=backorder-management-11.png)*

- You will have two options: select the first option, **Remove unavailable products and update the order to "Awaiting Pick and Pack" status**.
- Click **Confirm**.

![backorder-management-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/backorder-management-12.png?width=670&height=210&name=backorder-management-12.png)

### Email Notifications

Notifications can be enabled for Backorder Management. This includes:

- When an order is moved into an Awaiting Stock status

To enable these notifications, please see [Configuring Outgoing Email Notifications](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/configuring-outgoing-notification-emails-to-customers).

### Backorder Management on the Mobile App

#### **Mobile App (from version 6.24.0+)**

To improve clarity and reduce confusion during picking, Awaiting Stock orders display stock status using **distinct visual cues**:

- **Unassigned** and **Not Yet Received** items are shown in **red text**.
- The **quantity is displayed as a single total only**, e.g. **2 Units** rather than **0/2 Units**.
- The **circular status indicators** (used to show allocation progress) are **not displayed** for these orders.
- **Tapping on items** in Awaiting Stock orders is **disabled**—packers cannot open item rows.
- Sorting is still available and follows the same order as previous item listings.

These changes help warehouse staff quickly distinguish between what is ready for picking and what is pending allocation, without needing to open individual items or misinterpret availability.

#### **Example Display**

- If 2 cartons of an item are still awaiting stock assignment, the item will appear as:
  - **"2 Cartons"** in **red**
  - No status circle
  - Tapping disabled

<a id="bulk-export-purchase-orders"></a>
## Bulk Export Purchase Orders

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/bulk-export-purchase-orders_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to generate the Bulk Export Purchase Orders Report
- Report Fields

### Purpose

The Bulk Export Purchase Order page allows you to export a CSV spreadsheet from CartonCloud containing all data associated with your Purchase Orders which were either added or arrived over a specified date period.

Each Purchase Order Product record on a Purchase Order will generate a new row on the report.

### How to generate the Bulk Export Purchase Orders Report

- Navigate to Reports > Bulk Export Purchase Orders .
- Choose whether to use the date the Purchase Order was added to the system or the date the Purchase Order arrived into the Warehouse as the filter.
- Then choose the beginning and ending dates for the report to run.
- Select Go and the CSV file will be downloaded.

![bulk-export-purchase-orders-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-export-purchase-orders-0.png?width=670&height=288&name=bulk-export-purchase-orders-0.png)

### Report Fields

The generated report will contain the following fields for each Purchase Order Product line:

- id
- customer
- customer_reference
- status
- date_added
- last_modifed
- arrival_date
- adjustment
- invoice_id
- income
- expense
- warehouse
- charge_scheme
- value
- order_urgent
- customer_urgent
- Chilled Temperature
- Dry Temperature
- Frozen Temperature
- purchase_order_product_id
- customer_code
- date_allocated
- date_depleted
- product_name
- product_type
- product_status
- warehouse_location
- pallet_id
- product_unit_of_measure
- unit_quantity_inital
- unit_quantity_onhand
- unit_quantity_free
- expiry_date
- custom_field 1 to 10
- pop_custom_field 1 to 10

<a id="changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order"></a>
## Changing the Allocated Date of a Purchase Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Step by step guide
- Unable to change the allocated date of a purchase order

### Purpose

CartonCloud allows you to change the allocated date of a Purchase Order. This is the date that stock was assigned to a Warehouse Location and therefore the date that the system uses to begin billing for storage in most scenarios.

Being able to change the allocated date is used to fix minor mistakes in the receiving process (for example the Purchase Order arrived on Friday and you could not process it until next Monday). However please note that changing allocated dates *will* *affect storage changes and impact invoice calculation*.

### Step by step guide

1. At the Purchase Order verification stage, you can allocate some of the products and come back later to allocate the rest, so the allocated date is bound to the products and each product could have a different allocated date, on the Purchase Order view page you can find the allocated date range. Most of the time it is a single date.

![changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-0.png?width=670&height=338&name=changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-0.png)

2. Click the **Change** button next to Date Allocated.

3. A box will appear on the screen. Choose the new allocated date by clicking the text field in the modal box. The date selection range is restricted to present and past dates only. This is because:

- Someone might create a new Sale Order from this Purchase Order on the same day, so you cannot allocate the Purchase Order to a future date.
- There might be some Sale Orders already created from this Purchase Order in the past, so you can not allocate the Purchase Order to dates that are after when the Sale Order is packed.
- If you have moved some Purchase Order Products to other warehouse locations in the past, the system would have depleted the original Purchase Order Products and created new ones for the new warehouse locations, hence you can not change the allocated date to be later than that date you moved the Products in the past.

![changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-1.png?width=670&height=215&name=changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-1.png)

4. There is also the option displayed on the change date screen above, which defaults to only changing original Purchase Order products.

5. This means that it will change all pallets and products that were created at the time of receiving the Purchase Order if stock is split (e.g. new pallets are split off and created), then they have a new allocated date as at the time the user-created them in the system. To change those pallets as well from the Purchase Order, unselect the box and then the Allocated Date will change for all other non-original pallets as well. i.e. all the stock that was created downstream from the originals as well, effectively updating everything on the Purchase Order to the new Allocated Date.

6. When you click the **Update** button, it will update all the original Purchase Order Products (excluding the ones created by reallocation)

If necessary, storage charges will be recalculated automatically by the system.

### Unable to change the Allocated Date of a Purchase Order

If you have received an error message like the below then you are attempting to backdate a Purchase order's allocated date over a storage period which has already been billed.

![changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-2.png?width=670&height=37&name=changing-the-allocated-date-of-a-purchase-order-2.png)
The system blocks this behaviour as usually the reason to backdate the allocated date of stock is to ensure you are charging storage for its entire stay in the warehouse.

To stop this error from appearing and successfully backdate the allocated date you will need to go to all invoices in the error message and roll them back to "draft" status by following the below steps.

- Click the link in the error message.
- On the invoice, select **Edit**.
- Select Invoice History status, then select Draft.
- Select **Save** and the invoice will be changed to "Draft" status.
- Once this process has been followed for every invoice in the error message you will then be able to backdate the allocated date. Ensure you followed all steps from the above Step-By-Step guide including recalculation.
- You may then wish to update those invoices to "Approved" status again.

---

<a id="deleting-a-purchase-order"></a>
## Deleting a Purchase Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/deleting-a-purchase-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps
- Errors when deleting purchase orders

### Purpose

This article details how to delete a Purchase Order and therefore remove the stock which came into the warehouse on that Purchase Order from your warehouse.

### How to steps

- Navigate to the Purchase Order page, Warehouse > Purchase Order.
- Select the Purchase Order you wish to delete.
- Revert the status of the order to Draft.

Only Purchase Orders that are in Draft status can be deleted

- After reading the warning prompt, if you wish to still proceed, type I UNDERSTAND in the pop-up box.

![deleting-a-purchase-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deleting-a-purchase-order-0.png?width=559&height=366&name=deleting-a-purchase-order-0.png)

- Click the Delete button.

![deleting-a-purchase-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deleting-a-purchase-order-1.png?width=670&height=295&name=deleting-a-purchase-order-1.png)

- A prompt asking, if you are sure, will appear on the screen, select OK .

### Errors when deleting purchase orders

It is possible for errors to appear when a user is attempting to delete a Purchase Order.

**"Purchase Order contains Products which are associated with Packed Sale Orders"**

This error indicates that there is Purchase Order Products associated with the Purchase Order which are still linked to a Sale Order in Packed or Dispatched status, even when the Purchase Order Product has the same Initial/Onhand/Free quantity.

The error is caused by the following steps:

1. A Sale Order takes stock from an allocated Purchase Order
2. The Sale Order is Packed/Dispatched
3. A product on the Sale Order is edited/deleted creating a post-pack correction , putting the stock back onto the Purchase Order Product record, but still maintaining a link as to what "should" have been picked.

As the link between Sale Order and Purchase Order still exists, this prevents the Purchase Order from being deleted.

**How to Resolve:**

This error can be resolved by removing the link between Sale Order and Purchase Order. Note, if you have multiple affected Sale Order Products, you'll need to repeat these steps for each affected Sale Order:

1. Using the links provided, navigate to the affected Sale Order Product record.
2. From here, use the link to get to the associated Sale Order
3. Revert the status of the Sale Order to "Awaiting Pick and Pack" as shown below.

![deleting-a-purchase-order-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deleting-a-purchase-order-2.png?width=670&height=453&name=deleting-a-purchase-order-2.png)

When the status is reverted, all post-pack corrections are removed from the order, removing the link to the Purchase Order. You can now delete the Purchase Order.

You can also mark the order as packed in one-step using the Complete Packing button.

---

<a id="how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock"></a>
## How to change the status of a Purchase Order Product (Stock)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use cases
- How to update the status of a purchase order product (stock)
- Bulk edit purchase order product status

### Purpose

To update the status of a Product on a Purchase Order.

### Use cases

Changing the status of a Purchase Order Product (stock) is helpful in scenarios when:

- Stock arrives damaged.
- Stock goes missing in the Warehouse.
- Stock goes into Quarantine.

See the [Product Statuses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Statuses) article for further information on why using Product Statuses can be beneficial.

### How to update the status of a Purchase Order Product (Stock)

Please ensure you have read and followed the steps outlined [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/stock-adjustments) to find the stock you wish to adjust.

- Locate the stock you wish to adjust (using the instructions outlined here ).
- Click Change Status .

![how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-0.png?width=670&height=291&name=how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-0.png)

- Select the status to change from the Change Status To dropdown menu.
- Enter the quantity in the Quantity to Update field.
- Click Change Product Status .

Note, depending on your [Customer Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/customer-settings-warehouse-management), changing the status of a Purchase Order product [can trigger CartonCloud to stop charging storage](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-statuses).

![how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-1.png?width=670&height=268&name=how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-1.png)

- You will trace the Product Status change on the history tab on the Purchase Order Product.

![how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-2.png?width=670&height=189&name=how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-2.png)

### Bulk edit Purchase Order Product Status

- Navigate to the relevant Purchase Order you wish to update the Products status on, Warehouse>Purchase Orders.
- Select the Products tab.
- Click Bulk Edit Purchase Order Products Statuses .

![how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-3.png?width=670&height=196&name=how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-3.png)

- Enter the quantity to change in the Quantity to Update field.
- Select the status you wish to change to from the Change Status to dropdown.

If SSCC is enabled, you will have the option to create a new SSCC when the new POP record is created upon status or quantity change.

![how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-4.png?width=670&height=294&name=how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-4.png)

- The new statuses will be visible on the Purchase Order.

![how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-5.png?width=670&height=218&name=how-to-change-the-status-of-a-purchase-order-product-stock-5.png)

<a id="how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock"></a>
## How to Merge Pallets of Stock

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Merge pallets from the product
- Merge pallets from the warehouse location

### Purpose

For stock in a Bulk Warehouse Location, you can merge the stock into one pallet. By merging pallets, CartonCloud treats the stock as a single pallet for charging and stock picking on Sale Orders.

You can merge pallets of stock either from within the **Product** or from the **Warehouse Location**.

### Merge pallets from the product

To merge pallets from the Product:

- Navigate to the Products page, Warehouse > Products .
- Select the Product of stock you wish to merge pallets for.
- Select the Stock tab from within the Product.

![how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-0.png?width=670&height=310&name=how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-0.png)

- Select the stock line you wish to merge using the checkboxes.
- Select the blue Move button.

![how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-1.png?width=670&height=136&name=how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-1.png)

- Enter the quantity you wish to merge
- Choose the warehouse location you are merging the pallet into (where the other pallet you are merging it with should already be)
- Change the drop-down to Merge with Existing Pallet
- Select which Pallet you wish to Merge the stock into in the pop-up window, then Close the pop-up.
- Select Move, and the merge will be completed.

![how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-2.png?width=670&height=191&name=how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-2.png)

- The result should be 2 or more records (depending on the number of Pallets you are merging) with the same Pallet.

### Merge pallets from the Warehouse Location

Note that you can only merge pallets for stock in a Bulk Warehouse Location.

- Navigate to the Warehouse Location page, Warehouse > Warehouse Locations .
- Select the Bulk Warehouse Location that has the pallets you wish to merge.
- Select the Stock tab.
- Click Bulk Move Stock .

![how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-3.png?width=670&height=201&name=how-to-merge-pallets-of-stock-3.png)

- Enter the quantity you wish to move in the Move QTY box.
- Select the Bulk Warehouse Location you wish to move the stock to.
- Select Merge with Existing Pallet from the Pallet dropdown.
- Select the Pallet you wish to merge the pallet with.
- Select Close .
- Click Move .

---

<a id="how-to-record-unique-references-against-stock-that-is-already-in-the-warehouse"></a>
## How to record unique references against stock that is already in the warehouse

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-record-unique-references-against-stock-that-is-already-in-the-warehouse_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to record unique references against stock in the warehouse

### Purpose

To record unique references (for example, Serial number) against stock that is already in a warehouse. This process is useful when you first start to use the unique reference scanning in your operations and you need to record references against existing stock.

### Prerequisites

You need to have set up your unique references (Purchase Order Product Custom Fields) against the stock you wish to record the reference for. Please see [Purchase Order (inbound) unique reference scanning](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Purchase-Order-inbound-unique-reference-scanning) for more information.

### How to record unique references against stock in the warehouse

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/P4wcseNVmfU

- On the mobile app, select Scan Move .
- Scan the location the stock is in that you wish to record the unique reference against.
- Ensure the Move Cart is turned off .
- If a product is set up correctly for unique references and there is no unique reference recorded against it, you will see a barcode icon against the item.
- Select the barcode icon.

![how-to-record-unique-references-against-stock-that-is-already-in-the-warehouse-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-record-unique-references-against-stock-that-is-already-in-the-warehouse-0.png?width=297&height=602&name=how-to-record-unique-references-against-stock-that-is-already-in-the-warehouse-0.png)

![how-to-record-unique-references-against-stock-that-is-already-in-the-warehouse-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-record-unique-references-against-stock-that-is-already-in-the-warehouse-1.png?width=289&height=581&name=how-to-record-unique-references-against-stock-that-is-already-in-the-warehouse-1.png)

- Scan or manually record the unique reference against the item and select Done .

<a id="how-to-remove-all-stock-for-a-customer"></a>
## How to remove all stock for a Customer

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-remove-all-stock-for-a-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to remove all stock for a Customer
- Considerations

### Purpose

To remove all stock for a customer from a specific warehouse. This process removes the customer's stock through an adjustment Sale Order.

### Prerequisites

- Reconcile the customer's orders to check whether any stock is allocated. This process will not adjust any stock which is already allocated to orders.
- Ensure the setting "Create new sale order for every adjustment?" is disabled. This is to avoid the system creating a separate adjustment for each individual product for that customer.

### How to remove all stock for a Customer

- Navigate to Contacts > Customers .
- Select the Customer you wish to remove the stock for and click Edit .
- Select the Warehouse Management tab followed by the Storage tab.
- Select the Remove All of the Customers Stock from the Warehouse button.

![how-to-remove-all-stock-for-a-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-remove-all-stock-for-a-customer-0.png?width=670&height=199&name=how-to-remove-all-stock-for-a-customer-0.png)

### Considerations

- This process will only remove stock for the customer from the specific warehouse you are currently working in. If the customer has stock in multiple warehouses and you need to remove stock from all warehouses you will need to repeat this process for each warehouse.
- The adjustment Sale Order made from this process can then be removed if a mistake is made.
