<a id="how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer"></a>
## How to set up low stock notifications for your customer

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits of using low stock notifications
- When is a low stock notification sent?
- How to set up low stock notifications

### Purpose

In CartonCloud, you have the ability to set up low stock notifications for your customer's products. You can choose what level the stock needs to reach before a notification is sent to your customer (or the specified email address).

### Benefits of using low stock notifications

- Increased visibility for your customer
- Automatic updates without manual work or intervention
- Reduced number of emails/communication with your customer as they are notified automatically and instantly

### ​​​​​​​ When is a low stock notification sent?

A low stock notification will be sent out the day that the on-hand quantity goes below the threshold. The notification will only be sent out once. The notification will not be sent again until another instance when the on-hand quantity goes below the threshold (note, the on-hand quantity must first go back above the threshold before it goes back down below the threshold again).

### How to set up low stock notifications

To set up low stock notifications for your customer, you need to complete two steps:

**1. Enable the low stock notification against the relevant product and set the low stock threshold**

There are two ways you can enable and set the low stock notification (a) individually against the product or (b) in bulk using the export/import feature

**Update an individual Product:**

- Navigate to the relevant Product, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Edit the Product.
- Scroll down to where the Expiry Threshold Days are set. You will see a tick option,**Enable Low Stock Notification**.
- Tick the **Enable Low Stock Notification** option.
- The **Low Stock Threshold**field will then appear. Enter the threshold level.

![how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-0.png?width=670&height=341&name=how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-0.png)

- Scroll down and select **Save**.

**Update Products in bulk:**

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Select **More**>**Export Products**.
- Open the downloaded file.
- Scroll across to the column labelled **Low Stock Notification**.
- To enable it, type Yes for the row of the relevant Products.
- In the column labelled **Low Stock Threshold**, enter the threshold quantity.
- Save the file.
- Navigate back to CartonCloud and the **Products** page.
- Select **More**>**Import Products**. Select the file to upload.
- Once the file is processed, the Products will be updated.

**2. Enable the low stock notification against the customer and the relevant email address**

Note, to set up email notifications, you need to ensure the applicable notifications are selected in the Notifications tab. If you do not make a selection in the Notifications tab, the notifications will NOT work.

- Navigate to the Customers page, **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click **Edit**.
- Select the **Email** > **Addresse**s tab.
- If the email address is already listed, click **Edit** against the email address.
- if the email address does not exist, type the address into the **New email** field and click **Add new email**.

![how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-1.png?width=670&height=355&name=how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-1.png)

If you are adding a new email address, ensure you enter a name in the Name field.

- Tick the **Stock Notification** option and any other notifications you wish to set up for this email address.

![how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-2.png?width=670&height=314&name=how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-2.png)

- Scroll down to the bottom of the page and select **Save**.

You need to select notifications within both the Addresses and Notifications tab. Email notifications will not work if you do not select the appropriate notifications from the Notifications tab.

- Select the **Notifications** tab. This tab gives you greater control over what type of notifications you wish to enable. For example, if you selected Purchase Order Notifications against the email address in the Addresses tab, you would then need to select what type of Purchase Order notifications you want to enable from the Notifications tab. You will need to ensure the **Stock Notification Configuration** is ticked.
- Tick the relevant Notifications you wish to enable.

![how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-3.png?width=670&height=321&name=how-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customerhow-to-set-up-low-stock-notifications-for-your-customer-3.png)

If you have ticked a notification against an email address, you need to ensure they are also ticked in the Notifications tab in order for the notification to work.

- Scroll down to the bottom of the page and select **Save**.

---

<a id="import-stock"></a>
## Import Stock

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/import-stock_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps
- Including Custom Fields within the import file
- Dates within the import file
- Including Pallet Barcodes within the import file

### Purpose

The import stock feature allows you to bring stock into your Warehouse for a single Customer without generating inbound handling charges for that stock. This differs from creating a normal Purchase Order which will generate the inbound handling charges (if they are set up).

### How to steps

- Navigate to the Purchase Orders page, **Warehouse** > **Purchase Orders**.
- Select the More button and then click **Import Stock**.
- The Import Stock feature will require you to import a CSV file with the stock's details filled out within each column.
- To begin, you will need to select Download Sample Data. This will download a sample excel file with a format you can follow.

![import-stock-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/import-stock-0.png?width=670&height=281&name=import-stock-0.png)

- In the CSV file provided, fill each row for the stock you wish to import. Please note that you must use exactly the same Product Code and Product Name provided during the Product setup, otherwise, it will not be able to match up the imported stock to a Product record. If you are unsure what the product_name or product_code recorded is, it's best to refer back to the Products page in an extra tab of your browser.

Warehouse locations can either be allocated directly in the spreadsheet or left blank and allocated later when processing the generated Purchase Order.

- Once the spreadsheet is complete, save it to your computer and go back to the **Import Stock** page. Then select**Choose file** and choose the CSV file you just saved.
- Finally, select the customer the product belongs to and click **Upload File**.
- Provided the import was successful, a result page will display in the browser and a purchase order will be created for the new stock.

### Dates within the import file

When importing dates via the Stock import it is recommended that you follow the date format of YYYY-MM-DD.

- Dates that contain - are first parsed in as YYYY-MM-DD. If this does not yield a result they will be parsed in as MM-DD-YYYY.
- Dates that contain / or . are parsed as DD-MM-YYYY

### Including Custom Fields within the import file

When updating Custom Fields with an input type of date, the date format must be YYYY-MM-DD

If you have [Custom Purchase Order Product fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Custom+Fields+for+Purchase+Order+Products) set up for the Products you are importing it is possible to include the data for those fields within the file.

To do this you will need to create a new column and name it "custom_field_x" where x is the number of the custom field you wish to include.

In the example shown below, you can see we have included "custom_field_1" as a new column in the spreadsheet to match the Custom Field 1 created to store the Batch number.

The batch number for each product can then be stored in each row below that column. In the example provided "134235" will be stored as the Batch number for the stock with the product name "Red Cordial 1L Bottle".

### Including Pallet Barcodes within the import file

When importing stock you have the option to include the pallet barcode. This avoids having to adjust stock after the import and ensures the pallet barcode is assigned to the correct stock.

When including the Pallet Barcode on the import file it should be noted that:

- You will need to manually add a column to the import file with the heading pallet_barcode and then add the pallet barcode to this column on the file. It will not work without adding this heading.
- If the pallet barcode on the import is already in use, and contains stock which is allocated to a warehouse location, the warehouse location on the import must match the current location of the pallet. If not, the import will fail. Pallets cannot exist in two warehouse locations simultaneously.
- The Pallet Barcode must be a CartonCloud Pallet Barcode (generated from within CartonCloud. Please see Pallet Handling for steps on how to generate a pallet barcode within CartonCloud).
- The Pallet Barcode must be the full barcode.

See [Pallet Barcode Behaviour](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pallet-Barcode-Behaviour) and [Pallet Handling](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pallet-Handling) for more information.

---

<a id="pallet-barcode-behaviour"></a>
## Pallet Barcode Behaviour

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pallet-barcode-behaviour_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Pallet Barcode
- When is a Pallet Barcode generated
- When is a Pallet Barcode not generated
- Pallet Barcode example behaviour scenarios

### What is a Pallet Barcode

The Pallet Barcode is the unique barcode associated with a pallet in CartonCloud. This barcode is used to track, move, merge pallets and locate the pallet to a warehouse location. The Pallet Barcode can be automatically generated or manually assigned to a pallet, depending on the situation.

### When is a Pallet Barcode generated?

- A Pallet Barcode can be manually generated via the mobile app before it is located (see [Pallet Handling](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pallet-Handling) for more information)
- A Pallet Barcode is automatically generated when it is assigned to a Bulk Pallet Location
- A Pallet Barcode is automatically assigned when the stock is moved to a pallet barcode of existing stock in a warehouse location (it will take on the existing pallet barcode)
- If the pallet has a unique reference custom field then a Pallet Barcode will automatically be generated when the unique reference is captured (if the Pallet Barcode hasn’t already been manually assigned to the Purchase Order Products)
- A Pallet Barcode will be automatically generated for Purchase Order Products after they are bulk split. If the original Purchase Order Product being split already has a Pallet Barcode then it will be maintained, but the new split Purchase Order Products will receive new barcodes.

### When is a Pallet Barcode not generated?

If none of the above scenarios applies, then a Pallet Barcode will not generate when:

- You move an unallocated pallet with no Pallet Barcode to a single pallet warehouse location
- When you move one pallet with no Pallet Barcode from one single pallet warehouse location to another single pallet warehouse location
- If a Purchase Order Product already has a Pallet Barcode and all stock is being moved then a new Pallet Barcode will not be generated.

### Pallet Barcode behaviour example scenarios

**Stock is located from a Purchase Order to a single pallet warehouse location**

- A Pallet Barcode will not be generated (unless the Pallet Barcode is manually assigned or generated via the mobile app)

**Stock is located from a Purchase Order to a multiple pallet warehouse location**

- A Pallet Barcode will automatically be generated

**Stock is located from a Purchase Order with a unique reference into a single or multiple pallet warehouse location**

- Pallets with unique references will have a Pallet Barcode automatically generated when the unique reference is captured and the Pallet Barcode is retained regardless of the type of warehouse location it will be assigned to

**Stock is moved from a single pallet to a single pallet (with some stock)**

- If the pallet is not allocated to a warehouse location, the stock that moves will retain the Pallet Barcode.
- If the pallet was allocated to a single pallet warehouse location or bulk pallet location and the stock moves to a single pallet location then the Pallet Barcode on the moved product will be removed and it will have no Pallet Barcode.
- If the pallet was allocated to a single pallet warehouse location or bulk pallet location and the stock moves to a bulk pallet warehouse location the Pallet Barcode will change for the moved product.
- If the pallet was allocated to a single pallet or bulk pallet warehouse location and the product is moved but not allocated to a warehouse location the Pallet Barcode will be removed and the product will have no pallet

**Stock is moved and scanned directly to another Pallet Barcode**

- The stock will take on the Pallet Barcode it has been moved to and the warehouse location

---

<a id="pallet-handling"></a>
## Pallet Handling

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pallet-handling_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits / use cases
- How to pre-print pallet labels in bulk
- How to assign a pallet barcode during the inbound process
- How to print pallet labels during the inbound process
- How to print pallet labels from the web app
- How to apply pallet labels to stock already in the warehouse
- How to merge pallets when allocating pallets to a bulk location
- How to import Purchase Orders with a pallet barcode assigned

### Purpose

CartonCloud allows you to print, assign and scan pallet labels throughout the system. Pallet labels can be applied when stock arrives, or, to stock already in the warehouse. Pallet labels can be used to locate stock to a location, move stock between locations, to consolidate stock, or to split stock apart.

Pallet labels can be automatically generated when new stock arrives, or pre-printed in bulk and assigned to stock that is arriving. Pallet labels can also be used when picking to specify or verify the stock being picked.

Pallet labels can be printed either from the mobile or web app.

### Benefits/use cases

- Ability to print pallet labels in bulk (avoid continually accessing the printer, can instead only go to the printer once)
- Ability to assign a pallet barcode to a pallet (don't have to use the one automatically assigned if a pallet label has already been printed)
- Print pallet labels during the inbound process (don't have to pre-print them in bulk)
- Can easily can and move a pallet with pallet barcodes
- Streamline the inbound process, locate and move stock process with pallet barcodes. All stock on the pallet can be scanned once to move it with the pallet barcode.
- Pallet barcodes can be used for Reallocation
- Create a multi-product pallet which contains a mix of different products.

Note: CartonCloud currently only supports pallet labels which were generated from within CartonCloud itself. However, we’re working to enhance this to support externally-generated pallet labels, and will allow these to be specified on incoming Purchase Order docs so they can be scanned to allow for quicker receiving.

### How to pre-print pallet labels in bulk

- From the Purchase Orders mode within the App, select the menu navigation icon in the top left corner of the screen.

![pallet-handling-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-0.png?width=218&height=432&name=pallet-handling-0.png)

- Select Pallet Label Printing .

![pallet-handling-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-1.png?width=237&height=480&name=pallet-handling-1.png)

- Enter the number of pallets requiring labels and the number of copies per label.

![pallet-handling-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-2.png?width=254&height=512&name=pallet-handling-2.png)

- Click Print .

![pallet-handling-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-3.png?width=257&height=516&name=pallet-handling-3.png)

- You will now have a number of pallet labels, from here you can assign the pallet barcode to the pallets during the receival process. This process is outlined below.

### How to assign a pallet barcode during the inbound process

You can assign a pallet barcode to pallets on a Purchase Order at any point during the receival process. Once you have clicked ‘Receive’ against the order you can assign the pallet barcode before or after you have recorded the unique references. In the below case, the pallet barcode will be assigned before the unique reference is recorded against each line of stock.

- Click Receive against the relevant Purchase Order.

![pallet-handling-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-4.png?width=267&height=541&name=pallet-handling-4.png)

- Click the pallet you wish to assign a pallet barcode to.
- Select the carton icon next to the scan icon.

![pallet-handling-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-5.png?width=256&height=522&name=pallet-handling-5.png)

- Scan the pallet barcode and click Continue .

![pallet-handling-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-6.png?width=242&height=491&name=pallet-handling-6.png)

- If your products do not have unique references recorded against them (if using unique references the pallet barcode will automatically be assigned when the stock is received) and you do not have a pallet barcode to scan, you will need to generate the barcode before printing the label, click Generate Pallet Barcode .

![pallet-handling-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-7.png?width=240&height=482&name=pallet-handling-7.png)

- The pallet barcode has now been assigned to that pallet. You will see it against the Pallet Id field. You can now continue to receive the stock in and then locate it.

![pallet-handling-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-8.png?width=234&height=474&name=pallet-handling-8.png)

### How to print pallet labels during the inbound process

If you haven’t pre-printed your pallet labels (as outlined in the process above) you can choose to print your pallet labels during the inbound process. If you have not yet assigned a pallet barcode you will be asked if you wish to auto-generate a pallet barcode.

- Click Receive against the relevant Purchase Order.

![pallet-handling-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-9.png?width=255&height=516&name=pallet-handling-9.png)

- Select the pallet you wish to print the pallet label for.
- Select the print icon in the bottom right corner.

![pallet-handling-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-10.png?width=281&height=573&name=pallet-handling-10.png)

- If you have not yet assigned a pallet barcode you will be asked if you wish to auto-generate a pallet barcode. You will need to click Ok if you wish to print a pallet label.

![pallet-handling-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-11.png?width=280&height=564&name=pallet-handling-11.png)

- Click Print Pallet Label .
- Select the number of labels you would like to print.

![pallet-handling-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-12.png?width=300&height=609&name=pallet-handling-12.png)

- Once the pallet label has been placed on the pallet you can use this barcode to scan move and locate the pallet.

### How to print pallet labels from the web app

There are two ways in which you can print pallet labels from the web app. You can print them from within the Purchase Order (if the pallet ID is already assigned) or from the Pallet Label printing page if you have not yet assigned the pallet label.

#### Print label from within the Purchase Order

- Navigate to the relevant Purchase Order.
- Select the Products tab.
- Use the select box to select the relevant Pallet you wish to print the label for.
- Select Print Pallet Label .

![pallet-handling-13](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-13.png?width=670&height=271&name=pallet-handling-13.png)

- Click Print Now or Download PDF (depending on your printer setup).

#### **Print Pallet label from the Pallet Label Printing Page**

- Navigate to the Pallet Label Printing page by typing Pallet Label Printing into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Print Format of either ZPL or PDF.
- Select the number of pallet labels you wish to print and the number of copies of each label.
- Click Print Labels .

![pallet-handling-14](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-14.png?width=670&height=154&name=pallet-handling-14.png)

### How to apply pallet labels to stock already in the warehouse

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/C3QvsqlrnuQ

### How to merge pallets when allocating pallets to a bulk location

When receiving Purchase Orders on the web app and locating pallets into bulk locations you have the option of merging the pallets.

- On the Verify & Allocate Purchase Order page, you will notice the Pallet ID against the line of stock.
- Select the Pallet ID.

![pallet-handling-15](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-15.png?width=670&height=352&name=pallet-handling-15.png)

- Select the Create option to merge all pallets onto the one.

![pallet-handling-16](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pallet-handling-16.png?width=670&height=352&name=pallet-handling-16.png)

- Click Save .

### How to import Purchase Orders with a pallet barcode assigned

Purchase Orders can be imported (via the Purchase Order Parser) with pre-assigned pallet barcodes. This allows you to assign stock directly to specific pallets during import, reducing manual work when receiving palletised stock.

#### Benefits:

- **Reduces manual handling** when receiving pre-palletised stock.
- **Improves data accuracy** by automatically linking products to pallet IDs on import.
- **Supports pre-labelling workflows** for teams who print pallet labels in advance.
- **Prevents conflicts** with existing pallet data using smart validation.

<a id="photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders"></a>
## Photos and Documents on Purchase Orders

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Overview
- Workflows
- Use Cases / Benefits
- The difference between Documents Essentials and Advanced

### Purpose

Documents allow mobile and web app users to attach photos, videos and documents to Purchase Orders as they are received and verified.

### Overview

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/CcBSym1csjI

- A Document has attachments and attachments can be videos, photos or other documents (ie: PDF).
- Documents have two different visibility options:
  - **Internal only**: no customer access. Admins and packers can edit.
  - **Shared with customer:** customer can view. Admins and packers can edit.
  - A default visibility option can be selected from the Organisation Settings. More information here .
- Documents are split into two tiers, Essentials (available in all WMS plans), and Advanced (available through Warehouse Premium).

All accounts are able to trial Advanced Documents for free until June 2026. After this, only accounts with [WMS Premium](https://cartoncloudorg.lightning.force.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) will maintain Advanced Documents and all other accounts will switch to Essentials Documents.

- Capture and upload photos at receipt on the mobile or from your device’s photo library.
- Users can add and edit Documents on the web app but only add (not edit) on the mobile app.
- On the Purchase Order Allocated and Verified email if there are Documents associated with the Purchase Order and they are Customer level visibility, a link to the Document will be included in the email. See [Customer Settings - Email (Notifications)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Customer-Settings-Email-Notifications) for more information and the below screenshots for examples.

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-0.png?width=670&height=393&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-0.png)![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-1.png?width=670&height=294&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-1.png)

### Workflows

- [Photos and Documents on Purchase Orders (mobile app)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Photos-and-Documents-on-Purchase-Orders-mobile-app)- add Documents upon receiving stock in the warehouse via the mobile app.
- [Photos and Documents on Purchase Orders (web app)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Photos-and-Documents-on-Purchase-Orders-web-app)  - add Documents to the Purchase Order at any stage in the order process (any status) from the web app.

### Use Cases / Benefits

- Enables warehouse workers to provide photo (and video) evidence of received goods.
- Allows issues such as damages to be easily communicated and shared with customers.
- Provides greater transparency and visibility to customers.
- Provides greater transparency internally with photo visibility supplied at the time of receipt or damage and document history for who uploaded the attachment.
- Enables an advanced inbound process.
- Enables greater compliance and regulation standards for your customers.
- Increased service offering and value to your customers.

### The difference between Documents Essentials and Advanced

Advanced Documents provides additional capability for higher resolution images, significantly increases the number of attachments per document, provides additional storage capacity and adds other timesaving enhancements.

Advanced Documents is a paid add-on available with [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium). For more information on WMS Premium and to upgrade your account, please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

The detailed differences between the two are outlined below:

| **Essentials Documents** | **Advanced Documents** |
| --- | --- |
| Max 6 images per Document | Max 100 images per Document |
| Images are always compressed (POD resolution ~700 kb/image) | Default to full-resolution Compression options available via settings |
| Max attachment size 1mb | Max attachment size 500mb |
|  | Video support  Multi-photo mode |
| Deleted Documents and attachments cannot be restored | Deleted Documents and attachments can be viewed and restored by non-customer roles |
| 10gb included storage | 100gb included storage |
|  | Image Metadata - date, time and location Information (where available) |

---

<a id="photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app"></a>
## Photos and Documents on Purchase Orders (web app)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use Cases / Benefits
- Process
- Editing or deleting a Document
- Document History
- Image Metadata

### Purpose

The process for creating Documents on Purchase Orders on the web app. In addition, how to edit and delete documents via the web app.

Note, Documents can only be edited via the web app not the mobile app.

### Use Cases / Benefits

- Provide greater transparency and updates to your customers on their stock.
- Customers can view Documents from their CartonCloud login as long as the Document visibility is set to **Shared with Customer**.
- Provide greater transparency internally with Document visibility on orders and the history of who uploaded the Document and attachment.
- If you wish to take photos and record them against the Purchase Order once the stock is allocated to a warehouse location you can do so by taking a photo on the warehouse floor and uploading it on the web app.
- Reduce communication between you and your customer by uploading images and files directly to the Purchase Order for them to view.

### Process

Documents can be created on Purchase Orders at any stage through the order process. The Purchase Order can be in any status for a Document to be created. To create a Document on a Purchase Order:

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/tKTgbhXq3HQ

- Navigate to the relevant Purchase Order, **Warehouse**>**Purchase Orders**.
- Select the **Documents** tab. If there is already a Document against the Purchase Order you will see the number of Documents next to the tab title.

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-0.png?width=670&height=258&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-0.png)

- Select the +Add Document button.

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-1.png?width=670&height=260&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-1.png)

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-2.png?width=670&height=362&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-2.png)

- Select the **Name** for the Document from the drop-down. Note that names are not customisable, however, they will be in the future.
  - **Receival**: use this name when receiving stock that is not damaged.
  - **Receival (Damages):** use this name when receiving damaged freight.
  - A default visibility option can be selected from the Organisation Settings. For more information click here .
- Enter information related to the Document within the **Description** text box. This will be visible to anyone who has access to the Document.
- Select the visibility option: (a default visibility option can be selected from the Organisation Settings. More information [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Organisation-Settings-Warehouse-Order-Documents))
  - **Internal only**: only internal users of your CartonCloud account will be able to see the Document. This includes all User types apart from Customers. Only Admin and Packers can edit the Document (Documents can only be edited via the web app).
  - **Shared with Customer:**all user types in your CartonCloud account including Customers can see the Document. Only Admin and Packers can edit the Document (Documents can only be edited via the web app).
- Add attachments by selecting **Choose files**or utilise the**drag and drop**feature to upload the file.
- Select the files you wish to upload and select **Save**.

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-3.png?width=670&height=413&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-3.png)

- The Document will now be visible against the Purchase Order.

### Editing or deleting a Document

Once a Document is uploaded you can edit it to make changes, remove or add attachments and delete the Document. Note that Documents can only be edited via the web app.

**To edit a Document:**

- Select the Document and you will be in edit mode.
- Make any required changes and select **Save**.

**To delete a Document:**

- Select the Document you wish to delete to enter edit mode.

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-4.png?width=670&height=340&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-4.png)

- Scroll down and select the **red bin icon**.

### Document History

To access the Document history:

- Select the Document you wish to view the history for.
- Scroll down and select the **History** button.

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-5.png?width=670&height=291&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-5.png)

- You will now be able to see history related to the Document.

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-6.png?width=670&height=260&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-6.png)

### Image Metadata

Image Metadata is only included in [Advanced Documents](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-Documents). See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/WMS-Premium) for more information. Note: All accounts are able to trial Advanced Documents for free until June 2026. After this, only accounts with [WMS Premium](https://cartoncloudorg.lightning.force.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) will maintain Advanced Documents and all other accounts will switch to Essentials Documents.

When uploading an image to a Document on the web app, if date, time and location Metadata is available it will show against the file. This can be useful as it provides the exact location and date/time the image was taken.

**Considerations for Metadata to be available:**

- Only file types of images are able to store metadata. For example, a video will not show metadata.
- At present, only files uploaded via the web app can show metadata. Images uploaded from the mobile app will not provide metadata. This is coming soon in an app update.
- Only certain devices record metadata within an image and metadata is often removed when images are compressed (eg: images shared via WhatsApp generally get compressed and have location metadata removed).

**How to access Metadata:**

- Against the relevant Purchase Order, select the Documents tab.
- Select the relevant Document.

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-7.png?width=670&height=235&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-7.png)

- Select the relevant attachment.
- Click Show Metadata .

![photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-8.png?width=469&height=359&name=photos-and-documents-on-purchase-orders-web-app-8.png)

<a id="purchase-orders"></a>
## Purchase Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/purchase-orders_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Purchase Order
- How to create a Purchase Order
- Purchase Order Process Flow in CartonCloud
- Purchase Order List View

### What is a Purchase Order

For a stock to come into your Warehouse, a Purchase Order must be created.

### How to create a Purchase Order

The below pages outline how to create a Purchase Order and how to navigate the Purchase Order page within CartonCloud.

- Add a Purchase Order
- View Purchase Order
- Import Stock

### Purchase Order Process Flow in CartonCloud

The below process flow outlines the different statuses a Purchase Order moves through in CartonCloud.

![purchase-orders-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-0.png?width=670&height=212&name=purchase-orders-0.png)

- Draft: The Purchase Order has been created but is not yet approved. This status is only applicable for orders that have been manually added to CartonCloud. To progress to the next status of Not yet Received the Purchase Order must be approved and this can be done manually within the Purchase Order.
- Not yet received: The Purchase Order has been approved but is yet to arrive at the Warehouse.
- Received: The Purchase Order has arrived at the Warehouse but has not yet been put away to a Warehouse Location or checked off. To move to the next status of Verified, you must click Verify Purchase Order Products .
- Verified: The Purchase Order quantity and warehouse location have been verified.
- Allocated: The Purchase Order is now at its assigned warehouse location, and storage will begin on the Purchase Order.

For more information on the Purchase Order Process, please see the [Purchase Order Procedures](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Purchase-Order-Procedures) page.

### Purchase Orders List View

From the Purchase Orders page, you can view a list of Purchase Orders. This list can be filtered, and the columns displayed on the list can be customised.

**To filter the list:**

- Select the Filter tab.
- Select the filters you wish to apply - Customer, Product, Status, Adjustment, Is Invoiced and Date Added.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-20-2025-04-00-54-8736-AM.png?width=670&height=216&name=image-png-Nov-20-2025-04-00-54-8736-AM.png)

**To update the columns displayed on the list:**

- Select the cog gear icon in the top right.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-20-2025-04-00-41-4108-AM.png?width=670&height=216&name=image-png-Nov-20-2025-04-00-41-4108-AM.png)

- Tick the columns you wish to display and click Save .

![purchase-orders-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-3.png?width=670&height=324&name=purchase-orders-3.png)

**To delete Purchase Orders in bulk:**

- Click**Select All**or select individual Purchase Orders using the tick selection.

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Mar-16-2026-01-39-21-0331-AM.png?width=3390&height=1086&name=image-png-Mar-16-2026-01-39-21-0331-AM.png)**

- Click Delete.

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Mar-16-2026-01-44-07-4077-AM.png?width=3392&height=1002&name=image-png-Mar-16-2026-01-44-07-4077-AM.png)**

<a id="purchase-order-procedures"></a>
## Purchase Order Procedures

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/purchase-order-procedures_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Purchase Order
- How to create a Purchase Order
- Purchase Order Process Flow in CartonCloud

### What is a Purchase Order

For a stock to come into your Warehouse a Purchase Order must be created.

### How to create a Purchase Order

For information on how to create a Purchase Order see the

Add a Purchase Order

page.

### Purchase Order Process Flow in CartonCloud

The below process flow outlines the different statuses a Purchase Order moves through in CartonCloud.

![purchase-order-procedures-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-order-procedures-0.png?width=670&height=212&name=purchase-order-procedures-0.png)

Draft:

The Purchase Order has been created but not yet approved. This status is only applicable for orders that have been manually added to CartonCloud. To progress to the next status of

Not yet Received

the Purchase Order must be approved and this can be done manually within the Purchase Order.

**Not yet received:** The Purchase Order has been approved but is yet to arrive at the Warehouse.

**Received:** The Purchase Order has arrived at the Warehouse, but has not yet been put away to a Warehouse Location or checked off. If you have the [Send Purchase Order Goods Received confirmation email](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/customer-settings-email-notifications)turned on then the notification will be sent to the customer once the Purchase Order is in the Received status. You can then either move to the next status of Verified by clicking **Verify Purchase Order Products** or alternatively if you select the drop-down arrow and click **Bypass Verification Process** you can move straight to the allocation step. This means you will not verify the product against the received to the expected and move straight to assigning the product to a warehouse location. It is recommended you utilise the verification step to ensure the correct stock has been received.

**Verified:** The Purchase Order quantity has been verified. This step ensures the expected stock meets what has been received (quantity, expiry date, product). During this verification process, you can also assign the stock to a warehouse location. However, if you choose to conduct verification and allocation in two different steps (if you have one team verifying stock as they enter the warehouse and another team putting stock away) you can leave the location blank. **Note, storage will not start until a warehouse location has been assigned to the product.**

**Allocated:** The Purchase Order is now at its assigned warehouse location and storage will begin on the stock. If the allocation process is being completed separately from the verification stage, then this is when the stock is put away and assigned to its warehouse location.

**To view the Purchase Orders current status:**

- Navigate to the Purchase Order page by searching Purchase Order in the Search for anything bar.
- From the list view, you will be able to see the Status column.
- You can also view the status from within the Purchase Order itself by selecting the relevant Purchase Order and selecting the Details tab.

![purchase-order-procedures-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-order-procedures-1.png?width=670&height=272&name=purchase-order-procedures-1.png)

---

<a id="purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer"></a>
## Purchase Orders (Stock In) as a Customer

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Purchase Order
- Benefits of Purchase Orders
- How to add a Purchase Order
- Viewing a Purchase Order

### What is a Purchase Order?

A Purchase Order is an order with stock coming into the warehouse. In order for the stock to come into the warehouse and be processed, a Purchase Order must be created first.

### Benefits of Purchase Orders

- Allows you to more easily track your orders and inventory
- Record custom data against the orders and stock, for example, batch numbers, serial numbers, SSCC.
- Keeps record of what was expected to be received and what was actually received.
- Allows for notifications to be sent out for certain events during the order process.

### How to add a Purchase Order

There are a number of different ways a Purchase Order can be added to the system. It is highly recommend that orders are created automatically via a Parser or Integration. If you would like to be set up with a [Parser](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Parsers) or [Integration](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Integration-with-other-Software) please reach out to your CartonCloud account owner (3PL provider) or reach out to the CartonCloud team for more information via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) .

- Navigate to the Purchase Order page, Warehouse > Purchase Orders .

![purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-0.png?width=670&height=331&name=purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-0.png)

- Click +Add Purchase Order.

**![purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-1.png?width=670&height=329&name=purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-1.png)**

- Select the:
  - Arrival date : date the stock will be arriving at the warehouse
  - Customer reference : this is the key reference for the order.
  - Special instructions : any special instructions for the order

- Click Save .
- Click +Add Products to Purchase Order .

![purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-2.png?width=670&height=332&name=purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-2.png)

- Type in the name of the product you wish to add to the order and click Create .

![purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-3.png?width=670&height=329&name=purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-3.png)

- Update the quantity of the product.
- To add more products, click the +Add Product button in the top left.

![purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-4.png?width=670&height=319&name=purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-4.png)

- Once you have finished adding the products to the order, click the Details tab and then the green approved button at the bottom of the screen. Once the order is approved changes can not be made unless you contact your 3PL/CartonCloud account owner.

![purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-5.png?width=670&height=325&name=purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-5.png)

- The order is now approved and ready to be processed once it arrives to the warehouse.
- You can still mark the order as urgent, upload an invoice or if you wish to add another order you can duplicate the order.

![purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-6.png?width=670&height=325&name=purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-6.png)

### Viewing a Purchase Order

![purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-7.png?width=670&height=298&name=purchase-orders-stock-in-as-a-customer-7.png)
You can use the different tabs on the order to navigate to different information relating to the order.

- Details tab: basic details surrounding the order.
- Products tab: details of the stock on the order. List of products and the relevant data for each line of stock.
- Charges: charges associated with the order and the relevant invoice the order is associated with.
- Errors : any errors with the order.
- History : history of status changes of the order.
