<a id="view-purchase-order"></a>
## View Purchase Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/view-purchase-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Details
- Purchase Order Status
- Products
- Viewing Options
- Select All
- Print Labels
- Delete Products
- Charges
- Errors
- History
- Comments

### Purpose

The View Purchase Order page provides you with full control over your Purchase Order after the creation stage.

### Details

The Details tab allows you to edit the Purchase Order, view and update the status of the Purchase Order, and provides extra information relating to the Purchase Order.
![view-purchase-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-0.png?width=670&height=316&name=view-purchase-order-0.png)

### Purchase Order Status

This window provides the current status of the Purchase Order and allows you to either revert or update the status.

See [Purchase Order Procedures](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/purchase-order-procedures) for more information on Purchase Order statuses.

**Extra functionality buttons:**

| **Edit** | **Select to edit the Purchase Order.** |
| --- | --- |
| Actions | Once selected you have two drop-down options:   **Resend Verification Confirmation Email:**This action will only be an option once the email verification has been sent. By selecting this action, the verification email will be sent again.    **Duplicate:** a copy of the Purchase Order will be created. |
| Export/View | Once selected you have three drop-down options:   **Export Verification List:** this will export an xls file with the Product Verification List.    **Show Differences (Original vs Now):**this will display the original Purchase Order versus the current Purchase Order and the changes that have occurred.    **Show Original:** this will display the original Purchase Order that was inputted into CartonCloud. |
| Reject | In the case where Customers are submitting the Purchase Orders, you have the ability to reject the order. The status of the Purchase Order will now be **Rejected**. |
| Delete | Select to delete the Purchase Order. |

### Products

The Products tab allows you to view and select the stock entering your warehouse on the Purchase Order you are viewing.

![view-purchase-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-1.png?width=670&height=175&name=view-purchase-order-1.png)

### Viewing Options

![view-purchase-order-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-2.png?width=670&height=286&name=view-purchase-order-2.png)

| Cog options |  |
| --- | --- |
| Toggle Table Columns | Select which available columns you wish to view on the Product view page. |
| Toggle Table Data | Option to view historical purchase order product lines with zero initial quantity stock (handy if you are wanting to review previous movements). Unchecking this box will only show you the current purchase order product lines where stock is in the warehouse. |

### Select All

The Select All function allows you to select all Products on all pages. If filters are applied, only the filtered Products will be included in the select all.

This is useful if you wish to print all Purchase Order Products labels or delete Products in bulk.

To remove the selection, click the **X** icon in the top right corner.

![view-purchase-order-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-3.png?width=670&height=365&name=view-purchase-order-3.png)

### Print Labels

By selecting the applicable products or using the Select All function you can print the Purchase Order Product labels.

See [Label Printing](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/label-printing) for more information on how to print labels from within CartonCloud.

![view-purchase-order-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-4.png?width=670&height=365&name=view-purchase-order-4.png)

### Delete Products

By selecting the applicable products or using the Select All function you can delete Products from the Purchase Order.

You can not delete Products once the Purchase Order is verified.

![view-purchase-order-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-5.png?width=670&height=365&name=view-purchase-order-5.png)

### Charges

The charges tab outlines and breaks down all charges associated with the Purchase Order you are viewing. The page is broken into four boxes as described below:

**Purchase Order Charges:**

![view-purchase-order-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-6.png?width=670&height=345&name=view-purchase-order-6.png)

By selecting**Mark Charges Finalized** you are able to stop Users from changing prices related to the Purchase Order, essentially locking the other 3 boxes on this page from any data entry (however you can later mark the charges unfinalized if you need to make further changes).

**Assigned to Invoice** will display what Invoice the Purchase Order is set to be or is already being charged to the customer on and provides a link to it for your convenience.

**Rate Cards (Income)** displays the name of the Rate Card the Customer is using which in turn generates the rates being used within the Purchase Order. It also provides a link to the Rate Card for your convenience, allowing you easy access to update charges if required.

**Rate Cards (Expense)** displays the name of the Rate Card set against the Supplier (if you are using another companies warehouse and have them set up as a Supplier). This, in turn, generates the rates being used to determine your cost for the Purchase Order. It also provides a link to the Rate Card for your convenience, allowing you easy access to update costs if required.

**Charge Errors** indicates if the system has detected any problems with charges relating to the Purchase Order. This will most commonly be triggered when a Purchase Order is not charging anything.

**Income** provides you with the total amount being charged to the customer for this Purchase Order (inwards movement).

**Expense** provides you with the total amount the Purchase Order is costing you in the scenario where you have warehouse Suppliers set up.

**Adhoc Charge Data**

![view-purchase-order-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-7.png?width=475&height=288&name=view-purchase-order-7.png)

Adhoc Charge Data will allow you to add on charges which are not able to be calculated through the system (for example the system has no way of knowing whether you wrapped a pallet or not unless you tell it).

You can manually enter your Adhoc Charges from this screen including adjusting the Unit price if it is different from what you have set up within the Rate Card.

Ensure to select **Save** once entering any changes.

**Item Charge Data**

**![view-purchase-order-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-8.png?width=500&height=221&name=view-purchase-order-8.png)**
Item Charge Data is the Handling Charges associated with bringing in the stock. These charges can be set up from the Customer's Rate Card within the Handling Charges Tab. CartonCloud will attempt to automatically calculate these charges based on the quantities you are bringing in and the prices you have set within the Rate Card.

However, they can also be manually adjusted by the user on this page by changing the number within the quantity textbox, then selecting **Save**.

![view-purchase-order-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-9.png?width=670&height=128&name=view-purchase-order-9.png)

The charges box provides a detailed breakdown of the charges related to the Purchase Order you're viewing. For these to appear you must select **Automatically Calculate Income Charges** and the system will calculate all the charges currently applying to the Purchase Order. This will also be triggered automatically by the system when the Purchase Order is allocated to an Invoice.

**+Add Income Charge** allows you to add a manual charge on to the Purchase Order. This is useful for adding charges which are not commonly occurring and therefore don't warrant being set up as Adhoc charges.

### Errors

The errors tab provides a log of any errors that may occur when attempting to parse in a file or upload a file related to the Purchase Order.

### History

The history tab provides a list of all historical changes which are tracked by the system within the Purchase Order. This is useful to check who changed the status of a Purchase Order and at what time or how the Purchase Order was entered into CartonCloud, for example, a Purchase order created through a [Parser](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers)will show as "Created via Web Upload".

#### **Show Product Creations/Removals**

By selecting the 'Show Product Creations/Removals' you will be able to see when a product has been added and removed to an order.

![view-purchase-order-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-10.png?width=670&height=183&name=view-purchase-order-10.png)

![view-purchase-order-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-purchase-order-11.png?width=670&height=218&name=view-purchase-order-11.png)

### Comments

The comments tab allows you to record comments against a Purchase Order increasing communication within your operation.

<a id="what-is-initial-onhand-and-free-quantity"></a>
## What is Initial, Onhand and Free Quantity?

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/what-is-initial-onhand-and-free-quantity_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Initial
- Onhand
- Free quantity

### Purpose

Initial, Onhand and Free Quantities are quantities that are recorded within a Purchase Order Product Record (a stock record).

### Initial

Initial quantity is the number of items which first arrived into the warehouse under that Purchase Order Product record. This number will only change if the Purchase Order is updated to increase/decrease the amount of stock arriving on it.

### Onhand

Onhand quantity is the physical stock that is available to be packed right now. For example, if you have 5 Cartons of Soup in the warehouse, and then you process a Sale Order to pack 2 of those cartons, the onhand quantity would drop from 5 to 3 once the Sale Order is marked as packed.

### Free Quantity

Free quantity is the stock that is available to be added to a new Sale Order. For example, if you have 5 Cartons of Soup in the warehouse, and then you create a Sale Order containing 2 of those cartons, the free quantity would drop from 5 to 3. This differs from onhand quantity which is only decreased at the time the product is packed.

---

# Warehouse Management > Replenishment

<a id="how-to-create-a-replenishment"></a>
## How to create a Replenishment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-create-a-replenishment_

### Table of Contents

- Steps to create a Replenishment
- Save Replenishment prefill settings (Replenishment template)
- Replenishment page list view

Please note this is a [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) only feature. For more information on [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).

**Before creating a Replenishment, please note the below:**

- Ensure you have set up[Replenishment at the Organisation Settings and at the Product level](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-set-up-Replenishment) for the Products you wish to use Replenishment for.
- The settings you configured at the [Organisation Settings and the Product level](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-set-up-Replenishment) will be applied.
- Replenishments are customisable. You can create Product, Customer, Product Type, or Pick Face Location-specific Replenishments using the filter options.
- Replenishments can be duplicated. If you [save the Replenishment as a prefill setting](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/How+to+create+a+Replenishment#HowtocreateaReplenishment-settings), you can easily apply the same settings when creating a new Replenishment. This is extremely useful if you have identical recurring Replenishments.
- You can create Replenishments automatically using Replenishment Auto Generation (Advanced Automation) .

### Steps to create a Replenishment

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/noI84-ktDIY

- Navigate to the Replenishments page by typing Replenishments into the Search for anything bar at the top of the application.
- To add a new Replenishment, click the **+Add Replenishment**button in the top left corner.

Alternatively, for an automated process, you can use Advanced Automation - Replenishments to create automated Replenishments. See [Replenishment Auto Generation (Advanced Automation)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Advanced-Automation-Replenishment)[/articles/Knowledge/Advanced-Automation-Replenishment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Advanced-Automation-Replenishment) for more information.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Jun-01-2026-09-35-41-0400-PM.png?width=2070&height=794&name=image-png-Jun-01-2026-09-35-41-0400-PM.png)

- You will then be directed to the Add Replenishment page.

![how-to-create-a-replenishment-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-create-a-replenishment-1.png?width=506&height=532&name=how-to-create-a-replenishment-1.png)

If the Replenishment you create will be recurring, save the Replenishment as a prefill setting. See the [Prefill Setting section](https://help.cartoncloud.com#save-replenishment-settings)of this article for more information.

- Name the Replenishment in the **Name** field. You can insert a name placeholder by selecting the **Insert Placeholder** drop-down menu and choosing the appropriate name placeholder you wish to use.
- Select the date of the Replenishment from the **Planned Date**field. This can be today's date or a future date.
- If you would like to customise the Replenishment, you can utilise the **Filters** and/or **Stock Selection Options**. Use the below table to fill in the **Filters**and **Stock Selection Options** fields.

You can use the filters if you wish to create a Product or Customer-specific Replenishment. In addition, the Stock Selection Options allow you to limit what stock is used to replenish the pick face locations.

| Field | Field Description |
| --- | --- |
| Filters | *The filters allow you to customise the Replenishment and only include certain Customers, Products, Product Types, and/or Pick Face Locations.* |
| Customers | Select the Customers you wish to apply the Replenishment to. There is no limit to the number of Customers you select. If left blank, all Customers will be included in the Replenishment. |
| Products | Select the Products you wish to apply the Replenishment to. You will only be able to select products you have enabled Replenishment for and associated with the selected Customers. There is no limit to the number of Products you can select. If left blank, all Products with Replenishment activated will be included in the Replenishment. |
| Product Types | Select the Product Types you wish to apply the Replenishment to. There is no limit to the number of Product Types you can select. If left blank, all Product Types will be included in the Replenishment. |
| Pick Face Locations | Select the From and To Pick Face Locations you wish to apply the Replenishment to. You will only be able to select Pick Face Warehouse Locations. If left blank, all Pick Face Locations will be included in the Replenishment. |
| Stock Selection Options | *The Stock Selection Options allow you to limit what stock from what locations are used to replenish the pick face locations. This is useful if you wish to only replenish with stock from a certain location.* |
| Location Product Types | Select the Location Product Types (e.g. General, Chilled, Dangerous Goods) you would like the Replenishment to replenish the pick faces. If left blank, all Location Product Types will be included in the available locations to take stock from to replenish the pick faces with. |
| Stock Selection Locations | Select the Warehouse Locations you would like the Replenishment to take stock from to replenish the pick face locations. If left blank, all locations will be available to take stock from to replenish the pick face locations. |

- ​​​​​​​Select Save or if you wish to conduct the Replenishment instantly, select Start .

### Save Replenishment prefill settings (Replenishment template)

If you have identical recurring Replenishments, it is recommended you save them as a prefill setting. By saving the Replenishment in the prefill settings, you can use a template each time you create the same Replenishment. For example, if you run a daily Replenishment for Customer A, you would save it in the prefill settings and apply it each time you create the new Replenishment.

**To save Replenishment Prefill Settings:**

You can either save the prefill settings from within an already created Replenishment or whilst you are creating a Replenishment.

- If you are not already in the Replenishment and you wish to save the prefill settings, navigate to the Replenishments page and select the relevant Replenishment.
- Click the **Save Settings** button at the top of the page.

![how-to-create-a-replenishment-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-create-a-replenishment-2.png?width=611&height=365&name=how-to-create-a-replenishment-2.png)

- A pop-out window will appear. Name the settings and select Save .

![how-to-create-a-replenishment-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-create-a-replenishment-3.png?width=520&height=256&name=how-to-create-a-replenishment-3.png)

- This will now be an option in the Prefill Settings drop-down menu next time you create a Replenishment.

![how-to-create-a-replenishment-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-create-a-replenishment-4.png?width=398&height=180&name=how-to-create-a-replenishment-4.png)

### Replenishment page list view

From the Replenishments page list view, you can see all current, past, and planned Replenishments. This view highlights the key information of the Replenishment, including the Name, Customer, Planned, Start and Finish Date, and the Status.

You can filter and sort Replenishments using the filter and sort configuration buttons and the simple sort function (clicking the heading column to order the column). See the [Advanced sorting and filtering page](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Advanced-sorting-and-filtering) for more information on how to use this functionality.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Jun-01-2026-09-44-10-9800-PM.png?width=2070&height=794&name=image-png-Jun-01-2026-09-44-10-9800-PM.png)

<a id="how-to-run-a-replenishment"></a>
## How to run a Replenishment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-run-a-replenishment_

### Table of Contents

- Prerequisites
- Best practices
- How to steps
  - 1 . Open/download the Replenishment Report
  - 2. Use Scan Move (Move Cart) and the Replenishment Report to replenish pick face locations
  - 3. Complete the Replenishment on the web application
- Variances
- How to reset a Replenishment
- Sale Order stock selection optimisation

Please note this is a [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) only feature. For more information on [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

### Prerequisites

Before you run a Replenishment in your warehouse, you need to first fulfil the below prerequisites.

- [Enable Replenishment from the Organisation Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-set-up-Replenishment)
- [Created pick face warehouse locations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-set-up-Replenishment)
- [Set up Replenishment for the Product you wish to run the Replenishment for](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-set-up-Replenishment)
- [Created a Replenishment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-create-a-Replenishment) for the Product you wish to replenish

### Best practices

Once you have completed the above steps, you are ready to run a Replenishment. It is recommended you follow the below best practices for running a Replenishment.

- Do not process Sale Orders and Purchase Orders for the applicable Customers whilst conducting a Replenishment.
- It is strongly recommended that you use a Mobile device (either a Mobile Phone (iOS or Android) or a [Mobile Computer](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Scanning-Devices)) and [Scan Move 2.0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Scan-Move-2-0-Move-Cart) Move Cart to complete the Replenishment moves.
- It is recommended that you utilise a [barcode scanner](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Scanning-Devices) to maximise the benefits and functionality of the Scan Move 2.0 Move Cart.
- If you have a tablet or iPad, it is recommended you use the web application on the device in conjunction with Scan Move on your mobile device to complete the moves. You can mark off the moves on the web application as they are completed. If you do not have an iPad or tablet, then you can print the report and carry this with you through the warehouse as you conduct the moves. **📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/IyWpuZYw_ds

### How to steps

**1.** **Open/download the Replenishment Report**

- Navigate to the **Replenishments** page by typing **Replenishments** into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Replenishment you wish to run.
- Scroll to the bottom of the page and select the **Start** button in the bottom right corner.

Note, once you have selected Start, you still can [Reset](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-create-a-Replenishment) the Replenishment and return to the previous page to make any changes as required. The Start button can also be used as a preview button to show you what the Replenishment will look like with the option to edit it still.

- If you select **Save**, the Replenishment will save in the Replenishment view screen until you decide to edit it again. If you select **Cancel**, any changes made will be lost.

![how-to-run-a-replenishment-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-run-a-replenishment-0.png?width=479&height=395&name=how-to-run-a-replenishment-0.png)

- You will now see the Replenishment Report with the list of moves required to replenish the pick face locations.
- You can filter the moves by warehouse location (where stock is coming from) and pick face locations (where the stock is going to).
- If you use a tablet or iPad with the web application, you can use the **Done?** and **Issue?** tick boxes to mark off each move as it is completed.

![how-to-run-a-replenishment-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-run-a-replenishment-1.png?width=670&height=221&name=how-to-run-a-replenishment-1.png)

- If you do not have a tablet or iPad and will be using a printed version of the report, select the green **Print** button.

**Printable Replenishment Report:**

![how-to-run-a-replenishment-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-run-a-replenishment-2.png?width=670&height=374&name=how-to-run-a-replenishment-2.png)

**2.** **Use Scan Move (Move Cart) and the Replenishment Report to replenish pick face locations**

- Using either the printed Replenishment Report or a tablet/iPad and your mobile device, complete the Replenishment moves as directed by the report.

**You will need to use the Move Cart on your mobile device to complete the moves. See [Scan Move Move Cart](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Scan-Move-2-0-Move-Cart)for instructions on how to use the Move Cart.**

- As you complete each move, mark it on your report, or if you are using the web application (through a tablet device), you can use the **Issue?** and **Done?** tick boxes.

**3.** **Complete the Replenishment on the web application**

Once you have completed the physical movement of the Replenishment moves, you can mark the Replenishment as complete in CartonCloud.

To mark the Replenishment as complete in CarrtonCloud:

- Select the **Finish Replenishment**button.

![how-to-run-a-replenishment-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-run-a-replenishment-3.png?width=670&height=203&name=how-to-run-a-replenishment-3.png)

- A pop-out window will appear asking you to confirm the move. Select **Complete**.

![how-to-run-a-replenishment-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-run-a-replenishment-4.png?width=529&height=206&name=how-to-run-a-replenishment-4.png)

### Variances

If there is not enough stock to replenish the pick face locations with, you will have Variances. The Variances will show the quantity of stock that is not available but needed to replenish the pick face location.

To view the Variances for the Replenishment, click the blue **Variances** button. The number of variances for the Replenishment will appear in the white circle next to the Replenishment button.

If stock selection criteria are used, this may limit what the replenishment can show on the report and then cause a variance. There is a warning that displays if these settings have been used when creating the replenishment.

### How to reset a Replenishment

If at any time whilst completing the Replenishment you wish to reset the status to **In Progress,** you can select the **Reset** button at the top of the page. This will allow you to edit the Replenishment.

![how-to-run-a-replenishment-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-run-a-replenishment-5.png?width=670&height=82&name=how-to-run-a-replenishment-5.png)

### Sale Order Stock Selection Optimisation

Once the Replenishment is complete and the applicable stock is in pick face locations, CartonCloud will re-optimise the sale order stock selection. This means that it will ensure all relevant Sale Orders (ones with stock that use pick face locations) are assigned stock from pick face locations. This helps to ensure that pickers are picking from the pick face locations when picking and packing orders.

---

<a id="how-to-set-up-replenishment"></a>
## How to set up Replenishment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-set-up-replenishment_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to set up Replenishment
  - Configure Replenishment from the Organisation Settings
  - Create pick face locations
  - Enable Replenishment from the product level
- Export/import Replenishment settings
- The difference between Organisation Settings and product level Replenishment set up

Please note this is a [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) only feature. For more information on [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

### Purpose

To set up Replenishment, you will need to do so at the Organisation Settings and Product-Level. Replenishment is product-specific, meaning that you will need to activate and configure Replenishment at the product level for each product you wish to use Replenishment for.

See the [difference between Organisation Settings and Product Level set up](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/How+to+set+up+Replenishment#HowtosetupReplenishment-difference) at the end of this article for more information on the difference between the two configurations.

### How to set up Replenishment

Follow the below steps to set up Replenishment:

Please note that when running a Replenishment the [Stock Selection Method](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-CartonCloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-Stock-Selection-Methods) is taken into consideration with the below settings when selecting stock for the Replenishment.

**1.** **Configure Replenishment from the Organisation Settings**

- Navigate to **Organisation Settings** (**More**>**Organisation Settings**).
- Select the **Warehouse** tab.
- Scroll down to the bottom of the page to the heading **Replenishment Configuration**.

![how-to-set-up-replenishment-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-replenishment-0.png?width=670&height=304&name=how-to-set-up-replenishment-0.png)

- Select the Replenishment Report Logic you wish to use .
  - Default: standard replenishment logic which uses the Replenishment Quantity Configuration settings defined at the Product level
  - Overstock from Sale Order demand: uses the default report logic and will look at the level of stock required for Sale Orders in awaiting pick and pack status and will conduct an over replenishment to compensate for these Sale Orders. When running the Replenishment, the report will highlight if the move is for stock relating to a Sale Order in pick and pack status or not
- If you wish to apply a limit to the quantity of product picked from a pick face for a Sale Order, apply a percentage in the No Limit text bar under Sale Order Allocation Pick Face Quantity Depletion Limit. The percentage is calculated using the maximum quantity threshold or highest unit of measure from the product if the threshold is blank.
- Select the **Replenishment Stock Allocation Status**you wish to use. This will determine what stock is being used to replenish the pick face locations.
  - **Onhand:**uses all stock in the warehouse, including stock currently allocated to a Sale Order (only for orders that have not been picked or packed yet). This is useful as it will help move stock that is already allocated to a Sale Order into pick face locations, ready for when the order needs to be picked. Note, it is strongly advised if you are using this setting not to process Sale Orders for that product whilst conducting the Replenishment.
  - **Free:**only includes stock available in the warehouse and is not allocated to a Sale Order. It is advised you use this status if you are planning to process Sale Orders while conducting the Replenishment, as the stock allocated to a Sale Order will not be utilised to replenish the pick faces.
- Choose if you wish to enable Use Last Allocated Location for Minimum Trigger. This setting, when enabled, changes how minimum stock replenishment is triggered for products without a dedicated pickface. Instead of evaluating each location independently, CartonCloud will only check the last location where stock was allocated before determining if replenishment is required.
- Select **Save**.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/aEPCo2p9uSU

**2.** **Create Pick Face locations**

To create Pick Face Locations, see [Adding Warehouse Locations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Adding-Warehouse-Locations).

If you would like to change your existing Warehouse Locations into Pick Face Locations, follow the below steps:

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/zqIgpgAx96s

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page by typing Warehouse Locations into the Search for anything bar.
- Select **More** and **Export XLS**.

![how-to-set-up-replenishment-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-replenishment-1.png?width=670&height=222&name=how-to-set-up-replenishment-1.png)

- Open the downloaded XLS file.
- You will see all your Warehouse Locations. For the Warehouse Locations you wish to change to a Pick Face Location, change the **efficiency** level in **column K**.
- You will need to change the efficiency level to a number between 21 and 30 (30 being the most efficient) to update the location to a pick face location.
- Save the file once you have made the changes.
- In CartonCloud, on the **Warehouse Locations** page, select **More** and**Import XLS**.
- Select the file and select **Upload file**.
- You will be directed to the Import Validation Results page. Select the **Updated** tab to view all updated Warehouse Locations.

![how-to-set-up-replenishment-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-replenishment-2.png?width=670&height=264&name=how-to-set-up-replenishment-2.png)

- Check you have modified the correct Warehouse Locations and click **Confirm Import**.
- You will then receive the success banner message that the import was successful.

**3.** **Enable Replenishment from the Product level**

Once you have enabled Replenishment from the Organisation Settings, you can then configure Replenishment on a Product level for the Products you wish to use Replenishment for.

It is recommended that once you have set up one product for Replenishment, you use the [Export/Import function](https://help.cartoncloud.com#export-import-replenishment-settings) to set up other Products in bulk.

To enable Replenishment for a Product:

- Navigate to the **Products** page (Warehouse>Products).
- Select the applicable Product you wish to activate Replenishment for.
- Select the **Replenishment** tab.

![how-to-set-up-replenishment-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-replenishment-3.png?width=670&height=350&name=how-to-set-up-replenishment-3.png)

- Select **Yes** from the **Replenishment Active**drop-down menu.
- As the default, **Replenishment Report Logic** will be set to **Use Organisation Settings.**This will apply the logic you selected in Organisation Settings. If you wish to override these settings on a product level, select the applicable setting (either Default or Overstock From Sale Order Demand) from the drop-down menu.
- To customise the Product Replenishment configuration, fill in the fields highlighted below. If left blank, the default settings will be applied (the default setting is defined below).

![how-to-set-up-replenishment-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-replenishment-4.png?width=670&height=426&name=how-to-set-up-replenishment-4.png)

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| **Replenishment Quantity Configuration** |  |
| Minimum Quantity Trigger | Once the quantity goes below the set value, the replenishment will be triggered.  *Default is 50% of the largest unit of measure.* |
| Maximum Quantity Threshold | The maximum quantity that the location will allow to replenish up to.  *Default is 1 of the largest unit of measure.* |
| Replenishment Type | Define how to replenish and, for some types, the amount to replenish.  **To Max Qty:** when the replenishment triggers, it will bring the quantity back up to the maximum quantity.  **UOM Lots defined:** the amount you would like to replenish in each move until the maximum quantity is reached. The quantity to replenish will be rounded to the UOM.  **Exact Qty defined:**you can define the exactquantity you wish to replenish regardless of the maximum quantity. This means the maximum quantity can be exceeded. |
| **Warehouse Location Pick Face Selection** |  |
| Warehouse Locations | Select the pick face location being utilised for the Product. This is the pick face location that will be replenished. There is no limit to the number of pick face locations you can select.  *If left blank, CartonCloud will select the pick face locations that either have this product in them or the last stock in the location was this product.* |
| **Advanced Replenishment Configuration** |  |
| Sale Order Allocation Pick Face Quantity Depletion Limit | You can apply a limit to the quantity of Product that can be picked from a pick face for a Sale Order. This depletion limit can either be a percentage or unit.  *The default will apply the configurations set at the Organisation Settings level.* |
| Pick Face Custom Field Restrictions | Select which product custom fields must be unique in the same location during Replenishment. For example, if a product in that location has a certain expiry date, then only other products with the same expiry date may be replenished into the location.  *The default is no restriction.* |

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/RQAE0lECCsA

### Export/Import Replenishment Settings

Once you have set up Replenishment for one Product you can use the Export/Import function to set up Replenishment for other Products in bulk.
**To use the export/import function:**

- Navigate to the Products page (Warehouse>Products).
- Click **More**.
- Select **Export Replenishment Settings**.

![how-to-set-up-replenishment-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-replenishment-5.png?width=670&height=271&name=how-to-set-up-replenishment-5.png)

- This will export all Products (even if Replenishment hasn't been activated) and their current Replenishment settings into an xsl file type.
- Fill in the applicable columns on the file (some columns will have drop-down options).
- Leave the first four columns as is (they are highlighted blue).
- Save the edited file.
- Return to the Products page within CartonCloud and select **More** and then **Import Replenishment Settings**.
- You will receive a success message once the Products have been imported.
- Select the bell notification in the top right corner and select **View Results Here.**

Note, by hovering over the text box highlighted with your mouse, and a message will appear informing you on what has been updated or, if there is an error, what the error relates to.

### The difference between Organisation Settings and Product level Replenishment set up

The Replenishment configurations you set up in the Organisation Settings will apply to all your Products unless you choose to alter these at the product level. In addition, certain settings are product-specific, meaning you can only configure them at a Product level. This is helpful if you wish to use different Replenishment logic for each of your Products.

The below diagram highlights the different Replenishment settings and at what level they can be configured.

![how-to-set-up-replenishment-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-set-up-replenishment-6.png?width=324&height=403&name=how-to-set-up-replenishment-6.png)

---

<a id="replenishment"></a>
## Replenishment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/replenishment_

### Table of Contents

- What is Replenishment
- Benefits of Replenishment
- Replenishment process

Please note this is a [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) only feature. For more information on [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

### What is Replenishment

Replenishment is the process of moving stock, typically in bulk or larger quantities, to pick face locations that they have been depleted from. CartonCloud can generate a report highlighting the pick face locations that need to be replenished and the warehouse stock movements required to fulfil these pick face locations.

For an enhanced Replenishment process you can utilise Advanced Automation to create automated Replenishments. See [Replenishment Auto Generation (Advanced Automation)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Advanced-Automation-Replenishment) for more information.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/lJbAd-cMqNI

### Benefits of Replenishment

- Reduce time and cost of the picking process
- Streamlines the replenishment process of re-stocking warehouse locations that are quickly depleted
- Helps to optimise space in the warehouse

### Replenishment Process

The Replenishment process in CartonCloud is as follows:

1. [Set up Replenishment in your CartonCloud account](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-set-up-replenishment)
2. [Create a Replenishment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-create-a-replenishment)
3. [Run a Replenishment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-run-a-replenishment)

---

# Warehouse Management > Sale Orders

<a id="add-a-sale-order"></a>
## Add a Sale Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-a-sale-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps

### Purpose

To manually add a Sale Order in CartonCloud.

For information on how your Customers can add Sale Orders in CartonCloud using their login, please see [Sale Orders (Stock Out) as a Customer.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Sale-Orders-Stock-Out-as-a-Customer) To automatically create Sale Orders, please see the [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Parsers) page.

### How to steps

Navigate to the Sale Orders page by selecting Warehouse>Sale Orders from the main menu.

- Select **+Add Sale Order**.

![add-a-sale-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-sale-order-0.png?width=670&height=323&name=add-a-sale-order-0.png)

- On the Add new Sale Order page, complete the fields. You can use the descriptions below to assist you as you complete the fields.

**Sale Order Fields**

| **Field** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Attach Invoice | Allows you to attached a customer invoice to the Sale order quickly. Invoices can also be attached after the Sale order is created through the Customer Invoices tab. |
| Customer | The owner (supplier) of the goods. Sale Orders can only be created for the stock of a single Customer. |
| Customer Reference | A reference number for the Sales Order. Normally this is your Customer's Invoice Number |
| Delivery Address | Where the Sale Order is going. It is recommended that you enter a Delivery Address even if the order is being picked up from your warehouse. This helps you distinguish between different Sale Orders when looking at the list view. In addition, this address will be printed onto the Consignment label; therefore, this will again help you identify the order and w   here it needs to go. |
| Order will be picked up from Warehouse | Tick if the order will be picked up. This will put the Consignment created from the Sale Order onto the default run set up for the Warehouse; this is usually the "Pickup from Warehouse" delivery run but can be configured. If you do not wish to use a default Delivery Run, you can modify this against the Warehouse (See [Organisation Settings - Warehouse](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Organisation-Settings-Warehouse)). Note, if you are not using a default Delivery Run and have Zone Sets enabled, CartonCloud will use the Transport Lanes, and Zone Sets logic to determine the expected Delivery Run for the Sale Order. See [Setting up CartonCloud to automatically allocate Consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-CartonCloud-to-automatically-allocate-Consignments) for more information on allocating Consignments automatically. |

**Advanced Options**

| Packing Instructions | Special instructions that show on the Packing Slip and Pick/Pack screen. |
| --- | --- |
| Delivery Instructions | Special instructions that get copied into the Consignments Special Instructions |
| Sale Order Value | The value (invoice amount) of the Sale Order. This field is only required if you charge your customer picking fees based on Percentage Of Invoice. When adding the value, you can select the currency. Note, once the order is created, the currency can not be changed. |
| Cash On Delivery | Whether or not the Sale Order requires Cash On Delivery to be collected. This information is passed onto the Consignment created by the Sale Order. |
| Attach Invoice to Goods | If your customer wants to upload an Invoice file to CartonCloud, which is then printed and attached to the order, this should be set to Yes.   Note: If you select Yes and then don't upload and print an invoice, the consignment will remain in an "Awaiting Sale Order Invoice" status preventing it from being allocated to delivery runs.   This is implemented because if the customer has selected that they want an Invoice attached to the goods, and you're still waiting for the Invoice, you probably don't want to send the stock without the Invoice attached. |
| Required Ship Date | The date that the order should leave the warehouse. This is useful if you're sending with Onforwarders and have limited control over the Delivery Date. In this case, you often want the order to leave your warehouse as soon as possible, but then you may specify a required delivery date with the carrier. |
| Required Delivery Date | The date that the stock should be delivered. This affects the day that the related consignment is allocated. |
| Packer Assigned | If you wish to assign a packer to the order. This can be done at the time of adding the order, after the order has been added or via the mobile app. See [How to assign a packer to a Sale Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-Sale-Order) for more information. |
| Order Urgent | If an Urgent Order has been set up, then it will be used by selecting this option as Yes. |

- To add products to the Sale Order, select the Products tab or select the green button Add Product(s) on the Details tab.

![add-a-sale-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-sale-order-1.png?width=670&height=185&name=add-a-sale-order-1.png)

- Select the product from the **PRODUCT** drop-down menu and enter the quantity in the **QTY** box.
- Click the green **Search** button.
- CartonCloud will automatically select the stock to assign to the Sale Order based on the stock selection method selected at the Product settings. See [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/How-CartonCloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-Stock-Selection-Methods)
- If you want to override the selection, select the **x Clear Selection**button and enter the quantity value for the stock, you wish to select.
- Alternatively, if you are wanting to search for a specific stock item you can select the Search by Other Fields tab. This allows you to apply filters to the search results to narrow down the number of items being displayed.

![add-a-sale-order-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-sale-order-4.png?width=670&height=273&name=add-a-sale-order-4.png)

- You can filter by a combination of Product, Location, Pallet numbers or Custom Field values to help you select the correct stock to add to the Sale Order. You can use the Group option , which allows inventory with the same product and custom field values to be grouped together, showing a combined available quantity instead of multiple separate rows.
- Once you have selected the stock, click the green **Take Stock** button.

![add-a-sale-order-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-sale-order-5.png?width=670&height=265&name=add-a-sale-order-5.png)

- Select the **Charges** tab.
- Check that the charges are calculating correctly. CartonCloud will prompt you if something doesn't look right. For example, if you haven't loaded picking charges for a Unit of Measure, it will prompt you to fix it.

![add-a-sale-order-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-a-sale-order-6.png?width=670&height=185&name=add-a-sale-order-6.png)

- Return to the **Details** tab and select the green **Approve** button. This will change the status to *Awaiting Pick and Pack*andmake it visible within CartonCloud to your Packers.

See [Packing a Sale Order (on the web app)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Packing-a-Sale-Order-on-the-web-app) for the next steps on how to pack a Sale Order.

---

<a id="adding-a-comment-to-a-sale-order"></a>
## Adding a comment to a Sale Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-a-comment-to-a-sale-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- How to add a comment to a sale order

### Purpose

To add a comment to a Sale Order through the web app for users (excluding customers) to view (on the web app).

### Benefits

- To record important information against the Sale Order.
- To communicate key information in relation to the Sale Order with other users.

### How to add a comment to a Sale Order

- Navigate to the Sale Orders page, Warehouse > Sale Orders .
- Select the Sale Order you wish to add the comment to.
- Select the Comments tab.
- Click Add comment .

![adding-a-comment-to-a-sale-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-sale-order-0.png?width=670&height=342&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-sale-order-0.png)

- Enter the comment.
- Click Submit .

![adding-a-comment-to-a-sale-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-sale-order-1.png?width=670&height=342&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-sale-order-1.png)

- The comment will now be visible against the Sale Order on the web app for other users (excluding customers).

<a id="allowing-expired-stock-to-be-used-in-sale-orders"></a>
## Allowing Expired Stock to be used in Sale Orders

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/allowing-expired-stock-to-be-used-in-sale-orders_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Enabling expired stock use in sale orders

### Purpose

When perishable goods come into the Warehouse in the form of a Purchase Order they are given an expiry date. This expiry date is then used by CartonCloud to determine whether or not it can be packed as part of a Sale Order. By default, expired stock is not allowed to be used for packing Sale Orders. However, should a Customer wish to allow expired stock to be sent out, then a per-customer setting exists to enable this functionality. When this setting is enabled any available stock in the Warehouse, be it expired or not, can be used to pack a Sale Order.

### Enabling expired stock use in sale orders

To enable the use of Expired Stock in Sale Orders:

- Navigate to the Customers page, Contacts > Customers .
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click Edit .
- Select the Warehouse Management > Sale Order tab.

- Against If Sale Order is imported any (any) product(s) can only be filled with expired stock check Allow expired stock to be used

![allowing-expired-stock-to-be-used-in-sale-orders-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/allowing-expired-stock-to-be-used-in-sale-orders-0.png?width=670&height=334&name=allowing-expired-stock-to-be-used-in-sale-orders-0.png)

---

<a id="automatically-updating-sale-orders-to-dispatched"></a>
## Automatically updating Sale Orders to Dispatched

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/automatically-updating-sale-orders-to-dispatched_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Accessing the customer setting
- Sale orders are getting stuck in the 'packed' status
- Solution

### Purpose

If you wish to define when a Sale Order should be automatically updated to 'Dispatched' then this article will cover how to set this behaviour.

This configuration is controlled by a Customer setting, meaning the behaviour can be set up for each customer differently.

The setting's options allow control for a Sale Order to be automatically updated to Dispatched when:

- The Sale Order is Packed and the Consignment is created - Default setting
- The Consignment leaves the warehouse - if using the Transport module
- Never - if you never want the Sale Order status to automatically updated to dispatched

### Accessing the customer setting

- In the CartonCloud main menu, select Contacts > Customers
- Select the Customer you wish to configure. Or if you wish to do this for many customers (3+) then use the article WMS Settings Bulk Export/Import to change the field 'auto_dispatch'
- Now on the View Customer page, select Edit .
- Select the Warehouse Management tab, then Sale Order sub-tab
- Scroll down to the Status updates section
- Change the setting Automatically Update the Sale order to Dispatched based on your operational requirements.

### Sale Orders are getting stuck in the 'Packed' status

If you have set Sale Orders to automatically be updated to dispatched, but the status is getting stuck on 'Packed' then it is likely because there are Customer Invoices uploaded to the Sale Order(s) which are yet to be marked as printed.

### Solution

Once the attached Customer Invoices have been marked as printed, then the Sale order(s) will then be updated to the 'Dispatched' status.

See the article [Printing Sale Order Customer Invoices / Documents](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=532547479) for assistance with printing the Invoices if required and marking the Sale Order invoices as printed (therefore updating the status to 'Dispatched).

---
