<a id="changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date"></a>
## Changing a Sale Orders Packed Date or Dispatched Date

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps
- Impact on storage
- Change limitations

### Purpose

Since Sale Orders deduct stock from Purchase Orders, the packed / dispatch dates of the Sale Order can affect your storage charges. For this reason, you’re able to modify the Sale Order dispatched/packed date so you can modify storage charging.

These changes may cause errors. These errors are covered [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com#change-limitations).

### How to steps

- Navigate to the Sale Orders page, Warehouse > Sale Orders .
- Select the relevant Sale Order.
- Scroll down and expand the Specifics section.
- Select Change against the Date Packed field.

![changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-0.png?width=670&height=329&name=changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-0.png)

- Update the Date Packed and click Update .

![changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-0.png?width=670&height=329&name=changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-0.png)

### Impact on storage

Depending on the *Customer Setting - Deplete Purchase Order Product* , which determines when you stop charging storage on stock, will dictate the impact of updating the Date Packed or Date Dispatched.

The Change link with the exclamation mark next to the date information indicates which date will impact storage.

![changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-2.png?width=471&height=238&name=changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-2.png)

### Change Limitations

Changing the date may result in an error for the below reasons;

- The Date Packed must always be less than Date Dispatched.
- The Date Packed or Date Dispatched cannot be less than the date of the most recent product movement of the selected product.
- The Date Packed or Date Dispatched cannot be less than the date the Purchase Order that the stock arrived on is set to.

To check the Purchase Order Date and/or the most recent Move Date:

- Navigate to the relevant Sale Order.
- Select the Products tab.
- Select Edit against the product lines.

![changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-3.png?width=670&height=291&name=changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-3.png)

- Select the POP_ID.

![changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-4.png?width=670&height=202&name=changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-4.png)

- Expand the Specifics heading.
  - Original Allocated Date = Purchase Order Date
  - Allocated Date = Most Recent Move Date

![changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-5.png?width=443&height=294&name=changing-a-sale-orders-packed-date-or-dispatched-date-5.png)

---

<a id="copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments"></a>
## Copying Sale Order Customer Invoices to Consignments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Turning it on for all customers
- Turning it on for an individual customers
- How it works
- Updating or adding additional invoices

### Purpose

CartonCloud can be configured to automatically copy Customer Invoices from a Sale Order to a Consignment generated by the Sale Order. This includes invoices which are attached to Sale Orders through a

Parser

.

This setting can either be turned on at the Organisation Level (through organisation settings) or individually for each customer, through the Edit Customer page.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/C-uPIunBkv4

### Turning it on for all customers

If you wish for this behaviour to apply to all of your customers this can be done by first turning on the corresponding Organisation Setting.

- Go to the main menu and select More > Organisation Settings
- Select the Warehouse tab.
- Then change the setting Copy Sale Order Customer Invoice to Consignment to Yes.

### Turning it on for an individual customer

If you wish for this behaviour to apply to a particular customer this can be done by turning on the setting for that customer.

- Go to the main menu and select Contacts > Customers
- Select the Customer you wish to turn this on for
- Select Edit towards the bottom left of the page
- Select the Warehouse Management tab (the Sale Order sub-tab will automatically be selected)
- Scroll down to the Consignment settings heading
- Then change the setting Copy Sale Order Customer Invoice to Consignment to Yes

![copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-0.png?width=670&height=323&name=copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-0.png)

- Scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save for the change to be applied.

### How it works

When a Sale Order is created in CartonCloud an option is provided for the corresponding Customer Invoice to be attached to the order.

![copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-1.png?width=670&height=335&name=copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-1.png)
Alternatively, the Invoice can be attached at a later time using the Customer Invoices tab.

![copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-2.png?width=670&height=294&name=copying-sale-order-customer-invoices-to-consignments-2.png)
Now, when the Consignment is generated either automatically upon pack completion or through the Consignments tab the Customer Invoice will be copied across to the Consignment.

### Updating or adding additional invoices

If another Invoice is attached to the Sale order after the consignment has been generated then it will automatically be attached to the Consignment.

Deleting an invoice from a Sale Order will not result in that same invoice being deleted from the linked consignment, so deletion will need to be completed separately for both records.

---

<a id="creating-a-sale-order-with-bom-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built"></a>
## Creating a Sale Order with BOM products that are yet to be built

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-a-sale-order-with-bom-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Enabling the settings
- Step by step instructions

### Purpose

This article assumes some pre-requisite knowledge on the subject of Bill of Materials products and how they work inside CartonCloud. If you are not familiar with BOM products yet. Please read the [Bill of Materials (BOM)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=536609777) article before proceeding.

This article covers how to create a Sale Order containing Bill of Material Products that have not yet being built. This means the components to make that Product are in stock, but they have not yet been combined to build the single BOM product in the system.

For example, perhaps a warehouse sends out coffee hampers for a customer, containing different individual bags of coffee. This article will cover how to create a Sale Order for that Hamper and have it automatically select the individual bags of stock that need to be combined to build the hamper.

### Enabling the setting

This functionality requires the Product and Customer setting **"****If finished Bill of Material products (BOMs) are out of stock, take from individual components"**to be set to **Yes*.**

For further instructions on how to enable this setting. See the [Bill of Materials article](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=536609777#BillofMaterials(BOM)-configurablesettings).

**Or **Yes** at a customer level, and **Use Customer Setting** at the product level.*

### Step-by-step Instructions

- To begin, create a Sale Order by selecting Warehouse in the main menu > Sale Orders from the drop-down
- Now select +Add Sale Order towards the top left of the page.
- Fill in the Sale Order details for Customer, Delivery address, etc, as required. Then select Add Sale Order. The Sale Order will be created.
- Now viewing the Sale Order. Select the Products tab.
- If you attempt to add a BOM product which does not have any stock built yet, the system will display a message of "No stock available for this product".
- To get around this message, type the quantity of the BOM product that you wish to add to the Sale order, then select Add Without Assigning Stock .

![creating-a-sale-order-with-bom-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-sale-order-with-bom-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built-0.png?width=670&height=268&name=creating-a-sale-order-with-bom-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built-0.png)

- The system will navigate back to the View Sale Order page on the Products tab. Now, select Auto Assign all Unassigned Stock.
- The system will navigate back to the Details tab, select the Products tab again and observe that the BOM products will now have been replaced by the product components which make up that BOM product, in the correct quantities to build the quantity you have requested.

![creating-a-sale-order-with-bom-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-sale-order-with-bom-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built-1.png?width=670&height=332&name=creating-a-sale-order-with-bom-products-that-are-yet-to-be-built-1.png)

- The system will have already taken stock from the most efficient locations based on the stock selection methods you have set up. If you wish to change this to take stock from different locations manually, do so now by selecting Edit on the product line.
- Repeat the above steps for any extra BOM products you wish to add to the Sale Order.
- Once all stock has been added and the Sale Order is ready to be picked, select Approve on the Details page to change it to a status of 'Awaiting Pick and Pack'

---

<a id="creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out"></a>
## Creating Sale Orders - stock going out

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to create a Sale Order

### Purpose

Now that you know how to record stock coming into your warehouse in CartonCloud (Purchase Order) the next step is to learn how to record stock going back out (Sale Order).

When stock leaves your warehouse a Sale Order is the name of the document which records that stocks movement within CartonCloud.

A Sale Order automatically stops warehouses charges from continuing to accumulate against the corresponding stock, however, there are settings which can allow this to continue until the stock physically leaves the warehouse. Optionally, Sale Orders can also generate a Consignment Note upon creation, pushing the product details from the Sale Order into the created Consignment Note, but we will revisit and explain this functionality during the TMS setup.

### How to create a Sale Order

- Navigate to the Sale Orders page by selecting Warehouse>Sale Orders from the main menu.
- Select +Add Sale Order .

![creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-0.png?width=670&height=328&name=creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-0.png)

- On the **Add new Sale Order** page, complete the fields. You can use the descriptions below to assist you as you complete the fields.

**Sale Order Fields**

| **Field** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Attach Invoice | Allows you to attached a customer invoice to the Sale order quickly. Invoices can also be attached after the Sale order is created through the Customer Invoices tab. |
| Customer | The owner (supplier) of the goods. Sale Orders can only be created for the stock of a single Customer. |
| Customer Reference | A reference number for the Sales Order. Normally this is your Customer's Invoice Number |
| Delivery Address | Where the Sale Order is going. It is recommended that you enter a Delivery Address even if the order is being picked up from your warehouse. This helps you distinguish between different Sale Orders when looking at the list view. In addition, this address will be printed onto the Consignment label; therefore, this will again help you identify the order and w   here it needs to go. |
| Order will be picked up from Warehouse | Tick if the order will be picked up. This will put the Consignment created from the Sale Order onto the default run set up for the Warehouse; this is usually the "Pickup from Warehouse" delivery run but can be configured. If you do not wish to use a default Delivery Run, you can modify this against the Warehouse (See [Edit Warehouse Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-edit-warehouse)). Note, if you are not using a default Delivery Run and have Zone Sets enabled, CartonCloud will use the Transport Lanes, and Zone Sets logic to determine the expected Delivery Run for the Sale Order. See [Setting up CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments)to allocate Consignments for more information automatically. |

**Advanced Options**

| Packing Instructions | Special instructions that show on the Packing Slip and Pick/Pack screen. |
| --- | --- |
| Delivery Instructions | Special instructions that get copied into the Consignments Special Instructions |
| Sale Order Value | The value (invoice amount) of the Sale Order. This field is only required if you charge your customer picking fees based on Percentage Of Invoice |
| Cash On Delivery | Whether or not the Sale Order requires Cash On Delivery to be collected. This information is passed onto the Consignment created by the Sale Order. |
| Attach Invoice to Goods | If your customer wants to upload an Invoice file to CartonCloud, which is then printed and attached to the order, this should be set to Yes.   Note: If you select Yes and then don't upload and print an invoice, the consignment will remain in an "Awaiting Sale Order Invoice" status preventing it from being allocated to delivery runs.   This is implemented because if the customer has selected that they want an Invoice attached to the goods, and you're still waiting for the Invoice, you probably don't want to send the stock without the Invoice attached. |
| Required Ship Date | The date that the order should leave the warehouse. This is useful if you're sending with Onforwarders and have limited control over the Delivery Date. In this case, you often want the order to leave your warehouse as soon as possible, but then you may specify a required delivery date with the carrier. |
| Required Delivery Date | The date that the stock should be delivered. This affects the day that the related consignment is allocated. |
| Order Urgent | If an Urgent Order has been set up, then it will be used by selecting this option as Yes. |

- To add products to the Sale Order, select the **Products** tab or select the green button **Add Product(s)** on the **Details** tab.

![creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-1.png?width=670&height=266&name=creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-1.png)

- Select the product from the **PRODUCT** drop-down menu and enter the quantity in the **QTY** box.
- Click the green **Search** button.

![creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-2.png?width=670&height=180&name=creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-2.png)

- CartonCloud will automatically select the stock to assign to the Sale Order based on the stock selection method selected at the Product settings. See [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-cartoncloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-stock-selection-methods).
- If you want to override the selection, select the **x Clear Selection**button and enter the quantity value for the stock, you wish to select.
- Once you have selected the stock, click the green **Take Stock** button.

![creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-3.png?width=670&height=273&name=creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-3.png)

- Select the Charges tab.
- Check that the charges are calculating correctly. CartonCloud will prompt you if something doesn't look right. For example, if you haven't loaded picking charges for a Unit of Measure, it will prompt you to fix it.

![creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-4.png?width=670&height=265&name=creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-4.png)

- Return to the **Details** tab and select the green **Approve** button. This will change the status to *Awaiting Pick and Pack*andmake it visible within CartonCloud to your Packers.

![creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-5.png?width=670&height=265&name=creating-sale-orders-stock-going-out-5.png)

See [Packing a Sale Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app) for the next steps on how to pack a Sale Order.

---

<a id="deleting-sale-orders-in-bulk"></a>
## Deleting Sale Orders in Bulk

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/deleting-sale-orders-in-bulk_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- By manual selection
- Using filters and the select all button

### Purpose

This article covers how to delete Sale Orders in large quantities from the Sale Orders page.

To get to the Sale Order page, select **Warehouse** in the Main menu > **Sale Orders** from the drop-down.

### By Manual Selection

This simple method is best used when all the orders you wish to delete are on the same page (less than 30 orders).

- Select each Sale order you wish to delete.
- Multiple sale orders in a row can be selected by selecting the top order, holding the Shift key, then selecting the bottom-most sale order. This will cause all orders between the two to be selected.
- Select Delete and a pop up window will appear to confirm the deletion.
- Select OK and the orders will be deleted.

![deleting-sale-orders-in-bulk-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/deleting-sale-orders-in-bulk-0.png?width=670&height=321&name=deleting-sale-orders-in-bulk-0.png)

### Using Filters and the Select All button

This method can be used to delete all Sale Orders that are searched for through the Filter tab. This method is best used for large deletions (30+ Orders).

- On the Sale order page, select the Filter tab.
- Apply the necessary filters so that only the Sale Order you wish to delete appear in the search.
- Next, click the Select All button and all orders will be highlighted (including any that might be on the following pages.

- Select Delete All and the system will produce a warning message to ensure you wish to continue with the deletion. Remember, deletion cannot be undone!
- Provided you wish to continue, select OK .
- The Sale Order records have now been deleted from CartonCloud.

---

<a id="generating-a-consignment-from-a-sale-order"></a>
## Generating a Consignment from a Sale Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/generating-a-consignment-from-a-sale-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- WMS&TMS Accounts Set Up
- WMS Only Accounts Set Up

### Purpose

Consignments can be automatically created from a Sale Order upon packing completion or once picked, depending on your setup and workflows. This setup will be different depending on what CartonCloud modules are used:

- WMS & TMS Accounts: Consignment will be automatically generated from the Sale Order upon packing completion or the Sale Order being imported.
- WMS only Accounts: Warehouse Fulfilments (a type of Consignment) will be automatically generated from the Sale Order upon the order being picked. This set up is to be utilised in conjunction with the Pack Screen .

### WMS & TMS Accounts Set Up

To enable automatic Consignment generation from Sale Orders for WMS & TMS CartonCloud accounts the following settings need to be enabled:

- Navigate to Customers , Users > Customers .
- Select the Customer you wish to enable the workflow for.
- Click Edit .
- Select Warehouse Management > Sale Order .
- Scroll down to the section labelled Consignment .
- Update the Automatically Generate a Consignment from a Sale Order setting to either Yes, when Sale Order is Packed Only or Yes, on Sale Order Import or Pack Completion . Each setting is described below:

**Automatically Generate a Consignment from a Sale Order**

| **Option** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| No | Never create a Consignment from a Sale Order automatically. |
| Yes, when Sale Order is Packed Only | (default) Consignment is generated when the Sale Order finishes being packed. The Consignment then goes immediately to "In Warehouse" status. |
| Yes, on Sale Order Import or Pack Completion | Consignment is generated as soon as the Sale Order is imported, you then have the option of what the status of the Consignment should be:   **Initial Status Of Automatically Generated Consignments**       **Awaiting Sale Order Packing** - Consignment goes to the "Awaiting Sale Order Packing" status and does not get given a Delivery Run Date until packing completed      **In Warehouse**- Consignment goes to the "In Warehouse" status and is immediately given a Delivery Run Date for allocation. |

- You can also select the default screen after packing by updating the Sale Order Default After Pack Screen setting.

**Sale Order Default After Pack Screen**

| **Option** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Consignment (Label Printing) page | After you finish packing a Sale Order, you'll be immediately taken to the Consignment screen to print labels. |
| Back to Sale Order Page | After you finish packing a Sale Order, you'll be taken back to either the View Sale Order page or the View Wave Pick page (if picking Sale Order as part of |

**Default Sender Address for Consignments Generated from Sale Orders**

If you display the Sender Address on Manifests / Run Sheets, it can be important to show a specific Sender Address for each customer for whom you pick stock for. This option enables you to specify the Sender Address for the automatically generated consignments. If nothing is provided here it defaults to the address of your Warehouse.

### WMS Only Accounts Set Up

WMS only CartonCloud accounts can access Warehouse Fulfilments (a type of Consignment). This helps facilitate the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) workflow, where a Warehouse Fulfilment is generated once the Sale Order has been picked. This workflow allows for the product to be packed into the package (Consignment Item), print labels and complete the order fulfillment process.

By enabling Warehouse Fulfilments, an additional Sale Order status of 'Picked' will be enabled and allow the use of the Pack Screen.

Warehouse Fulfilments are optional.

**To enable Warehouse Fulfillments and use the Pack Screen:**

Warehouse Fulfilments are enabled from the Organisation Settings and can be further controlled at the Customer level (if you wish to only enable it for certain customers).

**Organisation Settings**

*This will turn on Warehouse Fulfilments for all Customers.*

- Navigate to Organisation Settings, More > Organisation Settings .
- Click the Warehouse > General tab.
- Scroll down to the setting Automatically Generate a Consignment from a Sale Order.
- Select either:
  - **Yes, when Sale Order is Picked Only** - a Consignment (Warehouse Fulfilment) will generate when a Sale Order is picked. **Yes, on Sale Order Import or Pick Completion** - a Consignment (Warehouse Fulfilment) will generate when a Sale Order is imported or upon pick completion.
- Scroll down and click Save .

If you wish to turn this off for certain Customers, you will need to do so from the [Customer Settings - Warehouse Management (Sale Order Tab)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Customer-Settings-Warehouse-Management)

---

<a id="how-cartoncloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-stock-selection-methods"></a>
## How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-cartoncloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-stock-selection-methods_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Intelligent pallet handling
- Choosing a stock selection method
- Method list and selection order further details
  - Location efficiency only
  - FEFO (First Expiry, First Out)
  - FIFO (First In, First Out)
    - LIFO (Last In, First Out)
- Stock Sub Selection Method

### Purpose

CartonCloud uses Stock Selection Methods to determine in which order stock should leave a warehouse. These methods are set up against the [Product](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Products)record so that specific products can be given their own selection logic. For example, products with expiry dates are treated differently than those without.

When setting up a product the stock selection method **must** be chosen. This article provides the information required for you to decide on a stock selection method for each product in your warehouse.

### Intelligent Pallet Handling

CartonCloud Intelligently handles Pallet Quantities (and preventing breaking pallets where possible). It does this by providing additional Stock Selection logic, and also implementing the Stock Sub-Selection Method

1. Look for locations which contain exactly the quantity required.
2. If the ordered quantity is one pallet load, prioritise full pallets (avoid building pallets up from part pallets)
3. If the ordered quantity is less than one pallet load, prioritise stocks which are part pallets (to avoid breaking up full pallets)
4. If the Stock Sub-Selection Method is "Minimise Picks", then prioritise locations with enough stock to fulfil the order (avoid using multiple locations where possible)

**Strict Mode** also has an effect on Pallet Handling. If Strict Mode is enabled then FEFO / FIFO / LIFO will be enforced even if it causes splitting of full pallets, or picking from part-pallets to build full pallets.

The exception here is if the Product has Replenishment enabled, and there is stock in a Pickface location, CartonCloud will always select this stock.

If Strict Mode is disabled, CartonCloud will break part-pallets and full-pallets into two groups. If it is looking for full-pallet quantities then it will search through all the full-pallets in FEFO / FIFO / LIFO order. Only if no full pallets exist will it revert to picking from part-pallets in FEFO / FIFO / LIFO order. If part-pallet stocks are being searched, it will first look through all part-pallet quantities in FEFO / FIFO / LIFO order before going onto full pallet quantities. This creates better efficiency in the picking, however, it means that stock is not strictly FEFO / FIFO / LIFO.

### Choosing a Stock Selection Method

Use the flowchart below to decide what Stock Selection Method your Product requires.

If you chose Location Efficiency only and aren't sure if your Warehouse Locations are set up with efficiency scores check out: [Setting up Warehouse Locations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Warehouse+Locations)

### Method list and selection order further details

#### **Location Efficiency Only**

Note: if using Location Efficiency Only you need to select Location Efficiency as your Stock Sub-Selection Method

Stocks are selected based on the following ordering when choosing stock by pick efficiency:

1. **Purchase Order Status** - Prioritise stock with a status of >= Received (Can be adjusted in Customer Settings for minimum status before picking allowed)
2. **Stock Sub-Selection Method** - Based on the Stock Sub-Selection Method CartonCloud will either try to minimise the number of locations that the stock is taken from or minimise the number of locations that will still hold stock after the order is packed. (Focusing on picking from locations with least stock).
3. **Pallet Quantities** - Uses Intelligent Pallet Handling - See the top of this page.
4. **Pick Efficiency** - Prioritise stocks based on Location Pick Efficiency
5. **Warehouse Location Name**- Sort based on the alphanumeric order of the name

#### **FEFO (First Expiry, First Out)**

Stocks are selected based on the following order when choosing stock by Expiry Date:

1. **Purchase Order Status** - Prioritise stock with a status of >= Received (Can be adjusted in Customer Settings for minimum status before picking allowed)
2. **Expiry Date Absent** - Prioritise stocks with no Expiry Dates loaded
3. **Expiry Date Order** - Prioritise stocks which are the soonest to expire -the oldest expiry dates will be selected first
4. **Pallet Quantities** - Uses Intelligent Pallet Handling - See the top of this page.
5. **Allocated vs Unallocated** - Check for Unallocated Location stock and use before allocated Location stock → this will be superseded and overridden by the minimum Purchase Order status mentioned at the start i.e. allocated will force all stock to have Warehouse Locations.
6. **Pick Efficiency** - Prioritise stocks based on Location Pick Efficiency - by locations
7. **Pallet Clearing**- Prioritise pallets with the least stock remaining (to try and clear up small pallets before starting on big ones).

#### **FIFO (First In, First Out)**

Stocks are selected based on the following ordering when choosing stock by Arrival Date:

1. **Purchase Order Status** - Prioritise stock with a status of >= Received (Can be adjusted in Customer Settings for minimum status before picking allowed)
2. **Arrival Date** - Prioritise stocks which have been in the warehouse the longest time by Arrival Date
3. **Pallet Quantities** - Uses Intelligent Pallet Handling - See the top of this page.
4. **Allocation Status** - Prioritise stocks which are not in a Warehouse Location (just arrived, send them back out rather than putting them away) → this will be superseded and overridden by the minimum purchase order status mentioned at the start i.e. allocated will force all stock to have Warehouse Locations.
5. **Pick Efficiency** - Prioritise stocks based on Location Pick Efficiency
6. **Pallet Clearing**- Prioritise pallets with the least stock remaining (to try and clear up small pallets before starting on big ones).
7. **Expiry Date** - Prioritise stocks which are the soonest to expire - i.e. the oldest expiry dates **(Provided the "ignore expiry date" setting isn't enabled on the product)**
8. **Warehouse Location Name**- Sort based on the alphanumeric order of the name

#### **LIFO (Last In, First Out)**

Stocks are selected based on the following ordering when choosing stock by Arrival Date:

1. **Purchase Order Status** - Prioritise stock with a status of >= Received (Can be adjusted in Customer Settings for minimum status before picking allowed)
2. **Arrival Date** - Prioritise stocks which have been in the warehouse the shortest time by Arrival Date
3. **Pallet Quantities** - Uses Intelligent Pallet Handling - See the top of this page.
4. **Allocation Status** - Prioritise stocks which are not in a Warehouse Location (just arrived, send them back out rather than putting them away) → this will be superseded and overridden by the minimum purchase order status mentioned at the start i.e. allocated will force all stock to have Warehouse Locations.
5. **Pick Efficiency** - Prioritise stocks based on Location Pick Efficiency
6. **Pallet Clearing**- Prioritise pallets with the least stock remaining (to try and clear up small pallets before starting on big ones).
7. **Expiry Date** - Prioritise stocks which are the soonest to expire - i.e. the oldest expiry dates **(Provided the "ignore expiry date" setting isn't enabled on the product)**
8. **Warehouse Location Name**- Sort based on the alphanumeric order of the name

**When all stock selection criteria match, use warehouse location name**
In the scenario that the system is choosing to select between two different pieces of stock and **ALL** of the selection criteria explained above matches, it will then fall back to the alphanumeric order of the warehouse location names containing the stock.

Example 1

- A Sale order needs 5 pallets of stock and the stock selection method is First In First Out (FIFO)
- There are 10 pallets of stock in location "Bulk A" and 10 pallets in "Bulk D", all with the same warehouse arrival dates.
- All other selection criteria are also equal between the pallets (see the full criteria in the FIFO section above).
- Since "A" comes before "D" alphabetically, the system selects the 5 pallets in "Bulk A" to fulfil the Sale Order.

Example 2

- A Sale order needs 5 pallets of stock and the stock selection method is First Expiry First Out (FEFO)
- Stock in location "Bulk 2" is selected first as it's expiry date is earlier than all available other stock. But it only contains 4 pallets, so 1 pallet still needs to be fulfilled.
- For the last pallet to be fulfilled, both locations "Bulk 1" and "Bulk 4" contain stock which is of equal selection criteria (based on the conditions outlined above on FEFO stock selection).
- As all other selection criteria are equal, the system chooses the stock from "Bulk 1", as 1 comes before 4 numerically.

### **Stock Sub-Selection Method**

Once you have selected a Stock Selection Method you must then choose a Sub-Selection Method. This means that if after the system uses the stock selection method if multiple locations meet that method's requirement the sub-selection method will be used to further optimise how you select stock.

This logic is secondary to the Stock Selection method, and will never override it.

**The available options are:**

| **Setting** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| **Location Efficiency** | The system will look at all the pallets available meeting the Stock Selection Method, then choose the location with the highest location efficiency first. *Warehouse Location efficiency scores are set up when [Setting up Warehouse Locations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Warehouse+Locations) and range from 1 (being the least efficient) through to 20 (being the most efficient)* |
| **Minimise Storage** | The system will look at all the pallets available meeting the Stock Selection Method, then choose the option which minimises the storage quantity by as much as possible, attempting to empty locations. |
| **Minimise Picks** | The system will look at all the pallets available meeting the Stock Selection Method, then choose the option which minimises the number of locations that Pickers will need visit to pick the order. For example, if you have an order for 30 cartons of soup, and the following stock available:   Location A - 20 Cartons of Soup   Location B - 10 Cartons of Soup   Location C - 50 Cartons of Soup   Location C will be chosen as it means the Picker will only need to visit 1 location to complete the order, rather than 2. |

---

<a id="how-the-pack-screen-changes-your-cartoncloud-wms"></a>
## How the Pack Screen Changes Your CartonCloud WMS

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-the-pack-screen-changes-your-cartoncloud-wms_

### Table of Contents

- Summary
- Why Warehouse Fulfilments?
- 1. TMS features now available in WMS
- 2. Modified Sale Order Statuses
- 3. New Organisation setting for Consignment / Warehouse Fulfilment generation
- 4. Maintaining existing workflows
- 5. Carrier integrations & Sale Orders
- 6. Allocating to drivers & Proof of Delivery (POD)
- Next Steps
- Frequently asked questions

With the release of CartonCloud’s Pack Screen, we’re making some important updates to the way the Warehouse Management System (WMS) works. This guide explains what’s changing, what stays the same, and what you need to enable in your account to take advantage of them.

We will be progressively rolling this out to all customers starting September 8th. We anticipate completing the rollout by the end of September. You will be notified in-app when this is available within your account.

**Live from the Warehouse! Watch Pack Screen in Action from our recent Webinar.** Take a step inside Motive 3PL’s warehouse, where we had a live look at CartonCloud’s brand-new [Pack Screen](https://csglb04.na1.hubspotlinks.com/Ctc/WZ+113/csGLb04/VVRmDS3MJhRbVvJBR871y-_cW3NdgT55BNZ1vMLtlV-3qn9qW8wLKSR6lZ3nWVVg_5Y7tTj0TW1tbBSL2h9FsSW6Y536p2Q6DHZW4_YBtX997-PgW6Xcb7242SDGqW3RsPnJ795XvHW3NXBmY7X3g_4W4V1g3l6C7nXwW2XvV-Q1fdrfQW80N7lK7F0_mkW3g4W4F5Rk5pGW2tDJDF7LRRn5VvSkTt4pK5LCN2hS_1VvCsCHW5Mb7ZW5J4dfRW2PyC5j170kbQW7HKmfZ4-KxbLW59s4R02V8ZtzW2SSxyg7Pmg75W8-rVkx7fQcnLW1lMZbk8-pwlGW24V7Pk7WsHvnW7rlG2P19gvkDVZLql51_46FqW6S14yH3jrl4dMqwXpksjzNXN6x0gP3bR_ZtW6R9LKw994gWrf4gSkwl04) feature. Discover how this simple, guided workflow helps teams pack faster, smarter, and with greater accuracy.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/6xVAO3m-uqs

### Summary

- Picking and Packing Sale Orders are being split into distinct steps.
- We are introducing a new Pack Screen and a new “Picked” status for Sale Orders.
- When packing a Sale Order, items can be packed into individual packages which each have their own weights and dimensions. This makes carrier bookings more accurate and keeps a record of which items were packed into which package.
- These enhancements are being included in all WMS accounts and will be made available between September 8th and the end of September. You will be notified in the web-app when it’s ready.
- By default, your existing workflows will be maintained, and you’ll need to enable the new functionality & workflows to use it.
- Update to mobile app version 6.29 or higher.

### Why Warehouse Fulfilments?

Until now, our WMS-only customers haven’t had access to Consignments, which meant some packing workflows were limited. By introducing Warehouse Fulfilments (a new type of Consignment), we’re removing these limitations and creating a more seamless packing & dispatch experience.

Key benefits include:

- Significantly improved packing workflow – our new Pack Screen creates a Warehouse Fulfilment and the associated Packages. To use the new Pack Screen, Sale Orders must be setup to generate Warehouse Fulfilments.
- Package-level data – each package (Consignment Item) within a Warehouse Fulfilment contains dimensions and weight.
- Item-to-package tracking – CartonCloud records which item(s) were packed into which box, improving accuracy and traceability.
- Label printing & carrier bookings – going forward, all carrier integrations will be built off Warehouse Fulfilments, giving consistency across WMS and TMS.
- Delivery tracking – Warehouse Fulfilments move through Shipped and Delivered statuses, providing visibility after the order has left the warehouse.

Note: Using Warehouse Fulfilments and the new Packing process is optional and no behavioural changes will occur automatically. To use the new workflows & capabilities, you must enable them by following the steps below.

### 1. TMS features now available in WMS

To support the new Warehouse Fulfilment workflow, several Transport Management System (TMS) features are now included for all WMS customers:

- Consignments (Warehouse Fulfilments) & Consignment Items (Packages) – when a Sale Order is Packed, a Warehouse Fulfilment and one or more packages will be created
- Transport Products – allowing you to setup standard shipping items that you use (eg: A4 Box, A3 Satchel, Pallet etc)
- Carriers & Delivery Runs – when configuring carrier integrations, our team will utilise our existing carrier and delivery run capability
- Run Sheets – allow Warehouse Fulfilments to be grouped together into a Manifest for carrier collection

This ensures you can pack orders, print labels, and process carrier bookings directly from the WMS.

Note: Once Warehouse Fulfilments are enabled, you must update the mobile app to version 6.29 or higher. App versions older than 6.29 will encounter errors when wave picking, and will bypass the picked status when picking individual orders, preventing the use of the Pack Screen.

### 2. Modified Sale Order Statuses

As CartonCloud now supports distinct “Pick” and “Pack” processes, we’ve made several changes to our statuses.

- The “Packing in Progress” status has been renamed to “Picking in Progress” to more accurately reflect the process being performed.
- If Sale Orders are setup to generate Warehouse Fulfilments, they will now enter a new “Picked” status. (Awaiting Pick and Pack → Picking in Progress → Picked → Packed → Dispatched).

Similar to “Picking in Progress”, the new “Picked” status is considered an in progress status, and therefore, Sale Orders in “Picked” status will only be automatically added to invoices once they are “Packed” or “Dispatched”.

Additionally, Consignments / Warehouse Fulfilments are now generated when Picking completes (previously they would generate on Pack completion).

### 3. New Organisation setting for Consignment / Warehouse Fulfilment generation

By default, existing **WMS-only** customers will have **Consignment (Warehouse Fulfilment) generation disabled**.

If you want to use the **Picked** status and the new **Pack Screen**, you’ll need to enable this via a new **organisation-level setting**:

- **Automatically Generate a Consignment from a Sale Order** .

Admins can turn this on once they’re ready to adopt the Pack Screen.

### 4. Maintaining existing workflows

We’ve made sure your existing workflows won’t break.

- If a Sale Order is **not generating a consignment**, it will skip the **Picked** status.

These orders will continue moving directly from **Picking in Progress → Packed / Dispatched**, exactly as they do today.

### 5. Carrier integrations & Sale Orders

If you have existing carrier integrations setup (or integrations into platforms such as Starshipit, Machship, Shipstation etc), the integration could have been setup in either of two ways:

1. Directly from the Sale Order (does not pass across package dimension information)
2. From Consignments & Consignment Items (Previously required either the TMS or our historical “Pack Screen” add-on).

If you have existing carrier integrations built directly from Sale Orders (1), and would like to have the integration updated to work off **Warehouse Fulfilments**, please contact our integrations team at:

📧 **[integrations@cartoncloud.com](mailto:integrations@cartoncloud.com)**

### 6. Allocating to drivers & Proof of Delivery (POD)

If you want to allocate consignments to drivers for POD, you will still need either:

- the full TMS , or
- the Warehouse POD add-on (part of WMS-premium).

Without one of these, consignments will not progress into driver allocation workflows.

### Next Steps

- Decide if you want to start using the Pack Screen .
- If yes, update your organisation setting to generate consignments from Sale Orders.
- Follow our Knowledge Base article on how to use the Pack Screen .
- Review whether you need the Warehouse POD add-on for driver allocation, and if so, reach out to our sales team
- Contact the integrations team if you have existing carrier integrations that you would like altered.
- Update all devices to mobile app to version 6.29 or higher.

### Frequently asked questions

**I’ve noticed that Warehouse Fulfilments (Consignments) are now being generated when Sale Order Picking completes, rather than when Packing is complete, why?**

If Warehouse Fulfilment generation is enabled, after an order is picked on mobile it takes you to the Consignment Items screen where [automatically generated consignment items](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products) are displayed. Because this screen requires a consignment to already exist, consignments are automatically generated on pick completion.

**I only have the WMS and currently pay for the “Pack Screen” add-on. Will I continue to pay for this?**

No, as the new Pack Screen & Warehouse Fulfilment functionality is now being provided to all WMS customers as a standard feature, you’ll no longer be charged for this add-on once the new  Pack Screen is enabled.

**What is the difference between a Warehouse Fulfilment and a regular Consignment?**

A Warehouse Fulfilment is a new type of Consignment specifically designed to be used with Sale Orders for the purpose of shipping with third-party carriers. Warehouse Fulfilments cannot be allocated to drivers or delivered using the mobile app, and do not support the full suite of Consignment Rating capabilities.

**Will I have to pay for Warehouse Fulfilment Consignments?**

No, Warehouse Fulfilments will not count toward your usage (Consignments or Warehouse Orders), they are included for free.

**I have both the TMS and WMS, and I want all Sale Orders to continue to create regular consignments because I deliver them myself. How can I achieve this?**

For customers using both the TMS and WMS, this will be the default behaviour (unchanged from how things currently work). If you would like to use Warehouse Fulfilments for some of your Sale Orders, please contact us so we can configure this.

**What determines whether a Sale Order will create a regular Consignment vs a Warehouse Fulfilment?**

The carrier. Every consignment is associated to a Carrier, and we (CartonCloud staff) can configure each carrier to either use regular consignments, or the new Warehouse Fulfilments. For example, if you send items with Auspost, Auspost would be set up as a new carrier and configured to create Warehouse Fulfilments. This way, anything shipped with Auspost will be treated as a Warehouse Fulfilment rather than a regular consignment.

**Will Warehouse Fulfilments appear on Consignment Reports and other places throughout CartonCloud?**

Initially yes, and we’ll be gathering feedback from our customers to determine exactly how and where Warehouse Fulfilments should display throughout CartonCloud.

**I only have the TMS, can I create Warehouse Fulfilments?**

No, Warehouse Fulfilments are only generated from Sale Orders, you can not create standalone Warehouse Fulfilments.

**Can a Sale Order create more than one Warehouse Fulfilment?**

Yes. A Sale Order may be split into multiple Warehouse Fulfilments if there are multiple tracking numbers. For example, if you are shipping using pre-purchased satchels such as Auspost Express satchels, each satchel has its own tracking number. If the Sale Order is packed into more than one satchel, then each satchel will become its own Warehouse Fulfilment. Conversely, if sending with services such as Auspost eParcel, multiple boxes can still be tracked under a single tracking number, so this would create a single Warehouse Fulfilment that contains multiple items.

**I ship a lot of things through Auspost, and I use a shipping platform such as StarShipit, ShipStation (or similar) to manage this. Can these now be shipped directly from CartonCloud?**

Yes. At present, our integrations team needs to configure the integration for you, but we are working to make this available via click+connect. If you would like to use our existing Auspost connection please contact us. Please note that we don’t yet have an interface on the Pack Screen to display the various shipping options and prices, (this is also coming soon), so if you need to perform manual selection you’ll need to continue to use Starshipit, Shipstation or similar.

**Do Warehouse Fulfilments impact the number of included API Calls?**

No. The number of included API calls is based on the number of Consignments and Warehouse Orders (Sale Orders + Purchase Orders) within your plan. As Warehouse Fulfilments are not counted toward usage for either of these, they do not have any impact on the number of included API calls.

---

<a id="how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order"></a>
## How to assign a packer to a Sale Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to assign a Sale Order in the web app
  - In bulk from the Sale Order list view
  - From within the individual Sale Order
- How to assign a Sale Order on the mobile app

### Purpose

To assign the task of packing a Sale Order to a packer. The packer will be recorded against the Sale Order in the web and mobile app. You can assign a Sale Order to a packer in either the web or mobile app.

### Prerequisites

To be able to assign a packer to a Sale Order the below is required:

- The user must be assigned the packer role. Please see [User Roles Explained](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/User-Roles-Explained)for more information.

### How to assign a Sale Order in the web app

There are a number of ways in which you can assign a Sale Order to a packer in the web app.

**In bulk from the Sale Order list view**

- Navigate to the Sale Order page, Warehouse > Sale Orders .

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-0.png?width=670&height=319&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-0.png)

- Use the select box to choose the Sale Orders you wish to assign to the packer. You can select multiple orders at once.
- Click Assign Packer .

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-1.png?width=670&height=316&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-1.png)

- Select the packer from the drop down menu and click Save .
- You will now be able to see the name of the packer assigned to the order on the Sale Order list view.

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-3.png?width=670&height=168&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-3.png)

- You can also see the packer who is assigned to the order from within the Sale Order.

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-4.png?width=670&height=309&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-4.png)

**From within the individual Sale Order**

- Navigate to the relevant Sale Order you wish to assign the packer to.
- Click Assign Packer.

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-5.png?width=670&height=280&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-5.png)

- Select the packer from the drop down menu and click Save .

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-6.png?width=670&height=222&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-6.png)

### How to assign a Sale Order on the mobile app

To assign a Sale Order on the mobile app you need to start the task. By starting the task the Sale Order will be assigned to the user who started the task.

- From the Task List, select the task you wish to assign yourself.
- Click Start Task .

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-7.png?width=247&height=493&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-7.png)

- Click Ok .

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-8.png?width=264&height=527&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-8.png)

- Initials of the packer who is assigned to the order will appear against the Sale Order

![how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-9.png?width=269&height=544&name=how-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-sale-order-9.png)

---

<a id="how-to-resend-a-sale-order"></a>
## How to Resend a Sale Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-resend-a-sale-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use case
- Steps to duplicate a sale order
- Invoicing for the duplicate order

### Purpose

To resend a Sale Order, you need to duplicate the original Sale Order.

### Use case

- The courier loses a Sale Order dispatched from your warehouse, and you need to resend it.
- An order is damaged in transit and needs to be sent out again.
- The original order was sent to the wrong address and needs to be sent out again but to the correct address.

### Steps to duplicate a Sale Order

- Navigate to the Sale Order you need to resend, Warehouse > Sale Orders >Select relevant Sale Order.
- Select the Details tab.
- Select the green Duplicate Sale Order button.

![how-to-resend-a-sale-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-resend-a-sale-order-0.png?width=670&height=266&name=how-to-resend-a-sale-order-0.png)

- Enter the duplicate Sale Order reference. It is suggested you add 'Resend' to the end of the reference.
- Select Duplicate .
- Then dispatch the Sale Order as normal.

### Invoicing from the duplicate order

Depending upon your agreements with your customer, you may need to zero out the charges on the order so that they are not charged for both orders.

Note, you will need to zero out the duplicate order as the original order may already have been invoiced and paid.

**The charges you will need to zero out on the order include:**

1. Item Charge
2. Adhoc Charge
3. Charges

**![how-to-resend-a-sale-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-resend-a-sale-order-1.png?width=670&height=270&name=how-to-resend-a-sale-order-1.png)**

**To zero out the charges on the duplicate order:**

- Navigate to the duplicate Sale Order.
- Select the Charges tab.
- Zero out any charges for the Item Charge Data and select Save. Repeat this process for the Adhoc Charge Data table.
- Scroll down to the Charges table and select Automatically Calculate Income Charges .
- Click on the individual charge.
- Click the red Delete button.
- Repeat this process for all charges.
- Click Mark Charges Finalized. This will add the Sale Order to the Invoice with no charges against the order.

![how-to-resend-a-sale-order-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-resend-a-sale-order-2.png?width=670&height=216&name=how-to-resend-a-sale-order-2.png)

---

<a id="marking-a-sale-order-as-urgent"></a>
## Marking a Sale Order as Urgent

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/marking-a-sale-order-as-urgent_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How customers mark a sale order as urgent
- Approving the request as an admin

### Purpose

If customers require Sale Orders to be picked urgently, they can mark the order as urgent. The urgent request then needs to be approved by an account administrator.

### How Customers mark a Sale Order as Urgent

- From the Customer login, navigate to Warehouse > Sale Orders.
- Select the relevant order and click Mark as urgent.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-38-18-0788-AM.png?width=670&height=286&name=image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-38-18-0788-AM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-40-15-3248-AM.png?width=670&height=285&name=image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-40-15-3248-AM.png)

- Once the order has progressed beyond "Awaiting Pick and Pack", the customer no longer has the option to "Make It Urgent" (as you're already processing).
- When Orders are added to a Wave Pick they are immediately updated to "Packing In Progress" status, so the Urgent Request needs to be made prior to the Wave Pick starting.

### Approving the urgent request as an Admin

The Urgent Request can be acknowledged (or rejected) up until it gets Packed. When the order is marked Packed, if the request stands, then it will be approved automatically.

- Navigate to Warehouse > Sale Orders .
- You will be notified of urgent order requests.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-49-41-2661-AM.png?width=670&height=283&name=image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-49-41-2661-AM.png)

- Click Click here .
- Click through to the urgent order.
- Click Respond to Urgent Request .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-53-50-6632-AM.png?width=670&height=275&name=image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-53-50-6632-AM.png)

- Update the order accordingly.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-54-32-8441-AM.png?width=670&height=247&name=image-png-Nov-12-2025-06-54-32-8441-AM.png)
