<a id="modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch"></a>
## Modifying the Product Quantity of a Sale Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps
- Behaviour by Order Status
- Integration Warning

### Purpose

You can modify product quantities on a Sale Order regardless of its current status. This provides flexibility to correct stock levels without needing to create additional Sale or Purchase Orders. This process is commonly referred to as *Post-Pack Stock Correction*, but it applies to all Sale Order statuses.

### How to steps

- Navigate to the relevant Sale Order

- Select the **Products** tab.
- Click **Edit** against the line of stock you wish to adjust.

![modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-0-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-0-1.png?width=670&height=224&name=modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-0-1.png)

- Update the quantity and click **Save**.

![modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-1-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-1-1.png?width=670&height=234&name=modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-1-1.png)

- You will now be able to see the adjustment that has been made.
- For Packed and Dispatched orders, the change will be highlighted.
- For earlier statuses, the updated quantity will appear without highlight.

![modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-2.png?width=670&height=291&name=modifying-the-product-quantity-of-a-sale-order-after-dispatch-2.png)

### Behaviour by Order Status

Modifying product quantities behaves differently depending on the Sale Order status. The table below will explain the behaviour of each Sale Order status when quantities are adjusted:

| **Status** | **Behaviour when modifying product quantity** |
| --- | --- |
| Draft | Product quantities can be freely edited |
| Awaiting Pick and Pack | Changes apply normally without visual highlighting |
| Packing in Progress | Changes apply normally without visual highlighting |
| Packed | Changes will be highlighted to show the differences when adjustments are made |
| Dispatched | Changes will be highlighted to show the differences when adjustments are made |

### Integration Warning

Amending product quantities after a Sale Order is Dispatched may cause issues with integrated systems.
For example, editing dispatched orders in CartonCloud may lead to mismatched data between CartonCloud and connected platforms (such as accounting or eCommerce systems).
It is strongly recommended to confirm the impact with your integration provider before making changes to a Dispatched Sale Order.

---

<a id="pack-screen"></a>
## Pack Screen

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pack-screen_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- Benefits
- Use Cases
- How to use the Pack Screen
  - Accessing the Pack Screen
  - Packing an Order (via scanning)
  - Packing an Order (without scanning)
  - Packing an Order with Carrier Connections
- Additional Pack Screen Features
- Video Tutorial
- How to Use the Pack Screen with Different Picking Workflows
- Scanning Capabilities
  - Transport Products for Scanning
- Pack Screen Photo Capture
- Recommended Packing Station Setup
- **Printing a Packing Slip from the Pack Screen**
- Known Limitations
- Enhancements Coming Soon

### Purpose

The CartonCloud Pack Screen allows you to pack Sales Orders that are in a ‘Picked’ status. The Pack Screen streamlines the final stage of order fulfilment by enabling an efficient and accurate packing workflow.

### Prerequisites

Before using the Pack Screen, please ensure the following:

- Turn on Warehouse Fulfilments (Consignment) auto-generation in the Organisation Settings (can be further controlled at the customer level if you wish to only enable it for certain customers). See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Organisation-Settings-Warehouse) for more details. (Note: this is enabled by default for new CartonCloud accounts)
- The Sale Order you wish to pack is in a ‘Picked’ status.
- You have barcode labels for either the Pick List, Customer Reference, or Totes to scan the order to pack.
- You have printed the Action Barcodes. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com#scanning-capabilities) for more information.
- Transport Products are set up, ideally with barcodes and dimensions. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-Transport-Products) for more information.
- You have reviewed the [Recommended Packing Station Setup](https://help.cartoncloud.com#recommended-packing-station-setup).
- Ensure Products are updated with weight information (if wanting to record total item weight). See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-a-Product) for more information.
- Sale Orders can't be packed through the Pack Screen if the Consignment is already on an approved Invoice. The Invoice status needs to be in Draft.
- If you are using Auto-Generated Consignment Items, please ensure you have selected the correct settings to either hide or show them on the Pack Screen. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products).
- If you are using Carrier Connections ensure you have Self-Managed Carrier Connections set up.

If you are an existing CartonCloud user, please review the [How the Pack Screen Changes Your CartonCloud WMS](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/How-the-Pack-Screen-Changes-Your-CartonCloud-WMS) guide for more information relating to the Pack Screen and Warehouse Fulfilments.

### Benefits

- Enables fast, barcode-driven packing workflows.
- Automatically applies product and packaging dimensions.
- Supports label printing and e-commerce workflows.
- Reduces human error and streamlines fulfilment.

### Use Cases

- High-volume e-commerce operations.
- Workflows utilising Pick to Tote or Split Pick and Pack Waves.
- Operations needing to pack large volumes efficiently with minimal data entry.
- Operations with dedicated packing stations.

### How to use the Pack Screen

The Pack Screen is broken into four sections:

![pack-screen-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-0.png?width=670&height=363&name=pack-screen-0.png)

| **Section** | **Purpose** |
| --- | --- |
| Green | This displays the order that is currently being packed. *In the future, it will support showing multiple orders when packing a wave.* |
| Blue | The products to be packed. |
| Red | Consignments (Warehouse Fulfilments) and Consignment Items (Packages). |
| Yellow | The delivery information and action buttons. |

**Tips:**

- It is recommended to use at least a 21” monitor. If you are using a laptop, iPad or similar, adjust your browser zoom if your screen does not display all sections clearly.
- The optimal way to use the Pack Screen is by only scanning barcodes and avoiding using the keyboard and mouse as much as possible.

### Accessing the Pack Screen

There are three ways to access the Pack Screen:

- **From the Warehouse Menu:**
  - Navigate to **Warehouse** > **Pack Sale Order**.
- **From the View Sale Order Screen:**
  - Navigate to a Sale Order that is in the “Picked” status.
  - Select **Pack Sale Order**.
- **From the Wave Pick Sale Order Screen:**
  - Navigate to a Wave Pick.
  - Select the **Sale Order** tab.
  - Click **Pack Order**.

#### Packing an Order (via scanning)

Using the Pack Screen with a barcode scanner is the most efficient workflow.

- From the **Pack Screen**, scan the Pick List or Tote to search for the order. The order must be in the current warehouse and be in a “Picked” status to appear in the search.

![pack-screen-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-1.png?width=670&height=371&name=pack-screen-1.png)

- Scan a Transport Product barcode.
- This will create a new Consignment Item with the corresponding information (code, description and dimensions).

![pack-screen-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-2.png?width=670&height=358&name=pack-screen-2.png)

- To pack an item, scan the Product’s barcode. If the Product is set up with weight information, the total item weight will be incremented as products are added.

![pack-screen-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-3.png?width=670&height=364&name=pack-screen-3.png)

- To add another Consignment Item, scan another Transport Product barcode and continue the packing process.
- Once packing is complete, double-check the weight using scales and, if needed, update the weight field.

![pack-screen-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-4.png?width=670&height=356&name=pack-screen-4.png)

- Check and update the Service Type if required.
- Scan the Complete Packing or Complete Packing and Print Labels barcode.

#### Packing an Order (without scanning)

The Pack Screen is designed to be used with a barcode scanner; however, it is still possible to use the Pack Screen without a scanner. Alternatively, you can use a combination of scanning and non-scanning depending on your workflow and operation requirements.

- From the Pack Screen, search for the order using the ID, Reference or Tote in the Order search bar.

![pack-screen-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-5.png?width=670&height=329&name=pack-screen-5.png)

- Click Add Item to add the first Consignment Item.

![pack-screen-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-6.png?width=670&height=327&name=pack-screen-6.png)

- Type to search for the Transport Product in the Product Code search box.

![pack-screen-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-7.png?width=670&height=355&name=pack-screen-7.png)

- Click products to pack them. By default, the entire quantity of the product will be packed. If you would like to move partial quantities, you can do so from the 3-dots menu.

![pack-screen-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-8.png?width=670&height=355&name=pack-screen-8.png)

- Once packing is complete, double-check the weight using scales and, if needed, update the weight field.

![pack-screen-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-9.png?width=670&height=346&name=pack-screen-9.png)

- Check and update the Service Type if required.
- Once all products have been packed, click Complete packing & print labels .

![pack-screen-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-10.png?width=670&height=375&name=pack-screen-10.png)

#### Packing an Order with Carrier Connections

This functionality is currently rolling out and may not be available on your account yet

Ensure you have [Carrier Connections](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-carrier-connections) set up. Please see here for more details.

Carrier Connections are used directly within the Pack Screen, allowing you to view and select freight options during the packing process. Within the Shipping Rate window on the Pack Screen, you can:

- Compare live shipping rates
- Select a carrier and service
- Book freight
- Print shipping labels

Following the same steps as above (with or without scanning), once you have packed the order the available shipping rates and carriers will appear under the Shipping Rate window. The rate that is auto-selected is determined by the Carrier Selection Rules.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Apr-22-2026-05-34-31-4111-AM.png?width=670&height=323&name=image-png-Apr-22-2026-05-34-31-4111-AM.png)

### Additional Pack Screen Features

- **Gross weight is used:** When available, Product UOM Gross Weight is used in Consignment Item Weight calculations. (Note: Directly Shippable Products always use Gross Weight and will not fall back to using Product Weight)
- **Directly Shippable Products**: Products Unit of Measure flagged as “directly shippable” will auto-create consignment items with weight and dimensions from product data (e.g. TVs, cartons). See [Directly Shippable Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Directly-Shippable-Products) for more information.
- **Transport Product weight toggle:** The Pack Screen includes a toggle to exclude Transport Product Weight from automatic item weight calculations. This toggle is enabled by default for directly shippable products
- **Product UOM weight visibility:** The Pack Screen displays the weight of the UOM being packed, making it easier to identify missing or incorrect product master data.
- **Weight calculation visibility:** A help pop-up explains how weights were automatically calculated
- **Workflow controls:** Pin/Lock/Unlock buttons let you adjust Pack Screen behaviour to suit various workflows and prevent accidentally packing additional items into directly shippable consignment items
- **Auto-generated item visibility:** Toggle the visibility of auto-generated consignment items directly within the Pack Screen (in addition to existing organisation and customer-level settings)
- Pack Screen Photo Capture: capture photos directly from the Pack Screen, allowing you to record exactly what was packed into each Consignment Item before sealing.

### Auto Pack / Bypass Pack Workflows

These workflows exist to ensure that every Sale Order Product (SOP) is packed to a consignment item before an order is marked as Packed. This is a system requirement: items must exist on a consignment for them to appear on pack lists and for fulfilment data to be reported back to connected systems (e.g. storefronts).

When Auto-generated consignment items are not configured — or no mapping rules exist — SOPs have no item to pack themselves to. In these cases, CartonCloud provides two automatic fallback behaviours that allow customers to bypass the physical packing process while still satisfying this requirement:

**Auto Packing (no items exist):** If an order is marked as Packed and no consignment items have been created, CartonCloud automatically generates a single "blank" item and packs all SOPs into it. Fields such as weight, dimensions, and transport product are left empty by default. This ensures every consignment has at least one item, even when packing is skipped entirely. *(Note: This workflow cannot be used with carrier integrations as item dimensions are not present. Note also that an upcoming release will auto-set the weight of this blank item.)*

**Auto Packing with Auto-generated Consignment Items:** If one or more consignment items have already been created, any unpacked SOPs automatically pack themselves to the first available item. This mirrors the mobile packing workflow without requiring manual packing steps, and leaves item dimensions and weight unchanged. This workflow is suitable for use with carrier integrations, as item dimensions can be configured via the auto-generation settings.

### Video Tutorial

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/6mn2UUlmKGc

### How to Use the Pack Screen with Different Picking Workflows

The Pack Screen is designed to work with various workflows, providing flexibility in how you pack orders. The CartonCloud workflows below work in conjunction with the Pack Screen:

**Note:** these workflows are only possible with Warehouse Fulfilments turned on.

- [Pick to Tote](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Pick-to-Tote): Totes can be scanned or entered manually to bring up the associated order for packing.
- [Single Orders](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Packing-a-Sale-Order-on-the-web-app): If picking and packing via the web app, you will be automatically taken to the Pack Screen for the packing step. If you are picking via the mobile app, or picking off paper, within the Pack Screen, you can search for and pack individual orders by scanning or typing the order’s UUID, Numeric ID or Customer Reference. If you have a printed Pick List, the barcode on the Pick List can be scanned.
- [Split Pick and Pack Waves:](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Wave-Pick-Process-Types) Orders that have been picked in a Split Pick and Pack Wave can be packed via the Pack Screen. The Pack Screen can be accessed either by searching for the order on the Pack Screen page or by using the Pack Order button on each order within the Wave.

### Scanning Capabilities

The Pack Screen is designed to be used in conjunction with a scanner to enable a more efficient and seamless workflow.

The Pack Screen’s search box allows you to search for a Sale Order by scanning or entering one of the following:

- Numeric ID (the barcode is displayed on the printed Pick List, this is set up by default)
- Customer Reference
- Tote Barcode
- Sale Order UUID

In addition, there are a number of other barcodes that can be used to complete various steps during the packing process:

| **Type** | **Barcode action** | **How to set up the barcode** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Transport Products | By scanning a Transport Product’s barcode, a new Consignment Item of that type is automatically added and populated with the corresponding dimensions and descriptions. | Transport Product barcodes are set up against the Transport Product. See [Setting up Transport Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-Transport-Products) for more information. |
| Products | By scanning a product’s barcode, you can pack a specific quantity of that product to the selected Consignment Item. | Product barcodes are set up against the Product and Product Unit of Measure. See [Add a Product](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-a-Product)and [Products Unit of Measure](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Products-Units-of-Measure)for more information. |
| Action Barcodes | CartonCloud features several action barcodes that can be used to complete packing and print labels. | It is recommended that the following action barcodes be printed and placed at the packing station. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hubfs/Knowledge%20Base%20Files/Action%20Barcodes%20(1).pdf) for a printer-friendly version.    Complete Packing - CCACT001   Complete Packing and Print Labels - CCACT002   *Note: if Packing is already completed, this will trigger a reprint of labels.*     Unlock consignment item - CCACT004   Lock consignment item - CCACT005   Pin consignment item - CCACT003  Take a photo - CCACT006 Print packing slip - Aggregated (whole order) - CCACT008  Print packing slip — Per Item (whole order) - CCACT009 |

#### Transport Products for Scanning

When you scan a Transport Product barcode in the Pack Screen, a new Consignment Item is created automatically. The product code, description, weight and dimensions are pre-filled, making the packing process faster and more accurate.

To use scanning workflows effectively:

- Set up Transport Products for commonly used packaging (e.g. boxes, satchels).
- Assign a unique barcode to each Transport Product.
- Follow the setup instructions [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-Transport-Products).

### Pack Screen Photo Capture

Pack Screen Photo Capture allows you to capture photos directly from the Pack Screen, allowing you to record exactly what was packed into each Consignment Item before sealing. This helps improve accuracy, accountability, and traceability.

Photos can be triggered using a barcode (CCACT006) or the Photo button on the Pack Screen page. Photos are automatically saved against the Sale Order as Packing Confirmation documents.

**Recommended Setup:**

- Use a USB camera mounted on an arm that sits above the packing station.

![pack-screen-camera-arm.png](https://cartoncloud.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1344831554/pack-screen-camera-arm.png?version=1&modificationDate=1773904736210&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=760&height=384)
- Position the camera to clearly capture the contents of each carton and what has been packed.
- Use the action barcode to trigger photo capture hands-free.

**How to take photos on the Pack Screen:**

- During packing, when a Consignment Item is selected, scan the barcode CCACT006 or click the Take Photo button.
- The image will be captured instantly using the connected camera and attached to the current Consignment Item.
- Repeat the process to take multiple photos for the same item if required.

**How photos are stored**

- Photos are saved as Packing Confirmation documents .
- They are attached to the relevant Sale Order.
- Each image is:
  - Linked to the specific item it was captured against.
  - Named using the item's label for easy identification.
- Photo visibility is controlled via Organisation Settings here .

### Recommended Packing Station Setup

For an efficient packing workflow, it is recommended that the packing station setup include:

- **A computer monitor (min: 21”, ideal:27”):** A larger screen provides a clear view of all the order details, products, and packages, reducing eye strain and the need to scroll.
- **A small mini PC:**A compact computer can be mounted directly behind the monitor to save space on your packing bench.
- **A USB barcode scanner (wired or wireless):** This is essential for quickly scanning Transport Products and Sale Order Products to ensure accuracy and speed up the packing process. A wireless scanner offers greater freedom of movement around the packing station.
- **A label printer:**A dedicated label printer is crucial for printing consignment labels, which are generated through the Pack Screen to finalise the fulfilment process.
- **A keyboard and mouse:** While the packing process is designed to be performed through the use of a barcode scanner, a keyboard and mouse are required for other parts of the CartonCloud application (and currently needed to enter package weights).
- **Digital Scales:**Scales are essential for entering the correct package weights. *Support for USB-connected scales will be available in a future update. See [here](https://www.printnode.com/en/docs/supported-scales) for a list of supported digitial scales.*

*![pack-screen-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pack-screen-11.png?width=434&height=413&name=pack-screen-11.png)*

### Printing a Packing Slip from the Pack Screen

The Pack Screen allows you to print or download a packing slip directly while packing a Sale Order. This means you can generate packing documentation without needing to return to the Sale Order screen.

CartonCloud provides two customisable document templates for packing slips, available at the organisation and customer level under

Document Templates

.

| **Template** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| [Sale Order Packing Slip (Aggregated)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/document-template-placeholders-sale-order-packing-slip) | The original packing slip template. Displays all items from the whole Sale Order in a single file. If the order spans multiple consignments, each consignment's items are repeated within the document. |
| [Sale Order Packing Slip Per Item](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/document-template-placeholders-sale-order-packing-slip-0) | A new template that renders once for each consignment item. All rendered pages are combined into a single PDF before being sent to the printer or downloaded. Ideal for printing a slip per carton or box. |

**To print or download a packing slip for the entire order from the Pack Screen:**

- [if !supportLists] [endif] Navigate to the Pack Screen for the relevant Sale Order.
- [if !supportLists] [endif] Click Print Packing Slip .
- Select Download or Print :
  - Download - saves the Packing Slip as a PDF to your device.
  - Print - sends the Packing Slip to your configured printer that can be seen in your Print Log .
- Select either Download (Aggregated) or Download (Per Item) depending on the format you require.

**To print or download a packing slip for a single item as you pack:**

- On the Pack Screen, locate the consignment item you have just packed.
- Click the Print button next to that item.
- [if !supportLists] [endif] Select Download or Print to generate the packing slip for that item only.

Packing slips are formatted for A4 paper. Routing them to a label printer (e.g. a Zebra printer) may produce unexpected results, as label printers interpret page sizes differently. It is recommended to use a standard A4 printer for packing slips.

**Using action barcodes to trigger printing:**

CartonCloud supports action barcodes that can trigger packing slip printing directly from a barcode scan — removing the need to interact with a mouse or keyboard.

There are three action barcodes available for packing slips:

| **Barcode** | **Action** |
| --- | --- |
| CCACT008 | Print packing slip — Aggregated (whole order) |
| CCACT009 | Print packing slip — Per Item (whole order) |
| CCACT010 | Print packing slip for currently focused item |

Action barcodes are available for printing only - not for downloading.

### Known Limitations

There are current limitations with the Pack Screen that will be addressed in future updates. The current limitations include:

- **Custom Field Verification**
  - The Pack Screen currently does not prompt for verification of custom fields such as batch, expiry or lot.
  - If the order was picked via the “Picking” mode on the mobile app, then the custom fields would have been verified at the point of picking.
  - Orders picked via Pick to Tote or Split Pick and Pack Waves will not have verification performed at the time of picking.
  - If strict custom field verification is required, please use the picking mode on the mobile (rather than wave picking).
- **Custom Field Capture**
  - The Pack Screen currently cannot capture custom fields such as serial numbers or MAC addresses. Orders requiring this will display an error.
  - If the order was picked via the “Picking” mode on the mobile app, then the custom fields would have been captured at the point of picking, allowing them to be packed with the Pack Screen.
  - If the order was picked via either Pick to Tote or Split Pick and Pack Waves, no capture would have been performed at the time of picking. It is recommended to use the mobile app’s pick mode to capture the data before packing via the Pack Screen.

Future updates will add both verification and capture capabilities.

### Enhancements Coming Soon

Several improvements to the Pack Screen are coming soon:

- **Adhoc Charges**: Add adhoc charges directly from the Pack Screen, including via barcode scanning.
- **USB Connected Scales**: Capture actual package weight via USB-connected scales.

---

<a id="packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app"></a>
## Packing a Sale Order (on the web app)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to pack a Sale Order

### Purpose

To pack a Sale Order using the web application.

Depending on your operations, you may choose to use the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) to pack your orders. If you would like to use the Pack Screen, please see [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) for set-up instructions.

### Prerequisites

To pack a Sale Order, the order must be in the [***Awaiting Pick and Pack***](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Sale-Orders) status. If the order is still in draft status, you will not be able to pack the order.

To approve the Sale Order and move it into Awaiting Pick and Pack status, select the green **Approve** button from the View Sale Order>Details page. For more information on this process, please see the [Sale Order page](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Sale-Orders).

### How to pack a Sale Order

- Navigate to the Sale Orders page by typing Sale Orders into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Awaiting Pick and Pack tab.

![packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-0.png?width=670&height=189&name=packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-0.png)

- Select the Sale Order to pack.
- Within the Details tab, select the green button Pack Sale Order.

Tip: Alternatively, you can select the green drop-down arrow and click Complete Packing. This will skip the input quantity being packed stage and move straight to 'Packed'. This is useful if you have already completed the packing in the warehouse and are updating your records in CartonCloud.

![packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-1.png?width=670&height=197&name=packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-1.png)

- Enter the quantity to pack by either typing in the number or using the arrow keys within the quantity box.

Tip: If you wish to generate an SSCC at this stage of packing the Sale Order, please see the [Enabling and using SSCC/GS1 Labels](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Enabling-and-using-SSCC-GS1-Labels)page. SSCC is a paid feature and to enable this feature you will need to reach out to the [CartonCloud team](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2).

- Click Finished Packing at the bottom of the screen.

![packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-2.png?width=670&height=214&name=packing-a-sale-order-on-the-web-app-2.png)

- You will then have the option to print labels.

Tip: See [Label Printing](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Label-Printing) for information on how to configure label printing with CartonCloud.

- If the default settings are on, the Sale Order will move straight to the Dispatched status. To change these settings, see Automatically updating Sale Orders to Dispatched .

In the below video, it is assumed you are also using CartonCloud Transport Management System (TMS) and, therefore, are generating Consignments from the Sale Orders.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/zyQHnf7e0Eg

<a id="photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders"></a>
## Photos and Documents on Sale Orders

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Overview
- Workflows
- Use Cases / Benefits
- The difference between Documents Essentials and Advanced

### Purpose

Documents allows mobile and web app users to attach photos, videos and documents to Sale Orders as they are picked and packed for dispatch.

### Overview

- A Document has attachments and attachments can be videos, photos or other documents (ie: PDF).
- Documents have two different visibility options:
  - Internal only: no customer access. Admins and packers can edit.
  - Shared with customer: customer can view. Admins and packers can edit.
  - A default visibility option can be selected from the Organisation Settings. More information [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Organisation-Settings-Warehouse-Order-Documents).
- Documents are split into two tiers, Essentials (available in all WMS plans), and Advanced (available through Warehouse Premium). All accounts are able to trial Advanced Documents for free until June 2026. After this, only accounts with [WMS Premium](https://cartoncloudorg.lightning.force.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) will maintain Advanced Documents and all other accounts will switch to Essentials Documents.
- Capture and upload photos when picking on the mobile or from your device’s photo library.
- Users can add and edit Documents on the web app but only add (not edit) on the mobile app.
- If you would like your Customer to be notified when Documents are uploaded against a Sale Order ensure they are set up with Sale Order Packed notification. These notifications will include Documents if they have been uploaded and are a Shared with Customer visibility level. See [Customer Settings - Email (Notifications)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Email-Notifications) for more information and the below notification example.

![photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-0.png?width=500&height=351&name=photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-0.png)

### Workflows

- [Photos and Documents on Sale Orders (mobile app)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Photos-and-Documents-on-Sale-Orders-mobile-app) - add Documents upon picking stock in the warehouse via the mobile app.
- [Photos and Documents on Sale Orders (web app)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Photos-and-Documents-on-Sale-Orders-web-app) - add Documents to the Sale Order at any stage in the order process (any status) from the web app.

### Use Cases / Benefits

- Provide photo evidence to your customers of what has been packed in the Sale Order. This is useful if the person receiving the order claims certain products were not included.
- To verify packing requirements with photo evidence. This is helpful if your customer requires orders packed a certain way.
- Provide greater transparency and updates to your customers on their orders.
- Customers can view Documents from their CartonCloud login as long as the Document visibility is set to **Shared with Customer**.
- Reduce communication between you and your customer by uploading images and files directly to the Sale Order for them to view.

### The difference between Documents Essentials and Advanced

Advanced Documents provides additional capability for higher resolution images, significantly increases the number of attachments per document, provides additional storage capacity and adds other timesaving enhancements.

Advanced Documents is a paid add-on available with [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium). For more information on WMS Premium and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

The detailed differences between the two are outlined below:

| **Essentials Documents** | **Advanced Documents** |
| --- | --- |
| Max 6 images per Document | Max 100 images per Document |
| Images are always compressed (POD resolution ~700 kb/image) | Default to full-resolution Compression options available via settings |
| Max attachment size 1mb | Max attachment size 500mb |
|  | Video support  Multi-photo mode |
| Deleted Documents and attachments cannot be restored | Deleted Documents and attachments can be viewed and restored by non-customer roles (coming soon) |
| 10gb included storage | 100gb included storage |
|  | Image Metadata - date, time and location Information (where available) |

---

<a id="photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app"></a>
## Photos and Documents on Sale Orders (web app)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use Cases / Benefits
- Process
- Editing or deleting a Document
- Document History
- Image Metadata

### Purpose

The process for creating Documents on Sales Orders on the web app. In addition, how to edit and delete documents via the web app.

Note, Documents can only be edited via the web app not the mobile app.

### Use Cases / Benefits

- Provide greater transparency and updates to your customers on their orders.
- Customers can view Documents from their CartonCloud login as long as the Document visibility is set to Shared with Customer.
- Provide greater transparency internally with Document visibility on orders and the history of who uploaded the Document and attachment.
- If you wish to take photos and record them against the Sale Order you can do so by taking a photo on the warehouse floor and uploading it on the web app.
- Reduce communication between you and your customer by uploading images and files directly to the Sale Order for them to view.

### Process

Documents can be created on Sale Orders at any stage through the order process. The Sale Order can be in any status for a Document to be created. To create a Document on a Sale Order:

- Navigate to the relevant Sale Order, **Warehouse** > **Sale Orders**.
- Select the **Documents** tab. If there is already a Document against the Sale Order you will see the number of Documents next to the tab title.

![photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-0.png?width=670&height=330&name=photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-0.png)

- Select the **+Add Document** button.

![photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-1.png?width=670&height=327&name=photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-1.png)

- Select the **Name** for the Document from the drop-down. Note that names are not customisable, however, they will be in the future.
  - **Packing Confirmation:** use this Name when confirming the packed order. For example, taking a photo of the packaging to confirm the order has been packed to the customer’s specifications.
  - **Other:**for anything other than Photos and Documents relating to packing confirmation.
- Enter information related to the Document within the Description text box. This will be visible to anyone who has access to the Document.
- Select the visibility option: (a default visibility option can be selected from the Organisation Settings. More information [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/organisation-settings-warehouse-order-documents))
  - **Internal only:** only internal users of your CartonCloud account will be able to see the Document. This includes all User types apart from Customers. Only Admin and Packers can edit the Document (Documents can only be edited via the web app).
  - **Shared with Customer:**all user types in your CartonCloud account including Customers can see the Document. Only Admin and Packers can edit the Document (Documents can only be edited via the web app).
- Add attachments by selecting **Choose files** or utilise the drag and drop feature to upload the file.

![photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-2.png?width=670&height=331&name=photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-2.png)

- Select the files you wish to upload and select **Save**.

![photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-3.png?width=670&height=340&name=photos-and-documents-on-sale-orders-web-app-3.png)

- The Document will now be visible against the Sale Order.

### Editing or deleting a Document

Once a Document is uploaded you can edit it to make changes, remove or add attachments and delete the Document. Note that Documents can only be edited via the web app.

**To edit a Document:**

- Select the Document and you will be in edit mode.
- Make any required changes and select **Save**.

**To delete a Document:**

- Select the Document you wish to delete to enter edit mode.

Scroll down and select the **red bin icon**.

### Document History

To access the Document history:

- Select the Document you wish to view the history for.
- Scroll down and select the **History** button.
- You will now be able to see history related to the Document.

### Image Metadata

Image Metadata is only included in [Advanced Documents](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-documents). See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/wms-premium) for more information. Note: All accounts are able to trial Advanced Documents for free until June 2026. After this, only accounts with [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/wms-premium) will maintain Advanced Documents and all other accounts will switch to Essentials Documents.

When uploading an image to a Document on the web app, if date, time and location Metadata is available it will show against the file. This can be useful as it provides the exact location and date/time the image was taken.

Considerations for Metadata to be available:

- Only file types of images are able to store metadata. For example, a video will not show metadata.
- At present, only files uploaded via the web app can show metadata. Images uploaded from the mobile app will not provide metadata. This is coming soon in an app update.
- Only certain devices record metadata within an image and metadata is often removed when images are compressed (eg: images shared via WhatsApp generally get compressed and have location metadata removed).

**How to access Metadata:**

- Against the relevant Sale Order, select the **Documents**tab.
- Select the relevant Document.
- Select the relevant attachment.
- Click **Show Metadata**.

<a id="pick-tolerance"></a>
## Pick Tolerance

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pick-tolerance_

### Table of Contents

- What is pick tolerance
- How to set the pick tolerance
- Benefits of using pick tolerance with products

### What is pick tolerance

If you have [Random Weight](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Variable-Weight-Packing) set up against a Product, the weight of each unit being picked will need to be recorded. For example, when packing cartons of meat, each carton is a slightly different weight and the customer charges per kilogram; therefore, you need to record the weight when picking the product.

With Random Weight enabled for a product, you can select a **Pick Tolerance**. This is a percentage of tolerance for the weight being picked. The acceptable tolerance is between the weight being picked and the weight requested on the Sale Order. For example, if the Sale Order says 3kg of Pork Strips and you have a Pick Tolerance of 10%, the picker can pick between 2.7 - 3.3 kgs, as that is 10% less or more than what has been requested against the order.

### How to set the pick tolerance

The Pick Tolerance is set up against the Customer; therefore, you can have different pick tolerances for each customer.

**To set a Pick Tolerance:**

- Navigate to the Customers page, Users > Customers .
- Select the Customer you wish to set a Pick Tolerance for.
- Scroll down to the bottom of the page and click Edit against the Customer.

![pick-tolerance-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pick-tolerance-0.png?width=670&height=165&name=pick-tolerance-0.png)

- Select the Warehouse Management tab and then the Sale Order tab.

![pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-1.png?width=670&height=222&name=pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-1.png)

- Scroll down to Random Weight Products and enter the Pick Tolerance percentage.

- Select Save .

![pick-tolerance-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pick-tolerance-2.png?width=670&height=318&name=pick-tolerance-2.png)

### Benefits of using pick tolerance with random weight products

- Provides guidelines for your pickers who are picking Random Weight Products
- Able to better meet customer expectations by ensuring pickers are picking within the correct weight ranges
- It gives your customer the option of having a pick tolerance and what the tolerance is
- Allows you to set customer expectations on how orders will be picked
- Reduces the time picking the product as pickers do not need to pick by an exact amount but rather just within the pick tolerance

---

<a id="picking-sale-orders-per-run-sheet"></a>
## Picking Sale Orders per Run Sheet

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/picking-sale-orders-per-run-sheet_

If you need to pick orders on a per-run basis or have drivers picking their own stock prior to leaving the warehouse, you can generate a Pick Sheet from a Run Sheet. Doing this requires you to allocate the Consignments associated with Sale Orders to a Run Sheet, then produce a Pick Sheet from the Run Sheet.

Alternatively, if you have multiple Sale Orders to pick for a Run Sheet we recommend using [Wave Picking by Run Sheet](https://help.cartoncloud.com/kb2/web-app-page-specific-support/administrator-pages/warehouse/sale-orders/wave-picking#WavePicking-CreatingaWavePickforaspecificRunSheet).

<a id="printing-sale-order-customer-invoices-documents"></a>
## Printing Sale Order Customer Invoices / Documents

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/printing-sale-order-customer-invoices-documents_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps
  - Option 1: download all invoices ready to print
  - Option 2: choose selected sale orders with invoices to print

### Purpose

This guide explains how to print Customer Invoices or Documents that are saved on a Sale Order within the Customer Invoices tab. These documents are typically handed to the driver or carrier with the goods at the time of collection.

### How to steps

There are several ways of doing this. All ways first require navigating to the Sale Orders page.

- To navigate to the Sale Order page, select Warehouse in the main menu, then Sale Orders from the drop-down.

#### **Option 1: Download all Invoices ready to print**

- First, ensure the Sale Orders that you wish to print Invoices for are already packed, and therefore have a current status of 'Packed'
- From the Sale Orders page, select **Download/Export**then in the drop-down select **Download All Invoices Ready to Print**
- A box will appear on the screen letting you know how many invoices are available. To proceed, select **Download.**
- The invoices will be downloaded through your web browser as a single PDF file
- Then, choose whether to Mark invoices as printed or not. (If you have the setting **[Automatically updating Sale Orders to Dispatched turned on](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Automatically+updating+Sale+Orders+to+Dispatched)**, this will result in the status of the Sale Order updating to 'Dispatched')
- You can now open the downloaded PDF File to print all the invoices that were ready

#### **Option 2: Choose selected Sale Orders with Invoices to print**

- Unlike Option 1, Sale Orders can be in ANY Status for this method to work
- From the Sale Orders page, select the Sale Orders you wish to print Customer Invoices for. To select Sale Orders, tick the box on the left of their line
- Optionally, use the Filter tab, or Invoice Ready to Print tab to easily locate the Sale Orders you may be looking for, then select them.
- Once the Sale Orders are selected, select **Download/Export** then in the drop-down select Download Selected Invoices
- The invoices will be downloaded through your web browser as a single PDF file
- Then, choose whether to Mark invoices as printed or not. (If you have the setting **[Automatically updating Sale Orders to Dispatched turned on](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Automatically+updating+Sale+Orders+to+Dispatched)**, this will result in the status of the Sale Order updating to 'Dispatched')
- You can now open the downloaded PDF File to print all the selected invoices

<a id="rejected-sale-orders"></a>
## Rejected Sale Orders

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/rejected-sale-orders_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Resolving rejected sale orders
- Resolving 'Product not found' error

### Purpose

When a Sale Order fails to successfully import into CartonCloud the order will move to a rejected status. The status of 'Rejected' will be visible in the status column on the Sale Orders page.

![rejected-sale-orders-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/rejected-sale-orders-0.png?width=670&height=144&name=rejected-sale-orders-0.png)

When an order is rejected, there will be an error reason for why the order failed. For example, there could be insufficient stock quantities, the product could not be found (product doesn't exist in CartonCloud) or there is no stock that matches the required expiry date. To view this error, you will need to select the relevant Sale Order and navigate to the errors tab (see [View Sale Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/BAHeHw)).

![rejected-sale-orders-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/rejected-sale-orders-1.png?width=670&height=115&name=rejected-sale-orders-1.png)

The way CartonCloud determines if a Sale Order should be rejected can be configured in the Customer Settings. For example, if the Sale Order imported has products with insufficient stock you can choose to reject the entire Sale Order or only the product lines that have insufficient stock. See [Edit Customer or Customer Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/customer-settings-basics) for more information.

The below video explains what a rejected Sale Order is and how to manage it.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/px1m3aeUzXY

### Resolving rejected Sale Orders

How to resolve a rejected Sale Order will depend upon the error type that prevented the Sale Order data from importing successfully. Some errors require manual intervention whilst others are more straightforward and can be re-processed once all conditions are met.

For example, if there is insufficient stock available the order will move to a rejected status and can be re-processed once the stock becomes available (see [Reprocessing rejected Sale Orders in Bulk](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk)). On the other hand, some errors, such as '**Product not found**' will require changes to be made before they can be re-processed. This prevents the re-processing of incorrect Sale Order data.

### Resolving 'Product not found' error

If you receive this error message when attempting to import a Sale Order, it means that CartonCloud could not find a match for some or all of the requested products. This could be because the product does not exist in CartonCloud or there was an error with the Product Code (SKU) data (e.g spelling mistake).

To resolve this error message follow the below steps:

- Via the Import Log , check that there are no spelling errors for the Product Code (SKU) on the Sale Order.
- If there are no errors on the Product Code, create a new product within CartonCloud (see Add a Product ).
- Add the product to the Sale Order with the required quantities.
- Mark the error as resolved within the Sale Order errors tab.
- The Sale Order can now be re-processed once stock is available.

---

<a id="reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk"></a>
## Reprocessing rejected Sale Orders in Bulk

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps
- Sale orders failing to reprocess
- Excluded sale orders from bulk re-processing

### Purpose

If a Sale Order is imported into CartonCloud but there is insufficient stock available to fulfill the order then the Sale Order will be rejected and its status updated accordingly. On large imports, this can sometimes result in many rejected Sale Orders sitting in the system, where they remain until the relevant stock is loaded in by a Purchase Order, or they are canceled entirely.

Once the stock is available, then the Sale Orders will need to be reprocessed. This article will cover how to easily reprocess rejected Sale Orders with just a few clicks.

There are different errors that can occur that prevent a Sale Order from importing successfully. Some errors, such as 'Product not found' require manual intervention and will be excluded from the bulk re-processing until the error is fixed. This prevents the re-processing of incorrect Sale Order data. For more information see [Excluded Sale Order errors from bulk re-processing.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Reprocessing+rejected+Sale+Orders+in+Bulk#ReprocessingrejectedSaleOrdersinBulk-product)

### How to steps

- From the main menu, select Warehouse > Sale Orders
- Now on the Sale Orders page, select the Filter tab.
- Apply the appropriate filters so that the system is only searching for orders that you wish to reprocess. Alternatively, not selecting any filters will show all results, meaning all orders in the "Rejected" status will be reprocessed.
- Select Go! and the Sale Orders will appear on the page.

![reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-0.png?width=670&height=470&name=reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-0.png)

- In the scenario above, a filter has been applied to only show orders for the customer "ABC Pty Ltd" and with the "Rejected" status type. This will restrict the system to only reprocessing orders for that specific customer "ABC Pty Ltd".

It is not necessary to filter by the Rejected status type, as reprocessing will only ever be attempted on these orders, however, it does allow the user to more easily see which orders are about to be reprocessed.

- Once filters have been applied. Click the Select All button and all Sale Orders on the page will be highlighted.
- A new button will then appear on the screen to re-process the orders. Select it.
- A confirmation box will appear on the screen as shown below. This explains what the system is about to do when reprocessing the orders, so read it carefully.

![reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-1.png?width=516&height=372&name=reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-1.png)

The order in which Sale Orders are reprocessed is by the date they were created.

- Provided you wish to proceed with reprocessing. Select OK.
- On success, a banner will appear at the top of the page.
- The result of the reprocess can then be viewed once completed by selecting the bell icon at the top right of the page.

### Sale Orders failing to reprocess

If there are Sale Orders which have failed to reprocess, then there is still likely not enough stock available to fulfil those order.

To get further detail on why an order failed, select it from the Sale Order page > then navigate to the **Errors** tab. A message will appear describing why that order failed.

![reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-2.png?width=670&height=185&name=reprocessing-rejected-sale-orders-in-bulk-2.png)
In the example above, the order contained 54 units of a product called "vcb", but only 14 are available. Therefore it was rejected by the system.

### Excluded Sale Order errors from bulk re-processing

When importing a Sale Order into CartonCloud there are different errors that can occur that prevent the data importing successfully. As mentioned above, when these errors do occur, such as insufficient stock, the order can be re-processed once the stock becomes available. However, some errors require manual intervention before they can be re-processed, such as if the product type is not found in CartonCloud when the Sale Order is imported. If this does occur an error message on the Sale Order will appear as **'Product not found'**. This means the product does not exist in CartonCloud and before it can be re-processed the product needs to be created.

To resolve this error message follow the below steps:

- Via the Import Log , check that there are no spelling errors for the Product Code (SKU) on the Sale Order.
- If there are no errors on the Product Code, create a new product within CartonCloud (see Add a Product ).
- Add the product to the Sale Order with the required quantities.
- Mark the error as resolved within the Sale Order errors tab.
- The Sale Order can now be re-processed once stock is available.

---

<a id="returning-stock-after-it-s-already-dispatched"></a>
## Returning Stock after it's already dispatched

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/returning-stock-after-it-s-already-dispatched_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- Benefits
- Use Cases
- Steps
- Video overview

### Purpose

This article explains how to return previously dispatched goods back into the warehouse using the **Return To Stock (RTS)** process. This is done by creating a linked **Purchase Order** from a completed **Sale Order**, allowing returned stock to be received and tracked correctly in your warehouse system.

### Prerequisites

Before following this process:

- The goods must have already been dispatched from the warehouse via a completed **Sale Order**.
- You must have appropriate user permissions to view and create **Sale Orders** and **Purchase Orders**.
- The product(s) being returned must be part of the original Sale Order.

### Benefits

- Accurately returns goods to available stock levels in CartonCloud.
- Ensures clear traceability by linking the return to the original Sale Order.
- Allows you to reprocess or redeliver returned goods using the same product data.

### Use Cases

Use this process when:

- Goods have been delivered but rejected by the customer.
- A driver has returned undelivered items.
- Stock was sent in error and needs to be returned to inventory.

### Steps

- Navigate to Warehouse > Sale Orders.
- Search for the relevant order.
- Open the dispatched Sale Order.
- Click Create RTS Purchase Order at the top of the Sale Order page.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-14-2025-12-10-31-4688-AM.png?width=670&height=304&name=image-png-Nov-14-2025-12-10-31-4688-AM.png)

- A new Purchase Order will be generated, with a reference formatted as: Original Sale Order Reference + "-RTS" (e.g. SO-12345-RTS)
- The returned Purchase Order will automatically include all products from the original Sale Order.
- If needed, adjust the product quantities or remove any lines not being returned.
- Receive the returned goods using the standard Purchase Order receipting process.
- If the returned goods need to be sent out again, you can duplicate the original Sale Order.

### Video overview

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/U0jUsdAm_w4

---

<a id="sale-orders"></a>
## Sale Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sale-orders_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Sale Order
- How to create a Sale Order
- Sale Order process flow in CartonCloud
  - Draft
  - Awaiting pick and pack
  - Packing in progress
  - Picking in Progress
  - Picked
  - Packed
  - Dispatched
  - Rejected
- Sale Order list view

### What is a Sale Order

When stock leaves your warehouse, a Sale Order is the document's name, which records that stock's movement within CartonCloud.

### How to create a Sale Order

A Sale Order can be created by:

- By yourself [manually in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-a-sale-order).
- By your [Customers in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer) through their login.
- Automatically by Parsers .

### Sale Order Process Flow in CartonCloud

The diagram below steps through the Sale Order Process and the different statuses a Sale Order will move through in CartonCloud.

![sale-orders-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-orders-0.png?width=670&height=252&name=sale-orders-0.png)

If [Warehouse Fulfilments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments) are enabled, the Sale Order will move through different statuses to complement the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) workflow:

![sale-orders-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-orders-1.png?width=670&height=227&name=sale-orders-1.png)

**Draft**

The Sale Order has been created but is not yet approved. To be able to approve the Sale Order, products must be associated with the order. To move the status to **Awaiting Pick and Pack,** the order must be approved, and this needs to be done manually within the Sale Order. This status is only applicable for Sale Orders that have been entered manually.

To approve the Sale Order and move it to Awaiting Pick and Pack status:

- Select the green **Approve** button from the **View Sale Order**> **Details** page.

![sale-orders-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-orders-2.png?width=670&height=247&name=sale-orders-2.png)

**Awaiting Pick and Pack**

The order has been approved, is now visible to warehouse staff, and is ready to be picked and packed. To begin packing the Sale Order, you must click **Pack Sale Order**.

**Packing in Progress**

The order is currently being packed.

**Picking in Progress (Warehouse Fulfilments enabled only status)**

The order is currently being picked.

**Picked (Warehouse Fulfilments enabled only status)**

The order has been picked.

**Packed**

The order has been packed and is ready to be dispatched. By default, this status is turned off so that when a Sale Order is packed, it will move straight from Awaiting Pick and Pack to Dispatched. To enable this status and manually move the order to Dispatched, you will need to configure this in the Customer Settings (see [Automatically updating Sale Orders to Dispatched](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/automatically-updating-sale-orders-to-dispatched)).

**Dispatched**

The Sale Order has been dispatched, and the Sale Order Warehouse process is now complete. If you have the CartonCloud Transport Management System and the correct setting is configured, the Sale Order will automatically create a Consignment, and the transport component of the process can begin (see [Generating a Consignment from a Sale Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/generating-a-consignment-from-a-sale-order)).

**Rejected**

When a Sale Order fails to import into CartonCloud. See [Rejected Sale Orders](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/rejected-sale-orders) for more information.

### Sale Order List View

From the Sale Order List View, you can filter orders using the filter tab or use the pre-defined status filter tabs such as 'Awaiting Pick and Pack' to show all orders in the status of Awaiting Pick and Pack.

In addition, you can use the action buttons at the top to perform tasks on individual orders or in bulk. To do so in bulk, select the tick box beside the orders you wish to perform the action on or click Select All.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-13-2025-12-43-29-3872-AM.png?width=670&height=321&name=image-png-Nov-13-2025-12-43-29-3872-AM.png)

| **Button** | **Action** |
| --- | --- |
| Select All | Select all orders on the page. Upon selecting this button you will be asked if you would like to select all orders on other pages as well. |
| Download/Export | Option to either export pick list, packing slip or download all invoices that are ready to print. |
| Mark Packed | Mark the order/s as packed |
| Re-process Orders | Re-process the selected order/s that are rejected. |
| Delete | Delete the order |
| Assign a Packer | To assign a packer to the Sale Order. This will show on the mobile and web app. See [How to assign a packer to a Sale Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-assign-a-packer-to-a-Sale-Order) for more information. |

---

<a id="sale-order-date-fields-explained"></a>
## Sale Order Date Fields Explained

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sale-order-date-fields-explained_

### Table of Contents

- [Purpose](https://help.cartoncloud.com#Purpose)
- [Sale Order Date Fields Explained](https://help.cartoncloud.com#Sale-Order-Date-Fields-Explained)

### Purpose

This guide will provide clarity on the Sale Order Date fields shown on the Sale Order screen and explain the difference between an "Expected" Ship Date and a "Requested" Ship Date.

### Sale Order Date Fields Explained

| **Sale Order Date Field** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- |
| Date Added | This is the date and time that the Sale Order was entered into Carton Cloud |
| Ship Date | This is the expected or requested delivery date of the Sale Order  (Expected) The "Ship Date" is populated using Expected Delivery Runs next delivery date. (Requested) The "Ship Date" is populated using the date specifically requested by the Customer when the Sale Order was entered |
| Date Packed | This is the date and time that the Sale Order was marked Packed in Carton Cloud |
| Date Dispatched | This is the date and time that the Sale Order was marked as Dispatched in Carton Cloud |

---

<a id="-sale-order-packing-slip-customisation"></a>
## Sale Order Packing Slip Customisation

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/-sale-order-packing-slip-customisation_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- When to Use Each Template
- How Each Template Behaves
- How to Set Up and Customise a Template

### Purpose

CartonCloud provides two Sale Order Packing Slip templates that can be printed or downloaded directly from the Pack Screen. Both templates are customisable, but they behave differently depending on how you need your packing documentation structured.

This article explains the difference between the two templates, when to use each one, and how to set them up.

### When to Use Each Template

|  | **Sale Order Packing Slip** | **Sale Order Packing Slip Per Item** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Best for | Orders where one document covering the whole order is sufficient. | Operations where each box or carton needs its own individual slip. |
| Output | One PDF per sale order. | A separate PDF per consignment item, combined into a single document. |
| Example use case | A customer wants a single packing list showing everything that was packed across the whole order. | A warehouse packs multiple cartons per order and needs a separate slip placed inside each one. |

### How Each Template Behaves

#### **Sale Order Packing Slip (Aggregated)**

The Sale Order Packing Slip (Aggregated) displays all items from the whole Sale Order in a single file. If the order spans multiple consignments, each consignment's items are repeated within the document.

For example: if an order has two consignments with two items each, all four items appear in the one PDF.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-58-4929-AM.png?width=670&height=354&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-58-4929-AM.png)

Example Sale Order Packing Slip Template with $BLOCK_CONSIGNMENTS$ and $BLOCK_CONSIGNMENT_ITEMS$ placeholders:

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-59-3483-AM.png?width=670&height=473&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-59-3483-AM.png)
Example Sale Order Packing Slip (Aggregated) Output:

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-57-0559-AM.png?width=670&height=529&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-57-0559-AM.png)

When using `$BLOCK_CONSIGNMENTS$` or `$BLOCK_CONSIGNMENT_ITEMS$` placeholders, only packed stock will appear. If the packing slip is printed before packing is complete, or part way through the packing process, products will not display on the document.

Example Sale Order Packing Slip **without**$BLOCK_CONSIGNMENTS$ placeholders:

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-56-6952-AM.png?width=670&height=357&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-56-6952-AM.png)

Example Sale Order Packing Slip (Aggregated) Output:

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-59-6797-AM.png?width=670&height=417&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-59-6797-AM.png)

#### **Sale Order Packing Slip (Per Item)**

The Sale Order Packing Slip (Per Item) template renders once per consignment item, then stitches all pages together into a single PDF before sending to the printer or making it available for download.

For example: if an order has two consignments with two items each, the template renders four times — one page per consignment item — and the results are combined into a single PDF.

Example of Page 1 of 2:

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-57-7760-AM.png?width=670&height=391&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-57-7760-AM.png)

Example Page 2 of 2:

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-59-0222-AM.png?width=670&height=372&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-59-0222-AM.png)

### How to Set Up and Customise a Template

Both templates are customisable and available at the organisation level and per customer under [Document Templates.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/document-templates)

**To download and customise a template:**

- In the Search for Anything bar, search for "Document Templates". ![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-57-3867-AM.png?width=670&height=134&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-57-3867-AM.png)
- Scroll down to locate Sale Order Packing Slip or Sale Order Packing Slip Per Item . ![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-58-1136-AM.png?width=670&height=134&name=undefined-Jun-12-2026-12-08-58-1136-AM.png)
- Click Download to download the current template.
- Open the template and make your edits using the Sale Order Packing Slip Placeholders . For existing customers,  the Sale Order Pack Slip default template has been left unchanged. If you would like it segmented by consignment item, download the Sale Order Pack Slip (Per-Item) default template and upload it as the Sale Order Pack Slip template.
- Once complete, click Upload next to the relevant template to save your changes.

Templates can be set at the organisation level (applies to all customers) or overridden at the customer level for specific customers. Customer-level templates take priority over organisation-level templates.

---

<a id="sale-order-procedures"></a>
## Sale Order Procedures

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sale-order-procedures_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Sale Order
- How to create a Sale Order
- Sale Order process flow in CartonCloud

### What is a Sale Order

When stock leaves your warehouse, a Sale Order is the name of the document that records that stock's movement within CartonCloud.

### How to create a Sale Order

For information on how to create a Sale Order, please see the [Add a Sale Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/GAaYHw) page.

### Sale Order Process Flow in CartonCloud

The diagram below steps through the Sale Order Process and the different statuses a Sale Order will move through in CartonCloud.

![sale-order-procedures-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-procedures-0.png?width=670&height=252&name=sale-order-procedures-0.png)

If [Warehouse Fulfilments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments) are enabled, the Sale Order will move through different statuses to complement the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) workflow:

![sale-order-procedures-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-procedures-1.png?width=670&height=227&name=sale-order-procedures-1.png)

**Awaiting Pick and Pack**

The order has been approved, is now visible to warehouse staff, and is ready to be picked and packed. To begin packing the Sale Order you must click **Pack Sale Order**.

- For packing a Sale Order through the mobile application see Packing a Sale Order .
- For packing a Sale Order using the web application please see Packing a Sale Order .

**Awaiting Stock**

Products are unassigned and awaiting stock. Please see [Backorder Management](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Backorder-Management) for more information.

**Packing in Progress**

The order is currently being packed.

**Picking in Progress (Warehouse Fulfilments enabled only status)**

The order is currently being picked.

**Picked (Warehouse Fulfilments enabled only status)**

The order has been picked.

**Packed**

The order has been packed and is ready to be dispatched. By default, this status is turned off so that when a Sale Order is packed it will move straight from Awaiting Pick and Pack to Dispatched. To enable this status and manually move the order to Dispatched you will need to configure this in the Customer Settings (see [Automatically updating Sale Orders to Dispatched](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/automatically-updating-sale-orders-to-dispatched)).

**Dispatched**

The Sale Order has been dispatched and the Sale Order Warehouse process is now complete. If you have the CartonCloud Transport Management System and the correct setting is configured the Sale Order will automatically create a Consignment and the transport component of the process can begin (see [Generating a Consignment from a Sale Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/generating-a-consignment-from-a-sale-order)).

**Rejected**

When a Sale Order fails to import into CartonCloud. See [Rejected Sale Orders](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/rejected-sale-orders) for more information.

**To view the Sale Orders' current status**

![sale-order-procedures-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-procedures-2.png?width=670&height=272&name=sale-order-procedures-2.png)

- Navigate to the Sale Orders page by searching **Sale Orders** in the Search for anything bar.
- From the list view, you will be able to see the **Status**column.
- You can also view the status from within the Sale Order itself by selecting the relevant Sale Order and selecting the **Details** tab.

<a id="sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer"></a>
## Sale Orders (Stock Out) as a Customer

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Sale Order
- Benefits of Sale Orders
- How to add a Sale Order
- View Sale Order
- Mark order as urgent

### What is a Sale Order?

A Sale Order is an outbound order with stock leaving the warehouse.

### Benefits of Sale Orders

- Helps to ensure the correct stock is assigned to the outbound order
- Pick and packing accuracy
- Visibility across orders leaving the warehouse
- Allows for automatic email notifications to be sent out for certain events during the order process

### How to add a Sale Order

There a number of different ways a Sale Order can be added to CartonCloud. It is highly recommended that orders are created automatically via a Parser or Integration. If you would like to be set up with a [Parser](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Parsers) or [Integration](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Integration-with-other-Software) please reach out to your CartonCloud account owner (3PL provider) or reach out to the CartonCloud team for more information via CartonCloud Help.

- Navigate to the Sale Orders page, **Warehouse** > **Sale Orders**.
- Click the **+Add Sale Order** button in the top left of the page.

- Enter the order reference, delivery address and attach an invoice if required.
  - **Reference:** this is the reference for the Sale Order (used for searching and appears on the invoice)
  - **Delivery address:** the final delivery address for the order.

- If you click the **Advanced Options** drop down you can add additional data to the order.

![sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-2.png?width=670&height=332&name=sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-2.png)

- **Packing instructions**: special instructions that show up on the packing slip and pick/pack screen.
- **Delivery instructions:** special instructions that get copied into the Consignment Special Instructions (if using the CartonCloud Transport Management System)
- **Sale Order Value:** the value (invoice amount) of the Sale Order
- **Required ship date:**the date that the order should leave the warehouse
- **Required delivery date**: the date that the stock should be delivered.
- Once all of the information has been filled in, click **Add Sale Order**.
- Click **+Add Products to Sale Order**.

- Select the product you wish to add to the order and enter the quantity. Select **Search**.

![sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-4.png?width=670&height=196&name=sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-4.png)

- Enter the quantity against the line of stock you wish to add to the order and click **Take Stock**.

- From the Details tab, you can either approve the order for packing or continue adding products to the order.

- Once the order is approved it will be available to your 3PL / CartonCloud account owner to pick and pack.

### View Sale Order

From the Sale Order page you can click into any order and view the details of the order.

![sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-7.png?width=670&height=291&name=sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-7.png)

You can use the different tabs on the order to navigate to different information relating to the order.

- **Details tab:**basic details surrounding the order
- **Products tab**: details of the stock on the order. List of products and the relevant data for each line of stock.
- **Customer invoices**: any invoices that have been uploaded against the order.
- **Charges:** charges associated with the order and the relevant invoice the order is associated with.
- **Consignments**: if your CartonCloud account owner is also using the TMS system, you may see the associated transport job (Consignment) associated with the Sale Order.
- **Errors:**any errors with the order
- **History**: history of status changes of the order

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/L6iyfHMOSRw

### Making an order Urgent

To mark select the **Make it urgent** button.

![sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-8.png?width=670&height=291&name=sale-orders-stock-out-as-a-customer-8.png)
