<a id="scan-order-tote"></a>
## Scan Order / Tote

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/scan-order-tote_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use Cases
- Prerequisites
- Process

### Purpose

The Scan Order/Tote screen lets users scan a Tote (coming soon) or order barcode to navigate directly to the pack screen for packing. This supports various workflows, including mobile picking with computer packing and wave picking.

### Use Cases

- Allows for an efficient way for packer users to navigate to the pack screen.
- If a user wants to pick on mobile and pack on the computer.
- If a user is using paper pick sheets, they can pick on paper, bring back to the desktop, and pack the order.
- To run Wave Picks.
- In preparation for CartonCloud’s new feature of Pick to Tote this will enable users to quickly navigate to packing orders from a Tote.

### Prerequisites

- The order must be in a status of ‘Packing in Progress’ for it to appear on the Scan Order / Tote screen.
- You need to scan the order barcode. The order barcode is the order id.
- Once CartonCloud’s new feature of Pick to Tote is available, there will be a field called Tote barcode which specifies the Tote has been used and that can be scanned to bring up the associated Sale Order.
- Only available for Sale Orders in the CartonCloud Warehouse module.

### Process

- Navigate to the Scan Order / Tote screen, **Warehouse**> **Scan Order / Tote**.

![scan-order-tote-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/scan-order-tote-0.png?width=670&height=353&name=scan-order-tote-0.png)

- Scan the order barcode (order id) into the input field.

![scan-order-tote-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/scan-order-tote-1.png?width=670&height=353&name=scan-order-tote-1.png)

- You will then be directed to the pack screen for the order you have scanned.

![scan-order-tote-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/scan-order-tote-2.png?width=670&height=353&name=scan-order-tote-2.png)

- You will now be able to pack the order on the web app.

<a id="stock-recall-process-batch-recall"></a>
## Stock Recall Process (Batch Recall)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/stock-recall-process-batch-recall_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Solution - stock movement report

### Purpose

When conducting a stock recall (this could be batch, serial number, or production date) and you need to be able to trace all relevant Sale Orders.

### Solution - Stock Movement Report

- Using the Reports tab at the top of the application, select Stock Movement Report.
- From here, you will be able to generate a report with the relevant Sale Orders in relation to the specific batch number.
- Select Customer or Product from the Filter By drop-down menu. Depending on how many products from the one customer you need to recall will determine the option you select here.
- Select the relevant customer or product you wish to create the report for from the Select the Customer or Select the Product drop-down menu.
- Select Physical Movement from the Movement Type drop-down menu.
- Select All from the Product Status drop-down menu.
- Click Add All Columns to include Batch as a column.
- Select the tick box next to Search with specified Batch and type in the relevant batch number.
- Select the date ranges you wish to include in the report.

![stock-recall-process-batch-recall-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/stock-recall-process-batch-recall-0.png?width=670&height=309&name=stock-recall-process-batch-recall-0.png)

- Select Show Report . All relevant Sale Orders will now be displayed on the page.

![stock-recall-process-batch-recall-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/stock-recall-process-batch-recall-1.png?width=670&height=200&name=stock-recall-process-batch-recall-1.png)

- You can then export the report by selecting the Export Excel button.
- You can then manually select each Sale Order from the Show Report screen to trace where the stock was delivered to.

![stock-recall-process-batch-recall-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/stock-recall-process-batch-recall-2.png?width=670&height=66&name=stock-recall-process-batch-recall-2.png)

---

<a id="uploading-invoices-or-documents"></a>
## Uploading Documents to a Consignment for stock going out

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/uploading-invoices-or-documents_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to upload invoices or documents to a delivery consignments for stock going out of the warehouse

### Purpose

Instead of uploading an invoice document to the Sale Order when creating it, you can alternatively upload it directly to the corresponding Consignment as a Consignment Invoice instead. Note, this process is only relevant if your CartonCloud account owner is using both the Transport and Warehouse CartonCloud system and has the correct settings enabled.

### How to upload invoices or documents to a delivery consignments for stock going out of the warehouse

- Navigate to the Sale Orders page, Warehouse > Sale Orders .
- Click on the relevant order.
- Approve the order by clicking Approve .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-25-2025-11-00-54-1660-PM.png?width=670&height=304&name=image-png-Nov-25-2025-11-00-54-1660-PM.png)

- Click Approve .
- Navigate to the Consignments tab and click on the linked Consignment.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-25-2025-11-02-34-4624-PM.png?width=670&height=286&name=image-png-Nov-25-2025-11-02-34-4624-PM.png)

- Select the Documents tab and click + Add Document .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-25-2025-11-05-12-3687-PM.png?width=670&height=291&name=image-png-Nov-25-2025-11-05-12-3687-PM.png)

---

<a id="view-sale-order"></a>
## View Sale Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/view-sale-order_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- View Sale Order Tabs
  - ​​​​​​​ Details
  - Products
  - Add a product
  - Stock optimisation stock selection lock
  - Optimise stock selection
  - Actions
  - Edit
  - Delete
  - View ​​​​​​​

### Purpose

The View Sale Order page provides you with full control over your Sale Order after the creation stage.

### ![view-sale-order-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-0.png?width=670&height=265&name=view-sale-order-0.png)

### View Sale Order Tabs

**Details**

The details tab allows you to progress through the statuses of the Sale Order. It also allows you to Edit, Reject (in the case where you have customers submitting Purchase Order) and Delete the Sale Order.

The information provided in the details box provides an overview of key details surrounding that particular Sale Order such as its reference, Delivery address and instructions and if it's being invoiced to a customer or not. The "Specifics" box provides more detailed information including which Warehouse the stock is entering. It also provides an option to Upload a Customer Invoice against the order.

If the Sale Order is associated with a Consignment and needs to be picked up from the warehouse this information will be displayed under the delivery address. However, once the Consignment has been collected this information will no longer be diplayed.

Additionally, you can roll back the Purchase Order from this page using the **Reset Status** button (once approved).

**Products**

The Products tab allows you to add and view the stock associated with the Sale order.

![view-sale-order-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-1.png?width=670&height=265&name=view-sale-order-1.png)

When viewing the products you have the option to expand or collapse the summary lines which are displayed per product. If the Sale Order contains more than 100 items it will load as collapsed by default and smaller orders will load with all product lines visible.

**Product lines collapsed**

![view-sale-order-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-2.png?width=670&height=160&name=view-sale-order-2.png)

**Product lines expanded**

![view-sale-order-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-3.png?width=670&height=265&name=view-sale-order-3.png)

**How to expand and collapse**

- Use the expand collapse icons on the far left to expand or collapse the product lines.

![view-sale-order-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-4.png?width=670&height=222&name=view-sale-order-4.png)

**Unassign stock**

Before an order is in a status of 'Awaiting Pick and Pack' you have the option to unallocate stock from a SOP (Sale Order Product) line. If you unallocate stock from an SOP line the line's requested quantity will remain, therefore, you will not lose the ability to see how much stock was originally requested. Once the order is in 'Packing in Progress' you will no longer have the ability to unallocate stock and if you have unallocated stock it will warn you before approving the order and then remove the unassigned products.

The unassign stock option allows for greater flexibility in order management and stock allocations according to real-time needs without the risk of losing track of order quantities. Therefore, you can more effectively manage inventory and order fulfilment processes, leading to improved operational efficiency and customer satisfaction.

**To unassign stock:**

- Navigate to the relevant Sale Order.
- Select the Product tab.
- Against the product summary row or against the individual product lines select the Unassign button.

![view-sale-order-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-5.png?width=670&height=146&name=view-sale-order-5.png)

- Once you have unassigned a product or product line you will then see a Assign button with the option to assign the stock.

Note that once stock has been unallocated the history will show any additional changes to allocation of stock in an aggregated format into one SOP and combine the quantities.

**Add a product**

- Select **+Add Product**.

![view-sale-order-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-6.png?width=670&height=101&name=view-sale-order-6.png)

- Select the relevant **Product** from the drop-down menu and **Unit of Measure**.
- Type in the quantity.
- Click **Search**.
- Select **Take Stock**.

**Stock Optimisation Stock Selection Lock**

When selecting the stock to add to the Sale Order, you have the option to lock the stock selection and prevent CartonCloud from changing what stock is associated with the Sale Order when conducting the stock optimisation process.

To do so, tick the **Prevent Change** box next to the product or to select all, select **Prevent Charges: Select All**.

![view-sale-order-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-7.png?width=670&height=188&name=view-sale-order-7.png)

**Optimise Stock Selection**

![view-sale-order-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-8.png?width=670&height=101&name=view-sale-order-8.png)

By selecting Optimise Stock Selection, CartonCloud will use the Stock Selection Method specified for the Product to re-optimise the stock selection for the Sale Order.

See [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-cartoncloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-stock-selection-methods) for more information.

**Actions**
![view-sale-order-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-sale-order-9.png?width=670&height=265&name=view-sale-order-9.png)

**Edit**
Select **Edit** to edit the quantity of the Sale Order Product. See [Adjusting Stock Quantity](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adjusting-stock-quantity) for more information.

**Delete**
To delete the stock from the Sale Order.

**View**
To view the Sale Order Product.

---

# Warehouse Management > Warehouse Locations

<a id="adding-warehouse-locations"></a>
## Adding Warehouse Locations

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-warehouse-locations_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Adding warehouse locations
  - Adding a single warehouse location
  - Adding warehouse locations in bulk
  - Adding warehouse locations via export/import
- Pick face warehouse locations (Replenishment)

### Overview

Warehouse locations can be created in 3 ways:

- **Adding a single warehouse location** - best when you only need to add a single warehouse location, for example, a bulk location.
- **Adding warehouse locations in bulk**- if you need to generate racking locations.
- **Adding warehouse locations via export/import -** if you need to generate an entire warehouse set of locations.

**Important factors to note before creating warehouse locations:**

- The **Name**field when adding a single pallet location is system generated. If you would like to manually populate the name you need to tick 'Set Name Manually'.
- The **Pick Efficiency** field is important as this will help determine the location that CartonCloud selects stock from. The Pick Efficiency ranges from 1 (being the least efficient) through to 20 (being the most efficient). See [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-CartonCloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-Stock-Selection-Methods) for more information.
- The Pick Order field has no impact on stock selection, it will just determine the sequence the locations are shown on pick lists and the mobile app.
- If creating a **Pick Face (for [Replenishment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Replenishment))**you will need to select a Pick Efficiency between 21 and 30 (30 being the most efficient).
- If you are **printing labels** with [Warehouse Location Labels](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Warehouse+Location+Labels), the total number of characters that can be used in the Warehouse Location Name is 14. For Location names that require more than 14 characters, labels will need to be printed manually.

### Adding warehouse locations

#### **Adding a single warehouse location**

- Navigate to **Warehouse Locations** (Warehouse > Warehouse Locations).
- Select **+Add a Single Warehouse Location.**
- From the **Capacity** drop-down, select either **Singlet Pallet**or **Multiple Pallets**.
- Complete the fields as required (refer to the [Warehouse Location Fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Warehouse+Location+Fields) guide if you are unsure what a particular field is for).
- Select **Create location**.
- A success banner will appear. By clicking on the banner you will be directed to the View Warehouse Location page and be able to see the newly created warehouse location.

**For single pallet:**

![adding-warehouse-locations-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-warehouse-locations-0.png?width=670&height=365&name=adding-warehouse-locations-0.png)
**For multiple pallets:**

![adding-warehouse-locations-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-warehouse-locations-1.png?width=670&height=365&name=adding-warehouse-locations-1.png)

**Guided Video**

Follow along with Vincent as he explains how to add a single warehouse location.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/rV7oK_rHwpQ

---

#### **Adding Warehouse Locations in Bulk**

- Navigate to **Warehouse Locations** (Warehouse > Warehouse Locations).
- Select the **More** button and **Add Warehouse Locations in Bulk** from the drop-down menu.

![adding-warehouse-locations-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-warehouse-locations-2.png?width=670&height=197&name=adding-warehouse-locations-2.png)

- Enter the starting and ending Bay, Level, and (optionally) Depth.
- Enter the [Pick Efficiency](https://3883312.hs-sites.com/location-efficiency) for each Level.
- Select the Warehouse Location Type.
- Select the Product Types the Warehouse Location can accept.
- Select **Generate**.

A success banner will display at the top of the browser informing you on how many locations were created. It is suggested you check this number against the number of locations you intended to create.

![adding-warehouse-locations-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-warehouse-locations-3.png?width=670&height=328&name=adding-warehouse-locations-3.png)

**Guided Video**

Follow along with Vincent as he explains how to add warehouse locations in bulk.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/TsLcXWD-I74

---

#### **Adding Warehouse Locations via Export/Import**

Before adding locations using this tool, we recommend adding at least one location using the "Add a single Warehouse location" method as this will populate the exported XLS file with an example location to reference.

- Navigate to **Warehouse Locations** (Warehouse > Warehouse Locations).
- Select **More** and then **Export to XLS** from the drop-down menu.

![adding-warehouse-locations-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-warehouse-locations-4.png?width=670&height=197&name=adding-warehouse-locations-4.png)

- Open the downloaded file using a spreadsheet program such as Excel.
- Follow the same format as the current warehouse locations and add the new locations into the XLS template.
- Ensure you **leave the id column blank on all new records** (as CartonCloud tries to override existing records if an id is provided).
- Save the file.
- From the **Warehouse Locations** page in CartonCloud, select **More** and **Import XLS**from the drop-down menu.
- Select the XLS file you saved.
- If the import is successful a success banner will be displayed. From here, scroll to the bottom of the confirmation page and click **Confirm Import**(if you do not, the changes to warehouse locations will **not** be applied).

If the import is unsuccessful due to an issue such as formatting, an Error banner will be displayed and the error will be described.

**Guided Video**

Follow along with Vincent as he explains how to add warehouse locations in bulk via export/import.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/98s4QoiCvBo

---

### Pick Face Warehouse Locations (Replenishment)

If you are using Replenishment for any Products in your warehouse you will need to create Pick Face Warehouse Locations.

To create a Pick Face Warehouse Location:

- Create Warehouse Locations following either of the three above processes, however, when selecting the Pick Efficiency ensure to select a **PICK FACE EFFICIENCY** level.

The Pick Face efficiency levels range from 21 being the least efficient through to 30 being the most efficient.

---

<a id="assigning-the-associated-product-types-to-a-warehouse-location"></a>
## Assigning the associated Product types to a Warehouse Location

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/assigning-the-associated-product-types-to-a-warehouse-location_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Editing a single location
- Editing multiple locations in bulk

### Purpose

By assigning an associated Product Type to a Warehouse Location you can mark that location to only store specific stock, for example, Frozen, Quarantine or Dangerous Goods.

For a further explanation about Product types please see the article [Setting up Product Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=530056207).

### Editing a single location

- Navigate to Warehouse > Warehouse Locations .
- Select the location you wish to change the Product type for.
- Click Edit .

![assigning-the-associated-product-types-to-a-warehouse-location-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-the-associated-product-types-to-a-warehouse-location-0.png?width=670&height=291&name=assigning-the-associated-product-types-to-a-warehouse-location-0.png)

- Scroll down to Warehouse Location Product Type.
- Select the Product Type you want to enable for this location. Keep in mind that a location can store multiple Product Types.

![assigning-the-associated-product-types-to-a-warehouse-location-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-the-associated-product-types-to-a-warehouse-location-1.png?width=670&height=294&name=assigning-the-associated-product-types-to-a-warehouse-location-1.png)

- Select Save.

### Editing multiple locations in Bulk

If you want to update the Product type of many Warehouse Locations at once then this can be done quickly through the **Edit Warehouse Locations in Bulk** feature.

- Navigate to Warehouse > Warehouse Locations .
- Next, select the More button and then select Edit Warehouse Locations in Bulk from the drop-down menu.

- Now either use Filters to find the Warehouse Locations you wish to change then select Search , or immediately select Search to bring up a list of all locations (which will likely be separated over many pages).
- Select the Warehouse Locations you wish to edit, then select Bulk Edit .
- In the Edit Location pop up. Tick the Change Product type box, then select which Product Types you would like to apply to the Location.
- Select Save.

---

<a id="delete-merge-a-warehouse-location"></a>
## Delete/merge a Warehouse Location

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/delete-merge-a-warehouse-location_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Merging warehouse locations
- How to merge a warehouse location
- Bulk merging warehouse locations
- Deactivating / reactivating warehouse locations

### Purpose

Warehouse Locations cannot be deleted directly due to dependency restrictions, as they may be in use by other records, such as Purchase Order Products.

For this reason, the only way to completely delete a Warehouse Location is to merge it with another Warehouse Location.

Alternatively, you can simply "Deactivate" a Warehouse Location if the Warehouse Location is empty.

Note, when merging warehouse locations, CartonCloud will alert you when the file size is exceeded and the merge/import will fail.

### Merging warehouse locations

Merging Warehouse Locations cannot be undone - it adjusts all historical and current stock to point to the new Warehouse Location.

As direct deletion of a warehouse location is not possible, Warehouse Locations must be "Merged" together in order to remove one that's not required. Merging warehouse locations should only be used if the Warehouse Location was added incorrectly and was never really in use. If you simply want to remove a Warehouse Location **that no longer exists** then Deactivate the Warehouse Location instead.

When two Warehouse Locations are merged, only ONE warehouse location will exist after the merge. For example, Location AA-01-01 is being merged into AA-01-02, meaning after the merge AA-01-01 will no longer exist.

### How to merge a Warehouse Location

- Navigate to Warehouse > Warehouse Locations .
- Select the relevant Warehouse Location.
- Click Merge Warehouse Location .

![delete-merge-a-warehouse-location-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delete-merge-a-warehouse-location-0.png?width=670&height=291&name=delete-merge-a-warehouse-location-0.png)

- From here, select which Warehouse Location you want to merge the Warehouse Location into.

Remember, only the location you select in the box below will exist after the merge.

![delete-merge-a-warehouse-location-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delete-merge-a-warehouse-location-1.png?width=670&height=233&name=delete-merge-a-warehouse-location-1.png)

- Click Save.

### Bulk Merging Warehouse Locations

You can also bulk-merge warehouse locations by doing the following:

1. Export Warehouse Locations.
2. Add an additional column to the Warehouse Locations file called 'merge_id'
3. On each location that you want to remove, put the ID of the Warehouse Location you want to merge INTO into the merge_id field.
4. Save the file and import it.

Locations of type Multiple Pallets cannot be merged into locations of type Single Pallet (import will fail on these locations). You can first change the location type to single pallet through export and import.

### Deactivating / Reactivating Warehouse Locations

Warehouse Locations can be deactivated **if they no longer contain any stock**so if you want to deactivate a location that still contains stock then you need to move the stock to another location first.

Once locations are deactivated, they can be reactivated for use at any time.

- Navigate to Warehouse > Warehouse Locations.
- Select the relevant Warehouse Location.
- Click De-activate .

You can also deactivate and reactivate locations in bulk from the [Bulk Edit Warehouse Locations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/createpage.action?spaceKey=KB2&title=Bulk+Edit+Warehouse+Locations&linkCreation=true&fromPageId=530056652)page.

---

<a id="editing-a-single-warehouse-location"></a>
## Editing a single Warehouse Location

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/editing-a-single-warehouse-location_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to edit a single warehouse location

### Purpose

To edit a single Warehouse Location.

### How to edit a single warehouse location

- Navigate to the relevant Warehouse Location, Warehouse > Warehouse Locations.
- Select the Warehouse Location you wish to edit.

![editing-a-single-warehouse-location-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/editing-a-single-warehouse-location-0.png?width=670&height=311&name=editing-a-single-warehouse-location-0.png)

- Click the blue Edit button .

**![editing-a-single-warehouse-location-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/editing-a-single-warehouse-location-1.png?width=670&height=285&name=editing-a-single-warehouse-location-1.png)**

- From here you can edit the below fields (see Warehouse Location Fields for more detailed descriptions)
  - Warehouse Location Name
  - Location Barcode
  - Product Type: the allowed Product Types in that Warehouse Location.
  - Capacity: the capacity of the Warehouse Location if it is single or multiple pallets.
  - Pick and Replenishment Efficiency: Pick Efficiency is used when selecting which stock to use automatically (see How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods for more information). The Pick Efficiency ranges from 1 (being the least efficient) through to 20 (being the most efficient). If creating Pick Faces (for Replenishment ) you will need to select a Pick Efficiency between 21 and 30 (30 being the most efficient).

**![editing-a-single-warehouse-location-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/editing-a-single-warehouse-location-2.png?width=670&height=303&name=editing-a-single-warehouse-location-2.png)**

- Once all changes have been made, click Save .

**![editing-a-single-warehouse-location-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/editing-a-single-warehouse-location-3.png?width=670&height=286&name=editing-a-single-warehouse-location-3.png)**

<a id="editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk"></a>
## Editing Warehouse Locations in Bulk

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to edit warehouse locations in bulk
- Bulk edit options

### Purpose

This guide covers how to edit Warehouse Locations in bulk via the Web Interface. You can also check out the article [Setting up Warehouse Locations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Warehouse+Locations).

### How to edit warehouse locations in bulk

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page, Warehouse > Warehouse Locations.
- Select More > Edit Locations in Bulk .
- Using the searching and filtering options, define specific ranges of locations or just search for all.

![editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-0.png?width=670&height=289&name=editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-0.png)

- Using Select All to highlight all locations to change, you can then Bulk Activate or Bulk De-activate , or Bulk Edit to change features of the locations.

![editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-1.png?width=670&height=321&name=editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-1.png)

### Bulk Edit Options

- If selecting Bulk edit, a new box will appear.

![editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-2.png?width=670&height=321&name=editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk-2.png)

- Changing these values will change the corresponding fields of the warehouse locations you have selected.
- An explanation of the fields is provided in the table below,

| **Setting** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- |
| Location Product Type | This will set the Warehouse Locations Product Type, this can affect the fees you charge for that warehouse location. (For example, you might charge a different fee for frozen space than you do for general) |
| Warehouse Location Capacity | This can be set to either single or multiple pallets. The multiple pallets option would be used in bulk locations where more than one pallet is stored within that location code. |
| Location Pick Efficiency | This value allows CartonCloud to make the picking process more efficient by |
| Change Product Type (Associated) | This will change the associated product type of the warehouse location. These are the product types that the warehouse location is allowed to hold. For example, a warehouse location may have a Location Product type of "Chilled", however, you may want the system to allow both chilled AND general stock to be stored in it. In this scenario, the location should be set with *Associated Product types* of "Chilled" and "General". |

- Select Save and the changes will be applied.

---

<a id="printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates"></a>
## Printing Warehouse Location Labels using Avery Templates

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to steps

### Purpose

By using Avery templates, you can easily print your warehouse locations onto labels to place on your warehouse racking.

### Prerequisites

- You must have already created Warehouse Locations in CartonCloud.
- Each Warehouse Location must have a barcode.

### How to steps

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page in CartonCloud, by typing Warehouse Locations into the Search for anything bar.
- Select **More** and **Export to XLS**.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-0.png?width=670&height=98&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-0.png)

- Save the XLS file.
- Navigate to the Avery Design & Print Online website - [https://www.avery.co.uk/](https://www.avery.co.uk/)
- Select the login logo in the top right corner and select**Design & Print Login** from the drop-down menu.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-1.png?width=670&height=211&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-1.png)

- Select the Sign Up button and create an account.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-2.png?width=670&height=306&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-2.png)

- Once you have created an account, select the **1 Choose Template** tab.
- Search for the template you wish to use in the top search bar. You will be able to find the label code on the front of the label packet.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-3.png?width=670&height=237&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-3.png)

It is recommended that you use [L7165](https://www.officeworks.com.au/shop/officeworks/p/avery-8up-laser-shipping-labels-100-sheets-av959006) labels.

- Select the template you wish to use and then click the green **Select This Template** button.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-4.png?width=670&height=237&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-4.png)

- You will then move to the Choose Design tab. Select the design you wish to use.

For simple white labels, it is recommended you select the first template

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-5.png?width=670&height=237&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-5.png)

- You will then move to the Customise tab.
- Click the top **Text**box and then **Add Text Box**.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-6.png?width=670&height=319&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-6.png)

- Do not type anything into the text box.

- Select the third box, **Import Data Mail Merge** and then **Start Import/Merge.**

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-7.png?width=670&height=319&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-7.png)

- Select Browse for file and select the Warehouse Locations XSL you downloaded from CartonCloud.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-8.png?width=670&height=256&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-8.png)

- Select the **2 Choose Fields** tab from the top blue bar.
- Untick the first column.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-9.png?width=670&height=256&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-9.png)

- Select the green **Next** button in the bottom right corner.
- Select and drag the **Name** field across into the **Arrange fields** box.
- Select the green **Next** button in the bottom right corner.
- Select the green **Finish** button in the bottom right corner.
- Select the **Text** box in the left panel and arrange the text so it is centred and at the size you require.
- Select the **QR and Barcodes** text box and select **Add Barcode or QR Code**.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-10.png?width=670&height=256&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-10.png)

- Select the **Spreadsheet or Sequential Number**optionby selecting the clear circle until it turns blue.
- Select the green **Next** button in the bottom right corner.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-11.png?width=670&height=314&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-11.png)

- Select and drag the Barcode field across into the **Enter alphanumeric and special characters** field.
- Select **Code 128** from the **Industry Standard Format** drop-down menu.
- Untick the Display text below the code option.
- Select the green **Finish** button.
- Arrange and re-size the barcode.
- To add images to the label, select the **Image** box and then **Add Image**.

![printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-12.png?width=670&height=333&name=printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates-12.png)

​​​​​​Image examples: arrows (point to the direction of the location) or a DG sign (to identify the DG warehouse location section).

- Select the **4 Preview & Print**tab from the top blue bar.
- Select the **Print** button.

Before printing your labels, make sure the printer has the correct label pages in the paper tray.

---

<a id="setting-up-warehouse-location-labels-barcodes"></a>
## Setting up Warehouse Location Labels / Barcodes

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-warehouse-location-labels-barcodes_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Setting up the Warehouse Barcode field on Warehouse Locations
- Printing Warehouse Location Labels

### Purpose

Once you have created your Warehouse Locations, you can print the associated barcode labels to place on each location within your warehouse. This will allow you to easily find warehouse locations and scan them for actions such as moving, picking and putaway (on the mobile app).

### Setting up the Warehouse Barcode field on Warehouse Locations

When scanning barcodes, CartonCloud will check both the Warehouse Location's "barcode" and "name" fields.

If no match is found on the "barcode" field, then the "name" field is used.

**Configuring a Warehouse that doesn't have Barcodes**

If your warehouse doesn't currently use barcodes, then you can follow the below steps to set the locations up with barcodes.

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page, **Warehouse**>**Warehouse Locations**.
- Click **More**>**Export to XLS**.
- Open the downloaded file.
- In the **name column**, select the cell in the first row of warehouse locations. Hold down **CTRL + SHIFT + down arrow**. This will highlight the whole column down from the first cell you selected.
- Copy the data.
- Paste the data in the **barcode column**.
- Save the file.
- Navigate back to the Warehouse Locations page. Select **More**>**Import XLS**.
- Select the file and click **Upload File**.
- Once the file has been imported, the Updated tab will show the changes made to the Warehouse Locations. Select **Confirm Import**.

**Configuring a Warehouse that already has Barcodes**

If your warehouse already uses warehouse location barcodes, you can load the existing barcodes into CartonCloud.

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page, Warehouse>Warehouse Locations.
- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page, **Warehouse**>**Warehouse Locations**.
- Click **More**>**Export to XLS**.
- Open the downloaded file.
- In the barcode column, enter the barcode label data(of your existing warehouse location barcodes).
- Save the file.
- Navigate back to the Warehouse Locations page. Select **More**>**Import XLS**.
- Select the file and click **Upload File**.
Once the file has been imported, the Updated tab will show the changes made to the Warehouse Locations. Select **Confirm Import**.

### Printing Warehouse Location Labels

See [Print Warehouse Location Labels](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/print-warehouse-location-labels) or [Printing Warehouse Location Labels using Avery Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/printing-warehouse-location-labels-using-avery-templates).

---

<a id="setting-up-warehouse-locationssetting-up-warehouse-locations"></a>
## Setting up Warehouse Locations

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-warehouse-locationssetting-up-warehouse-locations_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to create Warehouse Locations

### Purpose

Creating Warehouse locations within your Warehouse is necessary so that when stock is imported it can be allocated to a designated place.

For storage to be charged for the stock within your warehouse, the stock must be within a Warehouse Location.

### How to create Warehouse Locations

Warehouse locations can be created in 3 ways:

- **Adding a single Warehouse Location** - best when you only need to add a single warehouse location, for example, a bulk location
- [Adding warehouse locations in bulk](https://help.cartoncloud.com#adding-warehouse-locations-in-bulk) - this is best if you need to generate racking locations
- [Adding warehouse locations via import/export](https://help.cartoncloud.com#adding-warehouse-locations-via-export-import) - this is best if you need to generate an entire warehouse set of locations

**Important factors to note before creating warehouse locations:**

- The Name field when adding a single pallet location is system generated. If you would like to manually populate the name you need to tick 'Set Name Manually'.
- The Pick Efficiency field is important as this will help determine the location that CartonCloud selects stock from. The Pick Efficiency ranges from 1 (being the least efficient) through to 20 (being the most efficient). See [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-cartoncloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-stock-selection-methods) for more information.
- If creating a Pick Face (for Replenishment ) you will need to select a Pick Efficiency between 21 and 30 (30 being the most efficient).
- ​​​​​​​If you are printing labels with Warehouse Location Labels , the total number of characters that can be used in the Warehouse Location Name is 14. For Location names that require more than 14 characters, labels will need to be printed manually.

​​​​**Adding a single Warehouse location**

- Navigate to **Warehouse Locations** (Warehouse > Warehouse Locations).
- Select **+Add a Single Warehouse Location.**
- From the **Capacity** drop-down, select either **Singlet Pallet**or **Multiple Pallets**.
- Complete the fields as required (refer to the [Warehouse Location Fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Warehouse+Location+Fields) guide if you are unsure what a particular field is for).
- Select Create location .
- ​​​​​​​A success banner will appear. By clicking on the banner you will be directed to the View Warehouse Location page and be able to see the newly created warehouse location.

​​​​​​​**Single Pallet:**
**![setting-up-warehouse-locationssetting-up-warehouse-locations-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-warehouse-locationssetting-up-warehouse-locations-0.png?width=670&height=365&name=setting-up-warehouse-locationssetting-up-warehouse-locations-0.png)

Multiple Pallets:**
![setting-up-warehouse-locationssetting-up-warehouse-locations-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-warehouse-locationssetting-up-warehouse-locations-1.png?width=670&height=365&name=setting-up-warehouse-locationssetting-up-warehouse-locations-1.png)

 **Guided Video**

Follow along with Vincent as he explains how to add a single warehouse location.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/rV7oK_rHwpQ

**Adding Warehouse Locations in Bulk**

- Navigate to **Warehouse Locations** (Warehouse > Warehouse Locations).
- Select the **More** button and **Add Warehouse Locations in Bulk** from the drop-down menu.

- Enter the starting and ending Bay, Level, and (optionally) Depth.
- Enter the [Pick Efficiency](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-cartoncloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-stock-selection-methods) for each Level.
- Select the Warehouse Location Type.
- Select the Product Types the Warehouse Location can accept.
- Select **Generate**.

A success banner will display at the top of the browser informing you on how many locations were created. It is suggested you check this number against the number of locations you intended to create.

**Guided Video**

Follow along with Vincent as he explains how to add warehouse locations in bulk.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/TsLcXWD-I74

**Adding Warehouse locations via Export/Import**

Before adding locations using this tool, we recommend adding at least one location using the "Add a single Warehouse location" method as this will populate the exported XLS file with an example location to reference.

- Navigate to **Warehouse Locations** (Warehouse > Warehouse Locations).
- Select **More** and then **Export to XLS** from the drop-down menu.
- Open the downloaded file using a spreadsheet program such as Excel.
- Follow the same format as the current warehouse locations and add the new locations into the XLS template.
- Ensure you **leave the id column blank on all new records** (as CartonCloud tries to override existing records if an id is provided).
- Save the file.
- From the **Warehouse Locations** page in CartonCloud, select **More** and **Import XLS**from the drop-down menu.
- Select the XLS file you saved.
- If the import is successful a success banner will be displayed. From here, scroll to the bottom of the confirmation page and click **Confirm Import**(if you do not, the changes to warehouse locations will **not** be applied).

If the import is unsuccessful due to an issue such as formatting, an Error banner will be displayed and the error will be described.

**Guided Video**
Follow along with Vincent as he explains how to add warehouse locations in bulk via export/import.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/98s4QoiCvBo

Pick Face Warehouse Locations (Replenishment)

If you are using Replenishment for any Products in your warehouse you will need to create Pick Face Warehouse Locations.

To create a Pick Face Warehouse Location:

- Create Warehouse Locations following either of the three above processes, however, when selecting the Pick Efficiency ensure to select a **PICK FACE EFFICIENCY** level.

The Pick Face efficiency levels range from 21 being the least efficient through to 30 being the most efficient.

---

<a id="setting-up-warehouse-locations-pick-path-sequence"></a>
## Setting up Warehouse Locations Pick Path Sequence (Pick Order)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-warehouse-locations-pick-path-sequence_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Enable pick order
- Import / export warehouse locations
- Import error
- Applying the pick order when picking on the mobile app

### Purpose

Within CartonCloud it is possible to create an order within your Warehouse Locations that you wish to pick Sale Orders by. This requires you to update the pick_order field on each Warehouse location to assign it a numbered order in respect to all other locations that you wish to pick it by.

Products will then display on Sale Orders in the order where the first row is the Warehouse Location with the lowest pick_order number when compared to all other warehouse locations on the Sale Order.

### Enable pick order

Please note that the pick order is not applied in the Products tab when viewing a Wave Pick.

Firstly, you will need to enable the pick_order field against Warehouse Locations. If this setting is not enabled, you will not be able to see the 'pick_order' column in the below location export. To do this:

- Navigate to Organisation Settings, More>Organisation Settings.
- Select the Warehouse tab.
- Tick Sort Pick/Pack List by Warehouse Locations Pick Order .

![setting-up-warehouse-locations-pick-path-sequence-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-warehouse-locations-pick-path-sequence-0.png?width=670&height=251&name=setting-up-warehouse-locations-pick-path-sequence-0.png)

- Scroll down and select Save.

### Import / export warehouse locations

This method of adjusting Warehouse Locations data requires exporting a CSV file, updating it, and then importing the CSV back into the CartonCloud web app.

To export Warehouse Locations to be updated navigate to the Warehouse Locations page by selecting **Warehouse** in the main menu, then selecting **Warehouse Locations** in the drop-down box.

Start by Exporting your Warehouse Locations by selecting the **More** button, then **Export to CSV** in the drop-down menu.

Open the downloaded file using a spreadsheet program such as Excel.

From here, provide a numbered order against your Warehouse Locations based on the order you wish to pick.

In the example below, if products from A-01-03 and A-01-04 were on the same Sale Order, the product in A-01-04 would appear higher on the list, as it has a lower pick_order number.

We suggest incrementing the pick order in amounts of 10 as this will allow you to add in locations in between the current locations later. If a pick_order cell is left empty, the system will place it after warehouse locations with a number greater than 0.

Once completed, save the CSV file, and then import it back into CartonCloud by selecting the **More** button, then **Import CSV** in the drop-down menu, then selecting the CSV file you just saved.

If the import is successful, the warehouse locations will be updated and a Success banner will be displayed. From here you will need to scroll to the bottom of the confirmation page and click **Confirm Import** (if you do not, the changes to warehouse locations will not be applied).

Now when you create Sale Orders, products will be listed in the pick path sequence you have just set.

### Import error

If the import is unsuccessful due to an issue such as formatting, an Error banner will be displayed and the error will be described.

If you receive an error, you can find out information about why it's occurred by following the same actions as the animation below.

In the case below, a pick_order of -1 was given to a Warehouse Location, which is outside of the allowed range.

### Applying the pick order when picking on the mobile app

See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Details-page-and-items-list#items-list-sorting)for steps on how to apply the pick order when picking on the mobile app.

---

<a id="unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location"></a>
## Unable to allocate stock to a Warehouse Location

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location_

### Table of Contents

- Issue
- Why the issue has occurred
- Example scenario
- How to resolve the issue

### Issue

When allocating stock to a Warehouse Location, the Warehouse Location does not appear in the search, or the allocation/stock movement fails.

### Why the issue has occurred

The Warehouse Location only accepts certain Product Types, and the stock attempting to be allocated to the Warehouse Location does not match the specified Product Type.

### Example scenario

You have stock that is General Product Type, and you are attempting to allocate it to the DG Bulk Warehouse Location. However, the DG Bulk Warehouse Location only accepts stock with the Product Type of Dangerous Goods.

**On the Web App**: the Warehouse Location will not show when you search for it.

![unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-0.png?width=670&height=296&name=unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-0.png)

On the mobile app:

the move will fail, and an error message will appear.

Failed move

![unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-1.png?width=233&height=504&name=unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-1.png)

Error message

![unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-2.png?width=277&height=566&name=unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-2.png)

### How to resolve the issue

To resolve the issue, you will need to either allocate the stock to a different location (that accepts the Product Type) or update the allowed Product Types for that location.

You will need to check the stock's Product Type and the accepted Product Type of that Warehouse Location.

**Check 1 - Check Product's Product Type**

- Navigate to the relevant Product, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Check the **Product Type** against the Product.

![unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-3.png?width=670&height=207&name=unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-3.png)

**Check 2 - Check the Warehouse Location accepted Product Types**

- Navigate to the Warehouse Location you want to allocate the Product to, **Warehouse**>**Warehouse Locations**.
- Check the **Product Type** against the Warehouse Location.

![unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-4.png?width=670&height=355&name=unable-to-allocate-stock-to-a-warehouse-location-4.png)

If the Product Type against the Product is not listed as an allowed Product Type against the Warehouse Location. In that case, you will need to allocate the Product to a different location OR update the Warehouse Location allowed Product Types.

**Update Warehouse Location allowed Product Types**

You can edit the Warehouse Location's allowed Product Type by either editing a single Warehouse Location or editing multiple locations in bulk.

To edit a single Warehouse Location click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/editing-a-single-warehouse-location).

To edit Warehouse Locations in bulk click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/editing-warehouse-locations-in-bulk).

---

<a id="warehouse-location"></a>
## Warehouse Location Barcodes

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/warehouse-location_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Setting up the warehouse barcode field on warehouse locations
- Configuring a warehouse that doesn't have barcodes
- Configuring a warehouse that already has barcodes
- Printing warehouse location labels

### Purpose

Once you have created your Warehouse Locations, you can print the associated barcode labels to place on each location within your warehouse. This will allow you to easily find warehouse locations and scan them for actions such as moving, picking and putaway (on the mobile app).

### Setting up the warehouse barcode field on warehouse locations

When scanning barcodes, CartonCloud will check both the Warehouse Location's "barcode" and "name" fields.

If no match is found on the "barcode" field, then the "name" field is used.

### Configuring a Warehouse that doesn't have Barcodes

If your warehouse doesn't currently use barcodes, then you can follow the below steps to set the locations up with barcodes.

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page, **Warehouse**>**Warehouse Locations**.
- Click **More**>**Export to XLS**.
- Open the downloaded file.

- Save the file.

<a id="warehouse-location-group"></a>
## Warehouse Location Charge Group

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/warehouse-location-group_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use cases
- Considerations
- How to create a Warehouse Location Charge Group
- Warehouse Location Charge Group and Storage Charges

### Purpose

Warehouse Locations can be grouped into Charge Groups. All locations with the same Charge Group will be charged as a single location.

### Use cases

- This is useful if you have an area of small shelves that you wish to generate a single charge for.

### Considerations

- Warehouse Location Charge Group storage charging will only apply if using Per Location storage charge method.
- It is best practice to ensure the locations that are grouped are a single pallet capacity.
- If you are wanting the charges to be grouped for 'New Storage' you will need to set the Max Number of New Charges Per Location to 1 in the Rate Card (within the Storage Tab), otherwise grouping will only be applied for Existing Storage.
- It is best practice to utilise the Charge Product Type Option of Warehouse Location (against the Rate Card) and to ensure each Warehouse Location in the group has the same Product Type.
- If Warehouse Locations in the same group have different Product Types, the Product Type with the highest rate will be applied.

### How to create a Warehouse Location Charge Group

- When creating a Warehouse Location (following the Adding Warehouse Locations process), fill in the Warehouse Location Charge Group field with the group name.
- Apply this same name to each location you wish to be in the Warehouse Location Charge Group.

![warehouse-location-group-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/warehouse-location-group-0.png?width=670&height=328&name=warehouse-location-group-0.png)

### Warehouse Location Charge Group and Storage Charges

Storage charges for Warehouse Location Charge Groups are created in the same way as normal storage charges are following this process - [View Rate Card - Storage Charges.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/View-Rate-Card-Storage-Charges)

Please ensure you read the above [considerations](https://help.cartoncloud.com#considerations)before creating your storage charges for Warehouse Location Charge Groups.

---

<a id="warehouse-location-fields"></a>
## Warehouse Location Fields

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/warehouse-location-fields_

| **Field** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Capacity | The Capacity field impacts the way in which Storage Charges are calculated. **Single Pallet**: This is suitable for locations which normally only store a single pallet. For example, locations within Pallet Racking, ie: A-01-01. All stock loaded into the location is treated as being on a single pallet. All items loaded into this location are treated as being on the same pallet, and therefore, if [Location-based Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Rate+Card+-+Storage+Charges) are used, will only charge a single pallet for Storage. **Multiple Pallets:**Suitable for locations which store multiple pallets, for example bulk locations such as "Freezer Floor", or "Loading Room 3". When stock is allocated to Multiple Pallet locations, Individual "Pallet Ids" are created, so by default each stock record is treated as it's own pallet (and charged as it's own pallet). You have the ability to load multiple stock records onto the same Pallet Id, however this is not the default behaviour. |
| Estimated Max Number of Pallets | *This is a required field when adding a Multiple Pallet Warehouse Location.*  The estimated number of pallets that can be added to each location. If you are unsure what the estimated max number of pallet is please enter 1. |
| Name | The name of the Warehouse Location, for example A-01-01. Names can be automatically generated based on Row, Bay, Level and Depth. |
| Zone | The Warehouse Zone associated with the Warehouse Location. A Zone groups Warehouse Locations together and allows for efficient warehouse planning and operations. For more information please see [Warehouse Zones](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Warehouse-Zones). |
| Row, Bay, Level, Depth | This only applies to Single Pallet Locations. It is recommended the locations are named as follows:  ![warehouse-location-fields-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/warehouse-location-fields-0.png?width=670&height=333&name=warehouse-location-fields-0.png)      Row: A line of racking   Bay: How far to the right it is. Ie, the Left-Most location in the line is 01   Level: How high it is, where 01 is ground level, and 02 is the next pallet up.   Depth: If you use deep racking (ie: 2 or 3 deep pallet racking), the depth should be numbered such that the location at the front is 01. Example of racking when looking from the front (assuming this is single-depth ranking). ![warehouse-location-fields-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/warehouse-location-fields-1.png?width=642&height=130&name=warehouse-location-fields-1.png) **Examples:** A-01-01 → Bottom left corner in the line.   A-01-04 → Far Left, 4th location up.   A-05-02 → Far Right, 2nd location up |
| Charge Group | All locations with the same Charge Group will be charged as a single location. This is useful when you have an area of small shelves that is charged as a single rate (for all), by giving all the shelf locations the same Charge Group, they'll be treated as a single location when calculating storage charges. See: [Storage Charges](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Rate+Card+-+Storage+Charges) **(this feature only works with the 'Per Location' storage charge method)** |
| Location Barcode | When scanning location labels, by default CartonCloud looks at the location name, if this matches the barcode, ie: "A-01-01" then it'll match. However, in some cases there are existing barcodes on the warehouse racking, which CartonCloud can re-use. |
| Location Type | The [Product Type](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Types) of the location, for example: Chilled, Frozen, Ambient. This can be used to control what the location is able to hold, and also how it's charged (if [Charge Type Product Option](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Rate+Card+-+Storage+Charges) is set to "Warehouse Location") Note, you can only update and existing Warehouse Location's Location Type when there is no stock in the location. If you need to update the Location Type of an existing Warehouse Location you will need to move the sock out of the location first. |
| Accept Products of Type (Associated Product Types) | This allows you to specify which Product Types can be stored in the location. By default this is just the Location Type of the location.   For example, you may have Chilled Locations in which you also allow storage of Ambient Products, you can therefore make the location a Chilled Location with the Product Type, but allow it to store both Chilled and Ambient products. You would not, however, allow it to store Frozen products (as they'll all melt!) |
| Pick Efficiency | Pick Efficiency is used when selecting which stock to use automatically (see [How CartonCloud chooses outgoing stock - Stock Selection Methods](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-cartoncloud-chooses-outgoing-stock-stock-selection-methods) for more information). The Pick Efficiency ranges from 1 (being the least efficient) through to 20 (being the most efficient). If creating Pick Faces (for [Replenishment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/replenishment)) you will need to select a Pick Efficiency between 21 and 30 (30 being the most efficient).  Normally, locations that are at ground level, or can be reached by hand, would be considered highly efficient. However, locations that require a fork-lift (or are in deep-racking) would be less efficient. |

---

# Warehouse Management > Warehouses

<a id="add-edit-warehouse"></a>
## Add / Edit Warehouse

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-edit-warehouse_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to add a new warehouse
- Enabling users for the new warehouse
- Edit an existing warehouse

### Purpose

The Add Warehouse page will allow you to create a new Warehouse in your CartonCloud tenancy with its own Address, Warehouse Locations, and Stock. It is also possible to automate deliveries, leaving this warehouse to be allocated to a designated Delivery Run.

Please note: Activating or reactivating Warehouses will incur additional charges per Warehouse. Billing starts automatically once a Warehouse is activated and stops automatically upon deactivation of the Warehouse.
Please contact [accounts@cartoncloud.com](mailto:accounts@cartoncloud.com.au) for further information.

### To add a new Warehouse

- Navigate to the Warehouses page by typing "Warehouses" in the Search for anything bar.
- Select +Add Warehouse .

![add-edit-warehouse-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-edit-warehouse-0.png?width=670&height=328&name=add-edit-warehouse-0.png)

- Enter the Name and Address of the Warehouse .
- Ensure the Active option is enabled if you wish for the Warehouse to be in use immediately. Unticking this field means you will not be able to use the warehouse. Note: Activating additional warehouses will incur additional charges. Please contact accounts@cartoncloud.com. for further information.
- A 'PICKUP FROM WAREHOUSE' Delivery Run will be automatically created and assigned to the new warehouse.
- To update the Delivery Run allocate options you will need to do so after the Warehouse has been created.
- Once completed, click Save.
- You will now see the new Warehouse in the list of Warehouses.
- You can now change to operate within that warehouse using the drop-down menu at the top right of the browser.

![add-edit-warehouse-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-edit-warehouse-1.png?width=670&height=341&name=add-edit-warehouse-1.png)

### Enabling users for the new warehouse

Once you have created the new warehouse, you then need to ensure the correct users have access to the warehouse. Without enabling the warehouse on the users profile, they will not be able to access the warehouse. Click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/kb2/web-app-page-specific-support/administrator-pages/contacts/users/edit-user/adding-removing-warehouses-to-user-profiles) for steps on how to enable a warehouse for a user.

### Edit an existing warehouse

To edit an existing warehouse:

- Navigate to the Warehouses page by typing "Warehouses" in the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Edit against the warehouse you wish to edit.

![add-edit-warehouse-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-edit-warehouse-2.png?width=670&height=212&name=add-edit-warehouse-2.png)

- Update the relevant fields and click Save .
  - Name : name of the warehouse
  - Delivery Run Allocate Options: Use Postcode / Suburb to allocate the delivery, or select Use default Delivery Run if you want all deliveries leaving the warehouse to be allocated to the same Delivery Run, every time. Note, if you are not using a default Delivery Run and and have Zone Sets enabled, CartonCloud will use the Transport Lanes and Zone Sets logic to determine the expected Delivery Run for the Sale Order. See Setting up CartonCloud to automatically allocate Consignments for more information.
  - Address: the address of the warehouse.
  - Pickup Delivery Run: to update the pickup Delivery Run
  - Active : if the warehouse is active and in use, this should be enabled. If the warehouse is no longer in use untick this option.

<a id="setting-up-warehouses-multiple-sitessetting-up-warehouses-multiple-sites"></a>
## Setting up Warehouses (Multiple Sites)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-warehouses-multiple-sitessetting-up-warehouses-multiple-sites_

### Table of Contents

- [Purpose](https://help.cartoncloud.com#purpose)
- How to steps

### Purpose

If you are planning to use CartonCloud's WMS across multiple warehouse sites (for example, Sydney, Brisbane, Melbourne) then you will need to create a Warehouse in the system for each site. You will then be able to create pallet and bulk storage locations within each Warehouse and grant your Customers access to only the relevant Warehouse if required.

Activating additional warehouses will incur additional charges. Please contact [accounts@cartoncloud.com](mailto:accounts@cartoncloud.com.au) for further information.

### How to steps

- Navigate to the Warehouses page by typing Warehouses into the Search for anything bar.
- Click +Add Warehouse
- Name the Warehouse and add the Address.
- Click Save.
- Once saved, you will be able to see all your Warehouses listed.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-18-2025-06-24-57-6176-AM.png?width=670&height=188&name=image-png-Nov-18-2025-06-24-57-6176-AM.png)

- Once a new warehouse has been created, you will need to give users (including yourself) access to the warehouse.
- Navigate to **Contacts** > **Users**.
- Select the user you wish to give access to the warehouse.
- Click **Edit**.
- Select the Warehouse you wish to give them access to, then scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save.
- A new menu option will appear in the top right of the browser, allowing you to select which warehouse you want to operate within.

Any warehouse actions you take within CartonCloud from now on will occur within the currently selected Warehouse. Be sure to always have the correct Warehouse selected for the action you are taking.

---

<a id="warehouse-time-zones"></a>
## Warehouse Time Zones

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/warehouse-time-zones_

### Table of Contents

- How do warehouse time zones work?
- How to change the warehouse time zone
- Considerations when changing the time zone
- Time zones on the mobile app

### How do warehouse time zones work

The time zone selected for your warehouse will apply to all time and date stamps in the warehouse. This includes time and date stamps against orders, email notifications (the time they are sent) and reports.

If you have multiple warehouses in different time zones, you can operate each warehouse in its local time zone by changing the time zone in each warehouse.

### How to change the warehouse time zone

To change the warehouse time zone, you will need to reach out to our Support Team by lodging a case at CartonCloud Help. To help ensure the change is a smooth process, the CartonCloud team will make the change for you.

### Considerations when changing the time zone

Due to changing time zones being a large change to your account, the CartonCloud team will execute the change and help prepare you for the change. However, some key factors to note when changing time zones can be found below:

- The invoicing period you are currently in will either be slightly longer or shorter due to the change in time.
- The time your customers receive notifications will change to reflect the new time zone.
- Storage charges may need to be recalculated if the time zone change spans across a storage period when changing time zones. This will ensure all charges are allocated to the correct storage period.
- If you are using scheduled Bolts in your account and you only have one warehouse and, therefore, one time zone, the time the Bolts are triggered will reflect the new time zone you are using . However, if you have multiple warehouses and time zones , the scheduled Bolt will reflect the timezone of only one of the warehouses.
- On the first day, you change time zones, you may see once-per-day tasks (for example, daily email reports) occur twice that day. For example, if you are changing from the Sydney time zone to the Perth time zone and the time you switch crosses the task time (time the report will send), two tasks could occur on the same day. If the Consignment report is sent at 08:00 Sydney time daily, and the timezone change is made at 09:00 Sydney time (07:00 in Perth), a second Consignment daily report will occur on the same day shortly after 08:00 Perth time.
- If you use the repeating consignments feature and you change time zones before the repeated consignment creation is triggered and the next creation time is in the past relative to the new time zone, these consignments will be considered overdue (as they haven't been created yet). CartonCloud will create these overdue Consignments shortly after you have made the time zone switch.
- The delivered date shown against the Consignment will be reflective off the timezone it was delivered in not the warehouse time zone

### Time zones on the mobile app

All user types on the warehouse mobile app will see the date and time relevant to the warehouse they are operating in. Drivers, on the other hand, will see the local time. This is useful when deliveries are being completed across time zones; this allows for better visibility and clarity for your organisation as to when the delivery was completed.

---

<a id="warehouse-zones"></a>
## Warehouse Zones

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/warehouse-zones_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use Cases
- How to create a Warehouse Zone
- How to update a Warehouse Location with a Warehouse Zone

### Purpose

Warehouse Zones allow you to group Warehouse Locations together to more efficiently plan warehouse operations.

### Use Cases

- Enables zone-based Wave Picking for optimised pick routes.
- Zone-specific management for specialised storage requirements (cold storage, bulk areas and dangerous goods).
- Picker workload distribution based on zone assignments.
- Logical grouping of Warehouse Locations into defined zones, for example, Pick Faces.

### How to create a Warehouse Zone

A Warehouse Zone is created when it is added to a Warehouse Location.

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page, Warehouse > Warehouse Locations .
- Select the Warehouse Location you wish to assign the new Warehouse Zone to.
- Click Edit .

![warehouse-zones-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/warehouse-zones-3.png?width=670&height=375&name=warehouse-zones-3.png)

- Scroll down to Zone and type in the Warehouse Zone name you wish to create. Note, any other Warehouse Zones you have previously created will appear in the drop down as an option.

![warehouse-zones-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/warehouse-zones-1.png?width=670&height=357&name=warehouse-zones-1.png)

- Scroll down and click Save.
- The Warehouse Zone has now been created and will appear as an option when updating the Warehouse Zone for a Warehouse Location.

### How to update a Warehouse Location with a Warehouse Zone

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page, Warehouse > Warehouse Locations .
- Select the Warehouse Location you wish to assign the new Warehouse Zone to.
- Click Edit .

![warehouse-zones-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/warehouse-zones-2.png?width=670&height=371&name=warehouse-zones-2.png)

- Scroll down to Zone and search for the Warehouse Zone you wish to assign to the location. Select the Zone you wish to assign.

**![warehouse-zones-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/warehouse-zones-3.png?width=670&height=375&name=warehouse-zones-3.png)**

- Scroll down and select Save.

<a id="warehouses"></a>
## Warehouses

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/warehouses_

### Table of Contents

- What are warehouses?
- How to navigate to the warehouses page
- Warehouses page
- How to change between warehouses

### What are warehouses

Within CartonCloud, you can create different warehouses to match the number of different warehouses (or, if for a transport operation, your various depots) you have within your operations. For example, if you have one warehouse in Brisbane and another in Perth, you would create two different warehouses, one called Brisbane and the other in Perth. Within each of these warehouses, you have different warehouse locations, products, customers, settings and stock.

You do not need to have multiple warehouses; you can operate with just one.

Please note that activating additional warehouses will incur additional charges. Please contact [accounts@cartoncloud.com](mailto:accounts@cartoncloud.com.au) for further information.

### How to navigate to the warehouses page

- Type Warehouses into the Search for anything bar.

### Warehouses page

From the Warehouses page, you can

Add Warehouses

or

Edit

existing warehouses. For more information, see

Add/Edit Warehouse.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-07-2025-06-27-22-0701-AM.png?width=670&height=190&name=image-png-Nov-07-2025-06-27-22-0701-AM.png)

### How to change between warehouses

To change which warehouse on this page you are working on within CartonCloud, use the drop-down menu in the top right of the screen and select the desired warehouse name. Actions such as the creation of Sale Orders or Purchase orders are made regarding the warehouse chosen in this menu item.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Nov-07-2025-06-26-29-4663-AM.png?width=670&height=208&name=image-png-Nov-07-2025-06-26-29-4663-AM.png)
