# Warehouse Management > Wave Picking

<a id="creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet"></a>
## Creating a Wave Pick for a Run Sheet

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to create a Wave Pick for a Run Sheet
- How to complete a Wave Pick

### Purpose

To create a Wave Pick for a Run Sheet.

Alternatively, you can create a Wave Pick by the Customer. See [Creating a Wave Pick for a single Customer](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Creating-a-Wave-Pick-for-a-single-Customer) for more information.

To create a Wave Pick the Sale Orders you wish to use in the Wave Pick must be set to the "Awaiting Pick and Pack" Status. Those Sale Orders must also have consignments generated from them and those consignments must be already allocated to the Run Sheet you intend to include in the Wave Pick.

### How to create a Wave Pick for a Run Sheet

- Navigate to the Wave Picks page by selecting **Warehouse**>**Wave Picks**.
- Select the green **+Add Wave Pick**button from the top left corner.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-0.png?width=670&height=195&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-0.png)

- Select a Wave Pick Templates from the Prefill Settings drop-down menu or alternatively create a Wave Pick not using an existing template.
- Select Run Sheet from the Wave Pick Type drop-down menu.
- Select the Run Sheet you wish to create the Wave Pick for from the Run Sheets with Wave-Pick Capable Sale Order drop-down menu.

Note, for a Run Sheet to appear in this drop-down option, the Run Sheet will need to have Sale Orders associated with it that are in 'Awaiting Pick and Pack' status

- Select the Wave Pick Process Type from the Wave Pick Process Type drop-down menu.

See [Wave Pick Process Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Wave-Pick-Process-Types) for more information regarding the different Process Types and which will be best for your operations.

- If you wish to change the auto-generated name, then you can do so in the **Wave Pick Name**field.
- Select if you wish to filter the available Sale Order list by if the order is urgent or not.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-1.png?width=670&height=197&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-1.png)

- Select the Sale Orders you wish to include in the Wave Pick by ticking the **Select** box in the far left column.
- Once all relevant orders are selected, click **Begin Wave Pick.**

Note, when Sale Orders are added to a Wave Pick, their status is automatically updated to 'Packing in Progress'

### How to complete a Wave Pick

Once you have created the Wave, Pick you then have two options for completing the Wave Pick. You can either complete the Wave Pick;

- On the mobile app
- On the web app
- On the web app using paper

**Completing the Wave Pick on the mobile app**

For instructions on completing the wave pick through the mobile app, see [Scan Wave Picking](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Scan+Wave+Picking).

**Completing the Wave Pick on the web app**

When completing the Wave Pick on the web app, you can either pick **per-product** or **per-order**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-2.png?width=670&height=251&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-2.png)

**Picking Per-Product on the Web App**

- Select **View Pick Sheet** next to each product.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-3.png?width=670&height=178&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-3.png)

- Pick the required quantities. As the stock is picked, enter the quantity and select the **Completed** box.
- Select the green **Complete Picking** button.
- The **Product Status** will inform you if the picking has been completed or not.

**Picking Per-Order on the Web App**

- Select the blue **Pack Sale Order** button next to each Sale Order.

- Picking per order uses the same interface as regular, non-wave picking.
- Enter the **PACKED QTY**.
- Select the green **Finished Packing** button.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-4.png?width=670&height=170&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-4.png)

- You will be directed to the Sale Order/Consignment Screen. To go back to the Wave Pick from the Sale Order, select **Go Back to Wave Pick**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-5.png?width=670&height=171&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-5.png)

**Completing a Wave Pick on the Web App**

- Once all products/orders have been picked, select the green **Complete Wave Pick**button on the bottom of the screen.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-6.png?width=670&height=124&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-6.png)

- This will update the status of all orders to 'Pack' and delete the Wave Pick.

**To complete a Wave Pick using paper**

- Select the blue **Print/Export** button at the bottom of the screen.
- Select **Export Bulk Pick List**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-7.png?width=670&height=124&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-7.png)

- Open the downloaded XSL file (example of the file below).

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-8.png?width=670&height=156&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-8.png)

- Complete picks using the paper to mark off products as they are picked.
- To complete the packing process, select the blue **Print/Export**button at the bottom of the screen and click **Export Individual Pick Lists**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-9.png?width=670&height=88&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-run-sheet-9.png)

Even if using paper to complete the Wave Pick, you will need to complete the Wave Pick on the web app. See [Completing the Wave Pick](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+a+Wave+Pick+for+a+Run+sheet#CreatingaWavePickforaRunsheet-web)on the web app for more information.

---

<a id="creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer"></a>
## Creating a Wave Pick for a single Customer

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to create a Wave Pick for a single customer
- How to complete a Wave Pick
  - Picking per-product on the web app
  - Picking per-order on the web app
  - Completing a Wave Pick on the web app
- To complete a Wave Pick using paper ​​​​​​​

### Purpose

To create a Wave Pick for a single Customer. If you wish to create a Run Sheet for more than one Customer, you will need to follow [these](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Creating-a-Wave-Pick-for-multiple-Customers) steps.

### Prerequisites

- The Sale Orders you wish to use in the Wave Pick must be in 'Awaiting Pick and Pack' status.

### How to create a Wave Pick for a single Customer

- Navigate to the Wave Picks page by selecting **Warehouse**>**Wave Picks**.
- Select the green **+Add Wave Pick**button from the top left corner.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-0.png?width=670&height=195&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-0.png)

- Select a [Wave Pick Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Wave-Pick-Templates) from the Prefill Settings drop-down menu or alternatively create a Wave Pick not using an existing template.
- Wave Picks can be automatically created using Advanced Automation . This is a WMS Premium feature only please see here for more information.
- Select **Customer** from the Wave Pick Type drop-down menu.
- Select the Customer you wish to create the **Wave Pick for from the Customers with Wave-Pick Capable Sale Orders** drop-down menu.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-1.png?width=670&height=219&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-1.png)

- Select the Wave Pick Process Type. See [Wave Pick Process Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Wave-Pick-Process-Types) for more information regarding the different Process Types and which will be best for your operations.
- Edit the Wave Pick Name if you wish to change it from the auto-generated name.
- You can then have a number of filters to choose from to select which Sale Orders you wish to add to the Wave Pick. These filters include:
  - Product: the products on the Sale Order.
  - Expected Delivery Run: the expected Delivery Run of the Sale Order.
  - Urgent order: if the order is urgent or not.
  - SKU Count: the number of SKU's on the Sale Order.
  - Quantity Count: the quantity of item on the Sale Order.
  - Ship Date : the Ship Date of the Sale Order.
  - Required Delivery Date : the Required Delivery Date of the Sale Order.
  - Product Type : the Product Type of the products on the Sale Order. For more information on Product Types see here .
  - Product Group : the Product Group of the products on the Sale Order. For more information on Product Groups see here .
  - Products located in Warehouse Zones : to include products located in specific Warehouse Zones .
  - Product Filters Behaviour: if a product, product type or product group is selected then the product filter behaviour can be selected. The options include:
    - Find orders if they contain a product that matches the selected filters: Sales Orders that contain products selected, but the orders can also contain other products not selected.
    - Find orders only if all products match the selected filters: Sale Orders that only contain products selected.
    - Exclude orders containing products which match the selected products: Sale Orders containing products selected will not be included.

- When utilising the Product filter you will need to select a Product Filter Behaviour.
  - **Find orders containing at least one of the selected Products:** Sale Orders containing at least one of the selected Products will show as an available Sale Order to add to the Wave Pick.
  - **Find orders containing only the selected Products**: only Sale Orders with only the selected Product will show as an available Sale Order to add to the Wave Pick.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-2.png?width=670&height=371&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-2.png)

- This will now show you all available Sale Orders according to the filters selected that can be added to the Wave Pick (for a Sale Order to appear here it must be in a Awaiting Pick and Pack status and not be assigned to another Wave Pick)
- Select the Sale Orders you wish to include in the Wave Pick by ticking the Select box in the far left column.
- Once all relevant orders are selected, click **Begin Wave Pick**.

Note, when Sale Orders are added to a Wave Pick, their status is automatically updated to 'Packing in Progress'

### How to complete a Wave Pick

Once you have created the Wave Pick you then have two options for completing the Wave Pick. You can either complete the Wave Pick;

- On the mobile app
- On the web app
- On the web app using paper

**Completing the Wave Pick on the mobile app**

For instructions on completing the wave pick through the mobile app please see [Scan Wave Picking](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Scan-Wave-Picking)

**Completing the Wave Pick on the web app**

When completing the Wave Pick on the web app, you can either pick **per-product** or **per-order**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-3.png?width=670&height=251&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-3.png)

**Picking Per-Product on the Web App**

- Select **View Pick Sheet** next to each product.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-4.png?width=670&height=178&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-4.png)

- Pick the required quantities. As the stock is picked, enter the quantity and select the **Completed** box.
- Select the green **Complete Picking** button.
- The **Product Status** will inform you if the picking has been completed or not.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-5.png?width=670&height=128&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-5.png)

**Picking Per-Order on the Web App**

- Select the blue **Pack Sale Order** button next to each Sale Order.
- Picking per order uses the same interface as regular, non-wave picking.
- Enter the **PACKED QTY**.
- Select the green **Finished Packing** button.
- You will be directed to the Sale Order/Consignment Screen. To go back to the Wave Pick from the Sale Order, select **Go Back to Wave Pick**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-6.png?width=670&height=171&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-6.png)

**Completing a Wave Pick on the Web App**

- Once all products/orders have been picked, select the green **Complete Wave Pick**button on the bottom of the screen.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-7.png?width=670&height=124&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-7.png)

- This will update the status of all orders to 'Pack' and delete the Wave Pick.

**To complete a Wave Pick using paper**

- Select the blue **Print/Export** button at the bottom of the screen.
- Select Export Bulk Pick List .

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-8.png?width=670&height=124&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-8.png)

- Open the downloaded XSL file (example of the file below).

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-9.png?width=670&height=156&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-a-single-customer-9.png)

- Complete picks using the paper to mark off products as they are picked.
- To complete the packing process, select the blue **Print/Export**button at the bottom of the screen and click **Export Individual Pick Lists**.

Even if using paper to complete the Wave Pick, you will need to complete the Wave Pick on the web app.

---

<a id="creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers"></a>
## Creating a Wave Pick for multiple Customers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to create a single Wave Pick for multiple customers
- How to complete a Wave Pick

### Purpose

To create a single Wave Pick for multiple Customers.

To create a Wave Pick, the Sale Orders you wish to use in the Wave Pick must be in an 'Awaiting Pick and Pack' status.

### How to create a single Wave Pick for multiple customers

- Navigate to the Wave Picks page by selecting Warehouse > Wave Picks .
- Select the green +Add Wave Pick button from the top left corner.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-0.png?width=670&height=353&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-0.png)

- Select a Wave Pick Templates from the Prefill Settings drop-down menu or alternatively create a Wave Pick not using an existing template.
- Wave Picks can be automatically created using Advanced Automation . This is a WMS Premium feature only please see here for more information.
- Select Customer from the Wave Pick Type drop-down menu.
- Select Multiple Customers from the Customers with Wave-Pick Capable Sale Orders drop down.
- You can then have a number of filters to choose from to select which Sale Orders you wish to add to the Wave Pick. These filters include:
-
  - Customer: the Customer of the Sale Order.
  - Product: the products on the Sale Order.
  - Urgent order: if the order is urgent or not.
  - Expected Delivery Run: the expected Delivery Run of the Sale Order.
  - SKU Count: the number of SKU's on the Sale Order.
  - Quantity Count: the quantity of item on the Sale Order.
  - Ship Date : the Ship Date of the Sale Order.
  - Required Delivery Date : the Required Delivery Date of the Sale Order.
  - Product Type : the Product Type of the products on the Sale Order. For more information on Product Types see here .
  - Product Group : the Product Group of the products on the Sale Order. For more information on Product Groups see here .
  - Products located in Warehouse Zones : to include products located in specific Warehouse Zones .
  - Product Filters Behaviour: if a product, product type or product group is selected then the product filter behaviour can be selected. The options include:
    - Find orders if they contain a product that matches the selected filters: Sales Orders that contain products selected, but the orders can also contain other products not selected.
    - Find orders only if all products match the selected filters: Sale Orders that only contain products selected.
    - Exclude orders containing products which match the selected products: Sale Orders containing products selected will not be included.

Note: the Product filter is not restricted by the Customer filter and can be utilised independently of the Customer filter.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-1.png?width=670&height=374&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-1.png)

- When utilising the Product filter you will need to select a Product Filter Behaviour.
  - Find orders containing at least one of the selected Products: Sale Orders containing at least one of the selected Products will show as an available Sale Order to add to the Wave Pick.
  - Find orders containing only the selected Products : only Sale Orders with only the selected Product will show as an available Sale Order to add to the Wave Pick.
- This will now show you all available Sale Orders according to the filters selected that can be added to the Wave Pick (for a Sale Order to appear here it must be in a Awaiting Pick and Pack status and not be assigned to another Wave Pick).
- Select the Wave Pick Process Type from the Wave Pick Process Type drop-down menu (see Wave Pick Process Types for more information regarding the different process types and which will be best for your operations).
- Update the auto generated Wave Pick Name if you wish.
- Select the Sale Orders you wish to include in the Wave Pick by ticking the Select box in the far left column.
- Once all relevant orders are selected, click Begin Wave Pick.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-2.png?width=670&height=356&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-2.png)

- Note, when Sale Orders are added to a Wave Pick, their status is automatically updated to 'Packing in Progress'.

### How to complete a Wave Pick

Once you have created the Wave Pick you then have a few options for how you complete the Wave Pick. You can either complete the Wave Pick:

- On the mobile app
- On the web app
- On the web app using paper

#### **Completing the Wave Pick on the mobile app**

For instructions on completing the wave pick through the mobile app please see [Scan Wave Picking](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Scan-Wave-Picking)

#### **Completing the Wave Pick on the web app**

When completing the Wave Pick on the web app, you can either pick **per-product** or **per-order**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-3.png?width=670&height=251&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-3.png)

#### **Picking Per-Product on the Web App**

- Select **View Pick Sheet** next to each product.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-4.png?width=670&height=178&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-4.png)

- Pick the required quantities. As the stock is picked, enter the quantity and select the **Completed** box.
- Select the green **Complete Picking** button.
- The **Product Status** will inform you if the picking has been completed or not.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-5.png?width=670&height=128&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-5.png)

#### **Picking Per-Order on the Web App**

- Select the blue **Pack Sale Order** button next to each Sale Order.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-6.png?width=670&height=171&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-6.png)

- Picking per order uses the same interface as regular, non-wave picking.
- Enter the **PACKED QTY**.
- Select the green **Finished Packing** button.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-7.png?width=670&height=170&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-7.png)

- You will be directed to the Sale Order/Consignment Screen. To go back to the Wave Pick from the Sale Order, select **Go Back to Wave Pick**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-8.png?width=670&height=171&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-8.png)

#### **Completing a Wave Pick on the Web App**

- Once all products/orders have been picked, select the green **Complete Wave Pick**button on the bottom of the screen.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-9.png?width=670&height=124&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-9.png)

- This will update the status of all orders to 'Pack' and delete the Wave Pick.

#### **To complete a Wave Pick using paper**

- Select the blue **Print/Export** button at the bottom of the screen.
- Select **Export Bulk Pick List**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-10.png?width=670&height=124&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-10.png)

- Open the downloaded XSL file (example of the file below).

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-11.png?width=670&height=156&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-11.png)

- Complete picks using the paper to mark off products as they are picked.
- To complete the packing process, select the blue **Print/Export**button at the bottom of the screen and click **Export Individual Pick Lists**.

![creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-12.png?width=670&height=88&name=creating-a-wave-pick-for-multiple-customers-12.png)

Even if using paper to complete the Wave Pick, you will need to complete the Wave Pick on the web app. See [Completing the Wave Pick](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+a+Wave+Pick+for+a+single+Customer#CreatingaWavePickforasingleCustomer-web)on the web app for more information.

<a id="label-sorting"></a>
## Label Sorting

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/label-sorting_

### Table of Contents

- Wave picking label sorting
- Multiple field sorting
- Example of multiple field sorting
- Removing unwanted sort options

### Wave picking label sorting

Sale Order Picking Labels that are printed from Wave Picks can be sorted using the "Picking Label Sort Options" setting located in Organisation Settings → Features & Options → Picking Configuration.

![label-sorting-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-sorting-0.png?width=670&height=289&name=label-sorting-0.png)

This option allows for the labels to be sorted by multiple fields. The available fields are currently:

- Sale Order ID
- Product Type (eg. Chilled, Frozen, etc)
- Product SKU (Product Code)
- Sale Order Reference
- Warehouse Location (AA-01, AA-02, etc)

The options Product Type, Product SKU, Sale Order Reference and Warehouse Location are sorted in ascending alphabetical order. Sale Order ID sorts in ascending numeric order.

### Multiple Field Sorting

To sort labels using multiple fields, select the fields you wish to use and then drag the boxes around until they are in the order you wish to use. When using multiple fields, the labels are sorted using the options from left to right.

### Example of Multiple Field sorting

Say that you wanted to sort by Product Type, then by Warehouse Location, then by Product SKU.

The field would look like this:

![label-sorting-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-sorting-1.png?width=670&height=156&name=label-sorting-1.png)

### Removing Unwanted Sort Options

To Remove any unwanted sort options click the little 'x' icon on the tag for the option you wish to remove.

---

<a id="pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking"></a>
## Pick by Delivery Run using Wave Picking

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to pick by Delivery Run by creating a Wave Pick

### Purpose

If you wish to pick Sale Orders by Delivery Run, it is possible to create a Wave Pick.

### How to pick by Delivery Run by creating a Wave Pick

- Navigate to the Wave Pick page, Warehouse > Wave Picks .
- Click +Add Wave Pick .

![pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-0.png?width=670&height=109&name=pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-0.png)

- Select Customer as the Wave Pick Type .
- Select the Customer you wish to run the Wave Pick for.
- Select Split Pick and Pack Processes as the Wave Pick Process Type.

![pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-1.png?width=670&height=222&name=pick-by-delivery-run-using-wave-picking-1.png)

- Name the Wave Pick.

You may want to name it the Delivery Run.

- Order the Sale Orders by Expected Delivery Run by clicking the title Expected Delivery Run.
- Use the tick box to select the orders you wish to add to the Wave Pick. Because they are ordered by Expected Delivery, Run, you will be able to add all Sale Orders for the one Delivery Run to the Wave Pick.
- Scroll down to the bottom and click Begin Wave Pick .

You can repeat this process for each Delivery Run.

<a id="view-and-edit-wave-pick"></a>
## View and edit a Wave Pick

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/view-and-edit-wave-pick_

### Table of Contents

- Wave Pick List View
- Edit a Wave Pick in progress
- Edit a completed Wave Pick
- Wave Pick History

### Wave Pick List View

From the Wave Pick screen you can view all 'In Progress' and 'Completed' Wave Picks by utilising the In Progress and Completed tabs. In addition, you can use the Filter tab to filter the Wave Pick list view and find the relevant Wave Pick.

Wave Pick List View filters:

- Customer : the Customer of the Wave Pick. Even if it is a Multi-Customer Wave Pick the Wave Pick will still show if the Customer has Sale Orders on the Wave Pick.
- Status: status of the Wave Pick - In Progress or Completed.
- Type: the Wave Pick type, either Customer or Run Sheet.
- Process Type: the Wave Pick Process Type either, Bulk Pick, Split Pick and Pack Processes, Combined Pick and Pack.
- Date Added: the date the Wave Pick was added.
- Date Completed: the date the Wave Pick was completed.

![view-and-edit-wave-pick-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-and-edit-wave-pick-0.png?width=670&height=332&name=view-and-edit-wave-pick-0.png)

### Edit a Wave Pick in progress

The Wave Pick Type can be edited while the Wave Pick is in progress. This makes it easy to switch between workflows such as Split Pick & Pack and Pick to Tote without deleting or recreating the wave.

To update the Wave Pick Type:

- Select Edit against the Wave Pick.
- From the Wave Type drop down select the Wave Pick Type you wish to update it to.

![view-and-edit-wave-pick-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-and-edit-wave-pick-1.png?width=670&height=193&name=view-and-edit-wave-pick-1.png)

- Select Save .

Note: All picking and packing statuses for items in the wave will be reset.

### Edit a completed Wave Pick

You can not edit Completed Wave Picks only delete them. To delete a completed Wave Pick:

- Select the Completed tab heading.
- Select View against the relevant Wave Pick.

![view-and-edit-wave-pick-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-and-edit-wave-pick-2.png?width=670&height=353&name=view-and-edit-wave-pick-2.png)

- Select Delete Wave Pick .

![view-and-edit-wave-pick-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-and-edit-wave-pick-3.png?width=670&height=353&name=view-and-edit-wave-pick-3.png)

### Wave Pick History

Against the Wave Pick, you can see the history of the Wave Pick, showing when it was created, what orders were added or removed and if notes were added to the Wave Pick. This makes it easier to track changes and provide visibility to other users on the Wave Pick.

To access the History, select the History tab on the Wave Pick:

![view-and-edit-wave-pick-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-and-edit-wave-pick-4.png?width=670&height=285&name=view-and-edit-wave-pick-4.png)

You can also add comments to the history against the Wave Pick, by writing a comment in the Comments box and selecting **Add history**.

![view-and-edit-wave-pick-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-and-edit-wave-pick-5.png?width=670&height=285&name=view-and-edit-wave-pick-5.png)

<a id="advanced-automation-wave-picks"></a>
## Wave Pick Auto Generation (Advanced Automation)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-automation-wave-picks_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to steps
- Checking Automated Wave Pick History

### Purpose

Wave Pick Auto Generation allows for Wave Picks to be automatically generated on a defined schedule. By selecting a Wave Pick Template you can then define criteria on when a Wave Pick should be created and then what day and time it should be generated. This enables an efficient and streamlined wave pick process.

### Prerequisites

- Wave Pick Auto Generation is included in Advanced Automation, wich is only available for WMS Premium accounts. Please reach out to the team here for more information.
- You must first create Wave Pick Templates before creating the automation.
- Wave Pick Auto Generation will only work for Wave Pick Types of Multiple Customers and Single Customer. It will not work for Run Sheet Wave Pick Type.

### How to steps

- Navigate to the Wave Pick page, **Warehouse**>**Wave Picks**.
- Select **+Add Wave Pick**.
- Select a Wave Pick Template from the **Prefill Templates**. If you have not yet set up a Wave Pick Template please do so following the steps [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Wave-Pick-Templates).

![advanced-automation-wave-picks-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-wave-picks-0.png?width=670&height=125&name=advanced-automation-wave-picks-0.png)

- Select **Configure Automation**.

![advanced-automation-wave-picks-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-wave-picks-1.png?width=670&height=159&name=advanced-automation-wave-picks-1.png)

- Select the minimum and maximum number of Sale Orders to be included in each automated Wave Pick.

![advanced-automation-wave-picks-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-wave-picks-2.png?width=670&height=199&name=advanced-automation-wave-picks-2.png)

Note:

- The orders that meet the Wave Pick template settings will be found and then if there are enough orders to meet the minimum a Wave Pick will be generated.
- If the number of Sale Orders that match the Wave Pick Template does not meet the minimum number of orders specified then the automated Wave Pick will not run, regardless if there are orders that meet the Wave Pick template settings.
- If the maximum number of orders per automated Wave Pick is 30 and there are 60 Sale Orders that meet the Wave Pick template settings then two wave picks of 30 orders each will be automatically generated.

- Create a schedule for the automated Wave Pick to run from. This will determine the day and time that CartonCloud will attempt to generate Wave Picks using the selected Prefill Templates.
- Click into the **Days** field and select the days of the week you wish the Wave Pick to run.
- In the **Times** field click in to select the times on each day selected that the automated Wave Pick will run.

![advanced-automation-wave-picks-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-wave-picks-3.png?width=670&height=172&name=advanced-automation-wave-picks-3.png)

- Select **Save Schedule**.
- Name the automation and click Save .

![advanced-automation-wave-picks-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-wave-picks-4.png?width=507&height=259&name=advanced-automation-wave-picks-4.png)

- You can have multiple schedules running simultaneously for the one Wave Pick template. For example, you may have a weekday morning schedule and a weekend afternoon schedule for the one Wave Pick template.
- To update an existing schedule, ensure the schedule is selected, make the necessary changes and then click **Update Schedule**. Note, to **update an existing Schedule** select **Update Schedule**and to **create a new Schedule** select **Save Schedule**.

![advanced-automation-wave-picks-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-wave-picks-5.png?width=670&height=176&name=advanced-automation-wave-picks-5.png)

- Text will appear listing all of the schedules that will run for the selected Wave Pick template.

![advanced-automation-wave-picks-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-wave-picks-6.png?width=670&height=167&name=advanced-automation-wave-picks-6.png)

### Checking Automated Wave Pick History

To check the history of Automated Wave Picks:

- Select **More**>**Bolt Log**.
- Within the Bolt Log, the Automated Wave Pick history will display.
- The name of the Wave Pick Template and the created date of the schedule will display as the name of the log in the history.

![advanced-automation-wave-picks-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-wave-picks-7.png?width=670&height=262&name=advanced-automation-wave-picks-7.png)

---

<a id="wave-pick-process-types"></a>
## Wave Pick Process Types

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/wave-pick-process-types_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Bulk Pick
- Split Pick and Pack
- Combination
- Pick to Tote

### Purpose

Wave Pick process types determine how a Wave Pick is configured and how it is completed. A Wave Pick process type must be selected when creating a Wave Pick. There are four different process types each designed for differing warehouse requirements and processes:

- Bulk Pick
- Split Pick and Pack
- Combination
- Pick to Tote

Each process type is designed to optimise the picking workflow and streamline your operations.

See [Wave Picking](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/wave-picking) for more information on Wave Picking and how to create a Wave Pick.

### Wave Pick Process Types

#### Bulk Pick

When using Bulk Pick, you will be picking orders simultaneously by the product rather than order-by-order. This is especially useful if there are limited pick-face locations to pick from and forklifts are required to pick the products.Once an order is marked as picked the Sale Order will be updated to the 'Packed' status. When using this workflow the picking and packing processes are combined into one. Once the orders are picked they will be moved out of the Warehouse. For example, the orders are moved to a dock or delivery truck where they will be sorted for delivery using their labels.

Please note, if you are wanting to capture certain custom fields on outbound (i.e: recording serial numbers as they ship), you can not use a Bulk Pick Wave Pick. You will need to use either Split Pick and Pack or Combination Wave Pick.

**Example:**

![wave-pick-process-types-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-process-types-0.png?width=670&height=179&name=wave-pick-process-types-0.png)

A soft drink 3PL is using Bulk Wave Pick by the Run Sheet. They will pick all the different orders (by the soft drink type, not the Sale Order) and load them into the delivery truck. As the driver delivers the goods he will complete the 'packing' process by sorting the soft drinks by the order using their labels.

#### Split Pick and Pack

Split Pick and Pack works similarly to Bulk Pick, where orders will be picked by the product, not order-by-order, however, the packing and picking process is separated. Once picking is completed, the user will be prompted to then pack each Sale Order individually, however, this will not necessarily be the same user. In some cases, the pick and pack process may be split, in which case the packer will take over the wave pick once the picking is complete. This is useful when picking and packing occur at two different locations in the warehouse or completed by a different user.

**Example:**

![wave-pick-process-types-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-process-types-1.png?width=670&height=177&name=wave-pick-process-types-1.png)

The 3PL has a separate area for where packing occurs and two teams, one for picking and one for packing. Pickers will pick all orders by the product and then move the goods to the packing area where another team will pack the orders (using the wave pick) ready for dispatch.

#### **Combination**

Combination wave pick allows multiple Sale Orders to be grouped together for either a specific Customer or Run Sheet. This is the exact same way a Sale Order is normally picked and packed, however, it provides a way for orders to be grouped and then assigned to pickers. The Wave Pick can be assigned to the picker by naming the Wave Pick by the pickers name.

![wave-pick-process-types-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-process-types-2.png?width=551&height=293&name=wave-pick-process-types-2.png)

The 3PL has multiple pickers to which they assign wave picks. The pickers will complete both the pick and pack process as they move through the Warehouse.

#### Pick to Tote

Pick to Tote is a picking workflow designed to reduce the time spent picking. This is achieved by allowing pickers to pick multiple orders (usually 10-30) simultaneously, sorting them into totes as they go. This reduces the total walking time through the warehouse and the speed of the picking process. After picking the trolley containing the totes is wheeled back to a packing station where the packing is completed.

![wave-pick-process-types-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-process-types-3.png?width=670&height=215&name=wave-pick-process-types-3.png)

---

<a id="wave-pick-templates"></a>
## Wave Pick Templates

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/wave-pick-templates_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use Cases and Benefits
- Considerations
- How to create a Template
- How to apply a Template
- How to delete a Template
- How to update the Default Template

### Purpose

To create a Wave Pick template with pre-determined filters and settings that can be applied when creating a Wave Pick.

### Use Cases and Benefits

- Increased efficiency when creating Wave Picks.
- Easily apply the same logic to Wave Picks you create regularly.
- Ensure consistency when creating Wave Picks.

### Considerations

- Wave Pick Templates will only work for Single Customer and Multiple Customer Wave Pick Types. It will not work for the Run Sheet Wave Pick Type.
- For a completely automated Wave Pick workflow see Advanced Automation - Wave Picks

### How to create a Template

- Navigate to the Wave Pick page, Warehouse > Wave Picks .
- Click Add Wave Pick .
- Select the filters you wish to apply for the Wave Pick, including the Wave Pick name.

![wave-pick-templates-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-templates-1.png?width=670&height=351&name=wave-pick-templates-1.png)

- Click Save Settings .

![wave-pick-templates-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-templates-2.png?width=670&height=309&name=wave-pick-templates-2.png)

- Enter the name for the Wave Pick template and click Save .

![wave-pick-templates-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-templates-3.png?width=670&height=296&name=wave-pick-templates-3.png)

- This will now save the Wave Pick filters as a Template and be available in the Prefill Settings drop-down menu when creating your Wave Pick.

### How to apply a Template

- Navigate to the Wave Pick page, Warehouse > Wave Picks .
- Click Add Wave Pick .
- Against the Prefill Settings select the drop-down arrow. Select the template you wish to apply for the Wave Pick.

![wave-pick-templates-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-templates-5.png?width=670&height=292&name=wave-pick-templates-5.png)

- This will automatically apply the saved filters and search for Sale Orders. You can then select which Sale Orders you wish to add to the Wave Pick.

### How to delete a Template

- Navigate to the Wave Pick page, Warehouse > Wave Picks .
- Click Add Wave Pick .
- Against the Prefill Settings select the drop-down arrow. Select the template you wish to delete.
- Once the template is selected, click the Delete Settings button.

![wave-pick-templates-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-templates-7.png?width=670&height=299&name=wave-pick-templates-7.png)

### How to update a Template

The Default template is the template applied automatically when you create a Wave Pick and no other template is selected. To update the filters and settings for the Default template:

- Navigate to the Wave Pick page, Warehouse > Wave Picks .
- Click Add Wave Pick .

![wave-pick-templates-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-templates-8.png?width=670&height=354&name=wave-pick-templates-8.png)

- Select the template you wish to update from the Prefill Settings drop-down. Alternatively, if you are updating the Default template this will already be selected.
- Update the filters and settings.
- Select Update Settings .

![wave-pick-templates-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-pick-templates-9.png?width=670&height=292&name=wave-pick-templates-9.png)

---

<a id="wave-picking"></a>
## Wave Picking Explained

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/wave-picking_

### Table of Contents

- What is Wave Picking?
- How to create a Wave Pick
- Wave Pick Templates
- Wave Pick settings
  - How to forcefully mark orders as picked and packed

### What is Wave Picking?

Wave Picking is a way of picking multiple Sale Orders simultaneously. Wave Picking helps increase picking efficiency and enables several different workflows.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/nqbpnA7lrBk

### How to create a Wave Pick

There are three ways in which you can create a Wave Pick:

- [Creating a Wave Pick for a single Customer](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+a+Wave+Pick+for+a+single+Customer)
- [Creating a Wave Pick for multiple Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Creating-a-Wave-Pick-for-multiple-Customers)
- [Creating a Wave Pick for a Run Sheet](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+a+Wave+Pick+for+a+Run+sheet)

When creating a Wave PIck you must select a [Wave Pick Process Type](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Wave-Pick-Process-Types).

### How to complete a Wave Pick

Wave picking can be completed using the web app, the web app and paper or the mobile app.

It is recommended that you create the Wave Picks using the web app and then complete the picks using the CartonCloud mobile app (see [Scan Wave Picking](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Scan-Wave-Picking)  for instructions on how to run a Wave Pick on the mobile application).

### Wave Pick Templates

Wave Pick Templates allow you to more easily create Wave Picks with pre-defined (saved) search filters and settings. This enables a seamless and optimised Wave Pick creation process. See [Wave Pick Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Wave-Pick-Templates) for more information.

### Wave Pick Settings

You can configure several Wave Picking settings at both the [Organisation](https://help.cartoncloud.com#organisation)and [Customer](https://help.cartoncloud.com#customer)levels.

**Organisation Settings**

**How to access Wave Pick Organisation Settings:**

- In the Main menu of CartonCloud, select **More** > **Organisation Settings** > **Features and Options** tab.
- Scroll down to the Picking Configuration section
- All Organisation level Wave Pick settings can be found and updated here
- Don't forget to select **Save** at the bottom of the page if you make changes.

**The settings that can be configured at the Organisation Settings**

![wave-picking-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-picking-0.png?width=670&height=386&name=wave-picking-0.png)

| **Setting** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- |
| Allow Forceful Completion of Run Sheet or Multiple Customer Type Wave Picks | Sets whether or not users can forcefully complete Run Sheet or multiple customer type Wave Picks. This is only controlled at the Organisation Settings level as Run Sheets can contain multiple Customers. |
| Default Wave Pick Process Type | Sets the default Wave Pick process type used when adding a new Wave Pick.   The default value for the Customer Setting is to "Use Organisation Setting". Therefore, if you wish to set the default process type for **all** of your customers, you can change this Organisation Setting, and it will be applied to all Customers. However, if you have specific customer requirements, you will need to change the Wave Pick Process Type at the Customer Settings.   Note, if running a Wave Pick for multiple Customers the Organisation Settings will be applied. |
| Default Wave Picking Tab | Sets which tab is displayed initially when viewing a Wave Pick. This can either be the Products or Sale Orders tab. Regardless of your selection, you will be able to switch between the two views. |
| Print One Label per Sale Order Product | Sets whether or not to print one label for each Sale Order Product when in a Wave Pick instead of calculating measures and printing the appropriate number of labels. |
| The format of labels printed for Consignments from a Run Sheet type Wave Pick | Sets what format the PDF generated for labels will be done from a Run Sheet type Wave Pick. |

**Customer Settings**

**How to access Wave Pick Customer Settings**

- In the main menu of CartonCloud, select **Contacts** > **Customers**
- On the View, Customer page, select the Edit bottom towards the bottom left of the page
- Navigate to the **Warehouse Management** tab > then Wave Picks subtab.
- All Customer level Wave Pick settings can be found and updated here
- Don't forget to select **Save** at the bottom of the page if you make changes.

![wave-picking-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-picking-1.png?width=670&height=237&name=wave-picking-1.png)

| Setting | Explanation |
| --- | --- |
| Allow Wave Pick Sale Orders and Sale Order Products to be forcefully completed | This setting will allow Sale Orders, Sale Order Products, and the Wave Picks they are a part of to be completed without individually checking off the products. |
| Default Wave Pick Process Type | This setting determines the default Wave Pick Type for the Customer. If you have configured a default Pick Type at the Organisation Settings, this will automatically apply to every Customer unless you change this setting. |
| Disable Quantity Confirmation On Pick Sheet | This setting will allow Products in the Product Pick Screen of a Wave Pick to be completed without entering a quantity. Enabling this option removes the quantity input on the Pick Screen. |

### How to forcefully mark orders picked and packed

Once the above forcefully mark orders as picked and pack setting has been enabled (for either a run sheet or customer, depending on your requirement), a new button will appear on the View Wave Pick page.

![wave-picking-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-picking-2.png?width=670&height=234&name=wave-picking-2.png)

To forcefully complete the picking of select Products, select which products you would like to mark as picked.

![wave-picking-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-picking-3.png?width=670&height=194&name=wave-picking-3.png)

- Select the Mark Picked button.
- To confirm those products as picked, select the option Selected Sale Order Products, then click Mark Selected as Picked .
- Otherwise, mark the entire Wave Pick as picked by selecting Whole Wave Pick.
- Once all Products are marked as Picking Completed, it is possible to move on to the Packing process (provided the Wave pick is a split pick and process type).
- The packing process can either be forcefully completed as well by following the steps below or completed by marking off products either on the web app or mobile app.
- Forcefully completing the packing process of a Sale order is much the same as forcefully completing picking.
- To do this, select the Sale Order you wish to mark as packed, and then select Mark Packed for a new box to appear.
- A new box will appear, allowing you to either mark the select Sale Orders as packed, or mark the entire Wave pick as packed.
- Select Mark Selected as Packed to confirm.

**Quantity Confirmation Options**

With the option **disabled**:

![wave-picking-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-picking-4.png?width=670&height=133&name=wave-picking-4.png)

With the option **enabled**:

![wave-picking-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wave-picking-5.png?width=670&height=130&name=wave-picking-5.png)

# Warehouse Management > WMS Premium

<a id="advanced-automation"></a>
## Advanced Automation

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-automation_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- Overview
- Workflows
- Prerequisites

### Purpose

Advanced Automation includes two features - Wave Pick Auto Generation and Replenishment Auto Generation. These two features provide the ability to configure Wave Picks and Replenishments to be automatically generated.

Advanced Automation is only available for [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) accounts. For more information, please reach out to the team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

### Benefits

- Increases efficiency in the Wave Pick and Replenishment process.
- Removes the number of manual steps and tasks in the process.
- Reduces the risk of error as the repetitive task of creating the correct Wave Pick and Replenishment is removed.
- Helps to streamline warehouse processes.

### Overview

Create a pre-defined Wave Pick and/or Replenishment using templates and set a schedule for when the Wave Pick and/or Replenishment will be created. For example, you may have a Replenishment run at the end of each day or a daily Wave Pick the team completes each morning.

### Workflows

- Wave Pick Auto Generation
- Replenishment Auto Generation

### Prerequisites

Advanced Automation is only available for [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) accounts. For more information, please reach out to the team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

<a id="advanced-backordering"></a>
## Advanced Backordering

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-backordering_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use Cases
- Feature Settings

Note: Advanced Backordering is only available for accounts with [WMS Premium.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/WMS-Premium)For more information on WMS Premium and to upgrade your account, please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).

### Purpose

Advanced Backordering enhances CartonCloud’s standard [Backorder Management](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Backorder-Management) workflows with intelligent automation and greater control over stock allocation and order splitting. This functionality is available exclusively to [**WMS Premium**](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/WMS-Premium) accounts.

### Use Cases

Use Advanced Backordering when:

- You want to prevent unnecessary splitting of orders if stock is due shortly.
- You need to control whether or not stock is allocated to an order depending on how soon the full quantity will be available.
- You want to automate how backorders are managed, reducing the need for manual decision-making.

These capabilities help:

- Minimise order fragmentation.
- Ensure smarter use of available stock.
- Improve fulfilment timing accuracy.

### Feature Settings

Advanced Backordering includes two key configurable settings.

- Option to prevent splitting orders if stock is due within a set number of days.
- Setting to control stock allocation for Awaiting Stock orders - prevent holding stock for orders that can’t yet be shipped.

These settings can be found within the Customer Settings > **Warehouse Management**> **Sale Order** tab.

#### **1.Automatic Sale Order Splitting on Import - Only Split if No Stock in X Days**

**What it does**This setting lets you delay automatic order splitting if the missing stock is expected to arrive within a configurable number of days. Instead of immediately creating a separate Awaiting Stock Sale Order, the system waits. If the expected arrival date (from a linked Purchase Order) falls within the specified number of days, the order will not split. If no stock is expected within that window, the system will automatically split the order.

**How to access the setting:**

- Navigate to the Customer : Contacts > Customers
- Click Edit
- Go to Warehouse Management > Sale Order tab,
- Under the Sale Order Importing section, scroll down and select the setting, Assign whatever stock is available and move unavailable quantities to a new ‘Awaiting Stock’ Sale Order, but only if stock is not expected to arrive in a configure number of day .
- Enter the Number of days to wait before splitting unassigned stock into a new Sale Order. The date is based on the Expected Arrival Date of any required minimum Purchase Order Product status.
- With this setting selected, the Sale Order will only be split if the stock is not expected within the specified days.
- Click Save

This logic allows you to prevent unnecessary order splits and improve customer experience when stock is already on the way.

#### **2. Automatic Stock Allocation – Only Allocate if All Stock is Available or Expected Soon**

**What it does**This setting controls when CartonCloud will allocate stock to orders in **Awaiting Stock** status. There are two standard options available to all CartonCloud plans:

- Never : when a Purchase Order reaches the minimum Purchase Order Product status no action will be taken.
- Always : when a Purchase Order reaches the minimum Purchase Order Product status the system will attempt to fulfil any Sale Orders waiting for stock of the products on the incoming Purchase Order.

**The two Advanced Backordering options include:**

- Only allocate if all of the stock for the Sale Order is available: when a Purchase Order reaches the minimum Purchase Order Product status, the system will allocate stock to Sale Orders only if the allocation will completely fulfil the Sale Order.
- Only allocate if the remaining stock on an order is expected within the configured number of days: when a Purchase Order reaches the minimum Purchase Order Product status the system will allocate stock to Sale Orders only if the unassigned stock of the Order arrives within X days.

This enables more strategic allocation, ensuring partial orders don't consume stock needed for complete ones.

**How to access the setting:**

- Navigate to the Customer : Contacts > Customers
- Click Edit
- Go to Warehouse Management > Sale Order
- Under Automatic Sale Order Stock Allocation , select one of:
  - Only if all of the stock for the Sale Order is available.
  - Only if the remaining stock on an order is expected within the configured number of days. The date is based on the Expected Arrival Date of any required minimum Purchase Order Product status.
- Enter a value for X days if required.
- Click Save

This provides greater control over stock prioritisation, ensuring that inventory is used most efficiently.

---

<a id="advanced-documents"></a>
## Advanced Documents

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-documents_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to use Documents
- The difference between Advanced and Essentials Documents

Note: All accounts are able to trial Advanced Documents for free until June 2026. After this, only accounts with [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/wms-premium) will maintain Advanced Documents, and all other accounts will switch to Essentials Documents.

For more information on WMS Premium and to upgrade your account, please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

### Purpose

Documents allow mobile and web app users to attach images, video and comments to Purchase Orders as they are received and verified. This enables warehouse workers to provide photo (and video) evidence of received goods, highlighting issues such as damages, and selectively share these with customers. Documents is split into two tiers, Essentials (available in all WMS plans), and Advanced (available through Warehouse Premium).

### How to use Documents

Please see:

- Photos and Documents on Purchase Orders
- Photos and Documents on Sale Orders

### The difference between Advanced and Essentials Documents

Advanced Documents provides additional capability for higher resolution images, significantly increases the number of attachments per document, provides additional storage capacity and adds other timesaving enhancements.

The detailed differences between the two are outlined below:

| **Essentials Documents** | **Advanced Documents** |
| --- | --- |
| Max 6 images per Document | Max 100 images per Document |
| Images are always compressed (POD resolution ~700 kb/image) | Default to full-resolution Compression options available via settings* |
| Max attachment size 1mb | Max attachment size 500mb |
|  | Video support Multi-photo mode |
| Deleted Documents and attachments cannot be restored | Deleted Documents and attachments can be viewed and restored by non-customer roles* |
| 10gb included storage | 100gb included storage |
|  | Image Metadata - date, time and location Information (where available) |

**Multi-photo mode**

Multi-photo mode saves you time by allowing you to rapidly take multiple photos without having to close and reopen the camera.

**Video Support**

Like attaching Photos to documents, videos can also be taken and added to documents.

**Image Metadata**

When uploading an image to a Document on the web app, if date, time and location Metadata is available, it will show against the file.

---

<a id="custom-general-ledger-mapping"></a>
## Custom General Ledger Mapping

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/custom-general-ledger-mapping_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- Prerequisites
- Set Up Steps
  - 1 - Create an Account in CartonCloud
  - 2 - Map a Fee Category to an Account in CartonCloud
  - 3 - Map the Account in CartonCloud to the General Ledger Code for the Accounting Connector
- Examples

### Purpose

Custom General Ledger Mapping allows you to assign charges to custom and existing income Accounts in CartonCloud. These Accounts can also be mapped to the corresponding General Ledger Codes in an Accounting Connector, such as Xero. This enhances income tracking and provides flexibility in charge grouping for invoicing.

### Benefits

- More granular income tracking.
- Greater flexibility in charge grouping for invoicing.
- Improved alignment between Accounts in CartonCloud and the GL codes in the corresponding Accounting Connector.
- Seamless alignment between CartonCloud Accounts and your accounting software.
- Simplified end-of-period reconciliation by ensuring consistent account mapping.
- Real-time visibility into revenue streams by charge type.
- Ability to track profitability by service type or customer segment.
- Streamlined audit preparation with clear account mapping trails.

### Prerequisites

- Custom General Ledger Mapping is only available for [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/WMS-Premium) accounts. For more information please reach out to the team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).
- If mapping Accounts to the Accounting Connector, ensure you have an active Accounting Connector. Please see [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Accounting-Software-Integrations-Accounting-Connectors) for more information.

### Set Up Steps

Fee Categories in CartonCloud are associated with Accounts in CartonCloud. Each Account then needs to be mapped to the appropriate Accounting Connector Account (eg: “200 - Sales” in Xero). This ensures charges are grouped and accounted for under the correct accounts in CartonCloud and the Accounting Connector.

Example:

The Fee Category **Sale Order Urgent Fee**is linked to the CartonCloud Account **Pick Pack Income**, which is mapped to the Xero General Ledger Code**204 - Warehouse Income**.

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-0.png?width=541&height=126&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-0.png)

#### **1 - Create an Account in CartonCloud**

- Navigate to the Accounts page by typing in Accounts in the Search for anything bar. Alternatively, navigate to the Organisation Settings, More > Organisation Settings > Invoice > Accounts .
- Click +Add Account if you wish to create a new Account.

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-1.png?width=670&height=319&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-1.png)

- Enter the below details to create the new Account:
  - Name : Account name.
  - Description: Brief Account description for clarity.
  - Invoice Total Name: The name that will appear on the CartonCloud Invoice Summary to the customer.
  - Display When No Value: If set to No, the Account will not display on the invoice if the amount is $0.

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-2.png?width=670&height=310&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-2.png)

- Click Save .

#### **2 - Map a Fee Category to an Account in CartonCloud**

- Navigate to the Fee Category page by typing Fee Category into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Fee Category you wish to map. Or alternatively, you can create a Fee Category following the instructions here - [Fee Categories.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Charge-Subclasses-Fee-Category)

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-3.png?width=670&height=332&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-3.png)

- From the **Account** drop down, select the Account you wish to associate with the charge.
- Click **Save**.

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-4.png?width=670&height=240&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-4.png)

- The related charges will now appear under the assigned Account.

#### **3 - Map the Account in CartonCloud to the General Ledger Code for the Accounting Connector**

Expand for more...

The Account can be mapped to the Accounting Connector’s General Ledger Codes from the [Organisation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Organisation-Settings-Invoice) or [Customer Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Customer-Settings-Invoice). Mappings created at the Organisation Settings level will be the default for each customer and can then be adjusted at the [Customer Settings level](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Invoice)if customer specific mapping is required.

- Navigate to the Organisation Settings, **More** > **Organisation Settings**.
- Select the **Invoice** tab.
- For the connected Accounting Connector, select **Modify Settings**.

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-5.png?width=670&height=229&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-5.png)

- Match the CartonCloud Account to the respective GL code from the Account Connector.
- Click Save .

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-6.png?width=670&height=335&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-6.png)

### Examples

**Adhoc Charges**

Using Custom General Ledger Mapping you can split specific Adhoc Charges to different GL codes outside of the standard Pick Pack Income Account. For example, if you would like to seperate out Container Pack/Unpack or Pallet Wrapping. In the below examples, they are examples only and the names of the charges, Accounts and

**Pallet Wrapping**

- If you have not yet already created a Pallet Wrapping Adhoc Charge, do so following the process here - Adhoc Charge Setup .
- Create an Account (following Step 1 ) and call it Pallet Wrapping.

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-7.png?width=670&height=247&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-7.png)

- If you have not yet already created a Pallet Wrapping Fee Category, do so following the process here - Fee Categories.
- Map the Fee Category to the Account (following Step 2 ).

![custom-general-ledger-mapping-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-general-ledger-mapping-8.png?width=670&height=234&name=custom-general-ledger-mapping-8.png)

- Map the Pallet Wrapping Account to the General Ledger Code for the Accounting Connector (following Step 3 ).

<a id="advanced-automation-replenishment"></a>
## Replenishment Auto Generation (Advanced Automation)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-automation-replenishment_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to steps
- Checking Automated Replenishment History

### Purpose

Replenishment Auto Generation allows for Replenishments to be automatically generated on a defined schedule. By selecting a Replenishment Template you can then define criteria on when a Replenishment should be created and then what day and time it should be generated. This enables an efficient and streamlined Replenishment process.

### Prerequisites

- Replenishment Auto Generation is included in Advanced Automation, which is only available for WMS Premium accounts. Please reach out to the team here for more information.
- You must first create Replenishment Templates before creating the automation.

### How to steps

- Navigate to the Replenishment page, Warehouse > Replenishments .
- Select the +Add Replenishments button in the top left.

![advanced-automation-replenishment-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-replenishment-0.png?width=670&height=354&name=advanced-automation-replenishment-0.png)

- Select a Replenishment Template from the Prefill Templates. If you have note yet set up a Replenishment Template please do so following the steps here .
- Select Configure Automation.

![advanced-automation-replenishment-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-replenishment-1.png?width=670&height=306&name=advanced-automation-replenishment-1.png)

- Create a schedule for the automated Replenishment to run. This will determine the day and time that CartonCloud will attempt to generate Replenishments using the selected Prefill Templates.
- Click into the Days field and select the days of the week you wish the Wave Pick to run.
- In the Times field click in to select the times on each day selected that the automated Replenishment will run.

![advanced-automation-replenishment-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-replenishment-3.png?width=670&height=283&name=advanced-automation-replenishment-3.png)

- Select Save Schedule .
- Name the automation and click Save .

![advanced-automation-replenishment-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-automation-replenishment-4.png?width=670&height=225&name=advanced-automation-replenishment-4.png)

- You can have multiple schedules running simultaneously for the one Replenishment template. For example, you may have a weekday midday schedule and a weekend afternoon schedule for the one Replenishment template.
- To update an existing schedule, ensure the schedule is selected, make the necessary changes and then click Update Schedule . Note, to update an existing Schedule select Update Schedule and to create a new Schedule select Save Schedule .
- Text will appear listing all of the schedules that will run for the selected Replenishment Template.

### Checking Automated Replenishment History

To check the history of the Automated Replenishments:

- Select More > Bolt Log .
- Within the Bolt Log, the Automated Replenishment history will be displayed.
- The name of the Replenishment Template and the created date of the schedule will display as the name of the log in the history.

---

<a id="wms-premium"></a>
## WMS Premium

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/wms-premium_

### Table of Contents

- What is WMS Premium?
- What features are included in WMS Premium?
- How to get WMS Premium?

### What is WMS Premium?

WMS Premium is a powerful and advanced WMS package designed to elevate growing warehouses. CartonCloud's WMS Premium unlocks premium features such as enhanced automation, greater data analytics, improved security, and dedicated workflows—empowering you to scale your operations effortlessly.

![wms-premium-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/wms-premium-0.png?width=670&height=378&name=wms-premium-0.png)

### What features are included in WMS Premium?

- [Replenishment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Replenishment)s - Pick Smarter, Pick Faster! Set replenishment levels for each product, and keep on top of what needs replenishing. With a range of configurable rules to match your business, the Replenishment add-on takes your warehouse to the next level.
- [Business Intelligence (BI) Dashboard](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Business) - CartonCloud BI insights dashboard enables users to analyse data to make better data-led decisions and strengthen customer relationships by providing your clients with insights into their own business.
- [White Labelling](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Organisation-Settings-White-Labelling) - Provide a seamless brand experience for your customers. With WMS Premium, you can access White Labelling, allowing you to customise your WMS web app design.
- [Enterprise Security](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Organisation-Settings-Security) - Strengthen your security with Single Sign-On (SSO) and Enforced Multi-factor Authentication (MFA). Enterprise Security allows organisations to set up and configure SSO for all users within a particular domain (eg: yourcompany.com), and/or, enforce MFA for user specific user roles.
- [Warehouse Specific Rate Cards](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Customer-Settings-Warehouse) - Warehouse Specific Rate Cards allow you to assign default rate cards per warehouse per customer. This ensures that each warehouse can operate with its own set of rates per customer, streamlining the invoicing process and eliminating the risk of revenue loss due to incorrect rate card usage.
- [Advanced Documents -](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Advanced-Documents) - Deliver high volume, high quality stock images and video to your customers. With Advanced Documents, mobile app users have the ability to attach full resolution images and video to incoming stock reports.
- [Warehouse POD Module](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Warehouse-POD-Setup) - The Warehouse Proof of Delivery (POD) Module gives you access to CartonCloud’s sign on glass functionality from the WMS mobile app. This provides a secure and reliable way in which to sign for pick ups from your warehouse. No more worrying about missing paperwork, you can easily have pick ups signed for electronically and have access to the record when required.
- Advanced Automation - includes Wave Pick Auto Generation and Replenishment Auto Generation which allows you to automatically schedule and run Wave Picks and Replenishments.
- [Custom General Ledger Mapping](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Custom-General-Ledger-Mapping) - allows you to assign charges to custom and existing income Accounts in CartonCloud. These Accounts can also be mapped to the corresponding General Ledger Codes in an Accounting Connector, such as Xero.
- Advanced Backordering - enables advanced Backorder Management workflows with intelligent automation and greater control over stock allocation and order splitting.

### How to get WMS Premium?

For more information on WMS Premium and to upgrade your account please **reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).**
